kannaDa vAkyagaLa 
oLaracane 
Di. en. Sankara bhaT 
bhASA prakASana, Araga, tIrthahaLLi 
bi DA. Di. en Sankara baT. ellA hakkugaLannU kAdiriside. 
KANNADA VAAKYAGALA OLARACANE (The 
structure of Kannada sentences) by D.N.Shankara Bhat, 
Alilabagilu, Araga P.O., Tirthahalli 577 414; phone: 
9449774956. 
E-mail: <bhatdns@rediffmail.com> 
modalaneya accu : 2004 
eraDaneya accu : 2006 
mUraneya accu: 2012 
bi: barahagAra 
horapaDike : 
bhASA prakASana, 
Araga, tIrthahaLLi 
577 417 
hancike : 
atri buk senTar, 
4, SarAvati kaTTaDa, balmaTha, 
mangaLUru 575 001. 
accu : 
SrI Sakti elekTrik pres, 
13nE krAs, jayanagara, 
maysUru 570 014. 
munnuDi 
ippattAru vaSragaLa hinde kannaDa vAkyagaLu: Antarika racane 
mattu  arthavyavasthe  emba  hesarinalli  nannadondu  pustaka 
maysUrina  gItA  buk  havs  mUlaka  prakaTavAgittu.  adaralli 
kannaDa  vAkyagaLa  oLaracaneyannu  hosa  bhASAvijYAnada  dxSTi 
kOnada mUlaka pariSIlisalu prayatnisidde. adannE AdhAravAgirisi 
konDu Iga I hosadondu pustakavannu barediddEne. 
I pustakadalli arthavyavasthegintalU Antarika racanegEnE heccina 
ottu koTTiddEne. idallade, kaLeda ippattaydu vaSragaLalli naDesida 
adhyayana  mattu  samSOdhanegaLa  phalavAgi  kannaDa  vAkyagaLa 
oLaracaneya kuritu halavu hosa viSayagaLannu kanDuhiDididdEne, 
mattu  nannallidda  kelavu  haLeya  vicAragaLu  tappembudannU 
kanDukonDiddEne.  ivannu  baLasidudarindAgi  I  pustaka  haLeyada 
rinda halavu viSayagaLalli bhinnavAgiruvudannu kANabahudu. 
kannaDada  SAstrIya  barahagaLallella  avaSyaviruvallU  illadiru 
vallU  heccu  heccu  samskxta  padagaLannu  baLasuvudarindAgi  avu 
sAmAnyara  kayge  eTukadantAguvudE  jAsti.  kannaDada  vyAkaraNa 
pustakagaLu  kagganTugaLAgalu  idU  ondu  kAraNa.  I  pustakavannu 
bareyuvAga  AdaSTu  maTTige  kannaDada  padagaLannE  baLasuvudara 
mUlaka hELuva viSaya sulabhadalli arthavAguva hAge mADalu 
prayatnisiddEne. 
kannaDada savranAmagaLu 
kannaDa  vAkyagaLa  kuritu  mukhyavendu  tOrida  kelavu  viSaya 
gaLannaSTE  I  pustakadalli  vivarisalu  sAdhyavAgide.  bhASeyembudu 
ondu bahaLa jaTilavAda vyavastheyAgiddu, adara racaneya kuritu 
eSTu  hELidarU  mugiyadaSTu  viSayagaLive.  I  pustakada  prati 
yondu adhyAyada pratiyondu vibhAgada mElU intaha pustaka 
gaLannu  bareyalu  sAdhyavide.  antaha  pustakagaLannu  baredu  kannaDa 
bhASege  ondu  paripUrNavAda  vyAkaraNavannu  siddhapaDisuvalli 
yuva  vidvAmsarige  I  pustaka  porItsAha  koDuvantAgali 
embudE nanna hArayke. 
I  pustakada  hastapratiyannomme  Odi  nODi  tamma  amUlya 
vAda  salahegaLannu  koTTa  geLeya  si.  es.  rAmacandra  avarigU, 
idara  prakaTaNegAgi  anudAna  koTTiruva  maysUrina  bhAratIya 
bhASA  samsthAnakkU,  idara  mudraNadalli  `baraha'  emba  hesarina 
tantrAmSavannu ucitavAgi baLasikoLLalu oppige nIDiruva SESAdri 
vAsu  candraSEkharan  avarigU,  idannu  andavAgi  mudrisi 
koTTiruva  SrI  Sakti  ilekTrik  presna  rA.  SrI.  mOhana  mUtri 
avarigU  mattu  idara  mArATada  hoNe  hottiruva  atri  buk 
senTarina ji. en. aSOkavardhana avarigU nAnu AbhAri. 
maysUru 
mAcra 1, 2004 
Di. en. Sankara bhaT

adhyAya ondu 
pIThike 
1.1 mAtina kelasagaLu 
nAvu namma dinanityada jIvanadalli bEre bEre rItiya `mAtina kelasa' 
gaLannu naDesuvudakkAgi halavAru rItiya vAkyagaLannu baLasuttiruttEve. 
udAharaNegAgi,  tiLidiruva  sangatigaLannu  bEreyavarige  tiLisihELuvu 
dakkAgi keLage (1ka-gha)gaLalli koTTiruvantaha ondu rItiya vAkyagaLannu 
baLasuttEvAdare,  tiLiyade  iruva  sangatigaLannu  kELi  tiLidukoLLuvu 
dakkAgi  (2ka-gha)gaLalli  koTTiruvantaha  avakkinta  bhinnavAgiruva  bEre 
rItiya vAkyagaLannu baLasuttEve. 
rAju maradinda keLage hArida. 
(1kha)  doresvAmi nALe bengaLUrige hOguttAre. 
(1ga)  nanna hattira nUrayvattu rupAyi ide. 
(1gha)  I pustaka nammadu. 
(2ka)  maradinda keLage hAriddu yAru? 
(2kha)  doresvAmi nALe bengaLUrige hOguttArO? 
(2ga)  nimma hattira eSTu haNavide? 
(2gha)  I pustaka nammadO? 
idallade, mADalAgada kelasagaLannu innobbara hattira hELi mADisi 
koLLuvudu,  mADabEkendiruva  kelasagaLannu  mADalu  (avaSyabiddalli) 
innobbara  oppige  kELuvudu,  manassigAgada  kelasavannu  yArAdarU 
mADidalli  avarannu  tegaLuvudu,  manassige  hiDisida  kelasavannu  yArA 
darU  mADidalli  avarannu  hogaLuvudu,  ityAdiyAgi  halavAru 
rItiya  mAtina  kelasagaLannu  nAvu  namma  dinanityada  jIvanadalli  naDesa 
bEkAgiddu, idakkAgiyU nAvu bEre bEre rItiya  vAkyagaLannu baLasa 
ballevu.  
(3ka)  I silinDarannu horage irisi. 
(3kha)  ivattu nAvu bengaLUrige hOgONa. 
(3ga)  A huDugi eSTu cennAgi kuNiyuttiddALe! 
(3gha)  Ake ivattu athavA nALe barabahudu. 
    ondE  ghaTane  illavE  viSayavannu  tiLisuva  vAkyavannU  I  rIti 
bEre  bEre  mAtina  kelasagaLannu  sAdhisuvudakkAgi  baLasalu  sAdhyavide, 
mattu  adakkAgi  A  vAkyadalli  keLage  kANisiruvante  halavAru  rItiya 
badalAvaNegaLannu mADikoLLabEkAguttade. 
rAju pETege hOgiddAne. 
(4kha)  rAju pETege hOgiddAnO? 
rAju pETege hOgirabahudu. 
(4gha)  rAju pETege hOgali. 
(4Ga)  rAju pETege hOguvudu bEDa. 
mEle  koTTiruva  (4ka-Ga)gaLalli  `rAju  pETege  hOguvudu'  emba 
ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  ondE  ondu  vAkyavannu  aydu  bEre  bEre 
`mAtina  kelasa'gaLannu  naDesuvudakkAgi  baLasikoLLalAgideyembudannu 
gamanisabahudu.  (4ka)  vAkya  A  ghaTane  naDedideyendu  tiLisuttade, 
(4kha)  vAkya  adu  naDedideyE  endu  kELuttade,  (4ga)  vAkya  adu 
naDediralu  sAdhya  embudannu  tiLisuttade,  (4gha)  vAkya  adu  naDeyalu 
ADugana oppigeyideyembudannu sUcisuttade, mattu (4Ga) vAkya adu 
naDeyadante taDehAkuttade.  
vAkyagaLa mUlaka naDesalu sAdhyaviruva I halavu rItiya `mAtina 
kelasa'gaLalli  naDediruva  athavA  naDeyaliruva  ghaTanegaLannu  illavE 
sangatigaLannu  innobbarige  tiLisi  hELuvudE  atyanta  prAmukhyavAda 
kelasavendu  hELabahudu.  hAgAgi,  kannaDa  vAkyagaLa  oLaracaneyEnu 
embudannu tiLidukoLLabEkendiruvavaru modalige I rIti bEre bEre 
ghaTanegaLannu  illavE  sangatigaLannu  innobbarige  tiLisihELuvudakkAgi 
entaha  vAkyagaLannu  baLasalAguttade,  mattu  A  vAkyagaLa  oLaracane 
entahadu embudannu tiLidukoLLuvudu oLLeyadu.   
itara  mAtina  kelasagaLannu  naDesuvudakkAgi  baLasuva  vAkyagaLannella 
intaha ghaTane illavE sangatigaLannu tiLisi hELalu baLasuva vAkyagaLalli 
bEre  bEre  rItiya  badalAvaNegaLannu  mADuvudara  mUlaka  sAdhisalu 
sAdhyavide.  hAgAgi,  tiLisi  hELuva  vAkyagaLannu  mUla  vAkyagaLendU 
mattu  itara  vAkyagaLannu  antaha  mUla  vAkyagaLinda  tayArAguva 
`sAdhita'  vAkyagaLendU  kalpisikonDalli  kannaDa  vAkyagaLa  oLaracaneyannu 
tiLidukoLLuva kelasa sulabhavAgaballudu. 
    I  kAraNakkAgi,  mundina  ELu  adhyAyagaLalli  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLa 
oLaracaneyEnembudannu  mAtravE  vivarisi  hELuva  prayatnavannu 
mADalAgide.  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLallU  ondu  ghaTaneyannu  nEravAgi 
tiLisuvavugaLu  mattu  ondu  ghaTaneyalli  toDagiruva  vyakti,  vastu 
modalAdavugaLalli  ondakke  A  ghaTaneyondigiruva  `sambandha'vannu 
tiLisuvavugaLu embudAgi eraDu rItiyavugaLannu kANabahudu.  
rAju bengaLUrige hOda. 
(5kha)  rAju hOdaddu bengaLUrige. 
(5ka)dalli ondu ghaTane naDediruvudannu tiLisalAgide, Adare (5kha)dalli 
bengaLUru  emba  jAgakkU  mattu  A  ghaTanegU  naDuviruva  sambandha 
vannu tiLisalAgide 
idallade,  ghaTane  naDedide  illavE  naDeyalide  embudAgi  sUcisu 
vavugaLu  (5ka)  mattu  adannu  `allagaLe'yuvavugaLu  (5ga)  embu 
dAgiyU  mattu  sangati  ide,  ittu  athavA  iruttade  embudannu 
sUcisuvavugaLu  (5gha)  mattu  adannu  allagaLeyuvavugaLu  (5Ga) 
embudAgiyU bEre eraDu rItiyavannU kANabahudu.  
rAju bengaLUrige hOgalilla. 
(5gha)  rAju bengaLUrinalli iddAne. 
(5Ga)  rAju bengaLUrinalli illa. 
(5ka)dalli tiLisiruva ghaTane naDedillavembudAgi (5ga)dalli A ghaTane 
yannu  allagaLeyalAgide.  (5gha)dalli  ondu  sangatiyannu  tiLisalAgide 
mattu  (5Ga)dalli  adannu  allagaLeyalAgide.  ghaTaneyondige  adara 
ghaTakagaLallondannu  sambandhisuva  mattu  ghaTane,  sangati  illavE 
sambandhagaLannu allagaLeyuva vAkyagaLa oLaracaneyentahadu embudannu 
ombattanE adhyAyadalli vivarisalAgide. 
itara  mAtina  kelasagaLannu  naDesuvudakkAgi  entaha  vAkyagaLannu 
baLasalAguttade  embudannu  mattu  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLinda  antaha  vAkya 
gaLannu  tayArisuva  bage  hEge  embudannu  hattaneya  adhyAyadalli 
vivarisalAgide. I ombattu adhyAyagaLalli (2-10) baruva viSayagaLu 
entahavu  embudannu  keLagina  vibhAgagaLalli  svalpa  cuTukAgi  sUcisa 
1.2 kriyAvAkyagaLu mattu viSayavAkyagaLu 
tiLisuva  vAkyagaLalli  yAvudAdarondu  `ghaTane'yannu  (adu  naDediru 
vudannu  illavE  naDeyaliruvudannu)  tiLisuvavu  mattu  ondu  sangati 
yannu  tiLisuvavu  embudAgi  eraDu  mukhya  vibhAgagaLannu  mADa 
bahudu.  ghaTaneyannu  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLallella  A  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisu 
vudakkAgi  yAvudAdarondu  kriyApada  bandiruva  kAraNa  avannella 
`kriyAvAkya'gaLendu kareyabahudu. 
rAju maradinda keLage hArida. 
(6kha)  obba muduka nimmannu kANalu bandidda. 
(6ga)  doresvAmigaLu nALe bengaLUrige hOguttAre. 
(6gha)  SAmaNNOru nimmannu bahaLa hogaLidaru. 
mEle  (6ka-gha)dalli  bandiruva  vAkyagaLella  kriyAvAkyagaLu.  avu 
hAru,  baru,  hOgu  mattu  hogaLu  emba  kriyApadagaLa  mUlaka 
bEre  bEre  ghaTanegaLu  naDediruvudannu  illavE  naDeyaliruvudannu 
sUcisuttave. 
    sangatiyannu  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLallU  sAmAnyavAgi  ondu  kriyA 
pada bandiruttade. Adare idu intaha ellA vAkyagaLallU iru emba 
ondE  kriyApadavAgiruttade.  hAgAgi  kelavomme  adannu  baLasadiralU 
sAdhyavide.  sangatiyannu  tiLisuva  I  vAkyagaLu  ghaTaneyannu  tiLisuva 
vAkyagaLiginta  halavu  viSayagaLalli  bhinnavAgiruva  kAraNa,  ivannu 
bErondu hesarininda kareyuva avaSyakateyide. I pustakadalli ivannu 
`viSayavAkya'gaLendu kareyalAgide. 
rAjuvina kayyalli ondu haNNide. 
(7kha)  avara mane bahaLa doDDadide. 
(7gha)  A huDuga Odinalli svalpa hinde iddAne. 
SAleya huDugarige ivattu raje ide. 
(7ka-gha)dalli bandiruva vAkyagaLella viSayavAkyagaLu. ivu iru kriyA 
padada  mUlaka  bEre  bEre  rItiya  sangatigaLa  iruvikeyannu  sUcisu 
ttave.  
1.2.1 kriyApadada baLake 
mEle sUcisida hAge, kriyAvAkya mattu viSayavAkyagaLa naDuve kelavu 
prAmukhyavAda  vyatyAsagaLive.  udAharaNegAgi,  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  bEre 
bEre  kriyApadagaLu  kEndragaLAgi  baruttiddu,  avu  vAkyavu  tiLisabEkA 
giruva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuvuvAda  kAraNa,  avakke  heccina  prAmukhyate 
yide.  Adare,  viSayavAkyagaLallella  iru  emba  ondE  kriyApada  baru 
ttiddu,  adu  vAkyada  ghaTakagaLu  oTTAgi  sUcisuva  ondu  sangatiya 
iruvikeyannu  mAtra  tiLisuvudAda  kAraNa  adakke  antaha  mahatvada 
sthAnavilla. 
hAgAgi,  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  baruva  kriyApadavannu  baLasadiruvudu 
kaSTa,  Adare  viSayavAkyagaLalli  baruva  kriyApadavannu  (iru  embu 
dannu)  baLasadiruvudu  sulabha.  sAmAnyavAgi  ondu  sangatiya 
iruvikeya  kuritAgi  heccinadEnannU  hELabEkAgillavAdalli  I  rIti 
antaha viSayavAkyagaLalli kriyApadavannu baLasadiralu sAdhyavide.  
udAharaNegAgi,  ondu  sangati  iruvudu  illavE  iddudu 
yAvAga  embudAgi  adara  samayavannu  bEreyE  ondu  padada 
mUlaka  sUcisalAgideyAdare  (8ka-kha  nODi),  athavA  hAge 
sUcisuva avaSyakateyillavAdare (8ga), antaha sandabhragaLalli viSaya 
vAkyagaLannu iru kriyApadavilladeyU baLasalu sAdhyavide.  
(8ka)  makkaLige ivattu SAlege raje. 
(8kha)   SAmarAyara maneyalli nALe maduve. 
(8ga)   rAjuvina mane bahaLa cikkadu.   
(8ka)  mattu  (8kha)  vAkyagaLu  sangatigaLannu  tiLisuttiddu,  A  sangatigaLa 
samayavannu  ivattu  mattu  nALe  emba  padagaLa  mUlaka 
sUcisalAgide.  hAgAgi,  I  vAkyagaLalli  iru  padavannu  baLasuva 
avaSyakateyilla. idE rItiyalli (8ga) vAkyavu hindina mattu mundina 
samayagaLeraDakkU  sambandhisiruva  sangatiyondannu  tiLisuttideyAda 
kAraNa, adarallU iru padavannu baLasuva avaSyakateyilla. 
1.2.2 samaya sUcaneyalli vyatyAsa  
kriyAvAkya  mattu  viSayavAkyagaLa  naDuve  avu  sUcisuva  samaya 
bhEdadallU  vyatyAsavide.  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  baruva  kriyApadagaLu 
`hindinavu'  mattu  `mundinavu'  embudAgi  avu  tiLisuva  ghaTanegaLa 
kuritAgi  eraDu  rItiya  samayagaLannu  mAtra  sUcisaballuvu.  Adare 
idakke badalAgi, viSayavAkyagaLalli baruva iru kriyApada `hindinavu', 
`Iginavu'  mattu  `mundinavu'  embudAgi  avu  tiLisuva  sangatigaLa 
kuritAgi mUru bEre bEre samayagaLannu sUcisaballuvu.  
rAju marakke hattida. 
(9kha)  rAju marakke hattuttAne. 
(10ka)  Akege nimma mEle bahaLa kOpa ittu. 
(10kha) Akege nimma mEle bahaLa kOpa ide. 
(10ga)  Akege  nimma  mEle  (nALe  bhETige  hOguvAga)  bahaLa 
kOpa iruttade. 
kannaDadalli  iru  kriyApadakke  ittu,  ide  mattu  iruttade  emba 
mUru  kriyArUpagaLiddu,  avannu  baLasi  tayArisuva  viSayavAkyagaLu 
hindina  sangati,  Igina  sangati  mattu  mundina  sangati  embudAgi 
mUru  samayagaLalli  kANisikoLLuva  sangatigaLannu  sUcisaballuvu 
embudannu (10ka-ga) vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu.  
Adare kannaDada itara kriyApadagaLige hindina mattu mundina emba 
eraDu  samayagaLannu  sUcisuva  rUpagaLu  mAtra  iveyAda  kAraNa, 
avu  `hindina  ghaTane'’mattu  `mundina  ghaTane'’embudAgi  eraDu 
samayagaLalli kANisikoLLuva ghaTanegaLannu mAtra sUcisaballuvu.  
udAharaNegAgi, 
vAkyagaLalli  bandiruva  hattu 
kriyApadakke  hattida  mattu  hattuttAne  emba  eraDu  samayagaLannu 
sUcisuva  rUpagaLu  mAtra  ive.  hAgAgi  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  mAtina 
samayakkinta  modalu  naDeda  hattuvike  mattu  mAtina  samayada 
anantara naDeyuva hattuvike embudAgi hattuvikeyalli eraDu rItiya 
samayabhEdavannu mAtra I kriyApadada mUlaka nEravAgi sUcisalu 
sAdhya.  
viSiSTavAgi  ondu  ghaTane  mAtanADuva  samayadallEnE  naDeyu 
ttide embudAgi adara samayavannu sUcisabEkAdAga, kannaDadalli keLage 
(9ga)dalli  kANisiruva  hAge  kriyApadavannu  iru  embudara  Igina 
samayavannu  sUcisuva  rUpadondige  sErisi  baLasabEkAguttade.  (I 
(9ga)  vAkyakke  rUDhiyalliruva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  innondu 
arthavU ideyembudannu munde nODaliruvevu). 
rAju marakke hattuttiddAne. 
1.2.3 eraDara naDuvina sambandha 
kriyAvAkya  mattu  viSayavAkyagaLu  I  rIti  ondarindondu  bhinna 
vAgiveyAdarU  avugaLa  naDuve  hattirada  sambandhavide.  sAmAnyavAgi 
eraDu  viSayavAkyagaLu  tiLisuva  sangatigaLannu  ondu  kriyAvAkya 
sambandhisaballudu.  
(11ka)  rAju marada keLagiddAne. 
(11kha) rAju marada mEliddAne. 
(11ga)  rAju marakke hattida. 
(11ka-kha)gaLu viSayavAkyagaLu. avu eraDu bEre bEre sangatigaLannu 
tiLisuttave.  Adare,  (11ga)  ondu  kriyAvAkya.  adu  I  eraDu 
sangatigaLannu  sambandhisuttade.  adu  tiLisuva  ghaTaneyindAgi  (11ka) 
tiLisuva  sangati  (11kha)  tiLisuva  sangatiyAgi  badalAgide  endu 
hELabahudu. 
    I  rIti  kriyAvAkya  mattu  viSayavAkyagaLu  ondakkondu 
sambandhisiveyAdarU  avugaLa  naDuve  halavu  vyatyAsagaLiveyAda 
kAraNa,  kriyAvAkyagaLa  oLaracaneyannu  eraDaneya  adhyAyadallU 
mattu  viSayavAkyagaLa  oLaracaneyannu  mUraneya  adhyAyadallU 
vivarisa lAgide. 
1.3 vAkyada ghaTakagaLu 
mEle  vivarisiruva  eraDu  rItiya  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLallU  kEndrasthAna 
dalli  ondu  kriyApada  baruttade.  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  idu  A  vAkyagaLu 
tiLisuva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuttade  mattu  viSayavAkyagaLalli  avu 
tiLisuva  sangatiya  iruvikeyannu  sUcisuttade.  I  kEndradondige 
ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyalli  toDagikonDiruva  vyakti,  vastu,  viSaya 
modalAdavugaLannu  gurutisuvudakkAgi  I  vAkyagaLalli  kelavu  `ghaTaka' 
gaLU bandiruttave. udAharaNegAgi keLagina eraDu vAkyagaLannu gamanisa 
bahudu. 
(12ka)  rAju bekkige hAlu kuDisida. 
(12kha) I pustakakke kempu baNNada taTTi ide. 
(12ka)dalli  koTTiruva  kriyAvAkyadalli  kuDisida  emba  kriyApada 
mAtravallade  rAju,  bekkige  mattu  hAlu  emba  mUru  ghaTakagaLu 
bandive. I ghaTakagaLu kuDisuva ghaTanege sambandhisiruva mUru vyakti, 
prANi mattu vastugaLannu sUcisuttive.  
idE  rItiyalli  (12kha)dalli  koTTiruva  viSayavAkyadalli  ide 
kriyApada mAtravallade, I pustakakke mattu kempu baNNada taTTi emba 
eraDu  ghaTakagaLu  bandiddu,  avu  I  vAkya  tiLisuva  sangatige 
sambandhisiruva vastu mattu adara guNadharmagaLannu sUcisuttave. 
   ondu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyalli  toDagikonDiruva  vyakti,  vastu 
modalAduvannu  gurutisuva  ghaTakagaLa  tayArikeyalli  pada  mattu 
padakante  embudAgi  eraDu  maTTagaLalli  baruva  vAkyAngagaLu  baLake 
yAguttave.    ivugaLalli  modalaneyadu  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu 
`hesarisuva'  mUlaka  gurutisuttade  mattu  eraDaneyadu  avannE 
`varNisuva'  mUlaka  gurutisuttade.  I  eraDu  rItiya  vAkyAngagaLa 
baLakeyentahadu embudannu nAlkaneya adhyAyadalli vivarisalAgide. 
1.3.1 mukhyavAda mattu mukhyavallada ghaTakagaLu 
vAkyada kriyApadadondige baruva I ghaTakagaLu adu tiLisuva ghaTanege 
bEre  bEre  rItiyalli  sambandhisiruva  vyakti,  vastu,  viSaya  modalA 
davugaLannu sUcisuttave. ivannu mukhya ghaTakagaLu mattu mukhyavallada 
ghaTakagaLu embudAgi vingaDisi hELalu sAdhyavide. 
    sAmAnyavAgi  ondu  vAkyada  kEndravAgiruva  kriyApadada  svarUpa 
mattu  guNadharmagaLannavalambisi  baruva  ghaTakagaLannu  adara  mukhya 
ghaTakagaLendu  kareyabahudu.  udAharaNegAgi,  bILu  kriyApadaviruva 
ondu vAkyadalli obba vyaktiyannu (illavE ondu vastuvannu) sUcisu 
vantaha  ondE  ondu  mukhya  ghaTaka  mAtra  baruttade.  yAkendare, 
bILuva  ghaTanege  obba  vyakti  illavE  ondu  vastu  mAtravE  sambandhi 
siralu sAdhya.  
(13ka)  surESa bidda. 
(13kha) koDa bittu. 
Adare,  bILisu  kriyApadaviruva  vAkyadalli  ibbaru  vyaktigaLannu 
(illavE  obba  vyakti  mattu  ondu  vastuvannu)  sUcisabEkAguvudAda 
kAraNa,  adarondige  eraDu  mukhya  ghaTakagaLannu  baLasuva  avaSyakate 
yide. yAkendare, `bILisuva ghaTane'ge `bILuva vyakti (illavE vastu)' 
mAtravallade, `bILisuvantaha innondu vyakti'yU sambandhisiruttade.  
(14ka)  jAnaki surESanannu bILisidaLu. 
(14kha) jAnaki koDavannu bILisidaLu. 
eraDakkinta  jAsti  mukhya  ghaTakagaLu  bEkAguva  kriyApadagaLU 
kannaDadallive.  udAharaNegAgi,  koDu  kriyApadaviruva  vAkyadalli 
`koDuva  vyakti',  `koDuva  vastu'  mattu  `koTTudannu  paDeyuva  vyakti' 
embudAgi  mUru  vyakti  mattu  vastugaLannu  sUcisuva  ghaTakagaLannu 
baLasabEkAguttade. idE rItiyalli tinnisu kriyApadaviruva vAkyadalli 
`tinnisidavaru  yAru',  `tinnisiddu  yArige'  mattu  `tinnisiddu  Enannu' 
emba mUru praSnegaLige uttara koDaballa mUru ghaTakagaLannu baLasuva 
avaSyakateyide. 
(15ka)  rangEgavDaru ettugaLannu karImanige koTTaru. 
(15kha) sItAbAyi makkaLige tinDi tinnisidaLu. 
I  rIti  vAkyavondaralli  eSTu  mukhya  ghaTakagaLu  baruttave 
embudu  mAtravalla,  entaha  mukhya  ghaTakagaLu  baruttave  embudU 
vAkyada  kriyApada  entahadu  embudannavalambiside.  udAharaNegAgi, 
hOgu kriyApadaviruva vAkyadalli `hOguva vyakti' mattu `hOguva 
jAga'  embudAgi  obba  vyaktiyannu  mattu  ondu  jAgavannu  sUcisuva 
ghaTakagaLu  barabEkAguttadAdare,  mare  kriyApadaviruva  vAkyadalli 
`mareta vyakti' mattu `mareta viSaya' embudAgi obba vyaktiyannu mattu 
ondu viSayavannu sUcisuva ghaTakagaLu barabEkAguttade.  
(16ka)  rAju bengaLUrige hOda. 
(16kha) rAju Akeyannu maretiddAne. 
kriyAvAkyagaLalli I rIti kriyApadada svarUpavannavalambisi baruva 
mukhya  ghaTakagaLu  mAtravallade  bEre  kelavu  mukhyavallada  ghaTakagaLU 
baraballuvu. intaha mukhyavallada ghaTakagaLu ellA vAkyagaLigU samAna 
vAgiddu,  A  vAkyagaLu  tiLisuva  ghaTaneya  samaya,  jAga,  kAraNa, 
uddESa, modalAduvannu sUcisuttave.  
(17ka)  rAju bengaLUrige raylinalli hOda. 
(17kha) Ake bisilinalli happaLa oNagisidaLu. 
(17ga)  vatsalA sOmavAra ondu sinemA nODiddaLu. 
(17gha) Ata maNNinalli ondu gombe mADida. 
(17Ga) rAju hariyondige pETege hOda. 
mElina  vAkyagaLalli  raylinalli,  bisilinalli,  sOmavAra,  maNNinalli 
mattu  hariyondige  emba  mukhyavallada  ghaTakagaLu  bandiruvudannu 
gamanisabahudu.  ivu  heccu  kaDime  ellA  rItiya  vAkyagaLallU 
baraballa jAga, samaya, jotegAra modalAdavugaLannu sUcisuttave. 
    sangatiyannu  sUcisuva  viSayavAkyagaLallU  idE  rItiyalli 
mukhyavAda  mattu  mukhyavallada  ghaTakagaLu  baraballuvu.  viSayavAkya 
gaLallella  iru  emba  ondE  kriyApada  baruvudAda  kAraNa,  avugaLa 
llella  eraDeraDu  mukhya  ghaTakagaLu  baruttave.  Adare  avu  sUcisuva 
sangatiya  svarUpavannAdharisi,  I  ghaTakagaLu  bEre  bEre  rUpadalli 
baruttiddu, vastu, jAga, guNadharma modalAduvannu sUcisuttave. 
(18ka)  ivattu beLigge A TAnkiyalli ondu heNa ittu. 
(18kha) nArAyaNasvAmiya tale nuNNagide. 
(18ga)  I mudukanige nUru muDi gaddeyide. 
(18ka)  vAkyadalli  A  TAnkiyalli  embudu  ondu  jAgavannU  mattu 
ondu  heNa  embudu  ondu  vastuvannU  sUcisuvudakkAgi  bandiruva 
eraDu  mukhya  ghaTakagaLu.  ivu  oTTAgi  yAva  jAgadalli  yAva  vastu 
vide  emba  sangatiyannu  tiLisuttave.  I  vAkyadalli  I  eraDu  mukhya 
ghaTakagaLu  mAtravallade  sangatiya  samayavannu  sUcisuva  ivattu 
beLigge  emba  ondu  mukhyavallada  ghaTakavU  ide.  idu  ittu 
kriyApada 
kuritAgi  heccina  vivaragaLannu 
odagisuttade. 
    I  rIti  (18ka)  vAkya  ondu  jAgadalli  vastuvondara  iruvike 
yannu  sUcisuvudAdare,  (18kha)  vAkya  ondu  vastuvina  (nArAyaNa 
svAmiya  taleya)  guNadharmavondannu  (nuNNage  embudAgi)  tiLisu 
ttade,  mattu  (18ga)  vAkya  obba  vyaktigU  (I  mudukanigU)  mattu 
ondu vastuvigU (nUru muDi gaddegU) naDuve ondu sambandha ide 
embudannu tiLisuttade.  
sUcisuva 
samayada 
    I  mUru  rItiya  vAkyagaLalli  baruva  mukhya  ghaTakagaLa  naDuve 
kANisuva  vyatyAsagaLige  avu  sUcisuva  sangatigaLa  naDuviruva  vyatyAsa 
gaLE kAraNa. 
1.3.2 vibhakti pratyayagaLa baLake 
vAkyavondaralli  ondakkinta  jAsti  ghaTakagaLu  bandAga  avu  yAva 
rItiyalli  kriyApadadondige 
(endare  kriyApada 
sUcisuva  ghaTaneyalli  avu  hEge  toDagikonDive)  embudannu  tiLisu 
vudakkAgi avugaLondige vibhakti pratyayagaLannu illavE itara padagaLannu 
baLasabEkAguttade.  udAharaNegAgi,  keLage  koTTiruva  vAkyagaLannu 
gamanisabahudu. 
sambandhisive 
(19ka)  rAju hariyannu dUDida. 
(19kha) rAjuvannu hari dUDida. 
(19ka-kha)vAkyagaLalli  dUDu  kriyApadadondige  eraDu  bEre  bEre 
vyaktigaLannu  sUcisuva  rAju  mattu  hari  emba  ghaTakagaLu  bandive. 
ivugaLalli  ondannu  (endare  dUDuva  vyaktiyannu  sUcisuva  ghaTaka 
vannu)  yAva  vibhakti  pratyayavU  illade  hAgeyE  baLasalAgide  mattu 
innondannu  (endare  dUDalpaDuva  vyaktiyannu  sUcisuva  ghaTakavannu) 
annu emba vibhakti pratyayadondige baLasalAgide.  
    dUDuva  vyakti  (19ka)dalli  rAju  ghaTaka  mattu  (19ka)dalli  hari 
ghaTaka;  hAgAgi  iveraDU  vibhakti  pratyayavillade  bandive.  dUDalpaDuva 
vyakti (19ka)dalli hari ghaTaka mattu (19kha)dalli rAju ghaTaka; hAgAgi 
iveraDU annu pratyayadondige bandive. 
    I  rIti  ghaTakagaLigU  mattu  kriyApadakkU  naDuviruva  sambandha           
gaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  kannaDadalli  keLage  koTTiruva  nAlku  vibhakti  
pratyayagaLu baLakeyAguttave. 
bAdhita: annu (ghaTaneyinda bAdhitavAguva vyakti illavE vastu). 
suru: inda (ghaTane suruvAguva jAga). 
kone: ge (ghaTane konegoLLuva jAga). 
jAga: alli (ghaTaneya jAga). 
    I  nAlku  vibhakti  pratyayagaLa  mukhya  baLakegaLannu  keLagina  vAkya 
gaLalli kANabahudu. 
(20ka)  avaru A huDuganannu dUDidaru. 
(20kha)  avaru maneyinda horaTiddAre. 
(20ga)  avaru manege talapiddAre. 
(20gha)  avaru angaLadalli hADuttiddAre. 
    I  nAlku  mukhya  baLakegaLu  mAtravallade  bEreyU  halavu 
baLakegaLu  I  pratyayagaLigiddu  avu  sandabhrakkanusAravAgi  bEre  bEre 
rItiya  sambandhagaLannu  sUcisaballuvu  embudannu  keLagina  vAkyagaLalli 
kANabahudu. 
(21ka)  manOharanige Aru mandi huDugiyariddAre. 
(21kha) rangaNNa koDaliyinda marada gellugaLannu kaDida. 
(21ka)dalli  ge  pratyaya  manOharanigU  mattu  Aru  mandi  huDugi 
yarigU  naDuviruva  sambandhavannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  baLakeyAgide 
mattu  (21kha)dalli  inda  pratyaya  kaDiyuva  ghaTaneyalli  toDagisa 
lAgiruva  sAdhanavondannu  sUcisalu  baLakeyAgide.  intaha  heccina 
baLakegaLannella  mEle  sUcisiruva  mukhya  baLakegaLinda  sAdhisalu 
sAdhyavide embudannu eraDanE adhyAyadalli nODaliruvevu. 
1.3.3 eraDu rItiya sambandhagaLu 
vAkyada  mukhya  kriyApadakkU  mattu  adara  ghaTakagaLigU  naDuviruva 
sambandhavannu  mEle  sUcisida  hAge  vibhakti  pratyayagaLa  mUlaka 
tiLisalAguttade. intaha sambandhagaLu vAkyada arthakke sambandhisiveyAda 
kAraNa,  avannu  `artha'  sambandhagaLendu  kareyabahudu.  intaha 
sambandhagaLu  mAtravallade,  vAkyada  ghaTakagaLigU  mattu  mAtina 
sannivESakkU naDuve kANisuvantaha bEre kelavu sambandhagaLU ive. 
    udAharaNegAgi, ondu vAkyada mUlaka kELuganige tiLidiruvantaha 
ondu  viSayada  kuritAgi  ADuga  EnAdarondu  suddiyannu  tiLisuttira 
bahudu.  kannaDadalli  tiLidiruva  amSavannu  vAkyadalli  modalu  sUcisa 
lAguttade, mattu adakke sambandhisida suddiyannu anantara sUcisalAgu 
(22ka)  rAjuvannu surESa karediddAne. 
(22kha) surESa rAjuvannu karediddAne. 
(22ka)dalli  rAju  ghaTaka  modalu  bandide,  mattu  (22kha)dalli 
surESa  ghaTaka  modalu  bandide.  I  kAraNakkAgi  (22ka)dalli  ondu 
suddiyannu  rAjuvina  kuritAgi  tiLisalAgide  mattu  (22kha)dalli 
surESana kuritAgi tiLisalAgide. 
    intaha  suddigaLallU  yAvudAdarU  ondu  amSa  uLiduvakkinta 
prAmukhyavAgiralu  sAdhyavide.  kannaDadalli  sAmAnyavAgi  kriyApadada 
eDakke  baruva  amSa  uLida  amSagaLiginta  mukhyavAdudAgiruttade. 
udAharaNegAgi, keLage koTTiruva vAkyagaLalli nimma pustaka embudu 
(23ka)dallU mattu nanage embudu (23kha)dallU mukhya amSagaLAgi 
bandive. 
(23ka)  avaLu nanage nimma pustaka koTTiddALe. 
(23kha) avaLu nimma pustakavannu nanage koTTiddALe. 
    vAkyada ghaTakagaLigU  mattu mAtina sannivESakkU naDuve kANisuva 
intaha sambandhagaLannu `vyavahAra' sambandhagaLendu kareyabahudu. ivu 
gaLa  kuritAgi  heccina  vivaragaLannu  eraDaneya  adhyAyada  (2.7)nE 
vibhAgadalli kANabahudu. 
1.4 guNapadagaLa baLake 
mEle vivarisida hAge, vAkyavondaralli adara mukhya angavAgi ondu 
kriyApadavannU  mattu  A  kriyApada  sUcisuva  ghaTane  illavE  sangati 
yalli toDagiruva vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu sUcisuvudakkAgi bEre 
bEre  rItiya  ghaTakagaLannU  baLasuvudu  mAtravallade,  ghaTaneya  guNa 
dharmagaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  kelavu  guNapadagaLannU  baLasalu  sAdhya 
(24ka)  avaru kaLLanige cannAgi hoDedaru. 
(24kha) A huDuga bencina mEle neTTage nintiddAne. 
(24ga)  oleyalli nIru katakatane kudiyuttittu. 
(24gha) avanu gaDagaDa naDugida. 
(24ka)dalli cannAgi guNapada hoDedudu hEge embudannu tiLisuttade, 
mattu  (24ga)dalli  katakatane  guNapada  kudiyuvudu  hEge  embudannu 
tiLisuttade. 
    ghaTaneya jAga mattu samayagaLannu sUcisuvudakkAgi ghaTakagaLannu 
baLasuva badalu guNapadagaLannu baLasalU sAdhyavide. 
(25ka)  avanu nALe bengaLUrige hOguttAne. 
(25kha) avanannu alli yArU mAtanADisalilla. 
(25ka)dalli  nALe  guNapada  hOguva  ghaTaneya  samayavannU  mattu 
(25kha)dalli  alli  guNapada  (pratinAma)  mAtanADisadidda  jAgavannU 
sUcisuttave. 
    vAkyadalli kriyApadadondige baruva ghaTakagaLu mattu guNapadagaLu 
-  iveraDU  heccu  kaDime  ondE  rItiya  kelasagaLannu  naDesabEkAgide. 
hAgAgi,  avugaLa  naDuvina  vyatyAsa  aSTondu  kaTTuniTTinadEnalla. 
ghaTaneya kuritAgi kriyApada tiLisadiruva kelavu sangatigaLannu, illavE 
ghaTaneya  guNadharmagaLannu  avu  tiLisuttave.  idallade  vAkyada  kone 
yalli  baruva  kriyArUpadalli  kelavu  pratyayagaLa  mUlaka  cuTukAgi 
tiLisiruva  sangatigaLa  kuritAgiyU  ivu  heccina  vivaragaLannu  odagisu 
ttave  (guNapadagaLa  kuritu  heccina  vivaragaLige  Araneya  adhyAyavannu 
nODabahudu). 
1.5 oLavAkyagaLa baLake 
ghaTakagaLa  tayArikeyalli  padagaLannu  mAtravallade  iDI  vAkyagaLannE 
baLasalU  sAdhyavide.  ivu  nEravAgi  ondu  ghaTakada  jAgadalli  bara 
bahudu illavE ondu ghaTakada angavAgi barabahudu.  I rItiyAgi 
bErondu  vAkyada  angavAgi  baruva  vAkyagaLannu  `oLavAkya'gaLendu 
kareyabahudu. 
(26ka)  avanu ellige hOgiddAnO gottilla. 
(26kha) rAju iruva Urinalli Iga bhArI maLe. 
(26ka)dalli  avanu  ellige  hOgiddAne  emba  vAkya  oLavAkyavAgi 
bandide  mattu  idakkAgi  adakke  O  pratyayavannu  sErisalAgide.  idakke 
badalu  (26kha)dalli  rAju  (ondu  Urinalli)  iddAne  emba  vAkya 
ondu  ghaTakada  angavAgi  bandide  mattu  idakkAgi  adakke  a 
pratyayavannu sErisalAgide mattu adaralli bandiruva ondu Urinalli 
emba  ghaTakavannu  (adu  horavAkyadallU  baruva  kAraNa)  tegedu 
hAkalAgide. 
    ondu vAkyavannu bErondu vAkyada ghaTakavannAgi illavE ghaTakada 
angavannAgi  mADalu  entaha  vidhAnagaLannella  baLasabahudu  embudannu 
ELaneya adhyAyadalli vivarisalAgide. 
mattu 
Sarattu  embudAgi 
1.6 vAkyagaLa jODaNe 
I  rIti  ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyada  angavannAgi  mADuva 
badalu eraDu vAkyagaLannu jODisi hELalU sAdhyavide. hIge jODisi 
hELabEkAdalli  avu  sUcisuva  ghaTane  illavE  sangatigaLa  naDuve 
yAvu dAdarU ondu rItiya sambandhaviruvudu avaSya. mukhyavAgi 
kUDike,  badali 
mUru  rItiya 
sambandhagaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  I  rIti  vAkyagaLeraDannu  jODisi 
hELalAguttade. 
    kUDikeya  sambandhadalli  vAkyagaLeraDu  sUcisuva  ghaTane  illavE 
sangatigaLannu  sErisi  hELalAguttade.  idakkAgi  modalaneya  vAkyada 
koneyalli  mattu  padavannu  baLasabahudu  illavE  eraDara  kone 
yallU U pratyayavannu baLasabahudu. idallade, modalaneya vAkyada 
koneyalli  jODisuva  kriyArUpavannu  baLasuvudemba  mUraneya 
vidhAnavU kannaDadalli baLakeyallide. 
(27ka)  rAju manege hOda mattu snAna mADida. 
(27kha) rAju manegU hOda, snAnavannU mADida. 
(27ga)  rAju manege hOgi snAna mADida. 
(27ka)dalli mattu padada mUlaka eraDu vAkyagaLannu jODisalAgide 
mattu (27kha)dalli eraDu vAkyagaLallU U pratyayavannu baLasuvudara 
mUlaka  avannu  jODisalAgide.  (27ga)dalli  modalaneya  vAkyavannu 
adara kriyApadada hOgi emba jODisuva rUpada mUlaka eraDane 
yadarondige jODisalAgide. 
    badali  sambandhada  mUlaka  jODisiruva  vAkyagaLalli  averaDu 
sUcisuva  ghaTane  illavE  sangatigaLalli  ondu  mAtra  svIkxtavAga 
bEkendiruttade.  idakkAgi  modalaneya  vAkyada  koneyalli  illavE 
emba  padavannu  baLasuva  krama  kannaDadallide.  samskxtadinda  eravalAgi 
banda athavA emba padavU intaha jODaNeyalli baLakeyallide. 
manege 
hOgiddAne,  illavE  allellO 
aDagiddAne. 
(28kha) avarigondu kucri koDi athavA illige barahELi. 
    Sarattina  sambandhadalli  ondu  vAkya  sUcisuva  ghaTane  illavE 
sangati  innondu  vAkya  sUcisuva  ghaTane  illavE  sangatige  Sarattu

(29ka)  rAju bEgane bandare namage manege hOgabahudu. 
(29kha) rAju bEgane bandiddare namage manege hOgabahudittu. 
    vAkyagaLannu  jODisuvudakkAgi  mEle  koTTiruva  vidhAnagaLannu 
hEge  baLasalAguttade  embudannu  enTaneya  adhyAyadalli  vivarisa 
1.7 kannaDada kelavu vaySiSTyagaLu 
mEle  sUcisiruva  hAge,  I  pustakada  eraDaneya  adhyAyadinda 
hattaneya  adhyAyada  varegina  bhAgadalli  mukhyavAgi  kannaDa  vAkyagaLa 
racaneyentahadu embudannu vivarisalAgide. pustakada koneyalli baruva 
hannondaneya  adhyAyadalli  kannaDakkU  mattu  prapancada  itara 
bhASegaLigU  naDuve  vAkyaracaneyalli  entaha  vyatyAsagaLella  ive 
embudannu svalpa cuTukAgi prastApisalAgide. 
    vAkyagaLa oLaracaneyalli kannaDa bhASe prapancada itara bhASegaLinda 
halavu  rItiyalli  bhinnavAgide.  kannaDakkU  mattu  jagattina  itara  bhASe 
gaLigU  naDuve  kANisuva  I  vyatyAsagaLige  mukhyavAgi  eraDu  kAraNa 
gaLive.  
    tamiLu,  telugu,  malayALa,  tuLu  modalAda  itara  drAviDa 
bhASegaLigU  mattu kannaDakkU naDuve kANisuva  vyatyAsagaLige I ellA 
bhASegaLU  mUla  drAviDa  bhASeyondarinda  pratyEkavAguttiruvante 
avugaLalli  bEre  bEre  rItiya  badalAvaNegaLu  naDediruvudu  kAraNa. 
hosa  hosa  mAtina  sannivESagaLige  hondikoLLuvudakkAgi  bhASegaLalli 
intaha  badalAvaNegaLu  naDeyuttiruvudu  atyavaSya.  ivugaLa  mUlaka 
bhASegaLu tamma jIvantikeyannu uLisikoLLuttave.  
    drAviDa bhASAkuTumbakke sErade iruva jagattina itara bhASegaLigU 
mattu  kannaDakkU  naDuve  kANisuva  vyatyAsagaLige  prAmukhyavAgi  A 
bhASegaLu vAkyaracaneya niyamagaLannu bEre bEre mUla bhASegaLinda 
paDediruvudE kAraNa. I pustakada koneya (hannondaneya) adhyAya 
dalli  intaha  kelavu  vyatyAsagaLannu  pariSIlisalAgide.  ivu  bhASegaLu 
vikasanagoLLuva  samayadalli  edurAgidda  samasyegaLige  I  mUla 
bhASegaLu kanDukonDidda bEre bEre parihAragaLannu sUcisuttave.     
    kannaDakkU mattu prapancada itara bhASegaLigU naDuve kANisuva I 
vyatyAsagaLu  vAkyaracaneyalli  kannaDada  (mattu  itara  drAviDa  bhASegaLa) 
koDuge  entahadu  embudannu  sUcisuttave.  ivannu  kannaDada  vyAkaraNa 
sampattendu parigaNisabahudu.

adhyAya eraDu 
kriyAvAkyagaLa oLaracane 
2.1 pIThike 
kannaDada  kriyAvAkyagaLallella  ondu  kriyApada  bandiddu,  adu  vAkyada 
mukhya  angavAgiruttade.  I  kriyApada  sAmAnyavAgi  vAkyada  kone 
yalli baruttade. udA: 
rAju kannaDakavannu ellA kaDeyallU huDukida. 
(1kha)  sItAbAyi nALe Dillige hOguttALe. 
(1ga)  Akege lATariyalli hattu lakSada bahumAna bantu. 
(1gha)  huDugaru marakke hattidaru. 
mEle  koTTiruva  (1ka-gha)  vAkyagaLella  kriyAvAkyagaLAgiddu,  avugaLa 
mukhya angagaLAgi huDuku, hOgu, baru mattu hattu emba kriyA 
padagaLu A vAkyagaLa koneyalli bandive. ivugaLondige I vAkyagaLalli 
bEre kelavu padagaLU bandiveyAdarU avu kriyApadadaSTu prAmukhya 
vAduvalla.  I  itara  padagaLalli  yAvudannu  bEkiddarU  sandabhra 
kkanusAravAgi  baLasadiralu  sAdhyavide.  Adare  kriyApadavannu  A  rIti 
baLasadiruvudu bahaLa aparUpa. 
rAju kannaDaka huDukida. 
(2kha)  sItAbAyi nALe hOguttALe. 
(2ga)  sItAbAyi Dellige hOguttALe. 
(2gha)  Akege bahumAna bantu. 
(1ka)  vAkyadalli  jAgavannu  sUcisalu  bandiruva  ellA  kaDegaLallU 
embudannu  baLasadiralu  sAdhya  embudannu  (2ka)dalli  kANabahudu. 
idE  rItiyalli  (1kha)dalli  bandiruva  nALe  illavE  Dellige  emba 
pada  gaLannu  baLasadiralu  sAdhya  embudannu  (2kha-ga)  vAkyagaLalli  kANa 
bahudu. Adare kriyApadavannu I rIti baLasalillavAdare A vAkyavinnU 
konegonDillavEnO  endenisuttade,  illavE  adondu  viSayavAkya 
vAgibiDuttade. 
(3ka)  sItAbAyi nALe Dellige. 
(3kha)  huDugaru maradalli. 
(3ka)dalli hOguttALe emba kriyApadavannu biDalAgide. Adare idu 
nijakkU  ondu  ghaTaneyannu  tiLisuva  kriyAvAkyavAgi  kANisuva  badalu 
sItAbAyiya  kAryakramagaLannu  sUcisuva  paTTiya  ondu  angavAgi 
kANisuttade.  (3kha)dalli  kuLitiddAre  emba  kriyApada  bidduhOgide 
endu  hELuvudakkintalU  iddAre  emba  bErondu  kriyApada  biddu 
hOgide  (endare  adondu  viSayavAkya)  endu  hELuvudE  sari 
yendu tOruttade (3.2.3 nODi). 
2.1.1 kriyApadada pratyayagaLu 
intaha  vAkyagaLalli  baruva  kriyApada  I  rIti  ondu  ghaTaneyannu 
tiLisuvudu  mAtravallade,  ADugana  samayakke  sambandhisidante  A 
ghaTaneya  samayavannU  sUcisuttade,  mattu  A  ghaTaneyalli  nirata 
rAgiruva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLalli  ondannU  sUcisuttade.  I 
eraDu  kelasagaLannu  naDesuvudakkAgi  adarondige  eraDu  pratyayagaLu 
baruttave.  
udAharaNegAgi, mEle koTTiruva (2ka) vAkyada huDukida emba 
kriyArUpadalli  huDuku  kriyApadadondige  adu  tiLisuva  ghaTane 
yAvAga  naDedudu  (endare  (2ka)  vAkyavannu  yAva  samayadalli 
ADalAgittO  adakkinta  modalE  A  ghaTane  naDedittu)  embudannu 
tiLisalu  adarondige  id  pratyaya  bandide,  mattu  A  ghaTaneyannu  
naDesiruva vyakti yAru (obba ganDasu) embudannu tiLisalu a pratyaya 
(2kha)  vAkyada  hOguttALe  emba  kriyArUpadalli  hOgu 
kriyApadadondige I id pratyayada badalu utta pratyaya bandiddu, 
adu  A  kriyApada  tiLisuva  ghaTane  (2kha)nE  vAkyavannADiruva 
samayakkinta  anantara  naDeyuvantahadu  embudannu  sUcisuttade, 
mattu  adara  anantara  a  pratyayada  badalu  ALe  pratyaya  bandiddu, 
adu  A  ghaTaneyannu  naDesaliruva  vyakti  obba  hengasu  embudannu 
sUcisuttade.  
idE  viSayavannE  kriyApadadondige  baruva  bEre  pada  illavE 
padakantegaLa  mUlaka  heccu  vivaravAgi  tiLisalu  sAdhya  embudannu 
munde  nODaliruvevu.  (udAharaNegAgi  (2kha)  vAkyadalli  bandiruva 
nALe  emba  pada  ghaTaneya  samayavannU  mattu  sItAbAyi  emba 
pada  A  ghaTaneyannu  naDesaliruva  vyaktiyannU  heccu  vivaravAgi 
paricayisuttave.) 
    kriyApadagaLondige  I  rIti  ghaTaneyalli  toDagiruva  vyakti 
illavE  vastuvannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  mattu  ghaTaneya  samayavannu 
sUcisuvu  dakkAgi  mAtravallade  bEreyU  kelavu  kAryagaLannu 
sAdhisuvudakkAgi innU kelavu pratyayagaLannu baLasalu sAdhyavide. intaha 
pratyayagaLannu  paDediruva  kriyApadagaLa  padarUpagaLa  kuritAgi  heccina 
vivaragaLannu munde aydanE adhyAyadalli koDalAguvudu. 
2.1.2 vAkyaghaTakagaLu mattu guNapadagaLu 
mEle  sUcisida  hAge,  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  kriyApadadondige  baruva 
pada  illavE  padakantegaLigella  kriyAvAkyavu  tiLisuva  ghaTaneya 
viSayavAgi  heccina  vivaragaLannu  odagisuva  kelasavide.  ivannu  (ka)  A 
ghaTaneyalli 
samaya 
vyakti, 
modalAdavugaLannu  hesarisuva  illavE  varNisuva  `ghaTaka'gaLu  mattu 
(kha)  A  ghaTane  yAvAga,  elli  mattu  hEge  naDedideyembudannu 
tiLisuva `guNapada'gaLu (illavE kriyAviSESaNagaLu) embudAgi eraDu 
mukhya gumpugaLalli vingaDisalu sAdhyavide. 
toDagiruva 
vastu, 
SAmarAyara  magaLu  ninne  purabhavanadalli  purandaradAsara 
kItraneyondannu bahaLa sogasAgi hADidaLu. 
(4)nE vAkyadalli bandiruva SAmarAyara magaLu emba ghaTaka A 
vAkya  tiLisuva  ghaTaneyannu  (hADuvudannu)  naDesiruvudu  yAru 
embudannu  heccu  spaSTavAgi  tiLiyalu  sAdhyavAguvante  mADuttade; 
(idannE  kriyApadada  koneyalli  bandiruva  aLu  pratyaya  bahaLa 
cuTukAgi tiLisuttade); purabhavanadalli emba innondu pada A ghaTane 
naDedaddu  elli  embudannu  tiLisuttade;  mattu,  purandara  dAsara 
kItraneyondannu emba padakante hADiddu Enannu embudannu tiLisu 
ttade.  I  mUru  padakantegaLu  ghaTaneyalli  toDagiruva  vyakti,  vastu 
modalAduvannu gurutisuva angagaLu. 
idallade,  (4)nE  vAkyadalli  bEreyU  kelavu  padagaLu  bandiddu 
avu  A  vAkyadalli  kriyAviSESaNagaLAgi  baLakeyallive  embudannu 
gamanisabahudu.  ivugaLalli  ninne  embudu  hADiruva  samayavannu 
heccu spaSTavAgi tiLisuttave. (idannE kriyApadadondige bandiruva id 
pratyaya bahaLa cuTukAgi tiLisuttade); mattu bahaLa hAgU sogasAgi 
emba inneraDu padagaLu hADiruvudu hEge embudannu tiLisuttave.   
ghaTakagaLu  mattu  kriyAviSESaNagaLu  (guNapadagaLu)  embudAgi 
vAkyada  angagaLannu  mEle  sUcisida  hAge  eraDu  gumpugaLalli 
vingaDisalu  sAdhyavideyAdarU  avugaLoLage  halavu  sAmyagaLive 
embudannu  nAvu  mEle  1.3.3ralli  nODiruvevu.  avu  eraDU 
kriyApadagaLu  tiLisuva  ghaTaneya  kuritAgi  heccina  tiLuvaLikeyannu 
koDuva vAkyAngagaLAgiruvudE idakke kAraNa.  
    kriyApadadondige  baraballa  guNapadagaLa  kuritAgi  heccina  vivara 
vannu munde AranE adhyAyadalli koDalAguvudu. kriyApadadondige 
baraballa  ghaTakagaLu  entahavu  embudannu  I  adhyAyadalli  vivarisa 
2.2 ghaTakagaLalli vayvidhya 
vAkyavondaralli  kriyApadadondige  bEre  bEre  rItiya  ghaTakagaLu 
baralu sAdhyaviddu, avu entahavu embudu A kriyApadavu sUcisuva 
ghaTaneya  svarUpavannavalambiside.  udAharaNegAgi,  sAyu  kriyApada 
dondige  `sattavaru  yAru  (athavA  yAvudu)'  embudannu  tiLisuva 
ondu  ghaTaka  bandare  sAku,  Adare  kollu  kriyApadadondige 
`kondavaru  yAru'  embudannu  tiLisuva  ghaTaka  mAtravallade 
`kondaddu  yArannu  (athavA  yAvudannu)'  embudannu  tiLisuva 
innondu ghaTakavU baruva avaSyakateyide. 
(5ka)  doDDa bekku sattide. 
(5kha)  rAju doDDa bekkannu kondiddAne. 
idE  rItiyalli  araLu  kriyApadadondige  `araLuvudu  (athavA 
araLiruvudu)  yAvudu'  embudannu  tiLisuva  ondu  ghaTaka  bandare 
sAku,  Adare  eTaku  kriyApadadondige  `eTakuvudu  yAvudu' 
embudannu  tiLisuva  ghaTaka  mAtravallade  `eTakuvudu  yArige' 
embudannu tiLisuva ghaTakavU barabEkAguttade. 
gulAbi hU araLide. 
(6kha)  gulAbi hU avaLige eTakuttade. 
eraDakkinta  jAsti  ghaTakagaLu  barabEkAguva  kriyApadagaLU  kannaDa 
dalli  kelavive.  udAharaNegAgi  koDu  kriyApadadondige  `koTTavaru 
yAru', `koTTudu yArige' mattu `koTTudu yAvudannu' embudannu 
tiLisuva mUru ghaTakagaLannu baLasuva avaSyakateyide. idE rItiyalli 
hELu  kriyApadadondige  `hELiddu  yAru',  `hELiddu  Enu'  mattu 
`hELiddu  yArige'  emba  mUru  kELvigaLige  uttaragaLannu  koDaballa 
ghaTakagaLannu baLasuva avaSyakateyide. 
rAju harige eraDu sAvira rupAyi koTTa. 
(7kha)  ajji makkaLige ondu kate hELidaLu. 
I  rIti  kriyApadagaLu  sUcisuva  ghaTaneyannavalambisi  baruva 
ghaTakagaLu  mAtravallade  bEreyU  kelavu  ghaTakagaLu  vAkyadalli  baralu 
sAdhyavide.  ivu  ellA  rItiya  kriyApadagaLigU  samAnavAgiruvantaha 
ghaTakagaLu.  avugaLa  baruvike  kriyApadada  arthavannavalambisilla.  udA 
haraNegAgi,  mEle  koTTiruva  ellA  vAkyagaLallU  avu  sUcisuva 
ghaTane  `yAvAga  naDeyitu  (athavA  naDeyuttade)'  mattu  `elli 
naDeyitu  (athavA  naDeyuttade)'  embudannu  tiLisuva  ghaTakagaLeraDannu 
baLasalu sAdhyavide. 
rAjuvina angaLadalli mUru divasa hinde ondu gulAbi 
hU araLittu. 
rAju  harige  ivattu  beLigge  santeyalli  eraDu  sAvira 
I  rIti  ghaTaneya  samaya  mattu  jAgagaLannu  tiLisuva  ghaTakagaLu 
mAtravallade, adara uddESa (8ka), adannu naDesuvalli baLasida sAdhana 
(8kha),  sahAyakanAgidda  vyakti  (8ga),  modalAda  bEreyU  kelavu 
viSayagaLannu  tiLisuvudakkAgi  heccina  ghaTakagaLannu  baLasalu  sAdhyavide 
yembudannu keLagina vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu. 
(8ka)  jAnaki rAtriya pUjege hU koyyuttiddALe. 
(8kha)  Ata maNNininda ondu gombe mADida. 
rAju tanna tandeyondige pETege hOgiddAne. 
kriyApadagaLu  sUcisuva  ghaTaneyannu  avalambisi  baruva  ghaTaka 
gaLannu  vAkyada  `mukhya  ghaTaka'gaLendU  mattu  ghaTanege  sambandhisiruva 
itara  viSayagaLannu  tiLisuvudakkAgi  baruva  ghaTakagaLannu  `mukhyavallada 
ghaTaka'gaLendU  kareyabahudu.  I  eraDu  rItiya  ghaTakagaLalli  kriyA 
padagaLondige  baruva  mukhya  ghaTakagaLa  sankhye  mattu  svarUpagaLa 
nnAdharisi kriyApadagaLannu bEre bEre vagragaLAgi vingaDisalu sAdhyavide. 
2.2.1 mukhya ghaTakagaLu 
kannaDada  kriyAvAkyagaLannella  AguvikegaLu  mattu  mADuvikegaLu  embu 
dAgi  eraDu  mukhya  vibhAgagaLalli  vingaDisalu  sAdhyavide.  obba  vyakti 
illavE  prANiya  hatOTiyalliruva  ghaTanegaLu  mADuvikegaLu  mattu 
hAge  hatOTiyallillada  ghaTanegaLu  AguvikegaLu.  mADuvikegaLannu 
sUcisuva  vAkyagaLallella  avannu  hatOTiyallirisikonDiruva  ghaTaka 
vondu  mukhya  ghaTakavAgi  bandiruttade.  idannu  `mADuga'  endu 
kareyabahudu.  
Aguvikeyannu  sUcisuva  vAkyagaLalli  I  mADuga  emba  ghaTaka 
baruvudilla. Adare adakke badalAgi, ghaTaneya mUlaka yAvudAdarU 
ondu badalAvaNegoLagAguva ghaTaka baruttade. idannu `Aguga' endu 
kareyabahudu.  
(ka) Aguvikeyannu sUcisuva vAkyagaLu 
(9ka)  bAgilu tereyitu. 
(9kha)  baTTe oNagitu. 
(9gha)  aramaneya Ane sAyuttide. 
rAju bidda. 
(kha) mADuvikeyannu sUcisuva vAkyagaLu 
(10ka)  rAju ODida. 
(10kha) jAnaki hADidaLu. 
(10ga)  cikka magu naguttide. 
(10gha)  hakki hAritu. 
Aguvikeyannu  sUcisuva  (9ka-gha)  vAkyagaLalli  baruva  bAgilu,  baTTe, 
rAju  mattu  aramaneya  Ane  emba  ghaTakagaLige  (AgugagaLige)  A 
vAkyagaLu  sUcisuva  tere,  oNagu,  bILu  mattu  sAyu  emba 
ghaTanegaLa  mEle  hatOTiyilla;  Adare  mADuvikeyannu  sUcisuva 
(10ka-gha) vAkyagaLalli baruva rAju, jAnaki, cikka magu mattu hakki 
emba  ghaTakagaLige  (mADugagaLige)  A  vAkyagaLu  sUcisuva  ODu, 
hADu,  nagu  mattu  hAru  emba  ghaTanegaLa  mEle  hatOTiyide 
embudannu gamanisabahudu.    
idallade  Aguvikeyannu 
sUcisuva  vAkyagaLu  EnAyitu? 
embantaha  Agu  kriyApadaviruva  praSnegaLige  uttaravAgi  baraballuvu 
sUcisuva  vAkyagaLu  Enu  mADida? 
mattu  mADuvikeyannu 
embantaha mADu kriyApadaviruva praSnegaLige uttaravAgi baraballuvu 
embudannU gamanisabahudu. 
mADuvikeyannu  sUcisuva  vAkyagaLalli  `mADuga'  ghaTaka  mAtra 
vallade,  bErondu  Aguga ghaTakavU  baralu sAdhyavide. intaha  mADu 
vikeyannu  sUcisuva  vAkyagaLa  mUladalli  ondu  AguvikeyU  sEri 
konDiruvudE idakke kAraNa.  
(11ka)  bekku sattide. 
(11kha) nAyi bekkannu kondide. 
(12ka)  marada gellu baggitu. 
(12kha) rAju marada gellannu baggisiddAne. 
(11ka)  vAkyadalli  sAyu  kriyApada  bandiddu  adu  ondu  Aguvike 
yannu  sUcisuttade  mattu  adaralli  bekku  emba  Aguga  ghaTaka  mAtra 
bandide. idakke badalu (11kha) vAkyadalli kollu kriyApada bandiddu 
adu ondu mADuvikeyannu sUcisuttade mattu adaralli nAyi emba 
ondu  mADuga  ghaTaka  mAtravallade  bekku  emba  ondu  Aguga 
ghaTakavU  bandide.  I  (11kha)  vAkya  adara  mUladalli  (11ka) 
vAkyavannu  oLagonDide  embudannu  gamanisabahudu.  (12ka-kha)dallU 
hIgeyE. 
kannaDadalli mADuga mattu ADugagaLemba eraDu ghaTakagaLU ondE 
vAkyadalli  bandAga  avugaLalli  ondannu  innondarinda  pratyEkisuvu 
dakkAgi  Agugadondige  annu  emba  vibhakti  pratyayavannu  baLasuva 
kramavide (2.6 nODi).  
Aguvikeyannu  sUcisuva  vAkyadalli  `Aguga'  ghaTakadondige  kriyA 
padavu  sUcisuva  ghaTane  elli  naDeyitu,  yAva  kaDeyinda  naDeyitu 
mattu  yAva  kaDegAgi  naDeyitu  embudAgi  mUru  rItiya  jAga 
gaLannu sUcisuvudakkAgi `jAga', `suru' mattu `kone' emba ghaTakagaLu 
bandiralu  sAdhyavide.  I  mUru  ghaTakagaLu  sUcisuva  jAgagaLa 
naDuviruva vyatyAsagaLannu munde (2.4.4ralli) vivarisalAguvudu. 
(13ka)  mAvina maradalli hU biTTide. 
(13kha) aTTadinda ondu hagga nEluttide. 
(13ga)  hAgala baLLi mADige habbide. 
mADuvikeyannu  sUcisuva  vAkyagaLallU  mADuga  ghaTakadondige

sAdhyavide, mattu ivugaLondige bErondu Aguga ghaTakavU bandiralu 
sAdhyavide. I eraDu rItiya sAdhyategaLannu (14ka-ga) mattu (15ka-

(14ka)  puTTa magu kucriyalli kuLitide. 
(14kha) rAju maradinda iLida. 
(14ga)  jAnaki aTTakke hattidaLu. 
(15ka)  rAju haNavannu kapATinalli irisiddAne. 
(15kha) magu plETininda jEnannella nekkitu. 
(15ga)  sItAbAyi akkibuTTige segaNi ujjuttiddALe.

sUcisuva ghaTakagaLu bandiruvudannu gamanisabahudu. (15ka-ga) vAkya 
gaLalli  mADugadondige  ondu  AgugavU  bandiddu,  ivugaLondigU 
mUru rItiya jAgagaLannu sUcisuva ghaTakagaLannu baLasalAgide. 
    `prEraka'  emba  hesarina  Araneya  ghaTakavu  sAmAnyavAgi  kriyApada 
dondige isu emba pratyayavannu baLasiruvantaha vAkyagaLalli mAtravE 
kANisikoLLuttade.  
(16ka)  rAju bAgilu tereda.

(17ka)  saynikaru sereyALugaLannella kondaru.

(16kha)dalli  jAnaki  padavU  mattu  (17kha)dalli  vIrasEna  padavU 
`prEraka' ghaTakavannu sUcisuttive. I ghaTakavU mADuga ghaTakada hAge 
tanna bayakeyante kelasa naDesuttade, mattu A kelasavannu tanna hatOTi 
yallirisikonDiruttade.  Adare,  mADuga  ghaTakada  hAge  prErakavu  tAnE 
A  kelasavannu  mADuva  badalu  bErobba  vyakti  illavE  prANiya 
mUlaka adannu mADisikoLLuttade. 
    ghaTaneya  jAgavannu  sUcisuva  ghaTakagaLu  mAtravallade,  mEle 
(2.1.2)ralli  sUcisiruva  hAge  kelavu  sandabhragaLalli  samayavannu 
sUcisuva  ghaTakagaLU  vAkyada  ondu  mukhya  ghaTakavAgi  kANisikoLLa 
balluvu.  
2.2.2 mukhyavallada ghaTakagaLu 
mEle vivarisida Aru mukhya ghaTakagaLu mAtravallade kriyAvAkyagaLalli 
kriyApadadondige  kelavu  mukhyavallada  ghaTakagaLU  baraballuvu.  ivu 
ellA  rItiya  vAkyagaLallU  baraballuvAgiddu,  avugaLa  baLake  kriyA 
padada arthavannu avalambisiruvudilla. udAharaNegAgi  ellA rItiya 
kriyApadagaLondigU  avugaLa  jAga  mattu  samayagaLannu  sUcisuva 
mukhyavallada ghaTakagaLannu baLasalu sAdhyavide. 
(18ka)  gavDaru tamma tOTadalli I vaSra hatti beLediddAre. 
(18kha) Ata dEvasthAnada kereyalli mIyuttiddAne. 
(18ga)  rAju klAsinalli ondu kAdambari Oduttidda. 
(18ka)dalli  mADuga  ghaTakavAgiruva  gavDaru  mattu  Aguga  ghaTaka 
vAgiruva  hatti  embiveraDu  mAtra  mukhya  ghaTakagaLu.  jAgavannu 
sUcisuva tamma tOTadalli embudu mattu samayavannu sUcisuva 
I  vaSra  embudu  iveraDU  mukhyavallada  ghaTakagaLu.  yAkendare 
beLe  emba  kriyApada  sUcisuva  ghaTanege  Aguga  mattu  mADuga 
ghaTakagaLu mAtra nEravAgi sambandhisiruttave. 
    I  rItiyAgi,  ghaTane  naDeda  illavE  naDeyaliruva  jAga  mattu 
samayagaLu  mAtravallade,  adu  yAva  kAraNadinda  naDeyitu  mattu 
yAva  uddESavannu  sAdhisuvudakkAgi  naDeyitu,  adakkAgi  baLasida 
upakaraNa  yAvudu  mattu  adannu  naDesida  Sakti  yAvudu,  adannu 
naDesuvalli  mADuga  illavE  Aguganondige  jotegAranobbaniddalli 
Ata  yAru,  mADuga  illavE  agugavannu  hOluvantaha  `hOluga' 
yAru  ityAdigaLannu  sUcisuva  ghaTakagaLu  mukhyavallada  ghaTakagaLAgi 
vAkyagaLalli  baraballuvu.  intaha  mukhyavallada  kelavu  ghaTakagaLa 
baLakeyannu keLagina vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu.  
(19ka)  jOrAgi maLe banda kAraNa mESTu SAlege baralilla. 
(19kha) rAtriya pUjege Ake hU koyyuttiddALe. 
(19ga)  Ata kategaLannu kempu SAyiyalli bareyuttiddAne. 
(19gha) bisilige happaLa oNagitu. 
(19Ga) Ake koDadondige tambigeyallU nIru tumbisiddALe. 
(19ca) rAjuvinante jAnakigU kAlige peTTAgide. 
(19cha) magaLa maduvegAgi Ata hattu sAvira sangrahisiddAne. 
baru  kriyApadadondige  mukhya  ghaTakavAgi  ondu  mADuga  ghaTaka 
mattu  ondu  suru  illavE  kone  ghaTaka  bandare  sAku.  Adare 
(19ka)dalli  iveraDarondige  ghaTane  naDedudakke  kAraNavEnembudannu 
tiLisuva maLe banda kAraNa emba mUraneya mukhyavallada ghaTakavU 
    idE  rItiyalli  (19kha)dalli  bandiruva  rAtriya  pUjege  emba 
ghaTaka,  (19ga)dalli  bandiruva  kempu  SAyiyalli  emba  ghaTaka, 
(19gha)dalli  bandiruva  bisilige  emba  ghaTaka,  (19Ga)dalli  bandiruva 
koDadondige  emba  ghaTaka,  (19ca)dalli  bandiruva  rAjuvinante 
emba ghaTaka, mattu (19cha)dalli bandiruva magaLa maduvegAgi emba 
ghaTaka ivellavU mukhyavallada ghaTakagaLu. 
2.3 ghaTakagaLa naDuvina vyatyAsagaLu 
Aguga, mADuga, jAga, suru, kone, samaya mattu prErakagaLemba I 
ELu mukhya ghaTakagaLu yAva rItiyalli ondakkinta ondu bhinnavAgive 
embudannu svalpa vivaravAgi keLage pariSIlisalAgide. 
2.3.1 Aguga mattu mADuga 
ondu ghaTaneya mUlaka bEre bEre badalAvaNegaLige oLagAguva vyakti, 
vastu,  viSaya  modalAduvannu  `Aguga'  ghaTaka  sUcisuttade.  Adare 
intaha  badalAvaNegaLAvuvU  I  ghaTakada  hatOTiyalliruvudilla. 
ondu  ghaTaneyindAgi  adu  I  rIti  badalAvaNegaLigoLagAguttiruva 
badalu  hosadAgi  huTTikoLLuttirabahudu  illavE  tayArAguttira 
bahudu. 
(20ka)  rangarAyaru tamma bAviyannu muccisidaru. 
(20kha)  rangarAyaru ondu maneyannu kaTTisidaru. 
(20ka)  vAkyadalli  AgugavAgi  bandiruva  tamma  bAvi  emba  ghaTaka  A 
vAkyavu  sUcisuva  ghaTaneyinda  badalAvaNegoLagAgide  (adu  illa 
vAgide), Adare (20kha)dalli AgugavAgi bandiruva ondu mane emba 
ghaTaka  A  vAkyavu  sUcisuva  ghaTaneyinda  hosadAgi  tayArAgide 
embudannu gamanisabahudu. 
`mADuga'  ghaTakavU  Agugada  hAgeyE  kriyApadavu  sUcisuva 
ghaTaneyinda  badalAvaNegoLagAguttiralu  sAdhyavide.  Adare  antaha 
badalAvaNe  mADuga  ghaTakada  hatOTiyalliruttadeyembudE  Aguga 
ghaTakakkU mattu mADuga ghaTakakkU naDuviruva mukhya vyatyAsa. 
(21ka)  rAju manege ODida. 
(21kha) rAju mahaDiyinda keLage bidda. 
rAju  embudu  (21ka)dalli  mADuga  ghaTakavAgiyU  mattu  (21kha) 
dalli  Aguga  ghaTakavAgiyU  bandiruvudannu  gamanisabahudu.  (21ka) 
sUcisuva ghaTane rAjuvina hatOTiyallide, Adare (21kha) sUcisuva 
ghaTane Atana hatOTiyallilla. 
ondu  ghaTaneyannu  hatOTiyallirisikoLLalu  sAdhyavilladantaha 
mane,  mara  modalAduvannU  kelavomme  mADuga  ghaTakavAgi  vAkya 
gaLalli  baLasalu  sAdhyaviddu,  hAge  mADidAga  avakke  ghaTaneyondannu 
hatOTiyallirisikoLLuva Sakti bandiruva hAge kANisuttade. 
(22ka)  A bhUtada mane Aru janarannu bali tegedukonDide.   
(22kha) A Aladamara nUrAru hakkigaLige ASraya nIDide. 
(22ga)  Atana hADuvike marada mElidda kAgeyannu bedarisitu. 
2.3.2 jAga, suru mattu kone 
jAga,  suru  mattu  kone  emba  I  mUru  ghaTakagaLU  mukhyavAgi 
ghaTanege  sambandhisiruva  jAgavannu  sUcisuva  ghaTakagaLu.  ivugaLalli 
jAga  ghaTakavu  ondu  jAgadalli  naDeyuva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuvu 
dAdare,  suru  ghaTakavu  ondu  jAgavannu  `biTTu'  hOguvantaha 
ghaTaneyannU mattu kone ghaTakavu ondu jAgada `kaDegAgi' naDeyuva 
ghaTaneyannU  sUcisuttave.  I  mUru  rItiya  ghaTakagaLa  naDuviruva 
I vyatyAsavannu keLagina vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu. 
(23ka)  rAju tanna pustakavannu kapATinalli irisida. 
(23kha) rAju kapATininda ondu ilimariyannu tegeda. 
(23ga)  sItAbAyi akkibuTTige segaNi ujjidaLu. 
(23ka)dalli  irisu  kriyApada  bandiddu  idu  ondu  jAgadalli 
naDeyuva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuvudAda  kAraNa  adarondige  jAgavannu 
sUcisuva kapATinalli ghaTaka bandide. idakke badalu (23kha)dalli tege 
kriyApada  bandiddu,  idu  ondu  jAgavannu  biTTu  hOguva  ghaTane 
yannu  sUcisuvudAda  kAraNa  adarondige  kapATininda  emba  suru 
ghaTaka  bandide.  (23ga)dalli  ujju  kriyApada  bandiddu  adu  ondu 
jAgada  kaDegAgi  naDeyuva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuvudAda  kAraNa 
adarondige akkibuTTige emba kone ghaTaka bandide. 
kelavu  kriyApadagaLannu  I  mUru  rItiya  ghaTakagaLondigU 
baLasalu  sAdhyaviddu  avu  tammondige  bandiruva  ghaTakada  svarUpa 
vannAdharisi ondE ghaTaneya bEre bEre amSagaLige ottu koDaballuvu. 
(24ka)  makkaLella TerEsinalli ODuttiddAre. 
(24kha) makkaLella TerEsininda ODuttiddAre. 
(24ga)  makkaLella TerEsige ODuttiddAre. 
mElina  mUru  vAkyagaLallU  ODu  emba  ondE  kriyApada  bandide. 
Adare  (24ka)dalli  adu  TerEsinalli  emba  jAga  ghaTakadondige 
bandiruva kAraNa ODuva ghaTane ondu jAgadalli naDeyuttiruvudannU, 
(24kha)dalli  TerEsige  emba  suru  ghaTakadondige  bandiruva  kAraNa 
adE  ghaTane  ondu  jAgavannu  biTTu  naDeyuttiruvudannU  mattu 
(24ga)dalli  TerEsige  emba  kone  ghaTakadondige  bandiruva  kAraNa 
adE ghaTane ondu jAgada kaDegAgi naDeyuttiruvudannU sUcisuttade. 
2.3.3 suru mattu kone ghaTakagaLa heccina baLakegaLu   
suru  mattu  kone  ghaTakagaLu  nEravAgi  obba  vyaktiya  illavE  ondu 
vastuvina  kadaluvikege  sambandhisiruva  jAgagaLannu  sUcisuva  badalu 
ondu anubhavada `kadaluvike'yannU sUcisaballuvu.  
(25ka)  jAnaki tanna tAyiyinda ondu hADu kalitaLu. 
(25kha) jAnakige avaLa tAyi ondu hADu kalisidaLu. 
kali  kriyApada  suru  ghaTakadondigU  mattu  kalisu  kriyApada  kone 
ghaTakadondigU  baraballudu  embudannu  (25ka-kha)  vAkyagaLinda 
tiLiyabahudu. Adare illi nijakkU ondu vastuvina kadaluvike naDedilla. 
jAnaki  tannallillada  anubhavavondannu  paDediddu  adakke  mUla  avaLa 
tAyi  embudAgi  kadaluvikege  sambandhisida  ghaTakagaLu  illi  avugaLa 
heccina arthadalli baLakeyAgive. 
intaha  heccina  arthagaLalli  suru  ghaTakakkintalU  kone  ghaTakada 
baLake  kannaDadalli  heccu  rUDhiyallide.  I  viSayavannu  keLagina  udA 
haraNegaLu spaSTapaDisuttave. 
(26ka)  ajja makkaLigondu kate hELida. 
(26kha) narige drAkSe haNNu eTakitu. 
(26ga)  avaLige kOpa bandide. 
(26gha) avanige dikku tappitu. 
kone  ghaTakavannu  (26ka)dalli  `ajja  hELida  kate  yArannu  talapide' 
embudannu  sUcisuvudakkAyU,  (26kha)dalli  `drAkSe  haNNu  eTakuva' 
anubhava  yArigAyitu  embudannu  tiLisuvudakkAgiyU,  (26ga)dalli 
`kOpa baruva' anubhava yArigAyitu embudannu tiLisuvudakkAgiyU 
mattu (26gha)dalli `dikku tappuva' anubhava yArigAyitu embudannu 
tiLisuvudakkAgiyU baLasalAgide. 
    viSayavAkyagaLalli  ondu  guNadharmada  iruvikeyannu  sUcisuvu 
dakkAgiyU  kone  ghaTakavannu  baLasalu  sAdhyavide  embudannu  munde 
3.4ralli nODaliruvevu.   
2.4 kriyApadagaLa vibhajane 
kriyApadagaLondige  baruva  mukhya  ghaTakagaLa  sankhye  mattu  svarUpa 
iveraDU  avugaLa  arthavannavalambiside.  udAharaNegAgi,  heccina 
kriyApadagaLigU  isu  pratyayavannu  sErisi,  `avu  sUcisuva  ghaTane 
innobba vyaktiya prEraNeyinda naDedide' embantaha heccina arthavannu 
kriyApadagaLige  sErisalu  sAdhyavide.  I  rIti  heccina  arthaviruva 
kriyApadagaLondige  sAmAnyavAgi  ondu  heccina  mukhya  ghaTakavU 
bandiruttade.  
(27ka)  nIru kudiyitu. 
(27kha) jAnaki nIru kudisidaLu. 
(28ka)  namma Urige obba mAntrika bandidda. 
(28kha) namma Urige paTElaru obba mAntrikanannu barisiddaru. 
(27ka)dalli  kudi  kriyApadadondige  kudiyuva  vastuvannu  sUcisuva 
nIru  emba  Aguga  ghaTaka  mAtra  bandide.  Adare  (27kha)dalli  I 
kriyApadakke  isu  pratyayavannu  sErisi  tayArisida  kudisu  kriyApada 
bandideyAda  kAraNa  adarondige  jAnaki  emba  heccina  ghaTakavannu 
baLasabEkAgide.  idu  kudiyuva  ghaTanege  mADuganobbanannu  sErisu 
    (28ka)dalli  baru  kriyApadadondige  mADuga  mattu  jAgagaLu 
bandive,  Adare  (28kha)dalli  I  kriyApadakke  isu  pratyayavannu 
sErisideyAda  kAraNa  adarondige  mADuga  mattu  jAgagaLu  mAtra 
vallade ondu `prEraka'vU bandide. 
I rIti kriyApadagaLondige baruva mukhya ghaTakagaLa sankhye mattu 
svarUpa  iveraDU  avugaLa  arthavannavalambisiveyAda  kAraNa,  kriyA 
padagaLannu  avugaLondige  baraballa  mukhya  ghaTakagaLa  AdhArada  mEle 
bEre bEre vagragaLalli vingaDisalu sAdhyavide. 
2.4.1 ghaTakavillade baruva kriyApadagaLu 
kannaDada  heccina  kriyApadagaLigU  kaDimeyendare  ondAdarU  mukhya 
ghaTakada  avaSyakateyiruttade.  idakke  apavAdavAgi  guDugu,  mincu 
embantaha kelavE kelavu kriyApadagaLu mAtra yAva mukhya ghaTakavU 
illade baraballuvu. udA: 
(29ka)  ninne jOru mincuttittu. 
(29kha) jOru guDuguttA ide. 
mEle  (29ka)  vAkyadalli  mincu  kriyApadondige  ninne  mattu 
jOru  emba  eraDu 
mAtra  bandiveyallade 
guNapadagaLu 
ghaTakagaLAvuvU  bandilla.  (29kha)dalli  guDugu  kriyApadadondige 
jOru guNapada mAtra bandide. 
    Adare  intaha  kriyApadagaLondige  avugaLige  sambandhisiruva 
guDugu,  mincu  embantaha  nAmapadagaLannu  Aguga  ghaTakagaLAgi 
baLasalu  sAdhyavideyAda  kAraNa  (30ka-kha  nODi),  avannU  mElina 
niyamakke  apavAdagaLendu  tiLiyabEkAgilla.  idallade,  intaha  kriyA 
padagaLondige sAmAnyavAgi avu sUcisuva ghaTaneya samaya illavE 
jAgavannu  sUcisuva  ghaTakagaLU  baruttiddu  (31ka-kha  nODi),  I 
ghaTakagaLu  heccu  kaDime  avugaLa  mukhya  ghaTakagaLa  hAgeyE  vatrisu 
ttave. 
(30ka)  guDugu guDugitu. 
(30kha)  mincu mincitu. 
(31ka)  A Uralli dinAlU beLigge Aru ganTege guDuguttittu. 
(31kha) A kaDe jOrAgi mincuttide. 
2.4.2 ghaTaneya hatOTi     
mEle  sUcisiruvante,  kannaDada  kriyApadagaLannu  avu  tiLisuva  ghaTane 
hatOTiyalliruvantahadO  athavA  allavO  emba  viSayada  mEle 
eraDu  mukhya  vibhAgagaLalli  vingaDisalu  sAdhyavide.  hatOTiyallillada 
ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  kriyApadagaLu  Aguga  ghaTakadondige  baruttave 
yAdare  hatOTiyalliruva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  kriyApadagaLu 
mADuga ghaTakadondige baruttave. 
udAharaNegAgi,  kudi,  bEyu,  oNagu,  sAyu,  araLu 
modalAda kriyApadagaLu hatOTiyallilladiruva ghaTanegaLannu sUcisu 
ttiddu,  avugaLondige  ondu  Aguga  ghaTaka  mAtra  mukhya  ghaTakavAgi 
baraballudu,  mattu  ODu,  aLu,  malagu,  hAru,  kuNi  modalAda 
kriyApadagaLu  hatOTiyalliruva  ghaTanegaLannu  sUcisuttiddu  avuga 
Londige ondu mADuga ghaTaka mAtra mukhya ghaTakavAgi baraballudu.  
(32ka)  gulAbi hU araLide. 
(32kha) baTTe oNagitu. 
(32ga)  rAjuvina kappu nAyi sattide. 
(33ka)  rAju ODida. 
(33kha) magu aLuttide. 
(33ga)  avaLu kuNidaLu. 
    hatOTiyalliruva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  kriyApadagaLalli  kelavu 
ondu  mADuga  ghaTaka  mAtravallade  adarondige  ondu  Aguga  ghaTaka 
vannU  paDediralu  sAdhyavide.  udAharaNegAgi,  mADu,  eLe,  kare, 
taTTu,  neDu,  tinnu  modalAda  kriyApadagaLu  hatOTiyalliruva 
ghaTanegaLannu  sUcisuttiddu,  avugaLondige  mukhya  ghaTakavAgi  ondu 
mADuga ghaTaka mAtravallade ondu Aguga ghaTakavU baraballudu.  
(34ka)  rAju ondu gombe mADida. 
(34kha) Ane ondu maravannu eLeyuttide. 
(34ga)  avanu ondu giDa naTTiddAne. 
    idallade,  mEle  vivarisiruva  mUru  rItiya  kriyApadagaLallU 
kelavu  jAga,  suru  illavE  kone  emba  ghaTakagaLannu  paDeyaballuvu. 
udAharaNegAgi, karagu, tElu, tumbu, tuLuku, ingu modalAda 
kriyApadagaLu  hatOTiyallillada  ghaTanegaLannu  sUcisuttiddu  avuga 
Londige  mukhya  ghaTakavAgi  ondu  Aguga  ghaTaka  mAtravallade  ondu 
jAga ghaTakavU baraballudu. 
(35ka)  I hAlina puDi bisinIrinallU karaguttade. 
(35kha) nIrinalli kasa tEluttide. 
(35ga)  koDadalli nIru tumbitu. 
    idE  rItiyalli,  hatOTiyalliruva  ghaTanegaLannu  sUcisuva 
tangu,  nelesu,  aDagu,  ale,  toDagu  modalAda  kriyApada 
gaLondige  ondu  mADuga  ghaTaka  mAtravallade  ondu  jAga  ghaTakavU 
mukhya ghaTakavAgi baraballudu. 
(36ka)  kaLLaru ondu guheyalli aDagiddaru. 
(36kha) huDugaru bahaLa hottu kADinalli aleyuttiddaru. 
(36ga)  avaru I Urinalli nelesiddAre. 
    cellu,  bittu,  irisu,  tumbu  modalAda  hatOTiyalliruva 
ghaTanegaLannu  sUcisuva  kriyApadagaLondige  mADuga,  Aguga  mattu 
jAgagaLemba  mUru  rItiya  ghaTakagaLU  mukhya  ghaTakagaLAgi  bara 
balluvu. 
(37ka)  makkaLu I kONeyalli nIru celliddAre. 
(37kha) rAju tanna cIlavannu kapATinalli irisiddAne. 
(37ga)  Ake sihinIrannu I koDadalli tumbiddALe. 
    jAga  ghaTakada  badalu  suru  illavE  kone  ghaTakavannu  mukhya 
ghaTakavAgi paDediruva mEle sUcisidantaha mUru rItiya kriyApada 
gaLige udAharaNegaLannu keLage koDalAgide. 
(38ka)  aTTadinda ondu hagga nEluttide. 
(38kha) avana beraLige ondu muLLu cuccitu. 
(39ka)  avanu illinda tolagali. 
(39kha) rAju harige hoDeda. 
(40ka)  Ata bAviyinda nIru sEduttiddAne. 
(40kha)  Ake gAyakke mulAmu haccuttiddALe. 
Agugadondige  (38ka)dalli  suru  ghaTaka  bandideyAdare,  (38kha)dalli 
kone  ghaTaka  bandide.  idE  rItiyalli  mADugadondige  (39ka)dalli 
suru  ghaTakavU  mattu  (39kha)dalli  kone  ghaTakavU  bandiruvudannu 
kANabahudu. Aguga mattu mADugagaLeraDarondige suru mattu kone 
ghaTakagaLannu  paDediruva  kriyApadagaLige  udAharaNegaLannu  (40ka-
kha)gaLalli kANabahudu. 
2.4.3 Agu kriyApadada ghaTakagaLu 
ghaTakagaLa  maTTige  hatOTiyallillada  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  Agu 
kriyApada  antaha  itara  kriyApadagaLiginta  kelavu  viSayagaLalli  bhinna 
vAgide.  modalaneyadAgi,  adarondige  eraDu  ghaTakagaLu  baralu 
sAdhyaviddu,  avugaLalli  ondu  jAgavannU  mattu  innondu  A 
jAgadalli  naDediruva  ghaTane,  kANisuva  vastu  modalAduvannU 
sUcisuttave. 
(41ka)  Atana kAlinalli huNNAgide. 
(41kha) Ake neTTa giDadalli hUvAgide. 
(41ga)  avara maneyalli EnO galATeyAguttide. 
    eraDaneyadAgi,  I  kriyApadadondige  baruva  ghaTakagaLeraDU 
ondE  vyakti  illavE  vastuvannu  gurutisalu  sAdhyaviddu,  avu  A  vyakti 
illavE  vastuvige  eraDu  bEre  bEre  samayagaLalliruva  avasthegaLannu 
sUcisaballuvu.  Agu  kriyApada  I  eraDu  avasthegaLannu  sambandhisuva 
ghaTaneyannu sUcisuttade. 
(42ka)  rAju haNavantanAda. 
(42kha) rAjakumAra kappeyAda. 
(42ga)  avaru adhyakSarAguttAre. 
(42gha) avana tOLu Akeya taledimbAgide. 
(42ka)dalli bandiruva rAju mattu haNavanta emba eraDu ghaTakagaLU 
obbanE  vyaktiyannu  gurutisuttive  embudannu  gamanisabahudu.  idE 
rItiyalli  (42kha)dalli  bandiruva  rAjakumAra  mattu  kappe  emba 
eraDu ghaTakagaLU obbanE vyaktiyannu gurutisuttiddu, avu A vyaktiya 
eraDu avasthegaLannu sUcisuttive. 
    Agu  kriyApadadondige  baruva  ghaTakagaLeraDU  I  rIti  ondE 
vyakti  illavE  vastuvannu  gurutisuvudiddalli  avu  ondE  vibhakti 
rUpadalli  baLakeyAguttave.  intaha  vAkyagaLannu  mADu  kriyA 
padaviruva  bErondu  vAkyada  oLagirisi  hELidAga  I  viSaya  innaSTu 
spaSTavAguttade.  
(43ka)  rAjakumAra kappeyAda. 
(43kha) mantravAdi rAjakumAranannu kappeyannAgi mADida. 
(43ga)  avanu SrImantanAda.   
(43gha) avanannu SrImantanannAgi mADiddu avana buddhivantike. 
(43ka)dalli  bandiruva  rAjakumAra  mattu  kappe  emba  eraDu 
ghaTakagaLU  ondE  vibhaktiyalli  baruvuvemba  viSaya  A  vAkyavannu 
oLavAkyavAgi paDediruva (43kha) vAkyadalli spaSTavAgi kANisuttade. 
2.4.4 kadaluva mattu kadalada ghaTanegaLu 
jAgavondannu  sUcisabEkAgiruva  kriyApadagaLannu  kadaluva  ghaTane 
gaLannu  sUcisuvavugaLu  mattu  kadalada  ghaTanegaLannu  sUcisuvavugaLu  
embudAgi  eraDu  mukhya  vibhAgagaLalli  vingaDisalu  sAdhyavide.  ivu 
gaLalli kadalada ghaTanegaLannu sUcisuva kriyApadagaLondige jAga ghaTaka 
baraballudAdare  kadaluva  ghaTanegaLannu  sUcisuva  kriyApadagaLondige 
suru illavE kone ghaTakagaLu (athavA averaDU oTTAgi) baraballuvu.  
kadaluva  ghaTanegaLallella  yAvudAdarU  ondu  jAgadinda  illavE 
ondu jAgada kaDegAgi naDeyuva calane nEravAgi illavE sUkSmavAgi 
sUcitavAgiruttade.  I  calane  suruvAguvudelli  embudannu  suru 
ghaTakavU  mattu  adu  konegoLLuvudelli  embudannu  kone  ghaTakavU 
tiLisuttave.  kelavu  kriyApadagaLondige  I  eraDu  rItiya  ghaTakagaLalli 
ondu  mAtra  baraballudu,  Adare  bEre  kelavu  rItiya  kriyApada 
gaLondige iveraDU oTTAgi baraballuvu. 
(44ka)  jAnaki akkiyinda kallu hekkuttiddALe. 
(44kha) sItAbAyi akkibuTTige segaNi ujjuttiddALe. 
(44ga)  svAmigaLa savAri puNeyinda bombAyige hOgide. 
(44ka)dalli  bandiruva  hekku  kriyApada  ondu  jAgadinda  naDeyuva 
calaneyannu  sUcisuvudAda  kAraNa  adarondige  akkiyinda  emba 
suru  ghaTaka  bandide.  idakke  badalu  (44kha)dalli  bandiruva  ujju 
kriyApada  ondu  jAgada  kaDegAgi  naDeyuva  calaneyannu  sUcisuvu 
dAda kAraNa adarondige akki buTTige emba `kone' ghaTaka bandide.  
(44ga)dalli bandiruva hOgu kriyApada intaha eraDu rItiya 
calanegaLannU  (endare  ondu  jAgadinda  naDeyuva  calaneyannu  mattu 
innondu  jAgada  kaDegAgi  naDeyuva  calaneyannu)  sUcisuvudAda 
kAraNa  adarondige  puNeyinda  emba  suru  ghaTaka  mAtravallade 
bombAyige emba kone ghaTakavU bandide.  
kadalada  ghaTanegaLalli  I  rIti  calaneya  arthaviruvudilla.  hAgAgi 
antaha  ghaTanegaLannu  sUcisuva  kriyApadagaLondige  avu  sUcisuva 
ghaTane  elli  naDeyuttade  embudannu  tiLisuva  jAga  ghaTaka  mAtravE 
baraballudu. 
(45ka)  rAju haNavannu kapATinalli irisiddAne. 
(45kha) darODekOraru haNavannu kADinalli aDagisiddAre. 
(45ga)  mudukiya Sava bAviyalli tEluttide. 
2.5 vibhajaneya samasyegaLu 
I rIti kriyApadagaLondige entaha ghaTakagaLu mattu eSTu ghaTakagaLu 
mukhya  ghaTakagaLAgi  baruttave  emba  viSayada  AdhArada  mEle  avannu 
bEre  bEre  gumpugaLalli  vingaDisi  hELuvalli  ondu  mukhyavAda 
tondareyide. adEnendare, kannaDadalli baLakeyAguva halavu kriyApada 
gaLu  intaha  yAvudAdarU  ondu  gumpinalli  mAtravE  uLiyuva 
badalu eraDu athavA jAsti gumpugaLalli baruttave, mattu avu yAva 
gumpinalli  baruttave  embudara  mEle  avugaLa  arthadallU  vyatyAsa 
kanDubaruttade. 
2.5.1 hatOTiya sUcane 
ondu  ghaTaneyannu  varNisuva  samayadalli  adu  naDedideyendiSTE 
hELabahudu illavE adu obba vyakti illavE prANiya hatOTiyalli 
naDedideyendu sUcisabahudu. heccina kriyApadagaLannU I eraDaneya 
arthadalli baLasabEkiddalli avakke isu pratyayavannu sErisabEkAguttade. 
keLage  (ka)  vAkyagaLalli  hatOTiyallillada  ghaTanegaLannU  mattu  (kha) 
vAkyagaLalli hatOTiyalliruvavugaLannU sUcisalAgide 
(46ka)  nIru kudiyitu. 
(46kha) jAnaki nIru kudisidaLu. 
(47ka)  nIru mugiyitu. 
(47kha) jAnaki nIru mugisidaLu. 
    Adare  oDe,  beLe,  kadaDu,  magucu,  sigi,  muri,  hari,  Eru 
modalAda kelavu kriyApadagaLannu avugaLalli yAva badalAvaNeyannU 
mADade  hAgeyE  mEle  sUcisida  eraDu  sandabhragaLallU  baLasalu 
sAdhyavide.  
(48ka)  koDa oDeyitu. 
(48kha) sItAbAyi koDa oDedaLu. 
(49ka)  gellu muriyitu. 
(49kha) rAju gellu murida. 
(48ka)  vAkyadalli  oDe  kriyApada  ondu  hatOTiyallillada  ghaTane 
yannu sUcisuttideyAdare, (48kha) vAkyadalli adE kriyApada ondu 
hatOTiyalliruva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuttide.  (48ka)dalli  I  kriyA 
padadondige  ondu  Aguga  ghaTaka  (koDa)  mAtra  bandide,  Adare 
(48kha)dalli  adarondige  I  Aguga  ghaTaka  mAtravallade  ondu 
mADuga  ghaTakavU  (sItAbAyi  embudU)  bandide.  (49ka-kha) 
vAkya gaLallU hIgeyE.        
    turisu, meccu, oppu, tappu, hOgu, mare modalAda bEre 
kelavu  kriyApadagaLU  mElinavugaLa  hAgeyE  hatOTiyalliruva 
illavE  hatOTiyalli  illadiruva  ghaTanegaLannu  yAva  pratyayada 
sahAyavilladeyU  sUcisaballuvu.  Adare  I  kriyApadagaLu  tiLisuva 
ghaTane  hatOTiyallilla  embudannu  sUcisabEkiddalli,  antaha  ghaTane 
yalli  toDagiruva  vyakti,  prANi  modalAduvannu  mADuga  ghaTakada 
mUlaka sUcisuva badalu kone ghaTakada mUlaka sUcisabEkAguttade. 
(50ka)  janAdrana tale turisida. 
(50kha) janAdrananige tale turisitu. 
(51ka)  girISa pAThavannu maretiddAne. 
(51kha) girISanige pATha maretide. 
    hatOTiyallillada  ghaTaneyannAgali  illavE  hatOTiyalliruva 
ghaTaneyannAgali  pratyayavannu  baLasadEnE  sUcisaballa  bILu,  tEgu, 
AkaLisu  modalAda  bEreyU  kelavu  kriyApadagaLU  kannaDadallive. 
Adare  I  kriyApadagaLu  hatOTiyalliruva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuvAga 
mElina kriyApadagaLa baLakeyalli kANisida hAge avugaLondige baruva 
ghaTakagaLa sankhyeyalli illavE svarUpadalli badalAvaNeyAguvudilla. 
(52ka)  rAju bidda. 
(52kha) avanu AkaLisida. 
mElina  kriyApadagaLu  hatOTiyallillada  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuvu 
diddalli,  avugaLondige  baruva  ghaTakavannu  AgugavendU  mattu 
hatOTiyalliruva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuvudiddalli  adE  ghaTakavannu 
mADugavendU  parigaNisabEkAguvudembudE  ivugaLa  baLakeyalli 
kANisuva vaySiSTya.     
    udAharaNegAgi,  bILu  kriyApada  sAmAnyavAgi  bILuvavana 
hatOTiyallillada ghaTaneyannu sUcisuttade. Adare, kelavu viSiSTavAda 
sandabhragaLalli  (udAharaNegAgi  nATakadalli  pAtra  vahisuttiruva  obba 
vyakti  keLage  bILuvante  naTisabEkAgiruvAga)  adu  ondu  hatOTi 
yalliruva  ghaTaneyannU  sUcisuttiralu  sAdhyavide.  modalaneya  baLake 
yalli  adondu  Aguga  ghaTakadondige  bandideyendu  hELabEkAgu 
ttade  mattu  eraDaneya  baLakeyalli  adondu  mADuga  ghaTakadondige 
bandideyendu hELabEkAguttade. 
2.5.2 samagrateya sUcane 
kannaDada kriyApadagaLalli kelavu sUcisuva ghaTanegaLu Agugavannu pUtri 
yAgi  bAdhisuttave,  Adare  bEre  kelavu  Agugada  ondu  bhAgavannaSTE 
bAdhisuttave.  udAharaNegAgi,  keLage  koTTiruva  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu 
gamanisabahudu. 
(53ka)  rAju mEjannu muTTida. 
(53kha) rAju nadiyannu dATida. 
rAju  mEjina  tudiyannu  mAtravE  muTTiruvanAdarU  (53ka)  vAkya 
vannu baLasalu sAdhyavide, Adare (53kha) vAkyavannu baLasabEkiddalli Ata 
pUtriyAgi  nadiya  ondu  danDeyinda  innondu  danDege  hOgi 
talapiruvudu avaSya. dATu kriyApadavu sUcisuva ghaTane obba vyakti 
illavE  vastuvannu  pUtriyAgi  bAdhisuttade,  Adare  muTTu  kriyA 
padavu  sUcisuva  ghaTane  vyakti  illavE  vastuvina  ondu  bhAgavannaSTE 
bAdhisuttiralu sAdhyavide. 
    hattu,  Iju,  Odu  modalAda  kelavu  kriyApadagaLu  I  eraDu 
rItiya  ghaTanegaLannU  sUcisalu  sAdhyaviddu,  modalaneya  arthadalli 
avugaLondige  ondu  Aguga  ghaTaka  baruvudAdare,  eraDaneya  artha 
dalli ondu kone illavE jAga ghaTaka baruttade. 
(54ka)  Ata kAvEri nadiyannu Ijida. 
(54kha) Ata kAvEri nadiyalli Ijida. 
(55ka)  Ata ENiyinda maravannu hattida. 
(55kha) Ata ENiyinda marakke hattida. 
(54ka)dalli Iju kriyApadadondige mADuga mattu Aguga ghaTakagaLu 
bandiddu,  adakke  `Ata  kAvEri  nadiya  ondu  daDadinda  innondu 
daDakke  Ijida'  embudAgi  samagrArthavide.  Adare,  (54kha)  dalli  idE 
kriyApadadondige  mADuga  mattu  jAga  ghaTakagaLu  bandiddu,  adakke 
`Ata  kAvEri  nadiya  ondu  bhAgadalli  Ijida'  endiSTE  arthavide. 
(55ka-kha)dallU hIgeyE.  
    tumbu,  suli,  hinDu,  koyyu,  kuDi,  Odu,  bare  modalAda 
bEre  kelavu  kriyApadagaLU  idE  rItiyalli  vyakti,  vastu  modalA 
duvannu  pUtriyAgi  illavE  avugaLa  ondu  bhAgavannaSTE  bAdhisu 
ttiralu  sAdhyaviddu,  intaha  vyakti  illavE  vastuvannu  sUcisuva  ghaTaka 
gaLu  avugaLondige  Agugada  rUpadallAgalI  illavE  suru  athavA 
jAgada rUpadallAgalI baraballuvu.  
(56ka)  avanu A pustakavannu OdiddAne. 
(56kha) avanu A pustakadinda ondu kateyannu OdiddAne. 
(57ka)  Ake ondu pustakavannu barediddALe. 
(57kha) Ake ondu pustakadalli kaviteyannu barediddALe. 
(56ka)dalli Odu kriyApadadondige pustaka emba pada ondu Aguga 
ghaTakavAgi  bandide,  mattu  A  kriyApada  sUcisuva  ghaTane  pustakavannu 
pUtriyAgi bAdhisuttadeyemba artha A vAkyakkide. Adare, (56kha)dalli 
adE  kriyApadadondige  pustaka  emba  pada  ondu  suru  ghaTakavAgi 
bandide  mattu  A  vAkyakke  Odu  kriyApada  sUcisuva  ghaTane  pustakada 
ondu  bhAgavannaSTE  bAdhisuttadeyemba  arthavide.  (57ka-kha)gaLalli 
bandiruva bare kriyApadakkU I rIti eraDu  baLakegaLiruvudannu kANa 
bahudu. 
2.5.3 kadaluvikeya sUcane 
kriyApadagaLannu  kadaluvavu  mattu  kadaladavu  embudAgi  eraDu 
gumpugaLalli  vingaDisalu  sAdhya  embudannu  nAvu  mEle  (2.4.4ralli) 
nODiruvevu. kadaluva kriyApadagaLondige suru illavE kone ghaTaka 
baruvudAdare, kadalada kriyApadagaLondige jAga ghaTaka baruttade. 
    Adare,  addu,  bILu,  hAku  modalAda  kelavu  kriyApadagaLu 
ondu  jAga  ghaTakadondigAgalI  illavE  ondu  suru  athavA  kone 
ghaTakadondigAgalI  baraballuvAgiddu,  avu  entaha  ghaTakadondige 
baruttave  embudannAdharisi,  avugaLa  baLakeyalli  I  eraDu  rItiya 
ghaTanegaLU sUcitavAguttave. 
(58ka)  poIlIsaru  A  kaLLana  beraLannu  kudiyuva  eNNiyalli 
addidaru. 
(58kha) poIlIsaru  A  kaLLana  beraLannu  kudiyuva  eNNige 
addidaru. 
(59ka)  surESana hosa cenDu nIrinalli biddide. 
(59kha) surESana hosa cenDu nIrige biddide. 
addu  kriyApada  sAmAnyavAgi  ondu  calaneyannu  sUcisuttiruttade. 
Adare,  adarondige  (58kha)dalli  kANisida  hAge  ondu  kone  ghaTaka 
vannu  baLasidAga  I  calaneya  mEle  ottu  bILuttade,  mattu  (58ka) 
dalli kANisida hAge jAga ghaTakavannu baLasidAga calaneya mEle ottu 
bILuvudilla. 
    idE  rItiyalli  bILu  kriyApadadondige  jAga  ghaTakavannu 
baLasidAga  calaneya  mEle  ottu  bILuvudilla  (59ka),  Adare  kone

2.6 ghaTakagaLannu pratyEkisuvudu 
mEle  sUcisiruva  hAge,  kriyApadagaLondige  avu  tiLisuva  ghaTaneya 
svarUpavannAdharisi  bEre  bEre  rItiya  ghaTakagaLannu  baLasuva  avaSyakate 
yide.  ondu  vAkyadalli  ondE  mukhya  ghaTaka  bandideyAdare  adu 
yAvudu embudannu kriyApadada svarUpada AdhArada mEle tiLiyalu 
kaSTavAguvudilla.  udAharaNegAgi,  ondu  kriyApadavu  hatOTi 
yallilladiruva ghaTaneyannu sUcisuttideyAdare adarondige bandiruva 
ghaTaka AgugavendU mattu hatOTiyalliruva ghaTaneyannu sUcisuttide 
yAdare  adarondige  bandiruva  ghaTaka  mADugavendU  hELalu  sAdhya 
(60ka)  rAju daNida. 
(60kha)  rAju kuLita. 
(60ka)  vAkya  hatOTiyallillada  ghaTaneyondannu  sUcisuttiruva 
kAraNa,  adaralli  bandiruva  rAju  emba  pada  Aguga  ghaTakavannu 
sUcisuttide.  Adare  (60kha)  vAkya  hatOTiyalliruva  ghaTaneyondannu 
sUcisuttiddu,  adaralli  bandiruva  adE  pada  mADuga  ghaTakavannu 
sUcisuttide. 
    ondu vAkyadalli eraDu athavA jAsti ghaTakagaLu bandiveyAdalli, 
avugaLalli yAvudu yAva ghaTaka embudAgi avannu pratyEkisi hELuva 
avaSyakateyunTAguttade.  I  rIti  vAkyavondaralli  bandiruva  ghaTaka 
gaLannu  pratyEkisuvudakkAgi  vibhakti  pratyayagaLannAgalI  illavE  bEre 
yAvudAdarU padagaLannAgalI sErisuva krama baLakeyallide.  
    udAharaNegAgi  ondu  vAkyadalli  mADuga  mattu  AgugagaLemba

ondarondige (Agugadondige) annu emba vibhakti pratyayavannu baLasa 
lAguttade. 
(61ka)  hari bidda.

2.6.1 annu pratyayada baLake 
ondu  vAkyadalli  mADugavannu  sUcisuva  pada  obba  vyakti  illavE 
ondu  prANiyannu  gurutisuttiddu,  Agugavannu  sUcisuva  pada  ondu 
vastuvannu  gurutisuttideyAdalli,  averaDaralli  yAvudu  Aguga  mattu 
yAvudu  mADuga  emba  viSayadalli  samSaya  baruva  sambhava  kaDime. 
yAkendare,  antaha  sandabhragaLallella  vyakti  illavE  prANi  mADuga 
vAgiruttade mattu vastu AgugavAgiruttade. hAgAgi antaha vAkyagaLalli 
Agugavannu  gurutisuva  padadondige  annu  pratyayavannu  baLasadiralu 
sAdhyavide.

(62kha) jAnaki aDuge(yannu) mADidaLu. 
    Adare sAmAnyavAgi Agugavannu sUcisuva pada kriyApadada hattira 
bandiruvAga  mAtra  I  rIti  annu  pratyayavannu  baLasadiralu  sAdhya. 
adakkU  kriyApadakkU  naDuve  yAvudAdarU  bEre  pada  illavE 
pratyaya bandideyAdare idu sAdhyavAgadu.

2.6.3 sambandhavannu sUcisuva padagaLu

pratyayagaLu

mattu  prErakagaLeraDU  bandiveyAdare,  avugaLalli  Agugavannu  uLida

2.7 vyavahAra sambandha 
vAkyagaLalli  baruva  ghaTakagaLigU  mattu  kriyApadakkU  naDuviruva 
sambandhagaLannu  sUcisuva  bage  hEge  embudannu  nAvu  mElina 
vibhAgagaLalli  (2.1-2.6ralli)  nODiruvevu.  I  ellA  sambandhagaLU 
vAkyada  arthakke  sambandhisiveyAda  kAraNa  ivannella  oTTAgi  `artha' 
sambandhagaLendu  kareyabahudu.  ivannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  kannaDadalli 
prAmukhyavAgi vibhakti pratyayagaLa baLakeyAguttade. 
    intaha artha sambandhagaLannu mAtravallade vAkya ghaTakagaLa mUlaka 
bEre  kelavu  rItiya  sambandhagaLannU  sUcisuva  avaSyakateyide.  I 
sambandhagaLu  vAkyavondara  ghaTakagaLannu  A  vAkyada  hindina  vAkyagaLalli 
bandiruva ghaTakagaLondige mattu mAtina sannivESadondige sambandhisu 
ttave. ivannu `vyavahAra' sambandhagaLendu kareyabahudu. 
2.7.1 viSaya mattu suddi 
vAkyagaLannella ondu viSaya mattu A viSayada kuritAgi vAkya tiLisuva 
suddi  embudAgi  eraDu  vibhAgagaLalli  vingaDisalu  sAdhyavide.  kannaDa 
vAkyagaLalli sAmAnyavAgi modalige baruva ghaTaka viSayavannU  mattu 
adara  anantara  baruva  ghaTakagaLu  (mattu  kriyApada)  A  viSayada 
kuritAgi EnAdarU ondu suddiyannU tiLisuttave.  
(70ka)  rAju angaDige hOgiddAne. 
(70ka)dalli  modalige  bandiruva  rAju  emba  ghaTaka  ondu  viSaya 
vannU mattu adara anantara bandiruva angaDige hOgiddAne emba

2.7.2 mukhya amSa

`suddi'  vibhAgadalli  bandiruva  bEre  bEre  ghaTaka  illavE  kriyA 
guNapadagaLalli ondannu suddiya mukhya amSavannAgi mADalu I rIti 
kriyApadada eDakke irisi hELalu sAdhyavide.
