2.7.3 hinneNike 
ondu  vAkyadalli  hELalu  biTTu  hOda  amSavannu  vAkya  mugi 
doDaneyE  adara  `hinneNike'yAgi  sUcisalu  sAdhyavide.  udAharaNe 
gAgi keLagina vAkyagaLannu gamanisabahudu. 
(80ka)  rAjuvannu bahaLa hogaLidaru, heDmASTru. 
(80kha)  heDmASTru bahaLa hogaLidaru, rAjuvannu. 
(81ka)  ninne ondu Tivi tandidda, rAju. 
(81kha) rAju ondu Tivi tandidda, ninne. 
(80ka)dalli heDmASTru embudannu hinneNikeyAgi sUcisalAgide mattu 
(80kha)dalli  idakke  badalu  rAjuvannu  embudannu  hinneNikeyAgi 
mADa lAgide. 
    sAmAnyavAgi  eraDu  bEre  bEre  rItiya  sandabhragaLalli  intaha 
hinneNikegaLa baLakeyAguvudannu kANabahudu. modalaneyadAgi, mukhya 
amSavannu  hELuva  Aturadalli  ondu  amSa  biTTuhOgiddu  adannu 
anantara  hinneNikeyAgi  hELiralu  sAdhyavide;  mattu  eraDaneyadAgi, 
ondu amSavannu sUcisuva avaSyakateyillavendu modalu bhAvisiddu, 
suddiyannu  tiLisuvAga  adu  spaSTavAgalillavendu  anisidalli,  anantara 
hELadidda amSavannu hinneNikeyAgi tiLisiralu sAdhyavide.  
    vyavahAra  sambandhagaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  kannaDadalli  I  rIti 
ghaTakagaLa  jAgavannu  badalAyisuvudu,  otti  hELuvudu,  ghaTakagaLannu 
vAkyada  konege  vagrAyisuvudu,  avakke  kelavu  pada  illavE  pratyaya 
gaLannu  sErisuvudu,  modalAda  bEre  bEre  rItiya  vidhAnagaLa 
baLakeyAguttiddu  ivu  artha  sambandhagaLannu  sUcisuva  vidhAnakkinta 
tIra bhinnavAgive.  
    vyAkaraNagaLalli  sAmAnyavAgi  artha  sambandhakkEnE  heccina  gamana 
koDuttiddu,  vyavahAra  sambandhakke  jAsti  gamana  harisilla.  hAgAgi, 
ivugaLa  kuritAgi  namage  tiLidiruva  amSagaLu  bahaLa  kaDime  (jAsti 
vivaragaLige tirumalES (1979) mattu bhaT (1991) nODi). 
2.8 guNapadagaLa baLake 
kriyAvAkyagaLalli  mukhyavAda  mattu  mukhyavallada  ghaTakagaLu  mAtra 
vallade  ondu  athavA  jAsti  guNapadagaLU  baraballuvu.  ivu  kriyA 
padavu  tiLisuva  ghaTaneya  guNadharmagaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  baLake 
yAguttave.  ghaTane  entahadu  embudannu  mAtravallade  ghaTaneya 
samaya  mattu  jAgagaLannU  intaha  guNapadagaLu  sUcisaballuvu. 
hAgAgi,  vAkyadalli  baruva  I  guNapadagaLigU  mattu  ghaTaneya  jAga, 
samaya  modalAduvannu  sUcisuva  mukhyavallada  ghaTakagaLigU  naDuve 
hattirada sambandhavide. 
(82ka)  rAju sumatiyannu bahaLa hogaLida. 
(82kha) avaru nALe AphIsige hOguvudilla. 
(82ga)  alli nimmannu yArU mAtanADisuvudilla. 
    guNapadagaLa  baLakeya  kuritAgi  heccina  vivaragaLannu  Araneya 
adhyAyadalli koDalAgide. 
2.9 sArAmSa 
yAvudAdarU  ondu  ghaTane  naDedudannu  illavE  naDeyaliruvudannu 
tiLisabEkAdAga  kriyAvAkyagaLannu  baLasabEkAguttade.  intaha  kriyA 
vAkyagaLalli  mukhya  padavAgi  ondu  kriyApada  bandiruttade.  I  kriyA 
padadondige  mukhyavAgi  eraDu  pratyayagaLu  bandiruttave.  ivugaLalli 
ondu  ghaTaneya  samayavannu  sUcisuttade  mattu  innondu  ghaTane 
yalli  toDagikonDiruva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLalli  ondannu 
cuTukAgi sUcisuttade. 
    ghaTaneyalli toDagikonDiruva vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu heccu 
vivaravAgi  sUcisalu  kriyAvAkyadalli  ondu  athavA  jAsti  mukhya 
ghaTakagaLu  baruttave.  idallade,  ghaTaneya  samaya,  jAga,  uddESa, 
ghaTaneyalli  baLasida 
sUcisuvudakkAgi 
bEreyU kelavu (mukhyavallada) ghaTakagaLannu kriyAvAkyagaLalli baLasalu 
sAdhyavide. 
    ondu  vAkyadalli  eraDu  athavA  jAsti  ghaTakagaLu  bandiveyAdalli 
avugaLalli yAvudu yAva ghaTaka embudannu sUcisuvudakkAgi avuga 
Londige vibhakti pratyayagaLa illavE itara padagaLa baLakeyAguttade. 
    vAkyadalli  baruva  ghaTakagaLannu  mattu  kriyAguNapadagaLannu  hindina 
vAkyagaLa  ghaTakagaLondige  mattu  mAtina  sannivESadondige  sambandhisu 
sAdhana,  modalAduvannu 
vudakkAgi  vAkyadalli  avu  baruva  jAga,  otti  hELuvudu,  kelavu  pada 
illavE pratyayagaLa baLake modalAda vidhAnagaLannu baLasalAguttade. 
    kriyAvAkyagaLalli  baruva  kelavu  kriyAguNapadagaLu  ghaTanegaLa 
guNadharmagaLannU sUcisaballuvu.   
<a id="adhyAya-3"></a>
[English →](./25-kannaDa-vAkyagaLa-oLaracane-en#chapter-3--internal-structure-of-stative-sentences) | [Eke →](./25-kannaDa-vAkyagaLa-oLaracane-kn-eke#viSayavAkyagaLa-oLaracane)
adhyAya mUru 
viSayavAkyagaLa oLaracane 
3.1 pIThike 
kannaDadalli  mukhyavAgi  mUru  rItiya  viSayavAkyagaLu  baLakeyallive. 
ivu mUru rItiya sangatigaLannu tiLisuvudakkAgi baLakeyAguttave. I 
sangatigaLa  svarUpada  AdhArada  mEle  keLage  koTTiruvante  I  vAkya 
gaLannu  iruvikeya  vAkyagaLu,  guNavAkyagaLu  mattu  sambandha  vAkyagaLu 
embudAgi hesarisabahudu. 
iruvikeya  vAkyagaLu:  yAvudAdarondu  jAgadalli  vyakti, 
vastu modalAdavugaLa iruvikeyannu tiLisuva vAkyagaLu.  
(1ka)  mESTru klAsinalliddAre. 
(1kha)  nimma hosa pustaka mEjina mElittu. 
(1ga)  Akeya hattira ondu holige yantravide. 
(1gha)  I hAlinalli nALe ondu sabheyide. 
(1ka) vAkyadalli klAsu emba jAgadalli mESTru emba vyaktiya Igina 
iruvikeyannu  tiLisalAgide,  mattu  (1kha)  vAkyadalli  mEju  emba 
jAgadalli nimma hosa pustaka emba vastuvina hindina iruvikeyannu 
tiLisalAgide, ityAdi. 
guNavAkyagaLu:  yAvudAdarondu  guNadharmavannu  vyakti, 
vastu modalAdavugaLa mEle horisuva vAkyagaLu.  
(2ka)  Akeya tuTi bahaLa kempagide. 
(2kha)  nArAyaNasvAmiya tale nuNNagittu. 
(2ga)  A huli bahaLa hasidide. 
(2gha)  nimma kelasa avarige meccugeyAgide. 
(2ka) vAkyadalli bahaLa kempu emba guNadharmavannu Akeya tuTiya 
mEle  horisalAgide,  mattu  (2kha)  vAkyadalli  nuNNage  emba  guNa 
dharmavannu  nArAyaNasvAmiya  taleya  mEle  horisalAgide, 
sambandhavAkyagaLu:  yAvudAdarondu  vyakti,  vastu,  sangati, 
ghaTane modalAdavugaLondige bErondu vyakti, vastu, sangati, 
ghaTane  modalAdavugaLannu  sambandhisuva  vAkyagaLu.  intaha 
vAkyagaLu  ibbaru  vyaktigaLa  naDuviruva  sambandhagaLannu  (udA: 
nanTastike)  mAtravallade  obba  vyakti  mattu  ondu  vastuvina 
naDuviruva  sambandhavannAgali  (udA:  vyaktiya  anga,  sottu, 
dEhada illavE manassina sthiti, kelasa, ityAdi) illavE eraDu 
vastugaLa  illavE  sangatigaLa  naDuviruva  sambandhavannAgali 
(udA:  vastu  illavE  sangatiya  guNadharma,  anga,  ityAdi) 
sUcisaballuvu. 
(3ka)  A rAjanige mUvaru rANiyariddaru. 
(3kha)  sItApatige nAlku emmegaLive. 
(3ga)  Atana mAtige bahaLa beleyiruttade. 
(3gha)  poIlIsarige nimma mEle samSayavittu. 
(3ka)  vAkyadalli  rAja  emba  vyaktigU  mattu  mUvaru  rANiyarigU 
naDuviruva  sambandhavannu  sUcisalAgide,  mattu  (3gha)dalli  poIlIsa 
rigU mattu nimma mElina samSaya emba guNadharmakkU naDuviruva 
sambandhavannu sUcisalAgide, ityAdi. 
3.1.1 samayabhEdagaLu 
viSayavAkyagaLalli  baruva  iru  kriyApada  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  baruva 
itara kriyApadagaLiginta samayabhEdavannu sUcisuvudaralli bhinnavAgide. 
itara  kriyApadagaLige  hindina  mattu  mundina  embudAgi  eraDu 
samayagaLannu sUcisuva padarUpagaLu mAtra iveyAdare, iru kriyA 
padakke  hindina,  mundina  mattu  Igina  embudAgi  mUru  bEre  bEre 
samayagaLannu  sUcisuva  padarUpagaLive.  udAharaNegAgi  keLage  (4-
5)ralli koTTiruva vAkyagaLannu pariSIlisabahudu.  
rAju Iga maneyalliddAne. 
(4kha)  rAju ninne maneyallidda. 
rAju nALe maneyalliruttAne. 
rAju manege hOda. 
(5kha)  rAju manege hOguttAne. 
(4)ralli  mUru  bEre  bEre  vAkyagaLu  bandiddu,  ivugaLalli  iru 
kriyApada iddAne, idda mattu iruttAne emba  mUru bEre bEre 
rUpagaLalli  bandiruvudannu  gamanisabahudu.  ivu  A  vAkyagaLannu 
ADuttiruva samaya (Igina samaya), adakkinta hindina samaya mattu 
adara anantarada samaya (mundina samaya) embudAgi mUru bEre 
bEre samayagaLalli ondu sangatiya iravannu sUcisuttave.  
Adare  (5)ralli  eraDu  vAkyagaLu  mAtra  bandiddu,  ivugaLalli 
hOgu kriyApada hOda mattu hOguttAne emba eraDu rUpa 
gaLalli  mAtra  kANisikoLLuttade.  ivu  A  vAkyavannADiruva  samayakkinta 
hindina  samaya  mattu  adakkinta  mundina  samaya  embudAgi  eraDu 
samayagaLalli  naDeyuva  ghaTanegaLannu  mAtravE  sUcisaballuvu.  iru 
embudara  hAge  hOgu  embudakke  (mattu  itara  kriyApadagaLige) 
Igina  samayadalli  naDeyuttiruva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisalu  mundina 
samayada rUpakkinta bhinnavAda rUpavilla. 
ondu  mAtannu  ADuttiruva  samayadallEnE  naDeyuva  Igina 
samayada  ghaTaneyannu  antaha  vAkyagaLalli  sUcisabEkendiddalli, 
kannaDadalli  adakkAgi  A  vAkyagaLa  kriyApadadondige  iru  kriyApadada 
Igina  samayada  rUpavannu  sErisi  baLasabEkAguttade.  Adare  idakke 
ghaTane  naDeyuttA  ide  emba  artha,  illavE  ghaTane  halavu  bAri 
naDeyuttide emba arthavU baruttade. 
rAju pustaka OduttA iddAne. 
(6kha)  rAju taleyannu ADisuttA iddAne. 
(6ka)  vAkyakke  `pustaka  Oduva  ondu  ghaTane  naDeyuttA  ide'  emba 
arthavideyAdare,  (6kha)  vAkyakke  `taleyannu  ADisuvantaha'  halavu 
ghaTanegaLu ondAdarondarante naDeyuttive emba artha baruttade.  
kannaDadalli  I  rIti  ondu  viSaya  illavE  sangatiya  iravannu 
sUcisuva  iru  kriyApadakke  mUru  samaya  rUpagaLiveyAdarU 
ghaTanegaLannu  sUcisuva  itara  kriyApadagaLige  eraDu  samayarUpagaLu 
mAtra  kANisikoLLuvudakke  samayakke  sambandhisidante  sangati  mattu 
ghaTanegaLa  naDuviruva  vyatyAsavE  mukhya  kAraNa.  ondu  ghaTaneyannu 
tiLisuva  samayadalli  adu  ondO  naDediruttade  illavE  naDeya 
liruttade.  hAgAgi  adara  samayavannu  sUcisalu  eraDu  samaya 
rUpagaLiddare sAku. 
Adare  ondu  sangatiyu  adannu  tiLisuva  sandabhradalliyU 
irabahudu  illavE  adakkinta  hinde  illavE  mundeyU  irabahudu. 
hAgAgi  adara  iruvikeyannu  tiLisuva 
mUru 
samayarUpagaLa avaSyakateyide.  
kriyApadakke 
tiLisuva  samayadalli  ondu  ghaTane  naDeyuttirabEkAdare  adu 
kSaNikavAgilladirabEku  illavE  kSaNikavAgiddarU  halavu  bAri  naDeyu 
vantahadirabEku.  I  eraDu  heccina  arthagaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi 
kannaDadalli  saraLa  kriyArUpada  badalu  mEle  sUcisidante  kUDu 
kriyApadagaLannu baLasuva krama baLakeyalli bandide.        
kriyAvAkyagaLigU  mattu  viSayavAkyagaLigU  naDuve  samayakke 
sambandhisidante innondu mukhyavAda vyatyAsavide. kriyAvAkyagaLallella 
ghaTaneya  samayavannu  khaDDAyavAgiyU  sUcisalEbEkemba  niyama 
vide.  Adare  viSayavAkyagaLalli  I  rIti  khaDDAyavilla.  viSayada 
samaya aSTondu prAmukhyavAgillavAdalli adannu sUcisadE iralU 
sAdhya  vide  mattu  intaha  sandabhragaLalli  I  vAkyagaLannu  iru 
kriyApada villadeyU baLasalu sAdhyavide. 
rAju bombAyiyalli, avana henDati bengaLUrinalli. 
(7kha)  Akeya tuTi kempu.’ 
(7ga)  A rAjanige mUvaru rANiyaru. 
sAmAnyavAgi  intaha  iru  kriyApadavillada  viSayavAkyagaLu  mAta 
nADuva  samayakke  sambandhisida  sangatiyondannu  tiLisuttave.  Adare 
mEle  (7ga)dalli  kANisidante  adu  mAtanADuva  samayakkintalU 
vAkyada  mUlaka  nirUpisuva  samayakke  sambandhisidantaha  sangati 
yAgiralu sAdhyavide. 
3.1.2 kriyAvAkyagaLondige sambandha 
viSayavAkya  mattu  kriyAvAkyagaLu  halavu  viSayagaLalli  ondakkinta 
ondu  bhinnavAgiveyAdarU  avugaLa  naDuve  hattirada  sambandhavide. 
sAmAnyavAgi  ondu  kriyAvAkya  eraDu  viSayavAkyagaLannu  sambandhisu 
ttadeyendu hELalu sAdhyavide. 
rAju marakke hattida. 
rAju marada keLagiddAne. 
(8kha)  rAju marada mEliddAne. 
jAnaki ondu maguvannu haDedaLu. 
(9ka)  jAnakige makkaLilla. 
(9kha)  jAnakige ondu magu ide. 
(8)ralli bandiruva kriyAvAkyavu sUcisuva ghaTane (8ka) mattu (8kha) 
gaLalli  bandiruva  viSayavAkyagaLu  sUcisuva  eraDu  sangatigaLannu 
jODisi  hELuttaveyembudannu  gamanisabahudu.  marada  keLagiruva 
rAju  marakke  hattuva  mUlaka  marada  mEliruvavanAguttAne.  (9) 
rallU  hIgeyE;  makkaLillada  jAnaki  ondu  maguvannu  haDeyuvudara 
mUlaka ondu magu iruvavaLAguttALe. 
3.2 iruvikeya vAkyagaLu 
yAvudAdarondu jAgadalli vyakti, vastu, guNadharma modalAdavugaLa 
iruvikeyannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  iruvikeya  vAkyagaLu  baLakeyAguttave. 
hAgAgi,  intaha  vAkyagaLalli  jAgavannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  ondu  ghaTaka 
mattu  adaralliruva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi 
ondu ghaTaka embudAgi eraDu mukhya ghaTakagaLu barabEkAguttade. 
(10ka)  kappu maDakeyalli bisi nIride. 
(10kha) biLigiriyavara bekku bEvina marada tudiyallittu. 
(10ga)  Akeya huDuga nammalliruttAne. 
(10ka)dalli ondu jAgavannu sUcisuva kappu maDake emba ghaTakavU 
mattu  adaralliruva  ondu  vastuvannu  sUcisuva  bisi  nIru  emba 
ghaTakavU  bandiruvudannu  gamanisabahudu.  itara  vAkyagaLallU  idE 
rItiyalli eraDeraDu ghaTakagaLu bandiruvudannu kANabahudu. 
3.2.1 jAgada svarUpa 
kriyAvAkyagaLalli  ondu  ghaTane  illavE  calaneya  suru,  kone  mattu 
jAgavannu  sUcisaballa  mUru  rItiya  ghaTakagaLu  baraballuvembudannu 
nODiruvevu.  Adare 
nAvu  hindina  adhyAyadalli 
iruvikeya vAkyagaLalli vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa jAgavannu sUcisa 
balla ghaTakagaLu mAtra baraballuvu.  
    idakke  kAraNavEnendare,  suru  illavE  konegaLondige  baruva 
ghaTanegaLindalU  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLa  jAgavannu  sUcisuva 
sangatigaLE  siddhavAguvuvAda  kAraNa,  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLa 
jAgavannu  sUcisuva  viSayavAkyagaLige  suru  mattu  konegaLannu 
sUcisuva ghaTakagaLa avaSyakateyilla. 
(11ka)  bekku marada tudige hattitu. 
(11kha) bekku marada tudiyallide. 
(12ka)  rAyaru bengaLUrininda bandiddAre. 
(12kha) rAyaru bengaLUrinalli illa. 
(11ka)dalli hattu emba ghaTaneya koneyannu sUcisuvudakkAgi marada 
tudige  emba  ghaTaka  bandide.  Adare  A  ghaTaneyinda  siddhavAgiruva 
sangatiyannu tiLisuva (11kha) vAkyadalli marada tudiyalli embudAgi 
ondu jAgavannu sUcisuva ghaTaka bandide.  
    idE rItiyalli (12ka) vAkyadalli  ghaTaneya suruvannu sUcisuva 
bengaLUrininda  emba  ghaTakavU  mattu  (12kha)  vAkyadalli  A  ghaTane 
yinda  siddhavAgiruva  sangatiya  jAgavannu  sUcisuva  bengaLUrinalli 
emba ghaTakavU bandiruvudannu kANabahudu. 
    jAgavannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  kannaDadalli  alli  pratyaya  baLakeyAgu 
ttade.  hAgAgi,  I  pratyayavannoLagonDiruva  padagaLannu  heccina 
iruvikeya  vAkyagaLallU  kANabahudu.  I  pratyaya  mAtravallade, 
suttalU,  hattira,  hindugaDe  modalAda  bEre  kelavu  padagaLU 
jAgagaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  intaha  iruvikeya  vAkyagaLalli  bara 
balluvu. ivu jAgagaLa naDuviruva vayvidhyavannu sUcisuttave. 
(13ka)  avara maneya suttalU muLLina giDagaLive. 
(13kha) tandeya hattira maganU idda. 
(13ga)  maneya hindugaDe tarakAriya tOTa ide. 
(13gha) peTTigeya oLage ondu hAvittu. 
3.2.2 samayaghaTakada baLake 
jAga  mattu  jAgadalliruva  vyakti,  vastu  ityAdi  embudAgi  eraDu 
ghaTakagaLu  mAtravallade  iruvikeya  samayavannu  heccu  spaSTavAgi 
sUcisaballa samaya ghaTakavU iruvikeya vAkyagaLalli baraballudu.  
(14ka)  ninne rAtri I udyAnadalli ondu huli ittu. 
(14kha) mAdhavarAyaru Iga klAsinalli iddAre. 
(14ga)  ivattu beLigge A TAnkiyalli svalpa nIrittu. 
(14gha) mUru vaSragaLa hinde Ata mangaLUrinallidda. 
(14ka)dalli I udyAna embudAgi ondu jAgavannu sUcisuva ghaTaka 
mattu  ondu  huli  embudAgi  A  jAgadalliruva  ondu  prANiyannu 
sUcisuva  ghaTaka  mAtravallade  ninne  rAtri  embudAgi  ondu  samaya 
vannu sUcisuva ghaTakavU bandiruvudannu gamanisabahudu. 
sUcisuva  ghaTaka 
    iruvikeya  vAkyavondaralli 
sUcisuva  ghaTakavannu  baLasadiralU 
bandideyAdalli,  jAgavannu 
sAdhyavide.  jAgakkU  samayakkU  hattirada  sambandhaviruvudE  idakke 
kAraNavirabEku. 
samayavannu 
(15ka)  nALe rAtri ondu bhArI maduveyide. 
(15kha) ninne rAtri ondu ondu mITing ittu. 
(15ga)  ivattu mUru ganTege hosa udyAnada udghATaneyide. 
sAmAnyavAgi intaha vAkyagaLalli obba vyakti illavE vastuvina iravannu 
sUcisuvudakkintalU  ondu  ghaTaneya  iravannu  sUcisalAguttade. 
ghaTanegaLa  iruvikege  jAgakkintalU  samayavE  heccu  prAmukhyavAdu 
dAda  kAraNa,  ivu  ondu  niScitavAda  samayadalli  ghaTaneya  iravannu 
sUcisuva bErondu rItiya vAkyagaLu endU hELalu sAdhyavide. 
3.2.3 iru kriyApadada baLake 
viSayavAkyagaLalli  vastu,  vyakti  modalAdavugaLa  iravannu  sUcisuva 
kriyApadavannu  baLasadiralU  sAdhya  embudannu  mEle  3.1.1ralli 
nODiruvevu.  Adare  iruvikeya  vAkyagaLalli  I  rIti  iru 
kriyApadavannu  baLasadiruvalli  kelavu  nibrandhagaLive.  sAmAnyavAgi 
ondu  ghaTaneya  iravannu  sUcisuva  iruvikeya  vAkyagaLalli  mAtravE 
I rIti iru kriyApadavannu baLasadiralu sAdhya. 
(16ka)  avaralli nALe maduve (ide). 
(16kha) SAleyalli ivattu parIkSe (ide). 
    vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLa  iravannu  sUcisuva  vAkyagaLalli  I 
rIti  iru  kriyApadavannu  baLasadiruvudu  kaSTa.  Adare,  intaha  eraDu 
athavA  jAsti  iruvikeya  vAkyagaLannu  jODisi  hELalAgideyAdalli, 
avugaLa iru kriyApadavannu baLasadiralu sAdhyavide. 
(17ka)  ondu kayyalli koDe (ide) mattu innondaralli tarakAri 
(17kha) kONeya  naDuve  ondu  mEju  (ide),  mEjina  mEle 
kelavu  pustakagaLu  (ive),  mEjina  pakkakke  ondu  kapATu 
(ide), mattu mEjina keLage ondu sTUlu (ide). 
(17ga)  mAdhavarAyaru  klAsinalli  (iddAre),  mattu  huDugarella 
santeyalli (iddAre). 
3.3 guNavAkyagaLu 
guNavAkyagaLalli  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu  sUcisuva  ondu  ghaTaka 
mattu  A  ghaTakada  guNadharmavondannu  sUcisuva  innondu  ghaTaka 
ghaTakagaLu  baruttave.  ivugaLalli 
embudAgi  eraDu 
mukhya 
sAmAnyavAgi  guNadharmavannu  sUcisuva  ghaTaka  adannu  paDediruva 
vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu sUcisuva ghaTakada anantara baruttade. 
(18ka)  Ace maneya huDuga sappagiddAne. 
(18kha) I buTTiya haNNugaLu mettagive. 
(18ga)  I giDada nimbEhaNNu bahaLa doDDadAgide. 
vAkyadallU  hIgeyE.  I  eraDu 
(18ka)  vAkyadalli  Ace  maneya  huDuga  embudu  obba  vyaktiyannU 
mattu  sappage  embudu  A  vyaktiya  guNadharmavannU  sUcisuttave. 
vAkyagaLallU 
guNadharmavannu  sUcisuva  ghaTaka  age  pratyayadalli  konegoLLuttade 
embudannu gamanisa bahudu. 
    (18ga)  vAkya  iveraDakkinta  svalpa  bhinnavAdudu.  idaralli  ondu 
vastuvannu  sUcisuva  I  giDada  nimbEhaNNu  embudu  itara  eraDu 
vAkyagaLalli vyakti illavE vastuvannu sUcisuva ghaTakada hAgeyE ide; 
Adare,  A  vastuvina  guNadharmavannu  sUcisuva  bahaLa  doDDadAgi 
emba  ghaTaka  Agi  emba  kriyApadarUpadalli  konegonDiddu  itara 
eraDu  vAkyagaLalli  kANisuva  guNadharmavannu  sUcisuva  ghaTakakkinta 
bhinnavAgide. 
3.3.1 age pratyayada baLake 
age pratyayavannu baLasi tayArisiruva padagaLu kannaDadalli jAsti illa. 
kempage,  karrage,  beLLage,  nuNNage,  neTTage,  teppage,  teLLage,  dunDage, 
beccage,  mettage,  mellage,  sappage  modalAdavugaLu  I  vibhAgakke 
sErabahudAda padagaLu. 
(19ka)  Akeya makkaLu dunDagiddAre. 
(19kha) A baTTe bahaLa beLLagide. 
(19ga)  I buTTiya haNNugaLu mettagive. 
(19gha) tAtana tale nuNNagide. 
    age  pratyayadalli  konegoLLuva  I  ghaTakagaLa  mundeyU  Agi 
emba kriyArUpavannu baLasi hELalu sAdhyavide. 
(20ka)  Akeya tuTi bahaLa kempagide. 
(20kha)  Akeya tuTi bahaLa kempagAgide. 
Adare  I  eraDu  vAkyagaLa  naDuve  arthadalli  vyatyAsavideyembudannu 
gamanisabahudu.  (20ka)  vAkyakke  `Akeya  tuTi  kempu'  emba  ondu 
sangatiyannu  tiLisuva  artha  mAtra  ide,  Adare  (20kha)  vAkyakke  I 
artha  mAtravallade  `kempillada  tuTi  kempAgiruva'  ondu  ghaTaneyannu 
tiLisuva arthavU baralu sAdhyavide. 
3.3.2 Agi kriyArUpada baLake 
Agi embudu Agu kriyApadada `jODisuva' rUpa (10.2.4 nODi). 
intaha  jODisuva  kriyArUpagaLu  sAmAnyavAgi  ondu  ghaTaneyannu 
sUcisuva  vAkyavannu  adara  anantara  naDeyuva  innondu  ghaTane 
illavE  sangatiyannu  sUcisuva  vAkyadondige  jODisi  hELalu 
baLakeyAguttave. 
(21ka)  jAnaki nadiyannu dATi haLLiya kaDege naDedaLu. 
(21kha) Ata baTTegaLannu hinDi oNagalu hAkida. 
(21ga)  kusuma Atana kAlige eNNe hacci tikkidaLu. 
(21gha) Ata sanghada adhyakSanAgi ondu vaSra mugiyitu. 
(21ka)dalli  dATu  kriyApadada  jODisuva  rUpavAgiruva  dATi 
embudannu  baLasalAgide.  I  rUpada  mUlaka  (21ka)dalli  `nadiyannu 
dATuva'  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  vAkyavannu  adara  anantara  jaraguva 
`haLLiya  kaDege  naDeyuva'  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  vAkyadondige 
jODisi  hELalu  sAdhyavAgide.  itara  eraDu  vAkyagaLallU  hIgeyE 
(8.2.3 nODi). 
    Agi  emba  jODisuva  kriyArUpavannU  I  rIti  ondu  ghaTane 
yannu  sUcisuva  vAkyavannu  innondu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyannu 
sUcisuva  vAkyadondige  jODisuvudakkAgi  baLasalu 
sAdhyavide 
embudannu  mEle  (21gha)dalli  nODabahudu.  idallade,  Agi  emba 
kriyArUpavannu  guNapadagaLondige  sErisi  avannu  guNavAkyagaLalli 
sUcisuva  ghaTakagaLannAgi  badalAyisuvudakkU 
guNadharmagaLannu 
baLasalu sAdhyavide embudannu keLagina udAharaNegaLalli kANabahudu. 
(22ka)  A peTTigeyoLagiruva maNigaLella kempAgive. 
(22kha) A kereya nIru yAvAgalU bisiyAgiruttade. 
(22ga)  gavrIpatiya tangi bahaLa teLuvAgiddALe. 
(22gha) A kaTTaDa bahaLa ettaravAgide. 
I  mElina  vAkyagaLigella  eraDu  bEre  bEre  arthagaLu  baralu 
sAdhyavide.  udAharaNegAgi,  (22ka)  vAkyakke  `A  peTTigeyoLagidda  maNi 
gaLu modalu biLi baNNadavAgidduvu, Adare  Iga yAvudO kAraNa 
kkAgi  kempAgive'  emba  arthavAgali,  illavE  `A  peTTigeyoLagiruva 
maNigaLella  kempu  baNNadavu'  emba  arthavAgali  baralu  sAdhyavide.  I 
eraDaneya  arthadalli  Agi  kriyArUpada  mUlaka  biLi  guNapadavannu 
guNadharmavannu  sUcisuva  ghaTakavannAgi  mADalAgide.  adakke  I 
baLakeyalli Agu kriyApadavu sUcisaballa ghaTaneyannu tiLisuva artha 
villa embudannu gamanisabahudu.  
    itara kriyApadagaLa jODisuva rUpagaLannU I rIti guNadharma 
vannu  sUcisuva  ghaTakagaLannAgi  baLasuvudara  mUlaka  guNavAkyagaLannu 
tayArisalu  sAdhyavide.  udAharaNegAgi,  keLagina  vAkyagaLalli  baruva 
jODisuva  kriyArUpagaLige  eraDu  bEre  bEre  arthagaLiralu  sAdhya 
(23ka)  angaDiya bAgilu teredide. 
(23kha) A kapATina kannaDi oDedittu. 
(23ga)  hosa kucriya kAlu muridide. 
(23gha) A huli bahaLa hasidide. 
(23ka)  vAkyavu  `muccikonDidda  angaDiya  bAgilu  Iga  teredide' 
embudAgi  ondu  ghaTaneya  iravannu  tiLisuttirabahudu,  illavE 
`angaDiya  bAgilu  teredide'  embudAgi  ondu  sangatiya  iravannu 
mAtravE  tiLisuttirabahudu.  I  eraDaneya  arthadalli  teredu  emba 
jODisuva  kriyArUpakke  angaDiya  bAgilina  ondu  guNadharmavannu 
tiLisuva kelasavaSTE iruttade. 
    Adare  I  rIti  jODisuva  kriyArUpagaLannu  guNadharmavannu 
sUcisuva  ghaTakagaLAgi  baLasabEkiddalli,  avu  hatOTiyallillada  ghaTane 
gaLannu  sUcisuttiruvudu  avaSya.  hatOTiyalliruva  ghaTanegaLannu 
sUcisuva kriyApadagaLannu jODisuva rUpadalli baLasidAgalella avakke 
ghaTaneya arthavE baruttade. 
(24ka)  rAju angaDiya bAgilannu terediddAne. 
(24kha) Ake A kapATina kannaDiyannu oDediddALe. 
(24ga)  hosa kucriya kAlannu A nAyi muridide. 
mEle  koTTiruva  mUru  vAkyagaLigU  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  artha 
videyallade sangatiyannu sUcisuva arthavilla. 
    kadaluvikeyannu  sUcisuva  kriyApadagaLa  jODisuva  rUpagaLU 
intaha vAkyagaLalli sangatiya arthavannu koDalAravu. udAharaNegAgi, 
kriyApadadondige  kadaluvikeya  suru  illavE  konegaLannu  sUcisuva 
inda  mattu  ge  emba  pratyayagaLiruva  ghaTakagaLiveyAdalli  antaha 
kriyApadagaLa jODisuva rUpagaLige guNadharmada arthavilla. 
(25ka)  mADininda nIru sOruttittu. 
(25kha) Akeya kennege masi hiDidittu. 
    idallade,  intaha  vAkyagaLalli  baruva  jODisuva  kriyArUpagaLu 
`hindina  samaya'da  kriyArUpagaLAgirabEkemba  innondu  nibrandhavU 
iruva  hAge  tOruttade.  Igina  illavE  mundina  samayada  kriyA 
rUpagaLannu  iru  kriyApadadondige  jODisuva  kriyArUpadalli 
baLasidAgalella  avakke  ghaTaneya  artha  baruttadallade  sangatiya  artha 
baruvudilla. 
(26ka)  angaDiya bAgilu tereyalide. 
(26kha) angaDiya bAgilu tereyuttA ide.

(27kha) A kapATina kannaDi oDeyuttA ide.

3.3.3 guNapadagaLa vibhajane 
Agi  kriyArUpadondige  baraballa  guNapadagaLannu  mUru  mukhya 
vibhAgagaLalli vingaDisalu sAdhyavide.  
    (ka)  avugaLondige  guNavAkyagaLalli  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu 
sUcisuvudakkAgi baruva ghaTakagaLa svarUpavannAdharisi, avanu, avaLu, 
avaru,  adu  illavE  avu  emba  savrapadadondige  baruva  doDDa, 
kiri, oLLe, takka, haLe modalAdavugaLadu ondu vibhAga. 
(28ka)  A huDuga bahaLa doDDavanAgiddAne. 
(28kha) rAdhAmaNi bahaLa keTTavaLAgiddaLu. 
(28ga)  I uppinakAyi bahaLa haLeyadAgide. 
(28gha) vAdirAjara makkaLu doDDavarAgiddaru. 
(28Ga) nyUyAkrina kaTTaDagaLu atyanta ettaravAgive. 
    mEle  koTTiruva  savrapadagaLu  ondu  mattu  ondakkinta  jAsti 
(halavu)  embudAgi  eraDu  rItiya  vacanabhEdavannu  sUcisuttave. 
idallade,  ondakkinta  jAsti  iddalli  manuSyaru  mattu  itararu  embu 
dAgi  eraDu  rItiya  lingabhEdavannU,  mattu  ondE  iddalli  heNNu, 
ganDu  mattu  itara  embudAgi  mUru  rItiya  lingabhEdavannU 
sUcisuttave embudannu gamanisabahudu. 
    (kha)  samskxtadinda  eravalAgi  banda  prakhyAta,  dxDha,  prabala, 
krUra modalAda padagaLu I rIti savrapadagaLondige baruva badalu 
nu,  Lu,  vu  illavE  ru  emba  pratyayagaLondige  baruttave.  ivannu 
eraDaneya vibhAgadalli irisabahudu. 
(29ka)  A huDuga prakhyAtanAgiddAne. 
(29kha) jAnaki bahaLa gambhIraLAgiddALe. 
(29ga)  allina poIlIsaru prabalarAgiddaru. 
(29gha) I kamba dxDhavAgide. 
     mEle  koTTiruva  pratyayagaLu  manuSyEtararalli  vacanabhEdavannu 
sUcisuvudilla.  Adare  prakhyAtadantaha  kelavu  padagaLu  gaLu  emba 
heccina pratyayada mUlaka vacanabhEdavannU sUcisaballuvu. 
(30ka)  I kampeniya kAru bahaLa prakhyAtavAgide. 
(30kha)  I kampeniya kArugaLu bahaLa prakhyAtagaLAgive. 
    (ga)  ellA  sandabhragaLallU  ondE  rUpadalli  uLiyuva  dappa, 
gaTTi,  udda,  kempu,  giDDa,  tOra,  jOru,  teLu,  bisi  modalAda 
padagaLannu mUraneya vibhAgadalli irisabahudu. 
(31ka)  A huDuga bahaLa teLuvAgiddAne. 
(31kha) gavrIpatiya tangi uddavAgiddaLu. 
(31ga)  I kereya nIru yAvAgalU bisiyAgiruttade. 
(31gha) A janara kaNNugaLu kempAgidduvu. 
3.3.4 heccina ghaTakagaLu 
guNavAkyagaLalli  guNadharmavannu  sUcisuva  ghaTaka  mattu  A  guNa 
dharmavannu  paDediruva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu  sUcisuva  ghaTaka 
embudAgi eraDu  ghaTakagaLu mAtravallade bEreyU kelavu ghaTakagaLu 
baralu sAdhyavide.  
    udAharaNegAgi,  yAvudakke  sambandhisidante  obba  vyakti  illavE 
ondu  vastuvinalli  guNadharmavondu  kANisuttade  embudannu  tiLisalu 
guNavAkyagaLalli  alli  vibhaktiyalli  konegoLLuva  `jAga'  illavE 
`samaya'vannu sUcisuva ghaTaka baraballudu.  
(32ka)  A huDugi mAtinalli jOriddALe. 
(32kha) Ata maneyalli teppagiruttAne. 
(32ga)  cikkandinalli Ake teLLagiddaLu. 
    idE rItiyalli ondu guNadharmada vyAptiyannu sUcisuvudakkAgi 
ge vibhaktiyalli konegoLLuva `kone' ghaTakavU intaha guNavAkyagaLalli 
baraballudu.  
(33ka)  A cUri nanage iSTavAgide. 
(33kha) I angi avanige doDDadAguttade. 
(33ga)  I marada tunDu nanna kelasakke takkudAgide 
(33gha) nimma kelasa avarige meccugeyAgide. 
3.3.5 jODi guNapadagaLu 
aLate mattu bhavtika guNadharmagaLannu sUcisuva guNapadagaLalli udda-
giDDa, agala-sapura, ettara-taggu, dappa-teLu, dUra-hattira, doDDa-
cikka  modalAda  kelavu  padagaLu  viruddhArthada  jODigaLAgi  baruttave 
(4.3.2  nODi).  intaha  padagaLu  guNavAkyagaLalli  baruvAga  kelavu 
nibrandhagaLigoLagAguttave. 
    modalaneyadAgi,  intaha  jODigaLalli  baruva  eraDu  padagaLu 
ondE  guNadharmada  eraDu  angagaLannu  avu  eraDu  viruddha  dikkina 
lliruvavugaLembudAgi sUcisuttave. udAharaNegAgi, udda mattu giDDa 
emberaDu  guNapadagaLu  aLatege  sambandhisida  ondE  guNadharmada 
eraDu angagaLAgiddu, viruddhArthavannu koDuttave. 
    idallade,  intaha  guNadharmagaLige  ondu  vistAra  illavE  vyApti 
yiddu,  I  vyAptiyalli  baruva  bEre  bEre  bindugaLannu  sUcisuvu 
dakkAgi  svalpa,  bahaLa,  jAsti,  oLLe  modalAda  padagaLannu  I 
guNapadagaLondige sErisi hELalu sAdhyavide.  
    udAharaNegAgi,  udda-giDDa  emberaDu  guNapadagaLu  sUcisuva 
guNadharmada vyAptiyalli nAlku bindugaLannu kalpisikoLLalu sAdhyaviddu 
avannu  keLage  tOrisida  hAge  I  guNapadagaLondige  bahaLa  mattu 
svalpa emba padagaLannu sErisi sUcisalu sAdhyavide. 
 bahaLa udda - svalpa udda - svalpa giDDa - bahaLa giDDa  
    eraDaneyadAgi,  intaha  guNapadagaLu  sUcisuva  guNadharma  avu 
yAva rItiya vyakti, prANi, vastu modalAdavugaLalli kANisikoLLuttave 
embudannu  avalambiside.  udAharaNegAgi,  ondu  Ane  eSTE  cikka 
dAdarU  atI  doDDa  iliginta  doDDadAgiruttade.  (kaTTukategaLalli 
mAtra idakke apavAdagaLiraballuvu). 
    idallade,  intaha  guNadharmagaLu  avannu  kANuva  kaNNu,  baLasuva 
sandabhra, anubhavisuva vyakti, modalAdavugaLa mElU avalambisiralu 
sAdhyavide.  udAharaNegAgi,  obbanige  bisiyAgi  kANisuva  kAphi 
innobbanige  taNNagAgi  kANisabahudu;  obbanige  khAravAgiruva  tinDi 
innobbanige sappeyAgirabahudu; nODalu cennAgiruva haNNu tinnalu 
keTTudAgirabahudu;  bassinalli  hOgalu  bahaLa  dUravAgiruva  jAga 
vimAnadalli hOgalu bahaLa hattira vAgirabahudu; ityAdi. 
    mUraneyadAgi,  guNapadagaLa  jODigaLalli  sAmAnyavAgi  ondu 
padavu iDI guNadharmavannE sUcisuvantiruttade, mattu innondu A 
guNadharmada ondu angavannaSTE sUcisuvantiruttade.  
    udAharaNegAgi, doDDa mattu cikka emberaDu padagaLu sUcisuva 
aLateya  guNadharmavannu  doDDa  emba  ondE  padada  mUlaka 
pUtriyAgi  sUcisalu  sAdhyavide;  Adare,  cikka  emba  padada  mUlaka 
adara  ondu  angavannu  mAtravE  sUcisalu  sAdhya.  I  vyatyAsavannu 
keLagina vAkyagaLalli spaSTavAgi kANabahudu. 
(35ka)  avara mane eSTu doDDadu? 
-adu bahaLa doDDadu. 
-adu bahaLa cikkadu. 
(35kha) avara mane eSTu cikkadu? 
-adu bahaLa cikkadu. 
-adu (idakkinta) svalpa cikkadu. 
doDDa emba guNapadavannu baLasiruva (35ka)da kELvige doDDa mattu 
cikka  emba  eraDu  guNapadagaLannu  baLasiyU  uttara  koDalu  sAdhya. 
Adare,  cikka  emba  padavannu  baLasiruva  (35kha)da  kELvige  cikka  emba 
padavannu baLasiruva uttaravannu mAtra koDalu sAdhya.  
    idallade,  I  rItiyAgi  guNadharmada  ondu  angavannu  mAtravE 
sUcisaballa  guNapadagaLannu  kELvigaLalli  baLasidAga,  avu  A  guNa 
dharmakke  sambandhisida  aLateyeSTembudannu  mAtravE  kELuva  badalu 
adu eSTara maTTige kaDime embudAgi kELuttave. 
(36ka)  A kOlu eSTu udda ide? 
(36kha) A kOlu eSTu giDDa ide? 
udda  emba  padavannu  baLasiruva  (36ka)  kELvi  A  kOlina  aLate 
yeSTembudannu  mAtravE  kELuttide;  A  kOlu  udda  irabahudu 
illavE  giDDa  irabahudu;  Adare,  giDDa  emba  padavannu  baLasiruva 
(36kha)da kELvi adara aLate bEkAddakkinta eSTara  maTTige kaDimeyide 
embudannu kELuttide.  
    nAlkaneyadAgi,  I  rIti  jODigaLAgi  baruva  guNapadagaLalli

vide.  I  kAraNakkAgi  keLage  koTTiruvantaha  vAkyagaLalli  jODiyAgi 
baruva guNapadagaLannu mAtravE baLasalu sAdhya.

3.3.7 iruvikeya vAkyadondigiruva sambandha 
iruvikeya  vAkyagaLigU  mattu  guNavAkyagaLigU  naDuve  hattirada

embudAgi guNavAkya tiLisaballudu.

3.4 sambandha vAkyagaLu 
itara  eraDu  viSayavAkyagaLa  hAge  sambandha  vAkyagaLallU  mukhyavAgi 
eraDu ghaTakagaLiruttave. vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu sUcisuva ghaTaka 
vondu,  mattu  avakke  sambandhisiruva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu 
sUcisuva ghaTaka innondu. ivugaLalli modalaneyadu ge emba vibhakti 
pratyayadondige baruttade. 
(49ka)  manOharanige Aru mandi huDugiyariddAre. 
(49kha) A mudukanige nUru muDi gaddeyide. 
(49ga)  I pustakakke kempu baNNada taTTiyide. 
(49gha) puNe nagarakkondu kAprarESan ide. 
(49ka)dalli  manOharanige  emba  modalaneya  ghaTaka  obba 
vyaktiyannU mattu Aru mandi huDugiyaru emba eraDaneya ghaTaka 
A  vyaktige  sambandhisiruva  vyaktigaLannU  (avara  parimANavannU) 
tiLisuttave. 
    ge  pratyayakke  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  ghaTaneya 
koneyannu  sUcisuva  arthavideyembudannu  nAvu  hinde  2.2ralli 
nODiruvevu.  sambandhavAkyagaLallU  idakke  ondu  sambandhada  `kone' 
yannu,  endare  A  sambandha  elli  hOgi  nelesuvudO  antaha  vyakti, 
vastu, modalAduvannu sUcisuva arthavideyendu hELalu sAdhyavide. 
Adare  illi  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  kANisuva  hAge  I  pratyayakke  kadaluva 
arthavilla (2.5.3 nODi). 
3.4.1 heccina ghaTakagaLu 
sambandha  vAkyagaLalli  mEle  sUcisida  eraDu  ghaTakagaLu  mAtravallade 
bEre kelavu ghaTakagaLU baraballuvu. udAharaNegAgi, obba vyaktiyalli 
kANisuva  guNadharmakke  ondu  vyAptiyideyAdalli  adannu  sUcisuvu 
dakkAgi mUraneya ghaTakavondu antaha vAkyagaLalli baraballudu. idu 
jAga ghaTakada rUpadalliruttade. 
(50ka)  Akege I sIreya mEle Aseyide. 
(50kha) avanige tanna kelasadalli Sraddheyide. 
(50ga)  jAnakige SrIhariya mEle kOpavide. 
(50gha)  A huDuganige ATadalli mAtra utsAhavide. 
    idallade,  sambandhisuva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLa  jAga  mattu 
samayagaLannu  sUcisuva  mukhyavallada  ghaTakagaLU  intaha  vAkyagaLalli 
baraballuvu. 
(51ka)  avarige ivattu ondu mITing ide. 
(51kha) huDugarige nALe SAlege rajeyide. 
3.5 sArAmSa 
bEre bEre rItiya sangatigaLannu tiLisuvudakkAgi kannaDadalli mukhyavAgi 
mUru rItiya viSayavAkyagaLa baLakeyAguttade. jAgavondaralli vyakti, 
vastu  modalAdavugaLa  iruvikeyannu  tiLisuva  `iruvikeya  vAkyagaLu', 
vyakti, vastu modalAdavugaLa guNadharmavannu tiLisuva `guNavAkyagaLu', 
mattu  vyakti,  vastu,  guNadharma  modalAdavugaLalli  ondu  innonda 
roDane  sambandhisiruvudannu  tiLisuva  `sambandha  vAkyagaLu'  embudAgi 
ivannu mUru mukhya gumpugaLalli vingaDisabahudu. 
     I  ellA  vAkyagaLallU  iru  emba  ondE  kriyApada  baruttade. 
intaha vAkyagaLalli halavannu iru kriyApadavilladeyU baLasalu sAdhya 
    intaha heccina vAkyagaLallU eraDu mukhya ghaTakagaLu bandiruttave. 
avugaLondige kelavu amukhya ghaTakagaLU baraballuvu.

4.1 padagaLu mattu padakantegaLu 
nAmapadagaLa  maTTige  pada  mattu  padakante  embudAgi  eraDu 
maTTagaLalli  baruva  ghaTakagaLannu  kalpisikoLLuva  avaSyakateyide.  mara 
embudondu  nAmapada,  mattu  doDDa  mara  embudondu  nAma 
padakante.  I  eraDu  rItiya  ghaTakagaLa  naDuve  entaha  vyatyAsagaLella 
ive,  mattu  vAkyagaLalli  avugaLa  baLake  hEge  naDeyuttade  embudannu 
I adhyAyadalli pariSIlisaliruvevu. 
    mara emba nAmapadakke oLaracaneyembudilla. adara tayArikeyalli 
m, a, r, mattu a emba nAlku varNagaLannu baLasalAgideyAdarU 
adakkiruva arthavannu I varNagaLinda nEravAgi paDeyalu sAdhyavilla. 
A nAmapadakkondu svarUpavannu koDuvudu mattu uLida nAmapada 
gaLinda adu bErAgi nilluvante mADuvudu emba I eraDu kArya 
gaLannu  mAtra  adaralli  baruva  varNagaLu  naDesaballuvu.  adara  artha 
Enu embudu yAva arthadalli adu rUDhige bandide emba viSayada 
mEle mAtravE avalambiside. 
    Adare  doDDa  mara  emba  nAmapadakante  idakkinta  tIra  bhinna 
vAdudu.  adakke  doDDa  mattu  mara  emba  eraDu  padagaLa  kUDike 
yinda  tayArAda  arthaviruva  oLaracaneyide.  adara  angagaLAgi 
bandiruva  doDDa  mattu  mara  emba  eraDu  padagaLige  mAtra  bariya 
varNagaLa kUDikeyinda tayArAda arthavilladiruva oLaracaneyide.  
tayArikege 
    nAmapadagaLallU kelavannu bEre padagaLa illavE bEre pada mattu 
pratyayagaLa kUDikeya mUlaka tayArisiruvudannu kANabahudu. Adare, 
avugaLigiruva  I  oLaracane  avugaLa 
mAtra 
sambandhisiddallade 
nEravAgi  avugaLa  arthakke  illavE  baLakege 
sambandhisiddalla.  
    udAharaNegAgi, karihalage emba nAmapadavannu kari mattu halage 
emba  eraDu  padagaLa  kUDikeya  mUlaka  tayArisalAgide.  Adare,  I 
padagaLige  mattu  avugaLa  kUDikegiruva  arthada  mEle  karihalage  emba 
nAmapadada  artha  nintilla  embudannu  gamanisabahudu.  baLakeyalli 
karihalage  emba  pada  kappallada  vastuvannU  sUcisaballudu  (karihalage 
yondakke nIli  baNNa koTTiralu sAdhyavide) mattu  halageyallada vastu 
vondannU  sUcisaballudu  (gODeya  ondu  bhAgakke  baNNa  koTTu 
adannu karihalage endu karediralU sAdhyavide).  
    nAmapada  mattu  nAmapadakantegaLa  naDuviruva  I  vyatyAsada 
AdhArada  mEle  vAkyaracaneya  maTTige  avu  eraDu  `maTTa'gaLalli  baru 
ttave endu hELalu sAdhyavAguttade. Adare intaha vyatyAsa vAkyagaLalli 
baruva  itara  padagaLa  baLakeyalli  kANisuvudilla.  udAharaNegAgi, 
kriyApadagaLa  baLakeyalli  illavE  guNapadagaLa  baLakeyalli  I  rIti 
padagaLu  mattu  padakantegaLu  embudAgi  eraDu  rItiya  ghaTakagaLu 
kANisuvudilla. idakke keLage 4.1.1ralli sUcisiruva hAge ondu mukhya 
vAda kAraNavU ide. 
4.1.1 vyatyAsada avaSyakate 
vAkyagaLalli  baruva  nAmapada,  kriyApada  mattu  guNapadagaLige  bEre 
bEre  kelasagaLive.  kriyApadagaLu  ondu  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisalu  baLake 
yAguttave,  mattu  nAmapadagaLu  antaha  ghaTaneyalli  toDagikonDi 
ruva  vyakti,  prANi,  vastu,  viSaya  modalAduvannu  gurutisalu  baLake 
yAguttave. udAharaNegAgi keLagina vAkyavannu gamanisabahudu. 
jAnaki bassinalli bengaLUrige hOgiddALe.

4.1.2 kriyApada mattu guNapadagaLu 
nAmapadagaLu  naDesabEkAgiruva  I  `gurutisuva'  kelasakkinta  kriyA 
padagaLu  naDesabEkAgiruva  `sUcisuva'  kelasa  tIra  bhinnavAdudu.  avu 
ghaTaneyondannu  sUcisuvudu  mAtravallade  adu  innobbarige  tiLiyu 
vante  mADuvudu,  adara  viSayavAgi  innobbarinda  heccina  sangati 
gaLannu kELi tiLidukoLLuvudu, innobbara mUlaka antaha ghaTaneyannu 
mADisikoLLuvudu,  adara  viSayavAgi  beragannu  sUcisuvudu,  moda 
lAda bEre bEre mAtina kelasagaLalli A ghaTaneyannu toDagisabEkAgu 
    intaha  kelasagaLannu  naDesuvudakkAgi  kriyApadagaLalli  bEreyE 
kelavu guNadharmagaLu kANisikoLLuttave. ghaTaneya samaya, ghaTaneyalli 
toDagikonDiruva vyakti, ghaTaneya svarUpa modalAduvannu sUcisuva 
pratyayagaLu  adarondige  baruttave,  mattu  entaha  mAtina  kelasadalli 
A  ghaTaneyannu  toDagisalAgide  embudannu  sUcisuva  pada  illavE 
pratyayagaLU adarondige baruttave.  
huDuganannu SAlege sEriside. 
mElina vAkyadalli bandiruva sEru kriyApadadondige adu sUcisuva 
ghaTaneyannu  innobba  vyaktiya  (huDugana)  mUlaka  naDesalAgide 
embudannu  sUcisuva  isu  pratyayavU,  A  ghaTane  (4)nE  vAkyavannu 
ADiruva  samayakkinta  modalE  naDedudembudannu  sUcisuva  id 
pratyayavU  mattu  A  ghaTaneyannu  innobba  vyaktiya  mUlaka 
naDesidavanu (4)nE vAkyada ADuganembudannu sUcisuva e pratyayavU 
bandiruvudannu kANabahudu. 
    Adare nAmapadagaLa baLakeyalli kANisuvantaha hesarisuvudu mattu 
varNisuvudu  emba  eraDu  vidhAnagaLige  kriyApadagaLa  baLakeyalli 
yAva  sthAnavU  illavAda  kAraNa,  padagaLa  mattu  padakantegaLa  naDu 
viruva vyatyAsa avugaLa racaneyalli kANisuvudilla.  
    vAkyagaLalli  guNapadagaLu  naDesabEkAgiruva  kelasavU  nAmapada 
mattu kriyApadagaLu naDesabEkAgiruva kelasagaLiginta tIra bhinnavAdudu. 
avugaLalli  nAmapadagaLondige  baruvavugaLu,  kriyApadagaLondige 
baruvavugaLu  mattu  guNapadagaLondige  baruvavugaLu  embudAgi 
mUru  vidhadavugaLiddu,  ivakke  mUru  bEre  bEre  kelasagaLive.  nAma 
padagaLondige  baruva  guNapadagaLu  nAmapadakantegaLa  tayArikeyalli 
baLakeyAguttave  mattu  hosa  hosa  nAmapadagaLa  tayArikeyallU 
baLakeyAguttave. 
    kriyApadagaLondige baruva guNapadagaLu kriyApadagaLu sUcisuva 
ghaTaneya  kuritAgi  illavE  adaralli  toDagikonDiruva  vyakti,  vastu, 
viSaya modalAdavugaLa kuritAgi EnAdarU tiLisalu baLakeyAguttiddu 
avu  sUcisuva  guNadharmagaLu  nAmapadagaLondige  baruva  guNa 
padagaLu  sUcisuva  guNadharmagaLiginta  bhinnavAgive  embudannu  munde 
nODaliruvevu.  
    guNapadagaLondige  baruva  guNapadagaLu  avugaLa  pramANa,  vyApti 
modalAduvannu  sUcisuttave.  I  mUru  rItiya  guNapadagaLa  baLake 
yallU  hesarisuvudu  mattu varNisuvudu emba vidhAnagaLa avaSyakate 
yillavAda  kAraNa  avugaLa  racaneyallU  pada  mattu  padakantegaLa 
naDuviruva vyatyAsa kANisikoLLuvudilla. 
4.2 gurutisuva vidhAnagaLu 
vAkyavondaralli  kriyApadada  mUlaka  ghaTaneyondannu  sUcisuvAga 
lella  sAmAnyavAgi  A  ghaTaneyalli  toDagikonDiruva  vyakti,  vastu, 
viSaya  modalAduvannu  gurutisikoDuva  avaSyakateyiruttade.  udA 
haraNegAgi  koDu  kriyApadavannu  ondu  vAkyadalli  baLasuvudiddalli 
yAru  yArige  Enannu  koTTaru  embudannu  tiLisuvudakkAgi  ibbaru 
vyaktigaLannU mattu ondu vastuvannU gurutisikoDabEkAguttade. 
rAju jAnakige ondu pustaka koTTa. 
vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu  I  rIti  gurutisuvudakkAgi  nAvu  vAkya 
gaLalli  nAmapadagaLannu  illavE  nAmapadakantegaLannu  baLasuttEve. 
mElina  vAkyadalli  vyaktigaLibbarannu  gurutisalu  rAju  mattu  jAnaki 
emba  eraDu  nAmapadagaLannU  mattu  vastuvondannu  gurutisalu 
ondu pustaka emba nAmapadakanteyannU baLasalAgide. 
    sAmAnyavAgi  nAmapadagaLa  mUlaka  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavu 
gaLannu  hesarisi  gurutisuttEve  mattu  nAmapadakantegaLa  mUlaka 
varNisi gurutisuttEve.  hesarisuva nAmapadagaLu mEle (5)nE  vAkya 
dalli kANisuvante ankitanAmagaLirabahudu illavE keLage (6)nE vAkya 
dalli kANisuvante rUDhanAmagaLirabahudu.  
nAyige bedarida bekku marakke hattitu. 
I (6)nE vAkyadalli nAyi mattu bekku emba eraDu rUDhanAmagaLu 
eraDu  prANigaLannU  mattu  mara  emba  innondu  rUDhanAma  ondu 
vastuvannU hesarisuttive. 
4.2.1 hesarisuvudu mattu varNisuvudu 
mEle sUcisida hAge, vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu gurutisuvudakkAgi 
hesarisuvudu  mattu  varNisuvudu  embudAgi  eraDu  rItiya  vidhAna 
gaLannu baLasalu sAdhyavide. gurutisabEkAgiruva  vyakti illavE  vastuvige 
adaradE  Ada  hesarideyAdalli  (endare  ankitanAma  illavE  rUDha 
nAmavideyAdalli)  adannu  baLasuvudara  mUlaka  nAvu  A  vyakti 
illavE vastuvannu gurutisaballevu.  
    Adare mEle vivarisidante ellA rItiya vyakti illavE vastugaLigU 
avugaLadE Ada hesarugaLiruvudilla. yAkendare, I rIti vyakti,  vastu 
modalAduvannu  hesarisuvudakkAgi  nAvu  baLasabahudAda  mattu  nenapi 
nalliTTukoLLabahudAda nAmapadagaLa sankhyege ondu parimitiyide.  
    Adare  mAtinalli  nAvu  gurutisabEkAguva  vyakti,  vastu,  modalA 
davugaLige  mattu  avugaLalli  kANisuva  vayvidhyategaLige  parimitiyilla. 
hAgAgi,  ellA  sandabhragaLallU  nammedurigiruva  vyakti  illavE  vastu 
vannu hesarisuva vidhAnada mUlaka gurutisalu sAdhyavAgadu.  
    idallade,  halavu  sandabhragaLalli  obba  vyakti  illavE  vastuvina 
hesaru  namage  tiLididdarU  namma  kELugarige  adu  tiLidilladiralu 
sAdhyavide.  bEre  kelavu  sandabhragaLalli  adannu  nAvE  maretiralu 
sAdhyavide.  intaha  sandabhragaLallU  hesarisuvudu  emba  modalaneya 
vidhAnada  badalu  varNisuvudu  emba  eraDaneya  vidhAnavannu 
baLasabEkAguttade. I eraDu vidhAnagaLa baLakeyannu keLagina vAkyagaLalli 
kANabahudu.

4.2.2 hosa mattu haLe gurutisuvikegaLu 
obba  vyakti  illavE  ondu  vastuvannu  gurutisuvudakkAgi  rUDhanAma 
vondannu  baLasuvudiddalli,  A  vyakti  illavE  vastu  kELuganige  paricita 
vAgideyE  athavA  illavE  emba  viSayada  AdhArada  mEle  hosatu 
mattu  haLeyadu  embudAgi  eraDu  rItiya  gurutisuvikegaLannu 
baLasalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi keLagina vAkyagaLannu nODabahudu. 
(9ka)  Ake  rAjuvige  ondu  pustaka  koTTiddaLu,  mattu  ninne 
rAtri yella Ata A pustaka Oduttidda. 
(9kha)  Ake  rAjuvige  ondu  pustaka  koTTiddaLu,  mattu  ninne 
rAtriyella Ata ondu pustaka Oduttidda. 
(9ka)  vAkyada  prakAra,  Ake  rAjuvige  koTTidda  pustaka  mattu  rAju 
rAtriyella Oduttidda pustaka iveraDU ondE. Adare (9kha) vAkyada 
prakAra  avanu  rAtriyella  Oduttidda  pustaka  Ake  koTTidda 
pustakakkinta bErAgiralu sAdhyavide. I vyatyAsakke (9ka)dalli eraDaneya 
bArige  ondu  pustaka  embudara  badalu  A  pustaka  embudannu 
baLasiruvudu  mattu  (9kha)dalli  eraDu  bAriyU  ondu  pustaka 
embudannE baLasiruvudu kAraNa.  
    I  vAkyagaLalli  ondu  pustaka  embudu  ondu  vastuvannu  hosa 
dAgi  gurutisi  hELalu  baLakeyAguttade.  idakke  badalu  A  pustaka 
embudu  idakke  modalE  gurutisiruvantaha  vastuvannE  innomme 
gurutisi  hELuvudakkAgi  baLakeyAguttade.  hAgAgi,  modalaneyadu 
`hosa  gurutisuvike'yannU  mattu  eraDaneyadu  `haLe  gurutisuvike' 
yannU naDesuttave endu hELabahudu. 
     A  pustaka  embudU  kelavu  sandabhragaLalli  hosa  gurutisuvike 
yannE  mADaballudu.  udAharaNegAgi  ADuganu  tanna  edurinalliruva 
ondu  pustakavannu  beraLininda  tOrisuttA  keLagina  vAkyavannu  ADiruva 
nAdare adaralli bandiruva A pustaka embudakke hosa gurutisuvikeya 
artha baruttade. 
(10)  A pustakavannu nimage yAru koTTaru? 
    kannaDadalli  sAmAnyavAgi  haLe  gurutisuvikeyannu  sUcisalu  viSiSTa 
vAda  sAdhanavEnU  bEkAguvudilla.  nAmapadagaLannu  hAgeyE  baLasi 
dAgalella avu haLe gurutisuvikeyannE mADuttave. gurutisuvike hosa 
dendu  sUcisabEkAgiruvAga  mAtra  adakkAgi  hesarinondige  ondu 
illavE  obba  embudannu  (athavA  eraDu,  mUru  modalAda  bEre 
eNikeya  padagaLannu)  baLasabEkAguttade.  kelavu,  svalpa  modalAda 
aLateya padagaLannU I kAryakkAgi baLasalu sAdhyavide. 
    idallade,  omme  gurutisiruva  vyakti  illavE  vastuvannE  innomme 
gurutisi  hELabEkAgiruvAga  adannu  sUcisuva  nAmapada  illavE 
nAmapadakanteyannu  hAgeyE  innomme  baLasuva  badalu  pratinAma 
illavE savrapadavondannu baLasuva sAdhyateyU ide.

(11kha) nAvu  hariya  viSaya  mAtanADuttiddAga  avanE 
nammeduru bandu ninta.

4.2.3 tiLida mattu tiLiyada gurutisuvikegaLu 
gurutisabEkAgiruva  vyakti  illavE  vastu  intahadE  embudAgi 
ADuganige  tiLidillavAdalli  athavA  adannu  tiLisuva  bayake  avanigilla 
vAdalli  kelavu  viSiSTavAda  savrapadagaLannu  baLasuvudara  mUlaka 
avannu  A  rIti  tiLiyada  vyakti  illavE  vastuvembudAgi  gurutisi 
hELalu  sAdhyavide.  keLagina  vAkyagaLalli  intaha  tiLiyada  vyakti  illavE 
vastuvina gurutisuvikegaLu bandiruvudannu kANabahudu. 
(13ka)  ninne rAtri nammallige yAvanO obba muduka bandidda. 
(13kha) avanu A huDugige yAvudO ondu pustaka koTTidda. 
(13ga)  A muduki haNavannu illellO aDagisiTTiddALe. 
(13gha) avanu A huDugarige EnO koTTidda. 
hindina  divasa  tanna  manege  banda  muduka  yAru  embudu  sariyAgi 
tiLiyadiddalli  illavE  adannu  tiLisuva  bayakeyilladiddalli  Atanannu 
gurutisi  hELalu  (13ka)dalli  kANisidante  yAvanO  emba  savra 
padavannu  baLasalu  sAdhyavide.  idE  rItiyalli  yAvudO,  ellO 
mattu EnO emba savrapadagaLa baLakeyannu (13kha-gha) vAkyagaLalli 
kANabahudu  (intaha  savrapadagaLa  baLakeya  kuritAgi  jAsti  vivara 
gaLannu (bhaT 2003:159)ralli nODabahudu). 
4.2.4 gurutisada nAmapadagaLu 
kelavu  sandabhragaLalli  nAmapadagaLannu  illavE  nAmapadakantegaLannu 
viSiSTavAda vyakti illavE vastuvannu gurutisuvudakkAgi baLasuva badalu 
avu  sUcisuva  viSayavannu  mAtravE  tiLisuvudakkAgiyU  baLasalu 
sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi keLagina vAkyagaLannu gamanisabahudu. 
(14)  nAnu ondu emmeyannu konDukoLLabEkendiddEne. 
(14)ralli  ondu  emme  emba  nAmapadakante  eraDu  arthagaLalli 
bandiralu  sAdhyavide.  yAva  emmeyannu  konDukoLLuvudembudannu 
(14)ra ADuga AgalE nirdharisiruvanAdare, ondu emme embudu A 
emmeyannu gurutisuttirabahudu. Adare AtaninnU hAge nirdharisillavA 
dalli  adu  yAvudondu  viSiSTavAda  emmeyannU  gurutisadiralu 
sAdhyavide. 
    idallade bEre kelavu sAmAnya sangatigaLannu tiLisuva vAkyagaLallU 
nAmapada illave nAmapadakantegaLu gurutisuva kelasavannu mADadiralu 
sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi keLagina vAkyagaLannu gamanisabahudu. 
(15ka)  taDavAgi baruva huDugarige tinDiyilla. 
(15kha) hosa akki bEyisalu nIru svalpa kaDime hAkabEku. 
(15ga)  huli hattira baruvAga kOti eccarike koDuttade. 
mElina vAkyagaLalli huDuga, tinDi, hosa akki, nIru, huli mattu 
kOti emba nAmapadagaLu yAvudE ondu viSiSTavAda vyakti illavE 
vastuvannu  gurutisadiralu  sAdhyavide.  sAmAnyavAgi  ondu  nAmapada 
illavE nAmapadakanteyannu ondu vAkyadalli gurutisuvudakkAgi baLasa 
lAgideyE athavA illavE embudu A vAkyavannu yAva uddESadalli 
baLasalAgide embudannu avalambiside. 
4.3 varNisuva nAmapadakantegaLu 
vyakti, vastu modalAduvannu gurutisuvudakkAgi varNisuva vidhAnavannu 
baLasuvudiddalli,  adakkAgi  bEre  bEre  rItiya  nAmapadakantegaLannu 
tayArisikoLLabEkAguttade.  ivu  kELugarige  gurutisabEkAgiruva  vyakti, 
vastu modalAdavugaLa varNanegaLannu koDuttave.  
    intaha  nAmapadakantegaLalli  nAmapadakke  guNapadavondannu  sErisi 
tayArisidantahavugaLu  atyanta 
prAmukhyavAdavugaLu.  ivugaLalli 
baruva  guNapadagaLu  nAmapadagaLu  hesarisuva  vyakti  illavE  vastuvina 
guNa  dharmavondannu  sUcisuva  mUlaka  avugaLa  vyAptiyannu  kaDime 
mADuttave.  udAharaNegAgi  keLagina  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  gamanisa 
bahudu. 
(16ka)  nanage ondu hU bEkAgittu. 
(16kha) nanage ondu kempu hU bEkAgittu. 
ADuganige  bEkAgiruva  vastuvannu  (16ka)dalli  hU  emba  ondu 
nAmapadada  mUlakavU  mattu  (16kha)dalli  A  nAmapadadondige 
kempu  guNapadavannu  sErisi  tayArisida  kempu  hU  emba  nAmapada 
kanteya mUlakavU gurutisalAgide.  
    (16kha)dalli  hU  nAmapadadondige  kempu  guNapadavannu  baLasi 
dudarindAgi A padada vyApti (endare adu hesarisabahudAda vastugaLa 
sankhye)  kaDimeyAgide,  mattu  idarindAgi  ADuganige  entaha  vastu 
bEkAgide embudannu nirdharisuva kelasa sulabhavAgide.

    ondu  nAmapadadondige  innondu  nAmapadavannu  sErisiyU 
nAmapadakanteyondannu  tayArisalu  sAdhyavide.  Adare  idakkAgi 
averaDara  naDuve  avannu  sambandhisuva  a  pratyayavannu  baLasuva

bAla modalAda nAmapadakantegaLannu I vidhAnakke udAharaNegaLannAgi 
koDabahudu. 
    idallade, ondu iDI vAkyavannE nAmapadadondige irisi adannu 
ondu  nAmapadakanteyannAgi  mADi  hELalu  sAdhyavide.  idakkAgi  A

bahudu,  illavE  A  vAkyadalli  bEre  kelavu  rItiya  badalAvaNegaLannu 
mADikoLLabEkAgabahudu.

tiLiyadu. 
(18kha) avanu ivattu baruva sangati yArigU tiLiyadu. 
(18ga)  avana ivattina baruvike yArigU tiLiyadu.

4.3.1 padakantegaLu mattu jODupadagaLu 
mEle  sUcisiruva  hAge,  nAmapadakke  ondu  guNapadavannu  (illavE 
eNikeya  padavannu  athavA  bErondu  nAmapadavannu)  sErisi 
nAmapadakantegaLannU  tayArisabahudu  illavE  bErondu  hosatAda 
nAmapadavannU  tayArisabahudu.  ivugaLalli  eraDaneya  vidhAnada 
mUlaka  tayArAguva  nAmapadakke  `jODupada'  endu  hesaru.  udA 
haraNegAgi, huDugi nAmapadakke cikka guNapadavannu sErisi tayArisida 
cikka  huDugi  embudu  ondu  nAmapadakante,  mattu  amma  nAma 
padakke  adE  guNapadavannu  sErisi  tayArisida  cikkamma  embudondu 
jODupada. 
    ondu  padakke  innondu  padavannu  sErisi  ondu  hosatAda 
nAmapada(jODupada)vannu  tayArisuvudu  bhASeyalli  naDeyuva 
ondu  cAritrika  ghaTane.  idara  mUlaka  bhASeyalli  ondu  hosatA 
giruva  padavE  tayArAguttade.  Adare,  ondu  padakke  innondu  pada 
vannu  sErisi  padakanteyondannu  tayArisuvudu  antaha  cAritrika 
ghaTaneyEnalla. adu A bhASeyalliruva padagaLa baLake mAtra.  
    I  eraDu  vidhAnagaLa  naDuviruva  mukhya  vyatyAsavEnendare, 
padakantegaLa tayArikeyalli vAkyaracaneya niyamagaLu baLakeyAguttave, 
mattu  jODupadagaLa  tayArikeyalli  padaracaneya  niyamagaLu  baLake 
yAguttave. 
    idallade,  padakantegaLa  arthavannu  nEravAgi  avugaLa  angagaLAgi 
bandiruva padagaLa arthadinda paDeyalu sAdhyavide, Adare jODupada 
gaLa  arthavannu  heccina  sandabhragaLallU  A  rIti  nEravAgi  avugaLa 
angagaLAgi  bandiruva  padagaLa  arthadinda  paDeyalu  sAdhyavAgadu. 
jODupadagaLa  arthavEnu  embudannu  tiLidukoLLuvalli  avugaLa 
angagaLu svalpa sahAyavannu mAtravE odagisaballuvu.  
    udAharaNegAgi,  cikka  huDugi  emba  padakante  yAva  rItiyalli 
bEkiddarU  cikkavaLAgi  kANisuva  huDugiyobbaLannu  gurutisaballudu. 
Adare cikkamma emba jODupada tAyiya tangiyannu mAtra gurutisa 
balludallade adakkinta bhinnavAgiruva vyaktiyannu gurutisalAradu. udA 
haraNegAgi  vayassinalli  illavE  gAtradalli  cikkavaLAgi  kANisuva  `amma' 
nannAgalI illavE ammaniginta vayassinalli athavA gAtradalli cikkavaLAgi 
kANisuva  hengasannAgalI  (Ake  tAyiya  tangiyallavAdalli)  A  pada 
gurutisalAradu.  
    karihalage  emba  innondu  jODupadada  arthavannu  paDeyuvalli 
adara angagaLeraDU sahAyakavAguvudilla embudannu mEle 4.1ralli 
nODiruvevu. 
    jODupadagaLu  nAmapadagaLAgiruva  kAraNa,  avu  `hesarisuva' 
vidhAnada  mUlaka  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu  gurutisuttave.  Adare 
idakke  viruddhavAgi,  padakantegaLu  heccina  sandabhragaLallU  varNisuva 
vidhAnada  mUlaka  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu  gurutisuttave.  I 
eraDu  rItiya  ghaTakagaLa  naDuve  kANisuva  heccina  vyatyAsagaLigU 
bhASeyalli  avu  I  rIti  eraDu  bEre  bEre  kelasagaLannu  naDesa 
bEkAgideyembudE mukhya kAraNa (jAsti vivaragaLige (bhaT 2002:60) 
nODi). 
4.3.2 guNapadagaLa vibhajane 
kannaDadalli  guNapadagaLu  nAmapada  mattu  kriyApadagaLiginta  bhinna 
vAgiruva bEreyE ondu padavagradalli baruttave. mEle sUcisiruva 
hAge avu vAkyadalli nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLiginta bhinnavAgiruva 
kelasavondannu  (nAmapada  illavE  kriyApadavondara  vyAptiyannu 
kaDime mADuva kelasavannu) mADabEkAgiruvudE idakke kAraNa. 
    guNapadagaLu  I  rIti  kannaDadalli  bEreyE  ondu  padavagradalli 
baruttave  endu  hELuvudakke  kannaDadalli  avakkiruva  halavu  viSiSTavAda 
guNadharmagaLU  AdhAravAgaballuvu.  I  guNadharmagaLu  vAkyagaLalli 
guNapadagaLu mADabEkAgiruva viSiSTavAda kelasakkAgi kANisikoLLuttave.  
    udAharaNegAgi,  guNapadagaLannu  nAmapadagaLondige  (illavE 
kriyApadagaLondige)  avakke  yAva  pratyayavannU  sErisade  hAgeyE 
baLasalu sAdhyavide (udA: kempu hU, bEga banda). Adare nAmapada 
illavE  kriyApadagaLannu  bErondu  nAmapadadondige  I  rIti 
baLasabEkiddalli avakke a pratyayavannu sErisikoLLabEkAguttade (udA: 
marada kAlu, uLida anna). (jAsti vivaragaLige (bhaT 1994 mattu 
2002 nODi).  
    mEle  sUcisiruva  hAge,  guNapadagaLalli  nAmapadagaLondige 
baruvavu,  kriyApadagaLondige  baruvavu  mattu  bEre  guNapada 
gaLondige  baruvavu  embudAgi  mUru  upavagragaLive.  kappu,  biLi, 
doDDa,  haLe  modalAdavugaLu  nAmapadagaLondige  baruvavu,  bEga, 
mellage,  nuNNage  modalAdavugaLu  kriyApadagaLondige  baruvavu, 
mattu  mahaLa, bhArI modalAdavu guNapadagaLondige  baruvavu. I 
mUru  rItiya  guNapadagaLa naDuve halavu  vyatyAsagaLiddu, avella I 
guNapadagaLu  vAkyagaLalli  mADabEkAgiruva  bhinna  bhinnavAda  kelasagaLa 
mEle avalambisive. 
    I  mUru  rItiya  guNapadagaLalli  modalaneya  upavagrakke 
sErida  guNapadagaLu  mAtra  nAmapadakantegaLa  tayArikeyalli  baLake 
yAguttave. ivu mEle sUcisida hAge, nAmapadagaLu hesarisuva vyakti, 
vastu  modalAdavugaLa  guNadharmavondannu  sUcisuvudara  mUlaka 
avugaLa vyAptiyannu kaDime mADuttave. 
    I kelasavannu sAdhisuvudakkAgi kannaDada nAmapadakantegaLalli baruva 
guNapadagaLannu aydu upavagragaLalli vingaDisi hELalu sAdhyavide. 
    (1)  aLate:  I  upavagrada  guNapadagaLalli  ALa  embudondannu 
biTTu uLiduvella viruddhArthada jODigaLAgi baruttave.

    baNNavannu sUcisuva guNapadagaLalli kappu mattu biLi embavugaLu 
jODiyAgi  baruvuvAdarU  avannu  viruddhArthadavugaLendu  hELu

    (3) manuSyara  guNagaLu:  kannaDadalli  I  upavagrakke  sEruva 
guNapadagaLannu  eraDu  mukhya  upavibhAgagaLalli  vingaDisabahudu.

korategaLannu  sUcisuttiddu  modalaneya  vibhAgakkU  mattu  huccu,

gaLu  mAnasika  guNagaLannu  sUcisuttiddu  eraDaneya  vibhAgakkU  sEru

    (4)  vayassu:  vyakti  illavE  vastuvina  vayassannu  sUcisuva 
hosa,  haLe,  eLe,  mudi,  hiri,  kiri,  puTTa  modalAdavugaLu  I 
upavagrakke  sEruttave.  ivallade,  eraDaneya  upavagradalli  bandiruva 
doDDa  mattu  cikka  emberaDu  padagaLU  vayassannu  sUcisaballuvAda 
kAraNa avannU I upavagrakkU sErisalu sAdhyavide. 
    (5)  bele:  I  upavagrakke  sEruva  guNapadagaLalli  sari-tappu, 
heccu-kaDime,  kILu-mElu  emba  kelavu  padagaLu  jODigaLAgi

padagaLu  ondondAgi  baruttave.  oLLe  guNapadakke  jODiyAgi  keDu 
kriyApadada rUpavAgiruva keTTa embudu baLakeyallide.  
    (6)  dikku:  kannaDadalli  dikkannu  sUcisuva  mUDu,  tenka,  paDu 
mattu  baDaga  embavugaLU  guNapadagaLAgi  baLakeyallive.  ivugaLalli 
mUDu  kriyApadavAgiyU  baLakeyAguttade.  idallade,  oLa-hora, 
eDa-bala,  mEle-keLa-naDu  embavugaLU  bEre  bEre  jAgagaLannu 
sUcisaballa guNapadagaLAgive. 
4.3.3 nAmapadakantegaLalli guNapadagaLa baLake 
mEle  sUcisida  hAge,  nAmapadakantegaLalli  ondu  nAmapadadondige 
baruva I guNapadagaLu A nAmapada hesarisuva vyakti illavE vastuvina 
guNadharmavondannu sUcisuvudara mUlaka adara vyAptiyannu kaDime 
mADuttave.  
    udAharaNegAgi,  huDuga  nAmapadakke  cikka  guNapadavannu  sErisi 
nODabahudu.  huDuga  nAmapada  gurutisaballa  vyaktigaLiginta  cikka 
huDuga  emba  nAmapadakante  gurutisaballa  vyaktigaLa  sankhye  kaDime. 
yAkendare,  huDuga  nAmapada  yAva  vyaktigaLannella  hesarisaballudO 
avaralli cikka emba guNadharmaviruva vyaktigaLannu mAtra cikka huDuga 
emba padakante varNisuttade. 
guNapadagaLannu 
baLasuvudiddalli,  sAmAnyavAgi  heccu  nAmapadagaLondige  baraballa 
guNapadagaLu  modalu  baruttave  mattu  kaDime  nAmapadagaLondige 
baraballa  guNapadagaLu  anantara  baruttave.  udAharaNegAgi,  poIli 
guNapadadondige  baraballa  nAmapadagaLu  doDDa  guNapadadondige 
baraballa  nAmapadagaLiginta  bahaLa  kaDime.  hAgAgi  iveraDannU  oTTAgi 
ondE  nAmapadakanteyalli  baLasabEkAdAga,  doDDa  embudannu 
poIli  embudakkinta  modalu  baLasabEkAguttade  (udA:  avanobba 
doDDa poIli huDuga). 
nAmapadadondige  ondakkinta  jAsti 
    Adare kannaDada nAmapadakantegaLalli sAmAnyavAgi ondakkinta  jAsti 
guNapadagaLiruvudu  aparUpa.  kannaDadavE  Ada  guNapadagaLigintalU 
samskxtadinda  eravalAgi  banda  guNapadagaLu  I  rIti  padakantegaLalli 
oTToTTAgi  baruvudu  jAsti  (udA:  daynika  vAtrA  patrike,  prasiddha 
vayjYAnika samsthe, ityAdi). 
    I rIti ondu nAmapadadondige eraDakkinta jAsti guNapadagaLannu 
baLasideyAdalli, avannu yAva rItiyalli oTTu sErisalAgide embuda 
ralli vayvidhya kANisikoLLalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi halavu doDDa 
manegaLu  emba  padakanteyalli  bandiruva  halavu  emba  pada  doDDa 
emba  padada  hAge  manegaLu  embudakke  nEravAgi  sambandhisuttade. 
Adare, bahaLa doDDa manegaLu emba padakanteyalli bandiruva bahaLa 
emba pada I rIti nEravAgi manegaLu embudakke sambandhisuvudilla. 
idakke badalu adu doDDa embudakke sambandhisuttiddu, adara mUlaka 
manegaLu embudakke sambandhisuttade. 
4.3.4 eNikeya padagaLa baLake 
nAmapadagaLondige  padakantegaLalli  baraballa  innondu  rItiya  pada 
gaLendare ondu, eraDu, mUru modalAda eNikeya padagaLu. ivu 
guNapadagaLiginta  modalu  baruttave  (udA:  ondu  doDDa  mane, 
nAlku kempu hUgaLu). Adare I padagaLu eNisalu sAdhyaviruvantaha 
mane,  mara,  hU,  huDuga,  kate  modalAda  nAmapadagaLondige 
mAtra baruttave. sAmAnyavAgi eNisalu sAdhyavilladiruva nIru, eNNe, 
hiTTu modalAdavugaLondige baruvudilla. 
    kannaDadalli  ondarinda  hattaravarege  eNikeyannu  naDesalu  ondu, 
eraDu,  mUru  modalAda  biDi  biDiyAda  eNikeya  padagaLu  baLake 
yAguttave.  (ivugaLalli  ombattu  embudu  mAtra  cAritrikavAgi 
oLaracaneyiruva  eNikeya  pada).  janarannu  eNisabEkAdalli  mElina 
padagaLa  badalu  obba  (athavA  obbanu,  obbaLu,  obbaru),  ibbaru, 
mUvaru, nAlvaru modalAda viSiSTa padagaLa baLakeyide.  
    hattakkinta  jAsti  vastugaLannu  illavE  janarannu  eNisabEkAdAga, 
eraDu  athavA  jAsti  eNikeya  padagaLannu  oTTige  sErisi  hELabEkAgu 
ttade, mattu idakkAgi kannaDadalli keLage sUcisiruva hAge eraDu racane 
gaLu baLakeyallive. 
    hattarinda hattombattara varegina eNikeyannu naDesuvudakkAgi hattu 
embudakke  a  emba  sambandhisuva  pratyayavannu  sErisi  tayArisida 
hatta-  embudarondige  ondu,  eraDu,  mUru  modalAda 
padagaLagaLannu  baLasalAguttade.  Adare  I  racanegaLalli  hatta-  embudu 
hanna-, hadi- mattu hatta- emba rUpagaLalli kANisikoLLuttade.  
    idE  rItiyalli  ippattarinda  ippattombattara  varegina  eNikege 
ippatta embudakke ondu, eraDu modalAduvannu sErisi tayArisida 
racaneyannU  (udA:  ippattondu,  ippatteraDu,  ippatta  mUru, 
ityAdi)  mattu  mUvattarinda  mUvattombattara  varegina  eNikege 
mUvatta embudakke ondu, eraDu,  mUru  modalAduvannu sErisi 
tayArisida racaneyannU baLasuvudannu kANabahudu. 
    idE  rItiya  racaneyannu  nUrara  anantarada  eNikeyallU  kANa 
bahudu.  nUra  ondu  embudaralli  nUru  padakke  a  pratyayavannu 
sErisalAgide; nUra eppattondu embudaralli nUru mattu eppattu 
embuveraDakkU  adE  a  pratyayavannu  sErisalAgide;  mattu  hattu 
sAvirada  enTu  nUra  ayvatta  nAlku  embudaralli  sAvira,  nUru 
mattu ayvattu embavugaLige adE a pratyayavannu sErisalAgide. 
    ippattu,  mUvattu,  naluvattu  modalAda  eNikegaLalli  mAtra 
I  rIti  a  pratyayavannu  baLasuva  badalu  eraDu,  mUru,  nAlku 
modalAda  eNikeya  padagaLannu  nEravAgi  hattu  padakke  sErisalAgide. 
idu eNikeya padagaLalli kANisuva eraDaneya racane.  
    I  eraDaneya  racaneyallU  kelavu  sErikeya  badalAvaNegaLu 
naDediruvudannu  gamanisabahudu.  udAharaNegAgi,  eraDu  embudakke 
ippa- emba rUpavide, hattu embudakke attu, pattu, vattu moda 
lAda  rUpagaLive,  ityAdi.)  idE  rItiyalli  innUru,  munnUru, 
nAnnUru  modalAda  eNikegaLallU  eraDu  eNikeya  padagaLannu 
nEravAgi a pratyayavannu  baLasade sErisiruvudannu kANabahudu.  
    I  mElina  eNikeya  padagaLalli  a  pratyaya  bandalli  `kUDisu' 
emba artha baruttade, mattu A pratyaya bArade eNikeya padagaLeraDu 
nEravAgi sErikonDiruvalli `guNisu' emba artha baruttade embudAgi 
I eraDu rItiya racanegaLa baLakeyannu varNisabahudu. 
    eNikeyalli obba vyakti illavE ondu vastuvina jAgavannu sUcisu 
vudakkAgi  eNikeya  padagaLige  nE  illavE  neya  pratyayavannu  sErisa 
bEkAguttade.  udAharaNegAgi,  nAlkanE  huDuga  embudaralli 
nAlkanE embudu eNikeyalli obba huDugana jAga yAvudu embu 
dannu  sUcisuva  mUlaka  Atanannu  gurutisalu  sAdhyavAguvante  mADu 
ttade.  I  pratyayadeduru  ondu  embudara  badalu  modalu  embu 
dannU baLasalu sAdhyavide (ondanE huDuga, modalanE huDuga). 
4.3.5 aLateyannu sUcisuva padagaLu 
nAmapadavu  hesarisuva  vyakti  illavE  vastuvina  aLateyannu  sUcisuvu 
dakkAgi  adarondige  bEre  kelavu  padagaLannu  baLasalu  sAdhyavide.  ivu 
gaLalli  aLateyannu  nikharavAgi  tiLisuvavugaLu  mattu  ondu  andAjige 
tiLisuvavugaLu embudAgi eraDu vidhadavugaLiruvudannu kANabahudu.  
    udAharaNegAgi,  gENu,  moLa,  angula,  maylu  modalA 
davugaLu  aLateyannu  nikharavAgi  tiLisuttave.  sAmAnyavAgi  ivuga 
Londige eNikeya padagaLU bandiruttave. (udA: eraDu moLa baTTe, 
hattu ke.ji. akki, ityAdi). 
    halavu-kelavu,  bahaLa-svalpa,  hEraLa  modalAdavugaLu  aLate 
yannu ondu andAjige mAtra sUcisaballuvu. hAgAgi ivugaLondige 
eNikeya  padagaLu  baruvudilla.  (udA:  kelavu  janaru,  svalpa  nIru, 
hEraLa haNa, ityAdi). 
4.4 sArAmSa 
vAkyagaLalli  ondu  ghaTaneyannu  illavE  sangatiyannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi 
kriyApadagaLU,  mattu  antaha  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyalli  toDagi 
konDiruva  vyakti,  vastu,  jAga  modalAduvannu  gurutisuvudakkAgi 
nAmapadagaLU  baLakeyAguttave.  ivugaLalli  eraDaneya  kelasavannu 
naDesuvudakkAgi hesarisuva vidhAna mattu varNisuva vidhAna embudAgi 
eraDu bEre bEre vidhAnagaLannu baLasabEkAguttade. 
    varNisuva  vidhAnavannu  baLasabEkiddAga,  sAmAnyavAgi  nAmapada 
gaLannu guNapada, eNikeya pada, aLateya pada modalAdavugaLondige 
sErisi  ondu  `padakante'ya  rUpadalli  baLasuva  avaSyakate  kanDubaru 
ttade.  ondu  iDI  vAkyavU  intaha  padakanteya  angavAgiralu  sAdhya

adhyAya aydu 
kriyApadagaLa padarUpagaLu 
5.1 pIThike 
vAkyavondara  koneyalli  adara  kEndravAgi  baruva  kriyApadavannu 
sandabhrakkanusAravAgi halavAru rUpagaLalli baLasabEkAguttade. intaha 
rUpagaLalli  heccinavugaLallU  avu  sUcisuva  ghaTaneya  samaya  mattu 
A  ghaTaneyalli  toDagiruva  ghaTakagaLalli  ondu  (mADuga,  Aguga, 
illavE  prEraka)  embudAgi  eraDu  viSayagaLannu  cuTukAgi  tiLisalu 
eraDu pratyayagaLannu sErisabEkAguttade. 
nanna aNNa nALe beLigge nimage hattu sAvira koDuttAne. 
mElina  vAkyadalli  koDu  kriyApada  adara  koDuttAne  emba 
kriyArUpadalli  vAkyada  kEndravAgi  bandide.  I  kriyArUpadalli 
koDu  kriyApada  tta  mattu  Ane  emba  eraDu  pratyayagaLondige 
bandiruvudannu kANabahudu. 
    I  eraDu  pratyayagaLalli  tta  embudu  koDu  kriyApada 
sUcisuva  ghaTaneya  samaya  (1ka)  vAkyavannADiruva  samayakkinta 
mundinadu  embudannu  tiLisuttade,  mattu  adara  anantara  bandiruva 
Ane pratyaya I ghaTaneyannu naDesuva vyakti (endare adara `mADuga' 
ghaTaka) obba ganDasu embudannu tiLisuttade.  
    I  pratyayagaLu  mElina  eraDu  viSayagaLannu  bahaLa  cuTukAgi 
tiLisuttave.  avannE  heccu  vivaravAgi  tiLisalu  adE  vAkyadalli  nALe 
beLigge mattu nanna aNNa emba ghaTakagaLu bandive.   
    I  eraDu  rItiya  pratyayagaLu  mAtravallade,  vAkyavannu  entaha 
mAtina  kelasadalli  toDagisalAgide  embudannu  sUcisuva  bEre  kelavu 
pratyayagaLU  kriyArUpagaLalli  baraballuvu.  udAharaNegAgi,  koDali 
emba kriyArUpadalli mElina eraDu pratyayagaLa badalu al mattu 
i emba pratyayagaLu bandive. ivugaLalli modalaneyadu samayavannU 
mattu eraDaneyadu ondu `mAtina kelasa'vannU sUcisuttave (10.5.4 
nODi).  
    keLage  koTTiruva  (1kha)  vAkyadalli  koDali  emba  I  kriyArUpa 
vannu baLasalAgide, mattu A vAkyada ADuganige adannu baLasi bErobba 
vyaktiya mUlaka ondu kelasavannu mADisikoLLalu sAdhyavide. 
(1kha)  rAju nALe beLigge nimage hattu sAvira koDali. 
    idallade,  vAkyagaLannu  bEre  vAkyagaLa  illavE  bEre  vAkyagaLalli 
baruva padakantegaLa oLavAkyagaLannAgi mADi baLasabEkAgiruva sandabhra 
gaLallU avakke bEreyE kelavu pratyayagaLannu sErisabEkAgiddu, intaha 
pratyayagaLa  baLakeyindalU  mElinavakkinta  bhinnavAgiruva  kelavu  kriyA 
rUpagaLu siddhavAguttave.  
    udAharaNegAgi,  vAkyagaLannu  ondu  padakanteya  angavannAgi 
mADikoLLalu  avugaLa  kEndravAgi  bandiruva  kriyApadakke  a  emba 
`sambandhisuva'  pratyayavannu  sErisikoLLabEkAguttade.  I  pratyayavannu 
sErisidAga,  antaha  kriyApadagaLa  koneyalli  ghaTaneyannu  naDesuva 
vyaktiyannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  bandiruva  pratyaya  bidduhOguttade, 
mattu  avugaLalli  samayavannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  bandiruva  pratyaya 
dallU kelavu badalAvaNegaLu naDeyuttave. 
(2ka)  A huDugi mangaLUrige nALe hOguttALe. 
(2kha)  mangaLUrige nALe hOguva huDugi aLuttiddALe. 
(2ka)  vAkyada  kriyApadakke  a  pratyayavannu  sErisi,  adannu  (2kha) 
vAkyadalli ondu padakanteya angavannAgi mADalAgide. hIge mADuva 
samayadalli  adara  koneyalli  baruva  aLu  pratyayavannu  tegedu 
hAkalAgide,  mattu  mundina  samayavannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  adaralli 
utta pratyayada badalu uv pratyayavannu baLasalAgide. 
    vAkyagaLalli  I  rIti  bEre  bEre  kelasagaLigAgi entaha  kriyArUpa 
gaLella  baraballuvu  mattu  avugaLa  oLaracaneyEnu  embudannu  I 
adhyAyadalli vivarisalAgide. 
5.2 samayavannu sUcisuva pratyayagaLu 
vAkyada  mukhya  angavAgi  baruva  kriyApadagaLalli  `hindina  samaya' 
mattu `mundina samaya' embudAgi eraDu samayagaLannu sUcisaballa 
pratyayagaLu  baLakeyAguttave.  ivu  A  kriyApadagaLiruva  vAkyavannu 
yAva samayadalli ADalAgittO A samayada hinde naDediruva mattu 
munde naDeyaliruva ghaTanegaLannu sUcisuttave. 
(3ka)   Ata ivattu sanje mUru ganTege hADuttAne. 
(3kha)  Ata ivattu sanje mUru ganTege hADida. 
mElina  eraDu  vAkyagaLU  ondE  ghaTaneyannu  (endare  Atanu 
hADuva ghaTaneyannu) tiLisuttave. idallade, I ghaTaneya samaya I 
eraDu  vAkyagaLallU  ondE  (ivattu  sanje  mUru  ganTege). 
hIgiddarU, adannu sUcisuva hADu kriyApadavannu (3ka)dalli utta 
pratyayadondige baLasalAgide, mattu (3kha)dalli adannE id pratyaya 
dondige baLasalAgide.  
    I  vyatyAsakke  kAraNavEnendare,  I  eraDu  pratyayagaLu  ghaTaneya 
samayavannaSTE sUcisuva badalu A samayakkU mattu adannu tiLisuva 
vAkyada  samayakkU  naDuviruva  sambandhavannu  sUcisuttave.  (3ka) 
vAkyavannu  ADuva  samayadalli  A  ghaTane  naDedillavembudannu  (endare 
A ghaTane anantara naDeyuttade embudannu) adaralli bandiruva utta 
emba  `mundina'  samayada  pratyaya  sUcisuttade,  mattu  (3kha)  vAkya 
vannu ADiruva samayadalli A ghaTane naDedAgittu embudannu adaralli 
bandiruva id emba `hindina' samayada pratyaya sUcisuttade. 
5.2.1 mundina samaya  
mEle koTTiruva eraDu samaya pratyayagaLalli  mundina samayavannu 
sUcisuva  utta  pratyayakke  ellA  sandabhragaLallU  ondE  rUpavide. 
Adare,  I  pratyayadondige  baruva  kriyApadagaLalli  mAtra  keLage 
sUcisida hAge eraDu badalAvaNegaLu kANisikoLLuttave.  
    (ka)  ukAradalli  konegoLLuva  kriyApadagaLondige  I  pratyaya 
bandAga avugaLa koneya ukAra biddu hOguttade.

rUDhiyalli jaraguva ghaTanegaLannu sUcisuva arthavU ide embudannu 
keLagina vAkyagaLa baLakeyalli kANabahudu. 
(4ka)  avaru ivattu enTu ganTege angaDi tereyuttAre.

ghaTaneyondannu sUcisuttide. idakke badalu (5ka-kha)gaLalli bandiruva

(5ga)dalli  bandiruva  kriyArUpa  I  eraDu  rItiya  arthagaLannU 
koDaballudu. 
5.2.2 hindina samaya 
hindina  samayavannu  sUcisuva  pratyayakke  adara  eDakke  baruva 
kriyApada  mattu  balakke  baruva  ghaTaka  pratyaya  -  ivugaLannavalambisi 
halavu  rUpagaLive.  adarondige  baruva  kriyApadagaLallU  keLage 
sUcisiruva hAge halavu badalAvaNegaLu kANisikoLLuttave.   
    (1)  I  pratyayakke  ukAradalli  konegoLLuva  kriyApadagaLeduru 
id  emba  rUpavide,  mattu  idarondige  baruva  kriyApadagaLa 
koneyalliruva ukAra I pratyaya sEridAga biddu hOguttade.

emba  hindina  samayavannu  sUcisuva  pratyayavU  mattu  a  emba 
ghaTakavannu  sUcisuva  pratyayavU  sErive.  I  kriyArUpadalli  naDugu 
kriyApadada  koneya  akAra  bidduhOgide.  itara  kriyArUpagaLallU 
hIgeyE. 
    (2) ekAra mattu ikAragaLalli konegoLLuva kriyApadagaLa munde 
hindina samayavannu sUcisuva pratyayakke d emba rUpavide.

embudu  bandideyAdalli  adakke  id  embudara  badalu  i  emba 
rUpavide.  udAharaNegAgi,  keLagi  koTTiruva  naDugitu  emba 
kriyArUpadalli ghaTakavannu sUcisalu tu pratyaya bandideyAda kAraNa

5.2.3 apavAdagaLu 
mEle  sUcisida  badalAvaNegaLu  kannaDada  heccina  kriyApadagaLigU 
hindina  samayavannu  sUcisuva  pratyayavannu  sErisidAga  kANisikoLLu 
vantahavu.  I  badalAvaNegaLige  apavAdagaLAgi  uLiyuva  sumAru 
ayvattu-aruvattu  kriyApadagaLu  kannaDadallive.  ivugaLalli  entaha 
badalAvaNegaLella  naDeyuttave  mattu  ivugaLondige  baruvAga  hindina 
samayada  pratyayakke  entaha  rUpagaLella  kANisikoLLuttave  embudannu 
keLage sUcisalAgide (jAsti vivaragaLige SrIdhar 1990 nODi). 
    (1) ikAradalli konegoLLuva kriyApadagaLu:  avi,  ari,  kali 
mattu  bali  kriyApadagaLu  ikAradalli  konegoLLuvuvAdarU,  avuga 
Londige  baruva  hindina  samayavannu  sUcisuva  pratyayakke  adara 
munde  tu ghaTakavannu sUcisuva pratyaya bandAga ti emba rUpavU 
mattu itara pratyayagaLu bandAga t emba rUpavU ide.  
    kadi  emba  innondu  ikAradalli  konegoLLuva  kriyApadadeduru 
I  pratyayakke  adara  munde  tu  pratyaya  bandAga  di  emba  rUpavU 
mattu itara pratyayagaLu bandAga d emba rUpavU ide. I eraDu 
sandabhragaLallU I kriyApadada koneya ikAra biddu hOguttade.  
kadditu 
    (2)  ekAradalli  konegoLLuva  kriyApadagaLu:  ekAradalli 
konegoLLuva  dore,  nere,  bere,  mare,  kale,  koLe  mattu  moLe

5.2.4 Igina samaya 
kannaDadalli  iru  emba  ondu  kriyApadakke  mAtra  hindina  mattu

baruva iru kriyApadakke id emba rUpavide.

5.4 isu pratyayada baLake 
kannaDada heccina kriyApadagaLU mElina eraDu pratyayagaLannu paDeyuva 
modalu  isu  emba  innondu  pratyayavannu  paDeyaballuvu.  I 
pratyayakke  sandabhrakkanusAravAgi  bEre  bEre  arthagaLu  baruttiddu, 
ivugaLalli  ghaTaneyannu  mADuvante  vyaktiyobbanannu  prErEpisuvantaha 
artha prAmukhyavAdudu. 
(8ka)  sIte jAnakigondu patra baredaLu. 
(8kha)  sundari sIteya kayyalli jAnakigondu patra baresidaLu. 
saynikaru sereyALugaLannu kondaru. 
(9kha)  rAja saynikara mUlaka sereyALugaLannu kollisida. 
(8ka)dalli bare kriyApada nEravAgi samayavannu sUcisuva d pratyaya 
dondige  mattu ghaTakavannu sUcisuva  aLu pratyayadondige bandide. 
Adare (8kha)dalli idE kriyApada I eraDu pratyayagaLannu paDeyuva 
modalu isu emba bErondu pratyayavannu paDedide.  
    (8ka)dalli  bare  kriyApada  sIte  naDesida  ondu  ghaTaneyannu 
sUcisuttade;  (8kha)dalli  adE  kriyApada  isu  pratyayadondige 
bandideyAda  kAraNa,  sIte  A  ghaTaneyannu  naDesuvante  sundari 
prErEpisiruvaLembudannu sUcisuttade. 
    isu pratyayakke I rIti vAkyakkondu prEraka ghaTakavannu sErisuva 
kelasa  mAtravallade  bEreyU  kelavu  kelasagaLive.  vAkyadallondu 
mADuga  ghaTakavideyAdare,  antaha  vAkyavannu  I  pratyaya  keLage 
sUcisiruva hAge mUru rItigaLalli badalAyisaballudu. 
    (ka) mEle sUcisida hAge isu pratyaya A vAkyakke ondu prEraka 
ghaTakavannu  sErisaballudu.  intaha  sandabhragaLalli  vAkyada  mADuga 
ghaTaka  kayyalli  illavE  mUlaka  emba  padadondige  baruttade  (8kha, 
9kha nODi). 
    (kha)  eraDaneyadAgi,  isu  pratyaya  A  vAkyakke  ondu  hosa 
mADuga ghaTakavannu sErisaballududu. intaha sandabhragaLalli vAkyadalli 
modalu  mADugavAgidda  ghaTaka  AgugavAguttade;  vAkyadalli  modalu 
bErondu  Aguga  ghaTakavittAdare,  isu  pratyayavannu  baLasidAga  A 
Agugavannu biTTubiDabEkAguttade.  
(10ka)  rAmu nadiyannu dATida. 
(10kha) sItApati rAmuvannu dATisida. 
(11ka)  danagaLu hullu mEyuttive. 
(11kha) kxSNappa danagaLannu mEyisuttiddAne.

sItApati  emba  hosadondu  ghaTaka  adara  mADugavAgi  bandide. 
adaralli  modaligidda  (endare  (10ka)dallidda)  mADuga  ghaTaka  Aguga 
vAgide (rAmu ghaTaka annu pratyayadondige bandide) mattu modali 
gidda Aguga ghaTakavannu (nadi embudannu) vAkyadinda biTTu koDalAgide 
(11khadallU hIgeyE). 
    kannaDada  kelavu  kriyApadagaLu  I  eraDu  rItiya  vAkyagaLallU 
baLakeyAgaballuvu. udAharaNegAgi, keLage koTTiruva (12ka-ga) vAkya
