(12ka)  rAju mUru maylu ODida. 
(12kha) hari rAjuvina kayyalli mUru maylu ODisida. 
(12ga)  hari rAjuvannu mUru maylu ODisida. 
mEle  (12kha)dalli  hari  ghaTaka  prErakavAgi  bandiddu,  modalu 
mADugavAgidda  rAju  ghaTaka  mADugavAgiyE  uLidide  mattu 
kayyalli  emba  padadondige  bandide.  idakke  badalu  (12ga)dalli  hari 
ghaTaka  mADugavAgi  bandide  mattu  rAju  ghaTaka  AgugavAgi  (annu 
pratyayadondige)  bandide.  I  mUru  vAkyagaLallU  mUru  mayli 
embudu parimANavannu sUcisuva ondu amukhya ghaTaka. 
    (ga)  mUraneyadAgi,  isu  pratyaya  mADuga  ghaTakaviruva  vAkyakke 
ondu  hosa  mADugavannu  sErisuvudarondige  adaralli  modalidda 
mADuga ghaTakavannu kone ghaTakavAgi badalAyisaballudu. 
(13ka)  magu bALEhaNNu tinnuttA ide. 
(13kha) muraLi maguvige bALEhaNNu tinnisuttA iddAne. 
(14ka)  rAghava ondu kap majjige kuDida. 
(14kha) gangamma rAghavanige ondu kap majjige kuDisidaLu. 
(13kha)dalli muraLi emba ondu hosatAgiruva (endare (13ka)dalli 
illadidda) mADuga ghaTaka sErikonDide mattu adaralli modalige idda 
magu  emba  mADuga  ghaTaka  kone  ghaTakavAgi  badalAgiddu  ge  pratyaya 
dondige baLakeyAgide. 
    intaha  vAkyagaLallU  hosadAgi  ondu  mADuga  ghaTakada  badalu 
prEraka ghaTakavannu sErisikoLLalu sAdhyavide; hAge mADidAga modalidda 
mADuga  ghaTaka  mADugavAgiyE  uLiyuttadAdarU  kayyalli  emba 
padadondige baruttade. 
(15ka)  avanu mUru capAti tinda. 
(15kha) nAnu avanige mUru capAti tinniside. 
(15ga)  nAnu avana kayyalli mUru capAti tinniside. 
    (gha) mADuga ghaTakavillada vAkyagaLa kriyApadagaLige  isu pratyaya 
sEridAga avakkella hosadAgi mADuga ghaTakavondu sErikoLLuttade. 
(16ka)  nIru kudiyitu. 
(16kha) jAnaki nIru kudisidaLu. 
(17ka)  sItApatige parIkSeya suddi muTTide. 
(17kha) rAju sItApatige parIkSeya suddi muTTisiddAne. 
(16ka)dalli mADuga ghaTakavilla; Adare (16kha)dalli kudi kriyApadakke 
isu  pratyayavannu  sErisalAgideyAda  kAraNa,  adaralli  jAnaki  emba 
mADuga ghaTakavondu hosatAgi sErikonDide. 
    isu  pratyayada  baLakeyAdAga,  vAkyada  kriyApadavannavalambisi 
adara  ghaTakagaLalli  bEreyU  kelavu  badalAvaNegaLu  kANisuttave. 
udaharaNegAgi,  keLage  koTTiruva  nAlku  badalAvaNegaLannu  gamanisa 
bahudu.  
    (Ga)  meccu  illavE  nambu  kriyApadakke  isu  pratyayavannu 
sErisidAga,  adara  Aguga  mADugavAguttade,  mattu  mADuga 
AgugavAguttade. 
(18ka)  rAmu jAnakiyannu nambida. 
(18kha) jAnaki rAmuvannu nambisidaLu. 
    (ca)  hedaru,  sOlu,  rEgu,  oppu  modalAda  bEre  kelavu 
kriyApadagaLige  isu  pratyaya  sEridAga  avugaLa  kone  ghaTaka  mADuga 
ghaTakavAguttade. 
(19ka)  rAvaNa hanumantanige sOta. 
(19kha) hanumanta rAvaNanannu sOlisida. 
    (cha)  kANu  mattu  kELu  kriyApadagaLige  isu  pratyaya  sEridAga 
avugaLa mADuga ghaTaka kone ghaTakavAguttade. 
(20ka)  avanu ondu hADannu kELida. 
(20kha)  avanige ondu hADu kELisitu.  
    (ja)  tere,  oDe,  suDu  modalAda  bEre  kelavu  kriyApadagaLu 
mADuga  ghaTakadondigU  baraballuvu,  mADuga  ghaTakavilladeyU 
baraballuvu.  intaha  kriyApadagaLige  isu  pratyayavannu  sErisidalli, 
avu prErakadondige mAtra baraballuvallade prErakavillade baralAravu. 
(21ka)  bAgilu tereyitu. 
(21kha) huDuga bAgilu tereda. 
(21ga)  Ake huDugana kayyalli bAgilu teresidaLu. 
(21ka)dalli  tere  kriyApadadondige  Aguga  ghaTaka  (bAgilu)  mAtra 
bandide;  (21kha)dalli  adE  kriyApadadondige  mADuga  (huDuga) 
mattu  Aguga  (bAgilu)gaLeraDU  bandive;  (21ga)dalli  A  kriyApadakke 
isu  pratyayavannu  sErisalAgideyAda  kAraNa  adarondige  Aguga 
(bAgilu)  mattu  mADuga  (huDuga)  ghaTakagaLu  mAtravallade  prEraka 
ghaTakavU (Ake embudU) bandide. 
5.5 vAkyada naDuve kANisuva kriyArUpagaLu 
nAvu  iduvarege  pariSIlisida  kriyArUpagaLella  vAkyada  koneyalli 
baruva  mukhya  kriyApadada  rUpagaLu.  ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu 
vAkyadondige  jODisi  hELabEkAdAga  illavE  innondu  vAkyada 
illavE  padakanteya  oLavAkyavannAgi  mADi  hELabEkAdAga,  antaha 
vAkyadalli  baruva  mukhya  kriyApada  vAkyada  naDuve  kANisikoLLuttade. 
I rIti vAkyada naDuve kANisikoLLuva kriyApadakke vAkyada koneyalli 
baruva kriyApadakkinta bhinnavAda rUpaviruttade. 
    udAharaNegAgi,  vAkyada  naDuve  baruva  kriyApadadondige  ghaTaka 
vannu  sUcisuva  pratyaya  baruvudilla.  endu,  emba,  O  embantaha 
etti  hELuva  pada  illavE  pratyayagaLondige  baruva  kriyArUpagaLu 
mAtra  idakke  apavAdagaLu.  vAkyada  naDuve  baruva  kriyApadadondige 
samaya pratyaya baraballudAdarU adakke kelavu sandabhragaLalli vAkyada 
koneyalli baruva samaya pratyayakkinta bEreyE arthaviruttade.  
    I rIti vAkyada naDuve baruva kriyArUpagaLalli entaha pratyaya 
gaLella  baruttave  mattu  avugaLa  baLake  hEge  embudannu  keLagina  upa 
vibhAgagaLalli vivarisalAgide. 
5.5.1 jODisuva rUpagaLu 
ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyadondige  jODisi  hELuvudakkAgi 
mUru  vidhAnagaLu  baLakeyalliddu,  A  vAkyada  mukhya  kriyApadadalli 
kelavu  badalAvaNegaLannu  mADuvudara  mUlaka  adannu  innondu 
vAkyadondige  jODisuvudu  ivugaLalli  ondu  embudannu  nAvu 
munde  enTanE  adhyAyadalli  nODaliruvevu.  I  vidhAnadalli 
baLakeyAguva  jODisuva  kriyArUpadalli  samayavannu  sUcisuva 
pratyaya baruttade, Adare ghaTakavannu sUcisuva pratyaya baruvudilla. 
(22ka)  rAju manege hOgi nidde mADida. 
(22kha) jAnaki manege hOgi aDuge mADidaLu. 
(22ga)  rAju manege hOgalu rikSA hattida. 
hOguva  ghaTaneyannu  naDesida  vyakti  (22ka)dalli  obba  ganDasu  mattu 
(22kha)dalli  obba  hengasu;  hIgiddarU  iveraDu  vAkyagaLallU  hOgi 
emba ondE kriyArUpa jODisuva rUpavAgi bandide.  
    (22ka)  mattu  (22kha)  vAkyagaLalli  modalaneya  ghaTane  eraDane 
yadara modalE naDediruttade. Adare (22ga)dalli modalaneya ghaTane 
naDeyuvantahadAgide.  I  vyatyAsavannu 
eraDaneyadara  anantara 
sUcisuvudakkAgi  (22ka-kha)gaLalli  hOgi  emba  kriyArUpavannU, 
mattu (22ga)dalli hOgalu emba kriyArUpavannU baLasalAgide. I 
rIti  I  jODisuva  kriyArUpagaLu  ghaTanegaLa  samayadalli  kANisuva 
vyatyAsagaLannu  sUcisaballuvu,  Adare  avugaLa  ghaTakagaLalli  kANisuva 
vyatyAsagaLannu sUcisalAravu. 
5.5.2 samayavannu sUcisuva pratyayagaLu 
samayavannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  intaha  jODisuva  kriyArUpagaLalli 
baruva pratyayagaLigU mattu vAkyada koneya kriyArUpagaLalli baruva 
pratyayagaLigU naDuve halavu vyatyAsagaLive.  
    mEle  5.2ralli  vivarisiruva  hAge,  vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva 
kriyArUpagaLu  ghaTaneyondara  samayavannu  vAkyavannADuva  samayakke 
sambandhisidante  sUcisuttave.  A  ghaTane  vAkyavannADuva  samayakkinta 
hinde  naDedudembudannu  sUcisalu  avugaLalli  `hindina  samaya'da 
pratyayavU  mattu  adu  A  samayada  anantara  naDeyuvantahadu 
embudannu  sUcisalu  `mundina  samaya'da  pratyayavU  baLakeyAgu 
ttave. 
    ghaTaneya  samayakkU  mattu  vAkyada  samayakkU  naDuviruva 
sambandhavannu I rIti vAkyada koneya kriyArUpavE tiLisuva kAraNa 
adannE  puna:  vAkyada  naDuve  baruva  jODisuva  kriyArUpagaLu 
tiLisuva  avaSyakateyilla.  hAgAgi,  jODisiruva  eraDu  vAkyagaLu 
tiLisuva  ghaTanegaLa  naDuve  samayada  maTTige  entaha  sambandhavide 
embudannu  mAtra  jODisuva  kriyArUpadalli  baruva  samaya 
pratyayagaLu tiLisuttave. keLagina vAkyagaLalli I eraDu rItiya pratyaya 
gaLU bandiddu, avugaLa naDuviruva vyatyAsa spaSTavAgi kANisuttade. 
(23ka)  rAju manege hOgi nidde mADida. 
(23kha) rAju manege hOgi nidde mADuttAne. 
(23ka)dalli samayavannu sUcisuvudakkAgi hOgu kriyApadadondige 
i  pratyaya  bandide  mattu  mADu  kriyApadadondige  d  pratyaya 
bandide.  (idallade,  mADu  kriyApadadondige  ghaTakavannu  sUcisuva 
a pratyayavU bandide). illi i pratyaya manege hOguva ghaTane nidde 
mADuva  ghaTaneginta  modalE  naDedide  embudannu  tiLisuttade,  mattu 
d  pratyaya  nidde  mADuva  ghaTane  (23ka)  vAkyavannu  ADiruva 
samayakkinta modalE naDedide embudannu sUcisuttade. 
    (23ka)  vAkyadalli  manege  hOguva  ghaTane  A  vAkyavannADiruva 
samayakkinta  modalE  naDedideyemba  artha  sUcitavAguvudAdarU 
adu  nEravAgi  hOgu  kriyApadadondige  baruva  i  pratyayadinda 
sUcitavAguvudilla; adakke badalu, mADu kriyApadadondige baruva 
d  pratyayadinda  (mattu  manege  hOguva  ghaTane  nidde  mADuva 
ghaTaneginta modalE naDedide embudarinda) sUcitavAguttade.   
    i  pratyayakke  I  rIti  eraDaneya  ghaTanege  sambandhisidantaha 
samayavannu sUcisuva arthavideyallade vAkyavannu ADiruva samayakke 
sambandhisidante  samayavannu  sUcisuva  arthavilla  embudannu  mEle 
koTTiruva  (23kha)  vAkya  spaSTapaDisuttade.  I  vAkyadallU  hOgu 
kriyApadadondige  i  pratyaya  bandide.  Adare  mADu  kriyA 
padadondige  mundina  samayavannu  sUcisuva  utta  pratyaya 
bandideyAda kAraNa, illi manege hOguva ghaTane (23kha) vAkyavannu 
ADiruva  samayada  anantara  (endare  `mundina'  samayadalli)  naDe 
diralu sAdhyavide.  
    eraDu  ghaTanegaLa  naDuve  keLage  sUcisida  hAge  avu  naDeyuva 
samayakke sambandhisidante nAlku rItiya sambandhagaLiralu sAdhyavide. 
(1)  modalaneya  vAkya  sUcisuva  ghaTane  eraDaneya  vAkya 
sUcisuva ghaTaneginta modalu naDeyuvantahadirabahudu,  
(2)  modalaneya  vAkya  sUcisuva  ghaTane  eraDaneya  vAkya 
sUcisuva ghaTaneginta anantara naDeyuvantahadirabahudu,  
(3)  eraDu  vAkyagaLu  sUcisuva  ghaTanegaLU  ondE  samaya 
dalli naDeyuvantahavirabahudu, illavE  
(4) modalaneya vAkya sUcisuva ghaTane naDeyade eraDaneya 
vAkya sUcisuva ghaTane naDeyuvantirabahudu.  
I nAlku rItiya sAdhyategaLannu sUcisuvudakkAgi modalaneya vAkyada 
kriyApadadondige  nAlku  rItiya  pratyayagaLannu  baLasalu  sAdhyavide 
embudannu keLagina udAharaNegaLalli kANabahudu. 
(24ka)  nAnu sIbehaNNannu bEyisi kattariside. 
(24kha) nAnu sIbehaNNannu bEyisalu kattariside. 
(24ga)  nAnu sIbehaNNannu bEyisuttA kattariside. 
(24gha) nAnu sIbehaNNannu bEyisade kattariside. 
mElina  vAkyagaLalli  pratiyondarallU  sIbehaNNannu  bEyisuvudu 
mattu  sIbe  haNNannu  kattarisuvudu  embudAgi  eraDeraDu  ghaTane 
gaLannu sUcisalAgide.  
    (24ka)dalli  I  eraDu  ghaTanegaLalli  modalaneyadu  (bEyisu 
vudu)  eraDaneyadakkinta  modalu  naDedideyendu  sUcisalAgide; 
(24kha)dalli modalaneyadu eraDaneyadara anantara naDeyuvantahadu 
endu  sUcisalAgide;  (24ga)dalli  iveraDU  oTTige  naDedive  endu 
sUcisalAgide;  mattu  (24gha)dalli  modalaneyadu  naDeyade  eraDane 
yadu naDedideyendu sUcisalAgide. 
    eraDu ghaTanegaLa naDuve avugaLa samayadalli kANisuva I nAlku 
rItiya  sambandhagaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  avugaLalli  modalaneya 
ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  kriyApadadondige  anukramavAgi  i,  alu, 
uttA mattu ade emba nAlku pratyayagaLannu baLasalAgide.  
    ivugaLalli  i  pratyayavu  adakkiruva  kelavu  rUpagaLalli  hindina 
samayada  pratyayada  hAgeyE  kANisuttade;  Adare  bEre  kelavu 
rUpagaLalli adu bhinnavAgide. uttA pratyayavU mundina samayavannu 
sUcisuva  utta  pratyayavannu  hOluttade.  Adare  arthadalli  I 
eraDu  pratyayagaLU  mEle  vivarisida  pratyayagaLiginta  bhinnavAgive 
(jAsti vivaragaLige bhaT 1999:20-28 nODi). 
    ade  emba  nAlkaneya  pratyayavannu  mAtra  samaya  pratyayavendu 
parigaNisuva  badalu  allagaLeyuva  pratyayavendu  parigaNisalu  sAdhya 
vide.  yAkendare,  adu  samayada  maTTige  eraDu  ghaTanegaLu  sambandhi 
silla embudAgi sUcisuttideyendu hELalU sAdhya.  
    vAkyagaLannu  pada  illavE  padakantegaLondige  sambandhisuvudakkAgi 
baLasuva  a  pratyayadeduru  ad  emba  allagaLeyuva  pratyaya  baru 
ttadeyembudannu  nAvu  keLage  5.6ralli  nODaliruvevu.  jODisuva 
vAkyagaLalli  ghaTaneyondannu  allagaLeyuvudakkAgi  baruva  ade  emba 
pratyayakkU mattu I ad pratyayakkU naDuve sambandhavannu kalpisalu 
sAdhyavide.  
    baru  mattu  taru  emberaDu  kriyApadagaLige  ad  pratyayadeduru 
iruva  hAge  I  ade  pratyayadedurU  bAr  mattu  tAr  emba 
viSiSTavAda rUpagaLiveyembudannu illi gamanisabahudu. 
(25ka)  avanu bArade nAnu hOguvudilla. 
(25kha) avanu bArade namma kelasa keTTuhOyitu. 
5.5.3 i pratyayada rUpagaLu 
ondu  ghaTane  innondu  ghaTaneginta  modalE  naDedide  (athavA 
naDeyuttade)  embudannu  sUcisuva  i  pratyayakke  kriyApadagaLa 
svarUpavannAdharisi  bEre  bEre  rUpagaLive.  mEle  sUcisida  hAge,  I 
rUpagaLu kelavu viSayagaLalli hindina samayavannu sUcisuva pratyaya 
vannu  hOluvuvAdarU  bEre  kelavu  viSayagaLalli  adakkinta  bhinna 
vAgive. 
    ukAradalli konegoLLuva heccina kriyApadagaLigU hindina samaya 
vannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  id  pratyayavannu  sErisalAguttade.  ondu 
ghaTane  innondakkinta  modalu  naDeyuvantahadembudAgi  `modalina 
samaya'vannu sUcisuva pratyaya intaha kriyApadagaLondige i emba 
rUpadalli baruttade.

5.5.4 sambandhisuva rUpagaLu 
vAkyavondannu  ondu  pada  illavE  padakanteyondige  sambandhisuvu 
dakkAgi  adara  mukhya  kriyApadakke  a  emba  sambandhisuva  pratyayavannu 
sErisabEkAguttade.  I  pratyayadeduru  kriyApadadalli  samayavannu 
sUcisuva  pratyaya  kANisikoLLuttade,  Adare  ghaTakavannu  sUcisuva 
pratyaya kANisikoLLuvudilla.  
(27ka)  huDugi marakke hattidaLu. 
(27kha) marakke hattida huDugi hU koyyuttiddALe. 
(27ka)dalli  bandiruva  vAkyavannu  huDugi  padadondige  sambandhisi 
(27kha)dalli hELalAgide, mattu idakkAgi adara koneyalli bandiruva 
hattidaLu  kriyApadakke  a  pratyayavannu  sErisalAgide.  I  pratyaya 
deduru  ghaTakavannu  sUcisuva  aLu  pratyaya  bidduhOgide,  Adare 
samayavannu sUcisuva d pratyaya uLidukonDide. 
    hindina  samayavannu  sUcisuva  pratyayakke  adara  anantara  tu 
pratyayavannu  biTTu  itara  ghaTakagaLannu  sUcisuva  pratyayagaLu  bandAga 
yAva  rUpa  kANisuttadeyO  adE  rUpa  adara  anantara  I 
sambandhavannu sUcisuva a pratyaya bandAgalU kANisuttade.

5.6 kUDupadagaLu 
ondu  vAkyada  kriyApadavannu  adara  `jODisuva'  rUpakke  badalA

intaha  vAkyagaLalli  mUru  bEre  bEre  samayagaLannu  sUcisuva 
jODisuva kriyArUpagaLu baLakeyAguttave. 
(36ka)  rAju mangaLUrige hOgi ondu pustaka tandidda. 
(36kha) rAju ondu pustaka taralu mangaLUrige hOgidda. 
(36ga)  rAju mangaLUrige hOguttA ondu pustaka mugisida.

mattu hOguttA emba jODisuva rUpakke badalAyisalAgide. 
    kannaDadalli  I  jODisuva  vidhAnada  mUlaka  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu 
mAtravallade  eraDu  kriyApadagaLannU  oTTige  jODisi  hELalu

idE  rItiyalli  mEle  koTTiruva  itara  (37kha-gha)  vAkyagaLallU 
eraDu vAkyagaLa jODaNeyAgideyendu hELuvudu kaSTa. 
    I  vAkyagaLella  cAritrikavAgi  jODisiruva  vAkyagaLE.  Adare 
rUDhiyalli  I  jODaNegaLige  kelavu  heccina  arthagaLu  bandiddu, 
adarindAgi I vAkyagaLa eraDaneya kriyApadagaLu avugaLa mUlArtha 
vannu bahaLa maTTige kaLedukonDive. modalaneya kriyApada sUcisuva 
ghaTaneya  kuritAgi  heccinadannEnAdarU  hELuva  artha  mAtravE 
avakkiddu, adakkinta bhinnavAda bErondu ghaTaneyannu sUcisuva artha 
avakkilla. 
    hAgAgi,  intaha  vAkyagaLalli  eraDu  vAkyagaLu  jODikonDive 
yendu  hELuva  badalu,  eraDu  kriyApadagaLannu  oTTige  sErisi 
tayArisalAgiruva  kelavu  viSiSTavAda  kriyApadagaLu  bandiveyendu 
tOruttade.  udAharaNegAgi,  mEle 
hELuvudE  oLLeyadendu 
koTTiruva (36ka-gha) vAkyagaLalli kaccibiDu, hOgiru, hOguttiru 
mattu  baralAr-  emba  viSiSTavAda  kriyApadagaLu  bandiveyendu 
hELabahudu. 
    kelavu  viSayagaLalli  I  viSiSTavAda  kriyApadagaLu  nAmapadagaLa 
baLakeyalli  kANisuva  `jODupada'gaLannu  hOluttaveyembudannu 
gamanisabahudu. udAharaNegAgi, jODupadagaLa hAge ivugaLa artha 
vannu  avugaLa  angagaLAgi  bandiruva  padagaLa  arthadinda  nEravAgi 
paDeyalu sAdhyavAgadu. 
    Adare  mEle  4.2.1ralli  sUcisida  hAge  nAmapadagaLa  baLakeyalli 
jODupadagaLannu  racisikoLLuva  vidhAna  jArige  baralu  avannu 
hesarisuvudu mattu varNisuvudu embudAgi eraDu bEre bEre kelasa 
gaLalli toDagisabEkAguttadeyembudE mukhya kAraNa. Adare, kriyApada 
gaLa  baLakeyalli  I  eraDu  rItiya  kelasagaLu  baruvudilla.  avugaLa 
baLakeyalli kANisuva mEle vivarisidantaha viSiSTa rUpagaLige bEreyE 
kAraNagaLiddu,  avugaLindAgi  I  rUpagaLu  halavu  viSayagaLalli  
jODupadagaLiginta bhinnavAgive. 
    udAharaNegAgi,  I  viSiSTavAda  kriyArUpagaLalli  baruva 
modalaneya  kriyApadada  arthadalli  yAva  badalAvaNeyU  Agiruvu 
dilla.  adu  itara  baLakegaLalli  kANisuva  hAge  ondu  ghaTaneyannu 
sUcisuttiruttade.  eraDaneya  kriyApada  mAtra  tanna  svAtantryavannu 
kaLedukonDu  modalaneya  kriyApada  sUcisuva  ghaTaneya  kuritAgi 
heccinadEnannAdarU tiLisuva kAryadalli niratavAgiruttade. 
    jODupadada baLake idakkinta tIra bhinnavAdudu. adara angavAgi 
baruva  eraDu  nAmapadagaLU  tamma  mUlArthavannu  kaLedukoLLa 
balluvu  (4.3.1  nODi).  idallade  jODupadagaLannu  tayArisi 
baLasuva kelasa bhASeyannu baLasuva janara hatOTiyalliruttade. idakke 
badalu,  mEle  vivarisidantaha  kriyArUpagaLannu  yArU  prajYA 
pUvrakavAgi tayArisi baLasuva hAge kANisuvudilla. 
    jODupadagaLigU mattu I viSiSTavAda kriyArUpagaLigU naDuve 
intaha  halavu  vyatyAsagaLiruva  kAraNa,  I  kriyArUpagaLige  bEreyE 
ondu  hesarannu  koDuva  avaSyakateyide.  idakkAgi  ivannu  jODupada 
gaLendu  kareyuva  badalu  `kUDupada'  endu  kareyabahudu  (jAsti 
vivaragaLige bhaT 2002:179 nODi). 
5.6.1 samayada sUcane 
ondu  ghaTaneya  samayavannu  mUru  bEre  bEre  dxSTikOnagaLa 
mUlaka  sUcisalu  sAdhyavide  embudannu  nAvu  munde  hannondanemya 
adhyAyadalli  nODaliruvevu  (11.5).  I  mUru  dxSTikOnagaLannu 
samaya  sambandha,  Antarika  kAlavyavasthe  mattu  yathArthate  embudAgi 
hesarisabahudu.  heccina  bhASegaLU  ivugaLalli  yAvudAdarU  ondakke 
jAsti prAmukhyateyannu koDuttave.  
    kannaDada  maTTige  hELuvudAdare,  ghaTaneya  samayakkU  mattu 
adannu varadimADuttiruva ADugana samayakkU naDuviruva sambandhakke 
adara  kriyArUpagaLalli  heccina  prAmukhyateyide.  I  kAraNakkAgi, 
kannaDada  kriyArUpagaLalli  samaya  pratyayagaLannu  prAmukhyavAgi  I 
samaya  sambandhavannu  sUcisuvudakkAgiyE  baLasalAguttade.  ghaTanegaLa 
Antarika  kAlavyavasthe  mattu  yathArthategaLannu  kannaDada  kriyArUpagaLa 
mUlaka nEravAgi sUcisalu sAdhyavAgadu. 
    Adare mEle vivarisidantaha kUDupadagaLemba viSiSTavAda racanegaLa 
mUlaka  kannaDadalli  ghaTaneya  samayavannu  I  eraDu  dxSTikOnagaLa 
mUlaka  varadi  mADalu  sAdhyavide.  udAharaNegAgi,  kriyApadagaLa 
jODisuva  rUpagaLondige  biDu,  ADu,  bahudu,  iru  modalAda 
kriyApadagaLa pUrNarUpagaLannu sErisi racisida kUDupadagaLa mUlaka 
ghaTaneya  Antarika  kAlavyavasthe  mattu  yathArthategaLannu  sUcisalu 
sAdhyavide.

5.6.2 iru kriyApadada baLake

(40ka)  vAkyadalli  modalina  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  hOgi  emba 
kriyArUpadondige iru kriyApadada Igina rUpa (iddAne) bandide. 
idakke hOguva ghaTane pUrNagonDideyAdarU adara prabhAva pUtri 
aLidilla emba ghaTaneya kAlavyavasthege sambandhisida arthavide.  
    I  vAkyadallE  iru  kriyApadada  hindina  rUpavannu  baLasidalli  A 
ghaTane  pUtriyAgiruvudu  mAtravallade  adara  prabhAvavU  aLidide

Adare (40gha) vAkyakkilla embudannu gamanisabahudu.  
    idE  rItiyalli  iru  kriyApadada  mundina  rUpavannu  baLasi

samayadalli ghaTaneya prabhAva uLidiruttade emba artha baruttade. 
(40Ga)  nIvu baruvaSTaralli rAju cennayge hOgiruttAne. 
    hOgaliddAne  emba  kUDupadakke  munde  naDeyaliruva  ondu 
ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuva  arthavideyAdare,  hOgalidda  embudakke 
munde  naDeyabEkidda  (Adare  nijakkU  naDeyadiruva)  ghaTaneyannu 
sUcisuva (yathArthatege sambandhisida) arthavide. 
    hOguttiddAne embudakke mAtanADuva samayadalli naDeyuttA 
iruva  kSaNikavallada  ghaTaneyondannu  sUcisuva  arthavide.  ghaTane 
kSaNikavalla  emba  artha  adara  Antarika  kAlavyavasthege  sambandhisidudu. 
I  vAkyadallU  iru  kriyApadada  hindina  rUpavannu  baLasi  racisida 
hOguttidda  emba  rUpavannu  baLasidalli,  kSaNikavallada  hOguva 
ghaTane mAtina samayakkinta hinde naDedudemba Artha baruttade, mattu 
adE  kriyApadada  mundina  rUpavannu  baLasi  racisida  hOguttiru 
ttEne  embudannu  baLasidalli  antaha  ghaTane  mAtina  samayada 
anantara naDeyuvudemba artha baruttade. 
    intaha mUru rItiya kUDupadagaLallU iru kriyApada hindina, 
mundina  mattu  Igina  samayagaLannu  sUcisuttiralu  sAdhyavideyAda 
kAraNa,  samayada  maTTige  oTTu  ombattu  kriyArUpagaLu  intaha 
kUDupadada mUlaka siddhavAguttave.

5.6.3 koLLu padada baLake 
modalina  samayada  jODisuva  rUpadondige  koLLu  padada  bEre 
bEre kriyArUpagaLannu sErisi kUDupadagaLannu tayArisalu sAdhyavide. 
I  koLLu  padakke  svatantravAda  baLakeyilla.  cAritrikavAgi  idakke  paDe 
illavE  tegedukoLLu  emba  arthavide.  idara  mUlaka  tayArAguva 
kUDupadakke  ondu ghaTane tAnAgi naDedide illavE  obba vyakti adannu 
tanna hitakkAgi naDesiddAne emba arthavide. 
(41ka)  rAju mUru puTa bareda. 
(41kha) rAju mUru puTa baredukonDa. 
(41ka)da prakAra rAju mUru puTa barediruvudu tanna hitakkAgiyU 
irabahudu  illavE  bErobbana  hitakkAgiyU  irabahudu;  Adare 
(41kha)da prakAra Ata tanna hitakkAgi mAtravE mUru puTa barediddAne. 
Ata  bEreyavara  hitakkAgi  barediddAne  emba  viSayavannu  spaSTapaDisa 
bEkiddalli intaha vAkyagaLalli koDu kriyApadavannu  baLasiruva kUDu 
padavannu keLage (41ga)dalli kANisidante baLasabEkAguttade. 
(41ga)  rAju mUru puTa baredukoTTiddAne. 
    ondu  ghaTane  tAnAgi  naDedide  embudannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  I 
kUDupadavannu  baLasuvudu  sAdhya  embudakke  keLage  koTTiruva  (42ka-
kha) vAkyagaLu udAharaNegaLAgaballuvu. 
(42ka)  bAgilu tereyitu. 
(42kha) bAgilu teredukonDide. 
(42ka)da  prakAra  bAgilu  tereyalu  adannu  yArAdarU  terediruvudu 
kAraNavAgirabahudu,  Adare  (42kha)da  prakAra  adu  tAnAgi  (illavE 
gALige)  teredukonDide  (jAsti  vivaragaLige  bhaT  1978,  SrIdhar 
1990 nODi). 
5.7 sArAmSa 
tiLisuva  vAkyagaLa  koneyalli  mukhyakriyApadavAgi  baruva  kriyApada 
dondige  adu  sUcisuva  ghaTaneya  samayavannu  mattu  adaralli 
toDagiruva  ghaTakagaLallondannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  eraDu  pratyayagaLu 
baruttave. I pratyayagaLige bEre bEre rItiya kriyApadagaLeduru bEre 
bEre  rItiya  rUpagaLiddu  avu  entahavu  embudannU  mattu  I 
pratyayagaLondige  bandAga  kriyApadagaLalli  entaha  badalAvaNegaLella 
naDeyuttave embudannU mEle vivarisalAgide. 
    idallade, vAkyagaLeraDannu jODisi hELidAga illavE ondu vAkya 
vannu  innondu  vAkyada  oLavAkyavannAgi  mADi  hELidAga  avugaLalli 
baruva  kriyApadagaLa  rUpadalli  entaha  badalAvaNegaLella  kANisi 
koLLuttave embudannU mEle vivarisalAgide. 
    ondu  vAkyavannu  I  rIti  ondu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyannu 
tiLisuva kelasadalli baLasuva badalu adara mUlaka yAvudAdarondu 
kelasavannu  mADisikoLLuvudakkAgiyU  baLasalu  sAdhyavide.  antaha 
sandabhragaLalli adaralli baruva kriyApadadalli bEreyE kelavu badalA 
vaNegaLannu naDesabEkAguttade. I badalAvaNegaLu entahavu embudannu 
munde hattaneya adhyAyadalli vivarisalAguvudu.

[English →](./25-kannaDa-vAkyagaLa-oLaracane-en#chapter-6--use-of-qualifiers) | [Eke →](./25-kannaDa-vAkyagaLa-oLaracane-kn-eke#guNapadagaLa-baLake)
adhyAya Aru 
guNapadagaLa baLake 
6.1 pIThike 
kannaDada  vAkyagaLalli  mukhyavAgi  mUru  rItiya  guNapadagaLu  baLake 
yAguttave.  
    (1)  nAmapadagaLu  gurutisuva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLa 
guNadharmavondannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  padakantegaLalli  baruva 
doDDa,  cikka,  hosa,  haLe,  agala,  sapura,  kempu,  biLi 
modalAda guNapadagaLu,  
    (2)  kriyApadagaLu  tiLisuva  ghaTaneya 
guNadharmavondannu 
vAkyagaLalli  baruva  mellage,  bEga, 
sUcisuvudakkAgi 
doppane, daradarane, baLika, munce modalAda guNapadagaLu, 
mattu  
    (3)  I  eraDu  rItiya  guNapadagaLu  sUcisuva  guNadharmada 
pramANavannu  tiLisuvudakkAgi  avugaLondige  baruva  bahaLa, 
svalpa, oLLe, bhArI modalAda guNapadagaLu. 
I  mUru  rItiya  guNapadagaLa  baLakeyannU  keLagina  vAkyagaLalli  kANa 
bahudu. 
(1ka)  A doDDa maneyalli janaru mellage mAtanADuttAre. 
(1kha)  ivaradu bahaLa doDDa jagaLa. 
(1ga)  avaLu svalpa mellage naDeyuttiddALe. 
    nAmapadagaLondige  padakantegaLalli  baruva  guNapadagaLa  baLake 
yentahadu  embudannu  nAlkaneya  adhyAyadalli  vivarisalAgide.  kriyA 
padagaLondige  mattu  guNapadagaLondige  baruva  guNapadagaLa  svarUpa 
mattu baLakegaLentahavu embudannu I adhyAyadalli nODaliruvevu.   
6.2 guNapadagaLa naDuviruva sAmyagaLu 
nAmapada  mattu  kriyApadagaLondige  baruva  eraDu  rItiya  guNapada 
gaLa  naDuve  ondu  mukhyavAda  sAmyavide.  averaDU  yAvudAdarU 
ondu guNadharmavannu mAtravE sUcisuvudakkAgi baLakeyAguttave. I 
viSayadalli avu nAmapada mattu kriyApadagaLiginta bhinnavAgive.  
    nAmapadagaLu  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu  gurutisuvudakkAgi 
baLakeyAguttiddu,  avugaLa  mUlaka  halavu  guNadharmagaLu  sUcita 
vAguttiralu sAdhyavide. idE rItiyalli kriyApadagaLu ghaTaneyondannu 
tiLisuvudakkAgi baLakeyAguttiddu, A ghaTaneya mUlakavU halavu guNa 
dharmagaLu sUcitavAguttiralu sAdhyavide. 
    I  kAraNakkAgi,  yAvudAdarondu  guNapadada  baLake  avaSyavA 
giruvantaha  kelavu  sandabhragaLalli  guNapadavondannu  baLasade  bariya 
nAmapada  illavE  kriyApadagaLannu  baLasalu 
sAdhyavAguvudilla. 
kelavomme  hAge  baLasidarU  alli  guNapadavondu  sUcitavAgu 
ttiruttade.  intaha  sandabhragaLalli  mEle  vivarisiruva  eraDu  rItiya 
guNapadagaLU  (nAmaguNapadagaLu  mattu  kriyAguNapadagaLu)  bara 
balluvu  embudu  I  eraDu  rItiya  guNapadagaLa  naDuviruva  sAmya 
vannu sUcisuttade. 
    nAmapada illavE kriyApadagaLondige guNapadavondannu baLasalE 
bEkAguva  intaha  sandabhragaLalli  mukhyavAda  kelavannu  keLage  koDa 
6.2.1 guNadharmada pramANavannu sUcisuva padagaLu     
mEle  sUcisida  eraDu  rItiya  guNapadagaLU  guNadharmavondara 
pramANavannu  sUcisaballa  bahaLa,  svalpa,  bhArI  modalAda  guNapada 
gaLondige baraballuvu. 
(2ka)  idu bahaLa doDDa mara. 
(2kha)  avanu bahaLa bEga malagida. 
    pramANavannu  sUcisuva  guNapadagaLu  sAmAnyavAgi  nAmapada 
illavE  kriyApadagaLondige  nEravAgi  sErikoLLuvudilla.  kelavu 
sandabhragaLalli avannu A rIti sErisalu sAdhyavAguvudAdarU antaha 
baLakegaLalli yAvudAdarU ondu guNapada sUcitavAguttiruttade. 
(3ka)  avaru bhArI mane kaTTisiddAre. 
(3kha)  avaru tamma kannaDakavannu bahaLa huDukidaru. 
(3ka)dalli bhArI mane embudakke bhArI doDDa mane emba arthavU 
mattu  (3kha)dalli  bahaLa  huDukidaru  embudakke  bahaLa  hottu 
huDukidaru  emba  arthavU  baruttade.  hAgAgi,  illi  mUraneya 
vibhAgada  bhArI  mattu  bahaLa  emba  guNapadagaLu  nEravAgi  hELa 
diddarU sUcyavAgiruva guNapadagaLa pramANavannE tiLisuttive. 
6.2.2 hOlikeyannu sUcisuva vAkyagaLu      
hOlikeyannu  sUcisuva  vAkyagaLallella  yAvudAdarondu  guNapada 
baralEbEkemba  niyamavide.  idu  nAmaguNapadavirabahudu  illavE 
kriyAguNapadavirabahudu. 
(4ka)  adaraSTu doDDa kaTTaDa illilla. 
(4kha)  avaLaSTu mellage naDeyuvavarannu nAnu nODilla. 
(5ka)  adakkinta doDDa kaTTaDa illilla. 
(5kha)  avaLiginta mellage naDeyuvavarannu nAnu nODilla. 
intaha  hOlikeya  vAkyagaLalli  kelavomme  guNapadavondannu  baLasa 
diralu  sAdhyavide;  hIgiddarU  antaha  vAkyagaLalli  yAvudAdarondu 
guNapada sUcitavAgadiruvudilla.   
(6ka)  avaraSTu haNa nammallilla. 
(6kha)  nAnu avaraSTu Odalilla. 
6.2.3 beragannu sUcisuva vAkyagaLu 
beragannu sUcisuva vAkyagaLalli beragige AdhAravAgi yAvudAdarondu 
guNapadaviruva  avaSyakateyide.  Adare  idu  nAmaguNapadavirabahudu 
illavE kriyAguNapadavirabahudu. 
(7ka)  avaradu eSTu doDDa mane! 
(7kha)  avanu eSTu bEga ODida! 
intaha  vAkyagaLallU  kelavomme  guNapadavondannu  baLasadiralu  sAdhya 
vide.  Adare  avugaLallU  yAvudAdarondu  guNapada  sUcitavAga 
diruvudilla. 
(8ka)  avana hattira eSTu (tumbA) pustakagaLive! 
(8kha)  avanu hEge (jOrAgi) ODida! 
6.3 kelavu vyatyAsagaLu 
nAmapadagaLondige padakantegaLa angavAgi baruva nAmaguNapada mattu 
kriyApadagaLondige vAkyada angavAgi baruva kriyAguNapada iveraDara 
naDuve  mEle  vivarisidantaha  sAmyagaLu  mAtravallade  kelavu  vyatyAsa 
gaLU ive. I guNapadagaLu eraDu rItiya padagaLondige (nAmapada 
gaLondige mattu kriyApadagaLondige) bEre bEre rItiya kelasagaLannu 
naDesuvudakkAgi barabEkAguttade embudE avugaLa naDuve kANisuva I 
vyatyAsagaLige mUla kAraNa. 
6.3.1 niScitavAda jAga 
nAmapadagaLondige  baruva  guNapadagaLige  padakanteyalli  ondu 
niScitavAda  jAgaviddu  adannu    badalAyisuvudu  kaSTasAdhya.  idallade, 
adu  ondu  nAmapadada  adhInavAgiruva  kAraNa,  A  nAmapadavannu 
biTTu  bEre  kaDege  hOguva  svAtantryavU  adakkilla.  Adare,  kriyApada 
gaLondige  baruva guNapadagaLige I rIti  vAkyadalli ondu niScitavAda 
jAgavembudilla.  sAmAnyavAgi  avu  kriyApadada  edurigEnE  baruvu 
vAdarU  bEre  bEre  kAraNagaLigAgi  avannu  vAkyada  itara  jAgagaLige 
vagrAyisalu sAdhyavide. 
     padakantegaLalli guNapadagaLu nAmapadada modalu baruttave. avu 
nAmapadada  anantara  bandare  adondu  vAkyavAguttadallade  padakante 
yAgi  uLiyuvudilla.  udAharaNegAgi,  kempu  hU  embudu  ondu 
padakante, Adare hU kempu embudu ondu vAkya. 
(9ka)  A giDadallondu kempu hU araLide. 
(9kha)  A giDada hU kempu. 
    Adare  vAkyada  angavAgi  baruva  guNapadagaLannu  kriyApadada 
anantaravU  baLasalu  sAdhyavide.  idu  modalige  baLasalu  maretu 
hOgidda  guNadharmavondannu  sUcisuttirabahudu  illavE  A  guNa 
dharmada  mEle  heccina  ottu  koDalu  I  rIti  baLakeyAgirabahudu. 
I  viSayadalli  kriyAguNapada  vAkyada  itara  ghaTakagaLa  hAge  vatrisu 
ttade. avannU I rIti vAkyada konege vagrAyisalu sAdhyavide. 
(10ka)  avanu bahaLa mellage OduttAne. 
(10kha) avanu OduttAne, bahaLa mellage. 
(11ka)  avanige ondu cikka bahumAna sikkide. 
(11kha) avanige sikkide, ondu cikka bahumAna. 
(10ka)dalli  bandiruva  mellage  emba  kriyAguNapadavannu  (10kha)dalli 
vAkyada konege (endare kriyApadada anantarada jAgakke) vagrAyisalu 
sAdhyavAgide.  Adare,  (11ka)dalli  bandiruva  cikka  emba  nAmaguNa 
padavannu  I  rIti  vAkyada  konege  (endare  nAmapadada  anantarada 
jAgakke)  vagrAyisalu  sAdhyavAgadu.  (11kha)dalli  adannu  I  rIti 
vagrAyisalAgideyAdarU  adarondige  bahumAna  emba  nAmapada 
vannU  (endare  iDI  ghaTakavannE  vagrAyisabEkAgide)  embudannu 
gamanisabahudu. 
    vAkyada  angavAgi  baruva  kriyAguNapadagaLannu  vAkyada  oLagEnE 
bEre  jAgagaLigU vagrAyisalu sAdhyavide. Adare nAmapadagaLondige 
baruva guNapadagaLannu I rIti vAkyada bEre jAgagaLige vagrAyisalu 
sAdhyavAgadu. 
(12ka)  Ata sAyibAbanannu bahaLa cannAgi nambiddAne. 
(12kha) Ata bahaLa cannAgi sAyibAbanannu nambiddAne. 
    kriyAvAkyagaLalli  baruva  ghaTakagaLalli  ondannu  pratyEkisi  vAkyada 
uLida  bhAgadondige  adu  sambandhiside  embudannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi 
adannondu viSayavAkyada ghaTakavannAgi badalAyisalu sAdhyavide. 
(13ka)  avanu rAjuvige hoDeda. 
(13kha) avanu hoDedaddu rAjuvige. 
(13ga)  rAjuvige hoDedaddu avanu. 
(13kha)dalli  rAjuvige  emba  ghaTakavannU  mattu  (13ga)dalli  avanu 
emba  ghaTakavannU  (13ka)dalli  bandiruva  vAkyadinda  pratyEkisi,  eraDu 
rItiya viSayavAkyagaLannu tayArisalAgide. 
    vAkyadalli  baruva  kriyAguNapadagaLannU  I  rIti  pratyEkisi,  adu 
vAkyada  uLida  bhAgakke  sambandhisideyembudAgi  sUcisalu  sAdhyavide. 
Adare  padakanteyalli  baruva  nAmaguNapadagaLannu  I  rIti  pratyEkisi 
hELalu  sAdhyavAgadu.  avannu  padakanteyalli  hAgeyE  uLisikoLLuva 
avaSyakateyide. 
(14ka)  avanu bahaLa mellage naDeyuttAne. 
(14kha) avanu naDeyuvudu bahaLa mellage. 
(15ka)  avanige ondu cikka bahumAna sikkide. 
(15kha) avanige sikkidudu ondu cikka bahumAna. 
(14kha)dalli bahaLa mellage embudannu kriyApadadinda pratyEkisi adu 
kriyApadakke  (mattu  vAkyada  itara  bhAgagaLige)  sambandhiside  endu 
sUcisalu  sAdhyavAgide.  Adare,  (15kha)dalli  I  rIti  cikka  (illavE 
ondu  cikka)  embudannu  nAmapadadinda  pratyEkisalu  sAdhyavAgilla. 
adannu  bahumAna  emba  nAmapadadondigEnE  irisi  iDI  ghaTaka 
vannE A rIti sambandhisiruvantahadu embudAgi sUcisabEkAgide. 
sUcisuvudakkAgi  baLakeyAguva 
    guNapadagaLa 
bahaLa,  svalpa  modalAda  mUraneya  vibhAgakke  (6.1  nODi)  sEruva 
guNapadagaLU  nAmaguNapadagaLa  hAge  ondu  niScitavAda  jAgadalli 
baruttave;  kriyAguNapadagaLa  hAge  avannu  bEre  jAgagaLige  vagrA 
guNadharmavannu 
yisalu  sAdhyavAguvudilla  embudannU  mEle  koTTiruva  udAharaNe 
gaLinda tiLiyabahudu. 
6.3.2 E illavE U pratyayagaLa jote baLake 
kriyAguNapadavondakke  E  pratyayavannu  sErisuvudara  mUlaka  adannu 
otti hELalu sAdhyavide, mattu U pratyayavannu sErisuvudara mUlaka 
adondu heccina guNadharma embudAgi sUcisalu sAdhyavide. intaha 
eraDu vidhAnagaLallU nAmaguNapadagaLu baLakeyAgalAravu. 
(16ka)  avanu bahaLa jOrAgiyE naDeyuttidda. 
(16kha) avanu mellagU naDeyaballa. 
    I viSayadallU kriyAguNapadagaLu vAkyada itara ghaTakagaLa hAge 
vatrisuttave.  vAkyada  ghaTakagaLannU  avugaLa  hAge  E  illavE  U 
pratyayagaLondige baLasalu sAdhyavide. 
(17ka)  A mudukanE bahaLa jOrAgi naDeyuttidda. 
(17kha) A mudukanU bahaLa jOrAgi naDeyuttidda. 
6.3.3  pratidhvanisuva racaneyalli baLake 
obba  vyakti  illavE  vastuvannu  aspaSTavAgi  gurutisi  hELabEkAdAga  A 
vyakti illavE vastuvannu sUcisuva nAmapadadondige A nAmapadavannu 
pratidhvanisuva  innondu  padavannu  sErisi  hELuva  vidhAna  kannaDadalli 
baLakeyallide.  keLagina  (18ka-kha)  vAkyagaLalli  I  vidhAnada  baLakeyannu 
kANabahudu. 
(18ka)  idaralli EnAdarU kallugillu ideyO nODu. 
(18kha) allige hOgabEDa, hAvugIvu iddItu. 
(18ka)dalli kallu padada anantara A padada `pratidhvani'yante kANisuva 
gillu pada sEride. I eraDu padagaLa jODikege kallu ityAdi emba 
arthaviddu,  adu  gurutisabEkAgiruva  vastuvannu  I  jODike  svalpa 
maTTige aspaSTavAgi sUcisuttade.  
    idE  rItiyalli  (18kha)dalli  hAvu  padada  anantara  gIvu 
embudu  bandiddu,  I  jODikege  hAvu  ityAdi  emba  aspaSTavAda 
arthavide. 
    kriyApadagaLondige  baruva  guNapadagaLannu  I  vidhAnadalli  baLasi, 
avu sUcisuva guNadharma aspaSTavAdudu embudAgi sUcisalu sAdhya 
(19ka)  avanu bEgagIga ella baralikkilla. 
(19kha) nIvu  adannu  beLLage  giLLage  ella  mADuttEnendu 
kuLitare rAtriyAdItu. 
    Adare,  nAmapadagaLondige  baruva  guNapadagaLannu  I  vidhAnadalli 
baLasalu  sAdhyavAgadu.  idakke  kAraNavEnendare,  vyakti,  vastu  modalA 
davugaLannu  gurutisuva  kelasa  heccu  sulabhavAguva  hAge  mattu  heccu 
khacitavAguva  hAge  nAmapadagaLondige  I  guNapadagaLannu  baLasa 
lAguttade. hAgAgi avugaLa arthavannu `aspaSTa'vAgi mADuva mElina 
vidhAnakke avugaLa baLakeyalli yAva sthAnavU illa. 
    guNapadaviruva padakantegaLannu (endara vAkyada ghaTakagaLannu) mAtra 
I vidhAnadalli baLasalu sAdhyavide. Adare hAge baLasidAga, nAmapadada 
edurigiruva tanna jAgavannu guNapada biTTukoDuvudilla. 
(20)  ellAdarU kempuhUvu gempuhUvu sikkidare tanni. 
    illi  aspaSTavAgiruvudu  hUvina  baNNavalla,  hUvE  embudannu 
gamanisabahudu. 
6.3.4 pratyayagaLa baLake 
nAmapada  mattu  kriyApadagaLondige  baraballa  I  eraDu  rItiya 
guNapadagaLigU  avugaLadE  Ada  kelasagaLiddu,  adakkinta  binnavAda 
kelasavondaralli  avannu  baLasabEkiddalli  avakke  yAvudAdarondu 
pratyayavannu sErisuva avaSyakateyide.  
    udAharaNegAgi,  nAmapadagaLondige  baruvudu  nAmaguNapadagaLa 
kelasa.  idakke  badalu  avannu  kriyApadagaLondige  avugaLa  guNadharma 
vannu sUcisuvudakkAgi baLasabEkAgiddalli avakke yAvudAdarU pratyaya 
vannu sErisabEkAguttade.  
(21ka)  I kempu hU bahaLa cannAgide. 
(21kha) kammAranu nEgilina tudiyannu kempage kAyisida. 
(21ka)dalli  kempu  guNapada  hU  emba  nAmapadadondige  bandide. 
idannu  kAyisida  emba  kriyApadadondige  baLasuvudakkAgi  (21kha) 
dalli adakke age pratyayavannu sErisabEkAgide. 
    idE  rItiyalli  ondu  kriyAguNapadavannu  kriyApadada  badalu 
nAmapadadondige  baLasabEkiddalli  adarondige 
sambandhavannu 
sUcisuva a pratyayavannu sErisabEkAguttade. 
(22ka)  avanu A kelasavannu nALe mADali. 
(22kha) nInu nALina kelasavannu ivattE mADu. 
(23ka)  avanu mellage mAtanADida. 
(23kha) avana mellagina mAtu nanage kELisalilla. 
(22ka)dalli  jAgavannu  sUcisuva  nALe  guNapada  ondu  kriyApada 
dondige (mADali embudarondige) adara ondu ghaTakavAgi bandide. 
adannE ondu nAmapadadondige (mAtu embudarondige) baLasuvu 
dakkAgi  (22kha)dalli  adakke  a  pratyayavannu  sErisi  nALina  embudAgi 
badalAyisalAgide.  
    (23kha)dalli age pratyayavannu sErisi tayArisiruva mellage emba 
kriyAguNapadavU mAtu nAmapadadondige baruvudakkAgi I rIti a 
pratyayavannu  paDeyabEkAgide.  (I  eraDu  sandabhragaLallU  guNapada 
gaLa  koneyalli  in  embudu  sErikonDiddu,  adakke  heccina  artha 
vEnU illa.) 
    naDuve,  kaDege,  tudi(yalli)  modalAda  bEre  kelavu  kriyAguNa 
guNapadagaLannAgi 
padagaLannu  avugaLa 
badalAyisalu sAdhyavide. idakkAgiyU avakke sambandhavannu sUcisuva 
a pratyayavannu sErisuva avaSyakateyide. I pratyayadeduru avugaLalli 
bEre  kelavu  kUDikeya  badalAvaNegaLU  naDeyuttave  embudannu  kaTTa 
parimANavannu 
sUcisuva 
kaDege, motta modalu, tutta tudi(yalli)  embantaha udAharaNe 
gaLalli kANabahudu. 
6.3.5 guNadharmadalli vyatyAsa 
kriyAguNapada  mattu  nAmaguNapadagaLu  sUcisuva  guNadharmagaLa 
naDuveyU  ondu  prAmukhyavAda  vyatyAsavide.  kriyAguNapadagaLu 
sAmAnyavAgi  kSaNikavAda  illavE  bEgane  aLidu  hOguvantaha 
guNadharmagaLannu sUcisuttave. Adare nAmaguNapadagaLu heccu samaya 
uLidukoLLaballantaha guNadharmagaLannu sUcisuttave. 
    I  vyatyAsakke 
kAraNavEnendare,  kriyApadagaLu  ghaTanegaLannu 
sUcisuttiddu,  avugaLalli  heccinavU  ondu  bArige  naDedu  hOgu 
vantahavugaLu.  hAgAgi  avugaLondige  baruva  kriyAguNapadagaLu 
bEgane  aLiduhOguvantaha  guNadharmagaLannu  sUcisuttiddare  sAku. 
sAmAnyavAgi  ivu  ghaTane  naDeyuva  krama,  ghaTaneya  jAga  illavE 
ghaTaneya samayavannu sUcisuva guNapadagaLAgiruttave. 
    idakke  badalu,  nAmapadagaLu  sAmAnyavAgi  heccu  samaya 
badalAgade  uLiyuva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu  sUcisuttave. 
hAgAgi,  avugaLondige  baruva  nAmaguNapadagaLu  heccu  samaya 
uLiyuvantaha guNadharmagaLannu sUcisabEkAguttade. I guNapadagaLu 
sUcisuva aLate, baNNa, bhavtika guNadharmagaLu, ivella intaha svarUpa 
davAgive embudannu illi gamanisabahudu (4.3.2 nODi). 
6.3.6 vAkyaracaneya bEDikegaLu 
kelavomme  vAkyaracaneya  bEDikegaLannu  pUtrigoLisuvudakkAgi  kSaNika 
guNadharmagaLannu 
nAmaguNapada 
sUcisuva  kriyAguNapadagaLannu 
gaLannAgi  baLasuva  avaSyakate  kanDubaruttade.  udAharaNegAgi  ondu  
vAkyada  koneya  kriyApadakke  ike  pratyayavannu  sErisuva  mUlaka 
adannu  innondu  vAkyada  oLavAkyavannAgi  (ghaTakavannAgi)  mADuvu 
diddalli  adarondige  baruva  kriyAguNapadavannu  nAmaguNapadavAgi 
badalAyisuva avaSyakateyide (7.3.2 nODi). 
(24ka)  Ake gaTTiyAgi hADuttiddALe. 
(24kha) Akeya gaTTiyAda hADuvike illivaregU kELisuttide. 
    Adare  intaha  sandabhragaLalli  baruva  nAmaguNapadagaLu  nijakkU 
kriyAguNapadagaLAgiddu  ghaTaneyondara  guNadharmavannu  sUcisuttive 
embudannu gamanisabahudu. (24kha)dalli hADuvike emba nAmapadavu 
ondu  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuttide  mattu  I  ghaTaneya  guNadharma 
vondannu gaTTiyAda emba guNapada sUcisuttide. 
    idE  rItiyalli  SASvatavAda  guNadharmavondannu  sUcisuva 
guNapadavannu  kelavu  sandabhragaLalli  kriyAguNapadavannAgi  mADi 
baLasuva  avaSyakate  kanDubaruttade.  intaha  sandabhragaLalli  avu  nEra 
vAgi  ghaTaneya  guNadharmavondannu  sUcisuva  badalu  ghaTaneyalli 
toDagikonDiruva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLa  guNadharmavondannu 
sUcisuttave. 
(25ka)  Ake bALekAyiyannu teLLage kattarisuttiddALe. 
(25kha) avanu bAgilina hattira neTTage nintiddAne. 
(25ga)  rAju raggu hodedukonDu beccage malagiddAne. 
mElina  vAkyagaLalli  bandiruva  teLLage,  neTTage  mattu  beccage  emba 
guNapadagaLu  kattarisu,  nillu  mattu  malagu  emba  kriyApadagaLa 
viSESaNagaLAgi  bandiveyAdarU  avu  nEravAgi  A  kriyApadagaLu 
tiLisuva  ghaTanegaLa  guNadharmagaLannu  sUcisuvudakkintalU  avu  naDe 
dudarindAgi  illavE  naDeyuttiruvAga  avugaLa  ghaTakagaLalli  kANisuva 
guNadharmagaLannu  sUcisuttive.  udAharaNegAgi,  kattarisuva  ghaTane 
ondu  vidhavAgi  sAguttiruvudarindAgi  adara  mUlaka  teLLagAgiruva 
vastugaLu siddhavAguttive emba artha (25ka) vAkyakkide. 
guNadharmavannu 
nEravAgi  ghaTaneya 
6.4 aNakisuva guNapadagaLu 
kannaDadalli 
sUcisuvantaha 
guNapadagaLu jAstiyilla. Adare, ghaTanegaLu naDeyuvAga avugaLa saddu, 
nOTa,  spaSra  modalAda  guNadharmagaLa  viSayadalli  ADugana 
llunTAguva  anubhavagaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  antaha  anubhavagaLannu 
`aNakisu'vantaha  halavu  padagaLannu  guNapadagaLAgi  baLasuva  vidhAna 
kannaDadalli baLakeyallide.  
(26ka)  mElininda peTTige Dabbane keLage bittu. 
(26kha) avanu upparigeyinda daDadaDane keLagiLidu banda. 
(26ga)  dIpa miNimiNi uriyuttittu. 
(26gha) avaLu ellavannU paTapaTane hELi mugisidaLu. 
(26Ga) adarinda gammane vAsane horasUsuttittu. 
    kannaDadalli intaha guNapadagaLu keLagina udAharaNegaLalli kANisuva 
hAge mukhyavAgi mUru rUpagaLalli baLakeyAguttave.    
(1)  akSaragaLu  mUriddu,  eraDaneya  akSara  ottakSaravAgiruva 
padagaLu:  sarrane,  girrane,  caTTane,  doppane,  bussane,  taTTane, 
(2)  akSaragaLu  nAlkiddu,  mUraneya  akSara  ottakSaravAgiruva 
padagaLu:  gabakkane,  taTakkane,  kavakkane,  baDakkane,  tapakkane, 
caTakkane, pacakkane, duDummane, guLummane, ityAdi. 
(3)  akSaragaLu  aydiddu,  yAvudU  ottakSaravAgilladiruva 
katakatane,  caTacaTane, 
padagaLu: 
giragirane, 
pakapakane, 
karakarane, 
kacakacane, ityAdi. 
gaNagaNane,  daradarane, 
kilakilane, 
gaLagaLane, 
ivugaLalli  mUraneya  vibhAgakke  sErida  padagaLalli  kelavu  ane  emba 
pratyayavilladeyU  baLakeyAgaballuvu  (udA:  daradara,  caTacaTa, 
ityAdi).  idallade,  bEre  kelavu  padagaLu  yAvAgalU  ane  emba 
pratyayavilladeyE  baruttave  (udA:  kiNikiNi,  surusuru,  piLipiLi, 
    intaha  aNakisuva  guNapadagaLallella  modalige  yAvudAdarU 
suruvAguva 
aNakisuva padagaLu kannaDadalli illavendE hELabahudEnO.  
    idallade,  intaha  heccina  padagaLallU  giDDa  svaragaLu  mAtra 
baLakeyAguttave.  paTArane  mattu  taTArane  embantaha  kelavE  kelavu 
padagaLalli mAtra udda svara kANisikoLLuttade.  
    mUraneya  vibhAgakke  sEruva  aydakSaraviruva  guNapadagaLallella 
aNakavannu  sUcisuva  ondu  pada  eraDeraDu  bAri  baruttade.  idallade 
vyanjanavilladiruvudilla.  bahuSaH 
svaradalli 
intaha  guNapadagaLalli  udda  svara  mAtravallade  ottakSaravU  kANisi 
koLLuvudilla (bhaT 1999:192 nODi).    
6.5 jAgavannu sUcisuva guNapadagaLu 
ondu ghaTane naDeyuvudu elli embudAgi adara jAgavannu sUcisalu 
kannaDadalli  ondu  guNapadavannAgali  illavE  adakkinta  heccu  svatantra 
vAgiruva ondu ghaTakavannAgali baLasalu sAdhyavide. I eraDu rItiya 
vAkyAngagaLa  naDuve  jAsti  vyatyAsa  illa.  kelavu  sandabhragaLalli  nAvu 
baLasiruva  vAkyAngavannu  ondu  guNapadavendu  kareyabEkO  athavA 
ondu ghaTakavendu kareyabEkO emba viSayadalli samSayavunTAgalu 
illavE abhiprAyabhEdavunTAgalu sAdhyavide. 
    udAharaNegAgi, alli, illi, Ace, Ice, mEle, keLage, oLage, 
horage,  hattira,  dUra,  hinde,  munde  modalAda  bEre  bEre 
rItiya  jAgagaLannu  sUcisuva  padagaLannu  guNapadagaLendu  kareyalu 
sAdhyavide.  Adare  ivannE  baLasi  tayArisida  namma  maneyalli, 
mADina mEle, haTTiyinda dUra, halasina marada Ace modalAda 
padakantegaLu vAkyadalli bandAga avu mukhyavAda illavE mukhyavallada 
ghaTakagaLAgi kANisikoLLuttave. 
(27ka)  nimma pustakavannu illi irisiddEne. 
(27kha) avaru koTTa haNavannu kapATinalli irisiddEne. 
(28ka)  Atana gALipaTa bahaLa mEle hOgide. 
(28kha) avanu A pustakavannu tanna hosa mEjina mEle bareda. 
    I guNapadagaLu ondu ghaTaneya jAgavannu nEravAgi sUcisuttira 
bahudu,  illavE  ADugana  jAgakke  sambandhisiruva  hAge  sUcisuttira 
bahudu. udAharaNegAgi, sutta, oLage, naDuve modalAda guNapada 
gaLu  ghaTaneya  jAgavannu  nEravAgi  sUcisaballuvu.  avannu  vAkyadalli 
baLasidAga, avu ghaTanege sambandhisidante yAva jAgavannu sUcisuttave 
embudannu  tiLiyalu  A  vAkyavannADiruva  vyakti  elliddAne  embudannu 
tiLiyuva avaSyakateyilla. 
    Adare, Ace, Ice, alli, illi, mEle, keLage modalAda bEre 
kelavu guNapadagaLu ghaTaneya jAgavannu ADugana jAgakke sambandhisiruva 
hAge sUcisuttave. avannu vAkyadalli baLasidAga avu yAva jAgavannu 
sUcisuttave  embudannu  tiLiyalu  A  vAkyavannADiruva  vyakti  elli 
nintiddAne  embudannu  tiLiyuva  avaSyakateyide.  I  eraDu  rItiya 
guNapadagaLa  naDuviruva  I  vyatyAsavannu  keLagina  vAkyagaLalli  kANa 
bahudu. 
(29ka)  rAju illi hADuttiddAne. 
(29kha) rAju oLage hADuttiddAne. 
(29ka)  vAkyada  prakAra  rAju  hADuttiruvudu  elli  embudannu 
tiLiyalu  A  vAkyavannADiruva  vyakti  elliddAne  embudannu  tiLiyuva 
avaSyakateyide. Adare (29kha)dalli idu avaSyavilla.  
    I  guNapadagaLu  sUcisuva  jAga  ondu  calanege  sambandhisiruvu 
dAdalli,  avu  bariya  jAgavannu  sUcisuva  badalu  calaneya  suru 
illavE  koneyannu  sUcisalu  sAdhyavide.  idakkAgi  I  guNapada 
gaLondige inda mattu ge emba pratyayagaLannu baLasabEkAguttade. 
(30ka)  avanu illi hADuttiddAne. 
(30kha)  avanu illinda hOgiddAne. 
(30ga)  avanu illige bandiddAne. 
(30ka)dalli  illi  emba  pada  bariya  ondu  jAgavannu  sUcisuttide 
yAdare,  (30kha)dalli  illinda  embudu  ondu  calaneya  suruvannU 
mattu  (30ga)dalli  illige  embudu  ondu  calaneya  koneyannU 
sUcisuttive. 
6.6 samayavannu sUcisuva guNapadagaLu 
jAgavannu  sUcisuva  padagaLa  hAge  samayavannu  sUcisuva  padagaLU 
ondu  ghaTaneya  illavE  sangatiya  samayavannu  nEravAgi  sUcisa 
balluvu illavE adannE vAkyada ADugana samayakke sambandhisida hAge 
sUcisaballuvu.  idakkAgi  vAkyagaLalli  eraDu  rItiya  padagaLa  baLake 
yAguttade. 
    vAkyada  mukhya  kriyApadadalli  baruva  pratyayagaLu  ghaTaneya 
illavE  sangatiya  samayavannu  vAkyada  ADugana  samayakke  sambandhi 
siruva hAge mAtravE sUcisuttave embudannu nAvu hindina adhyAya 
gaLalli  (2.1.1  mattu  3.1.1ralli)  nODiruvevu.  (kriyApadagaLa 
jODisuva rUpagaLu mAtra idakke apavAdagaLAgive (5.2 nODi)). 
    ghaTaneya  samayavannu  ADugana  samayakke  sambandhisiruva  hAge 
sUcisuva  guNapadagaLu  kriyApadadalli  baruva  pratyayavu  sUcisuva 
samayavannE  heccu  vivaravAgi  tiLisuttave.  idannu  keLagina  vAkyagaLalli 
kANabahudu. 
(31ka)  mAruti nALe ALandige hOguttAne. 
(31kha) sItAbAyi ninne ondu sinemA nODidaLu. 
(31ka) vAkyada mukhya kriyApadadalli utta pratyaya bandiruva kAraNa, 
adu  A  vAkyavannADiruva  samayada  anantara  naDeyuva  ghaTane 
yondannu sUcisuttide mattu adE vAkyadalli baruva nALe emba pada 
adE samayavannu heccu vivaravAgi tiLisuttide.  
    idakke badalu (31kha) vAkyada mukhya kriyApadadalli id pratyaya 
bandiruva  kAraNa,  adu  A  vAkyavannADiruva  samayakkinta  modalu 
naDediruva  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuttide,  mattu  A  vAkyadalli  bandiruva 
ninne emba pada adE samayavannu heccu vivaravAgi tiLisuttide. 
     I  padagaLondige  suru  mattu  konegaLannu  sUcisuva  inda 
mattu  ge  pratyayagaLu  baralu  sAdhyaviddu,  avakke  ghaTane  suruvAgiruva 
mattu konegonDiruva samayagaLannu sUcisuva arthavide. 
(32ka)  avanu ninneyinda upavAsa mADuttiddAne. 
(32kha) avana upavAsa ninnege mugiyitu. 
6.7 sArAmSa 
kannaDa  vAkyagaLalli  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLa  guNadharmavannu 
sUcisuvavu,  ghaTanegaLa  guNadharmavannu  sUcisuvavu  mattu  guNa 
dharmagaLa  pramANavannu  sUcisuvavu  embudAgi  mUru  rItiya 
guNapadagaLu  baLakeyallive.  ivu  kelavu  viSayagaLalli  samAnavAgive 
Adare bEre kelavu viSayagaLalli ondakkinta ondu bhinnavAgive. ivugaLa 
naDuve kANisuva vyatyAsagaLalli heccinavU ivu vAkyagaLalli bEre bEre 
rItiya  kelasagaLannu  naDesuvudakkAgi  baLakeyAguttave  emba  viSayada 
mEle avalambisive. 
    ghaTaneya  samaya,  jAga  mattu  prakAragaLannu  sUcisuvavuga 
LembudAgi  kriyApadagaLondige  baruva  guNapadagaLannu  mUru  mukhya 
gumpugaLalli  vingaDisabahudu.  ivugaLalli  mUraneya  gumpige  sErida 
guNapadagaLalli heccinavU kannaDadalli aNakisuva padagaLAgi baLakeyallive.

adhyAya ELu 
oLavAkyagaLu 
7.1 pIThike 
eraDu  athavA  jAsti  vAkyagaLannu  oTTu  sErisi  ondE  vAkyavannAgi 
mADi  hELalu  kannaDadalli  mukhyavAgi  eraDu  vidhAnagaLive.  ondu 
vAkyavannu  innondaroLage  irisi  hELuvudu  ondu  vidhAna,  mattu 
eraDu  athavA  jAsti  vAkyagaLannu  mattu,  athavA,  Adare  modalAda 
padagaLa  mUlaka,  illavE  U,  E  modalAda  pratyayagaLa  mUlaka 
jODisi  hELuvudu  innondu  vidhAna.  ivugaLalli  modalaneya 
vidhAnavannu  I  adhyAyadallU  mattu  eraDaneya  vidhAnavannu  munde 
enTanE adhyAyadallU vivarisalAguvudu. 
    ondu  vAkyavannu  innondaroLage  irisi  hELidAga  avugaLalli 
horage  nilluva  vAkyavannu  `horavAkya'vendU  mattu  oLage  nilluva 
vAkyavannu  `oLavAkya'vendU  kareyabahudu.  udAharaNegAgi  keLage 
koTTiruva mUru vAkyagaLannu hOlisi nODabahudu. 
(1ka)  ivattu bEgane barabEku. 
(1kha)  SAmarAyaru (EnO) hELiddAre. 
SAmarAyaru ivattu bEgane barabEkendu hELiddAre. 
(1ka)  vAkyavannu  (1kha)  vAkyada  `oLage'  (EnO  emba  padada  jAga 
dalli)  irisi  (1ga)  vAkyavannu  tayArisalAgide,  mattu  idakkAgi  (1ka) 
vAkyada koneyalli endu padavannu sErisalAgide.  
    bEre bEre rItiya uddESagaLannu sAdhisuvudakkAgi I rIti ondu 
vAkyavannu innondu vAkyada oLage irisi hELalu sAdhyaviddu, idakkAgi 
I  uddESagaLannanusarisi  bEre  bEre  vidhAnagaLannU  baLasabEkAguttade. 
udAharaNegAgi,  obba  vyaktiyu  Enu  hELiruvanembudannu  etti  hELa 
bEkiddAga  mEle sUcisidante Ata baLasiruva  vAkyakke endu padavannu 
sErisi adannu oLavAkyavannAgi mADi baLasalu sAdhyavide.  
    idakke  badalu,  obba  vyakti  illavE  ondu  vastuvannu  varNisuva 
vidhAnada  mUlaka  gurutisabEkAgiruvAga,  adakkAgi  ondu  vAkyavannu 
baLasalu sAdhyaviddu, antaha vAkyavannU innondu vAkyada oLage irisi 
hELalu  sAdhyavide.  Adare,  idakkAgi  A  vAkyadalli  bEre  kelavu  rItiya 
badalAvaNegaLannu  mADikoLLabEkAguttade  embudannu  keLage  koTTiruva 
(2ka-gha) vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu. 
(2ka)  haNNu cannAgilla. 
(2kha)  rAju ondu haNNu koTTidda. 
(2gha)  rAju yAva haNNannu koTTiddanO adu cannAgilla. 
rAju koTTidda haNNu cannAgilla. 
(2ka)dalli bandiruva haNNu emba pada ondu vastuvannu gurutisuttade. 
adE  vastuvannu  innaSTu  spaSTavAgi  varNisalu  (2kha)  vAkyavannu  (2ka) 
vAkyada  oLage  irisi  hELalu  sAdhyavide.  idakkAgi  A  vAkyadalli  bEre 
eraDu  rItiya  badalAvaNegaLannu  mADabEkAguttade  embudannu  (2ga) 
mattu (2gha) vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu. 
    I  rIti  ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyada  oLavAkyavannAgi 
baLasuva  mukhya  sandabhragaLu  yAvuvu  mattu  antaha  sandabhragaLalli 
entaha  badalAvaNegaLannella  A  vAkyagaLalli  mADikoLLabEkAguttade 
embudannu keLage svalpa vivaravAgi tiLisalAgide. 
7.2 etti hELuvudu 
innobbana  mAtannu  illavE  abhiprAyavannu  etti  hELalu  kannaDadalli 
mukhyavAgi  eraDu  vidhAnagaLu  baLakeyallive.  A  mAtannu  illavE 
abhiprAyavannu  sUcisuva  vAkyavannu  ante  padadondige  baLasuvudu 
ondu  vidhAna,  mattu  A  vAkyakke  endu  padavannu  sErisi  adannu 
bErondu  vAkyada  oLavAkyavannAgi  mADi  baLasuvudu  innondu 
vidhAna. 
(3ka)  ivattondu sabheyideyante. 
(3kha)  ivattondu sabheyideyendu rAju tiLisiddAne. 
    (3ka)  vAkyadalli  ivattondu  sabheyide  emba  vAkyavannu  ante 
padadondige baLasalAgide mattu (3kha)dalli adE vAkyakke endu pada 
vannu sErisi adannu rAju (EnannO) tiLisiddAne emba vAkyada oLa 
vAkyavannAgi mADi baLasalAgide. 
    idallade,  etti  hELaliruva  vAkyavannu  ettihELuva  cihneya  oLage 
irisuva  innondu  vidhAnavU  barahadalli  baLakeyallide.  I  cihneya 
baLakeyannu keLagina vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu. 
``ivattondu sabheyide'' endu rAju tiLisida. 
(4kha)  rAju tiLisida: ``ivattondu sabheyide''. 
7.2.1 ante embudara baLake 
sAmAnyavAgi,  ondu 
sangatiyannu  niScitavAgiyU  intahavarE 
hELiruvarembudAgi  tiLisalu  sAdhyavilladantaha  (illavE  hAge  tiLisuva 
avaSyakateyilladantaha)  sandabhradalli  A  sangatiyannu  etti  hELuvu 
dakkAgi ante padada baLakeyAguttade. idara baLakeyAguvalli A hELike 
gaLa mUla yAvudembudannu (adannu yAru elli yAvAga hELidaru 
embudannu) sUcisuva paddhatiyilla.  
    idallade,  obba  vyakti  tanna  viSayavAgi  ante  padavannu  baLasi 
EnAdarU  hELuvudiddalli,  adu  Atana  hatOTiyallillada  ghaTaneya 
kuritAgirabEku  illavE  Ata  bAlyadalli  naDesida  (mattu  itararinda 
tiLidukonDiruva) kelasada kuritAgirabEku emba niyamavide. 
nAnu pAsAgiddEnante. 
(5kha)  nAnu bahaLa tanTe mADuttiddenante. 
    sAmAnyavAgi ante pada etti hELabEkAgiruva vAkyada koneyalli 
baruttade. kelavomme adannu vAkyada naDuveyU baLasuva sAdhyateyide. 
udAharaNegAgi, vAkyada ondu bhAgavannu mAtra otti hELuvudiddalli, 
antaha bhAgadondige adu vAkyada naDuveyU baraballudu. 
rAmanAyakarige 
sikkideyante. 
(6kha)  rAmanAyakarigante madhureyalli ondu praSasti sikkiddu. 
rAmanAyakarige madhureyallante ondu praSasti sikkiddu. 
madhureyalli 
praSasti 
(6kha)dalli  rAmanAyakarige  embudannu  mattu  (6ga)dalli  madhure 
yalli  embudannu  otti  hELalAgideyAda  kAraNa,  ante  pada  A 
padagaLondige bandide. 
    ante  embudara  mUlaka  etti  hELuva  vAkyavannu  ondu 
kELviyAgi  badalAyisalu  sAdhyavideyAdarU  allagaLeyuva  vAkyavAgi 
badalAyisalu  sAdhyavAgadu.  idakke  viruddhavAgi  allagaLeyuva  vAkya 
vannu  ante  embudara  mUlaka  etti  hELabahudu,  Adare  kELvi 
yondannu A rIti etti hELalu sAdhyavAgadu. 
(7ka)  maduvege hOgabEkanteyO? 
(7kha)  avanu maduvege hOguvudillavante. 
(7ka)  vAkyadalli  ante  embudara  mUlaka  etti  hELiruva  vAkya 
vondannu  kELviyAgi  badalAyisalAgide  mattu  (7kha)dalli  ante 
embudara  mUlaka  allagaLediruva  vAkyavondannu  etti  hELalAgide 
embudannu gamanisabahudu.  
    kELvigaLa  hAgeyE  itarara  mUlaka  kelasa  mADisalu  baLasuva 
vAkyagaLannu  illavE  beragannu  sUcisuva  vAkyagaLannu  I  rIti  ante 
emba  padavannu  baLasi  etti  hELalu  sAdhyavAgadu.  Adare,  kELuganu 
bErArigO  hELiruva  mAtondannu  illavE  kELugana  viSayavAgi 
bErArO  hELiruva  sangatiyondannu  adu  nijavE  embudAgi  kELi 
tiLiyalu adannu ante padadondige baLasalu sAdhyavide. 
(8ka)  nIvu mITingige hOgalillavante? 
(8kha)  nIvu ninneyE bandiddIrante? 
    vAkyavondannu  ante  padadondige  baLasidAgalella,  adaralli 
baruva  puruSavAcaka  padagaLannu  mattu  samayavannu  sUcisuva 
padagaLannu  etti  hELuva  sandabhrakke  hondikoLLuvante  badalAyisuva 
avaSyakateyide. udAharaNegAgi mEle (8kha)dalli ante padadondige 
bandiruva  vAkyavannu  adara  ADuganu  nIvu  ninneyE  bandiddIri 
embudAgi etti hELiruvudannu gamanisabahudu. 
    nijakkU I vAkyavannu ramESanemba bErobba vyakti rAju ivattu 
bandiddAne  embudAgi  hELirabahudu.  A  vAkyavannu  ADuganu 
rAjuvige  ante  padada  mUlaka  (mAraneya  divasa)  ettihELa 
bEkAgiruva sandabhradalli adaralli banda rAju padakke badalAgi nIvu 
emba  puruSavAcaka  padavannU,  ivattu  padakke  badalAgi  ninne 
padavannU mattu bandiddAne emba kriyArUpakke badalAgi bandiddIri 
emba kriyArUpavannU baLasabEkAgide embudannu gamanisabahudu.   
7.2.2 oLavAkyada baLake 
innobba  vyaktiya  mAtannu  etti  hELabEkAdAga,  A  mAtige  endu 
padavannu  sErisi,  adannu  bErondu  vAkyada  oLavAkyavannAgi  mADi 
hELuvudu  eraDaneya  vidhAna.  idu  mElina  vidhAnadinda  halavu 
viSayagaLalli  bhinnavAgide.  udAharaNegAgi,  A  mAtannu  yAru 
hELiddu,  yArondige  hELiddu,  elli  hELiddu,  yAvAga  hELiddu, 
hEge hELiddu embudannella I vidhAnadalli baLakeyAguva horavAkyada 
mUlaka tiLisalu sAdhyavide. 
(9ka)  piknikkige  baruvudillavendu  ninne  sanje  pATriyalli 
kANasikkiddAga rAju nanna hattira guTTAgi tiLisidda. 
(9kha)  rAju piknikkige baruvudillavante. 
illi  piknikkige  baruvudilla  embudu  oLavAkya.  adannu  yAvAga 
hELiddu  embudannu  horavAkyadalliruva  ninne  sanje  emba  ghaTaka, 
elli  hELiddu  embudannu  pATriyalli  kANasikkidAga  emba  ghaTaka 
(idarallU  ondu  oLavAkyavide),  yAru  hELiddu  embudannu  rAju 
emba ghaTaka, yAroDane hELiddu embudannu nanna hattira emba ghaTaka 
mattu hEge hELiddu embudannu guTTAgi emba guNapada tiLisuttave. 
    ante  padada  baLakeyalli  idAvudU  sAdhyavillavembudannu  (9kha) 
dalli kANabahudu. 
    idallade,  horavAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  kriyApada  etti 
hELuvudara uddESavEnembudannu tiLisuttade. I horavAkyadalli bEre 
bEre kriyApadagaLu baralu sAdhyaviddu avu intaha bEre bEre rItiya 
uddESagaLigAgi innobbara mAtannu etti hELalu sAdhyavide embudannu 
sUcisuttave. 
(10ka)  khanDitavAgiyU baruttEnendu Ata mAtu koTTidda. 
(10kha) oLage kAliDakUDadendu Ata AjYApisidda. 
(10ga)  ninne rAtri nimmallige barabEkendu Akege anisittu. 
(10gha)  Ake ellige hOgiddALendu Ata praSnisida. 
    ante  padada  baLakegU  mattu  endu  padada  baLakegU  naDuve 
halavu  vyatyAsagaLive.  mEle  sUcisida  hAge,  etti  hELuva  vAkyavannu 
yAru  yAvAga  elli  hELiruvarembudannu  spaSTavAgi  tiLisabEkA 
giruvAga  ante  embudannu  baLasalu  sAdhyavAgadu.  antaha  sandabhra 
gaLalli endu embudannE baLasabEkAguttade.  
    idallade,  endu  embudarondige  sEri  baruva  vAkya  ondu 
horavAkyada angavAgi baruvudAda kAraNa, A vAkyada kuritAgi innU 
EnEnu  hELabEkendideyO  adellavannU  I  horavAkyadalli  hELalu 
sAdhyavide. 
    innobbara  mAtannu  illavE  abhiprAyavannu  mAtravallade  tannadE 
mAtannu illavE abhiprAyavannU endu padada mUlaka etti hELalu 
sAdhyavide. 
(11ka)  nAnu elligU hOguvudillavendu rAjuvina hattira 
        hELidde. 
(11kha) nanage elligU hOgabEkendu anisuvudilla. 
kelasa

cennAgi 
porItsAhiside. 
    etti  hELuva  oLavAkyavondakke  horavAkyavAgi  kriyAvAkyagaLu 
mAtravallade  viSayavAkyagaLU  baralu  sAdhyaviddu,  ivU  kUDa  etti 
hELuvudakkiruva uddESavEnembudannu tiLisuttave. 
(12ka)  AkeyannE maduveyAguvudendu rAjuvina nirdhAra. 
(12kha) nimma haNa hindirugisiddEnendu nanna nenapu. 
(12ga)  nimage hosa sIre sikkideyendu Akege matsara. 
(12gha) avanige nimmannu kANabEkendide. 
    ante  mattu  endu  embavugaLa  baLakeya  naDuviruva  innondu 
vyatyAsavEnendare, ante embudannu baLasabEkiddalli ettihELuva vAkya 
dalli  etti  hELuva  sandabhrakkanusAravAgi  badalAvaNegaLannu  avaSya 
vAgiyU  mADabEkAguttade,  Adare  endu  embudara  baLakeyalli 
intaha badalAvaNegaLannu mADade iralU sAdhyavide.  
(13ka)  nAnu ivattu bEgane hOgabEkante. 
(13kha) nAnu ivattu bEgane hOgabEkendu rAju hELiddAne. 
(13ga)  nIvu nALe bEgane barabEkendu rAju hELida. 
nijakkU  rAju  hELiddu  ``nIvu  nALe  bEgane  barabEku''  endA 
giddarU,  adannu  etti  hELuva  sandabhrakke  hondikoLLuvante  ``nAnu 
ivattu  bEgane  hOgabEku''  embudAgi  (13ka)  mattu  (13kha) 
gaLalli  badalisalAgide.  Adare  (13ga)dalli  intaha  badalAvaNegaLannu 
mADadeyU  A  vAkyavannu  endu  padada  mUlaka  etti  hELalu 
sAdhyavAgide embudannu  gamanisabahudu. idu  ante embudara baLake 
yalli sAdhyavAgadu. 
    etti  hELuva  vAkyada  koneyalli  `illavE'  emba  arthaviruva  O 
pratyaya  bandideyAdalli,  emba  padavannu  baLasadeyU  A  vAkyavannu 
oLavAkyavannAgi mADi baLasalu sAdhyavide. 
(14ka)  avaLu yAke bandiddALO. 
(14kha) avaLu yAke bandiddALO nanage gottilla.

7.3 varNisuvudu 
kriyeyondaralli  niratarAgiruva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLannu 
gurutisuvudakkAgi  hesarisuvudu  mattu  varNisuvudu  emba  eraDu 
vidhAnagaLannu baLasalu sAdhya embudannu nAvu mEle nAlkanE adhyAya 
dalli nODiruvevu. I eraDu vidhAnagaLallU nAvu baLasuvudu ondu 
padakanteyannE.  
    Adare, varNisuva vidhAnadalli  adakkAgi baLakeyAguva padakanteya 
angavAgi ondu iDI vAkyavannU baLasalu sAdhyavide. idu hesarisuva 
vidhAnadalli  sAdhyavAgadu.  intaha  baLakeyalli  varNisuva  padakanteya 
angavAgi baruva vAkya adara `oLavAkya'vAgi baruttade. 
(16ka)  jAnaki maysUrininda ondu sIre tandiddaLu. 
(16kha) A sIre Iga haridu hOgide. 
(16ga)  jAnaki  maysUrininda  yAva  sIreyannu  tandiddaLO  A 
sIre Iga haridu hOgide. 
(16kha)dalli  A  sIre  emba  padakante  varNisuva  vidhAnada  mUlaka 
ondu vastuvannu gurutisuttade. I vastuvina viSayavAgi innU heccina 
sangatigaLannu  tiLisuvudakkAgi  a  padakanteyalli  (16ka)  vAkyavannu 
oLavAkyavannAgi mADi hELalu sAdhyavide embudannu (16ga) vAkyadalli 
kANabahudu.  idakkAgi  (16ka)  vAkyada  koneyalli  O  pratyayavannu 
baLasabEkAgide  mattu  adu  gurutisabEkAgiruva  vastuvannu  hesarisuva 
sIre padadeduru yAva emba aniScita savrapadavannu irisabEkAgide.  
    ondu  vAkyavannu  varNisuva  padakanteya  oLavAkyavannAgi  mADi 
hELalu  kannaDadalli  halavu  vidhAnagaLu  baLakeyallive.  mEle  sUcisida 
hAge,  aniScita  savrapadavondannu  (mattu  O  pratyayavannu)  baLasi 
hELuvudu  ondu  vidhAnavAdare,  vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  kriyA 
padakke  a  pratyayavannu  sErisuvudara  mUlaka  adannu  nAmapadada 
dondige baLasalu sAdhyavAguvante mADuvudu innondu vidhAna. I 
eraDaneya vidhAnada baLakeyannu keLage (16gha)dalli kANabahudu. 
(16gha) jAnaki  maysUrininda  tandidda  A  sIre  Iga  haridu 
hOgide. 
I  vidhAnadalli  oLavAkyavAgi  baruva  (16ka)  vAkyada  kriyApadavannu 
(tandiddALe  embudannu)  adara  sambandhisuva  rUpakke  (tandidda  emba 
rUpakke)  badalAyisalAgide  mAtravalla,  adara  horavAkyadalliruva 
((16kha)dalliruva)  padakke  samanAgiruva  sIre(yannu)  emba  padavannu 
A vAkyadinda tegeduhAkalAgide. 
    vAkyavondannu  varNisuva  padakanteya  oLavAkyavannAgi  mADi 
baLasalu  kannaDadalli  innU  ondu  vidhAna  baLakeyallide.  idakkAgi  A 
vAkyada  koneyalli  emba  illavE  ennuva  emba  padavannu  sErisi 
hELabEku.  I  vidhAnavannu  kelavu  viSiSTavAda  sandabhragaLalli  mAtra 
baLasalu sAdhya embudannu munde (7.4.4)ralli nODaliruvevu.  
(17ka)  avanige haNa sikkilla. 
(17kha) A viSaya nanagU gottide. 
(17ga)  avanige haNa sikkillavemba A viSaya nanagU gottide. 
(17ka)  vAkyakke  emba  padavannu  sErisi  adannu  (17kha)  vAkyadalli 
bandiruva A viSaya emba padakanteya oLavAkyavannAgi mADi (17ga) 
vAkyavannu tayArisalAgide. 
    vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  kriyApadavannu  nAmapadavAgi  badalA 
yisuvudara mUlaka adannondu padakanteyannAgi mADalu sAdhyavide, 
mattu  I  rIti  badalAgiruva  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyada  oLavAkya 
vannAgi  mADi  baLasalu  sAdhyavide.  idallade,  oLavAkyada  koneyalli 
embudu  padavannu  irisi  adakkEnE  vibhakti  pratyayagaLannu  sErisi 
hELalU sAdhyavide. 
(18ka)  sItAdEvi hADiddALe. 
(18kha) sItAdEvi hADidudannu ellarU kELiddAre. 
(18ga)  sItAdEviya hADuvikeyannu ellarU kELiddAre. 
(18gha) sItAdEvi hADiddALembudannu ellarU kELiddAre. 
(18ka)  vAkyavannu  ondu  padakanteyannAgi  mADi  adannu  annu 
pratyayadondige (18kha) mattu (18ga) vAkyagaLalli baLasalAgide mattu 
(18gha) vAkyadalli A vAkyavannu hAgeyE uLisi adareduru embudu 
padavannu baLasalAgide embudannu gamanisabahudu. 
    idallade  vAkyada  koneya  kriyApadadeduru  alu  pratyayavannu 
sErisuvudara  mUlakavU  adannu  innondu  vAkyada  oLavAkyavannAgi 
badalAyisalu  sAdhyavide.  intaha  oLavAkyada  mUlaka  horavAkyavu 
sUcisuva ghaTaneya uddESavEnembudannu tiLisalu sAdhyavAguttade. 
(19ka)  sItAdEvi kacEriyalli hADuttALe. 
(19kha) kacEriyalli hADalu sItAdEvige kare bandide. 
    ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyada  illavE  adaralli  bandiruva 
padakanteya  oLavAkyavannAgi  mADalu  I  rIti  halavu  vidhAnagaLu 
kannaDadalli baLakeyalliddu, ivakkella bEre bEre uddESagaLive. Adare I 
ellA  vidhAnagaLigU  samAnavAgiruvantaha  ondu  uddESavU  ide. 
adEnendare,  I  ellA  vidhAnagaLU  gurutisabEkAgiruva  vyakti,  vastu, 
viSaya illavE ghaTaneyannu varNisi hELuvudakkAgi baLakeyAguttave.  
    oLavAkyavannu  I  rIti  vAkyada  anga  (ghaTaka)vannAgi  mADalu 
baLasuva  vidhAnagaLu  entahavu  embudannu  keLagina  aydu  (7.3.1-5) 
upavibhAgagaLallU,  mattu  padakanteya  angavannAgi  mADalu  baLasuva 
vidhAnagaLu  entahavu  embudannu  mundina  vibhAgada  nAlku  (7.4.1-
4) upavibhAgagaLallU vivarisalAguvudu. 
7.3.1 vAkyada angavAgi baLake 
mEle  sUcisidante,  vAkyavondannu  innondu  vAkyada  angavannAgi 
nAlku 
vidhAnagaLannu baLasalu sAdhyavide. 
mADabEkiddalli  adakkAgi 
padakanteyannAgi) 
    (1) embudu padavannu A vAkyakke sErisuvudu,  
    (2) udu pratyayavannu A vAkyada kriyArUpakke sErisuvudu, 
    (3) ike pratyayavannu A vAkyada kriyApadakke sErisuvudu, mattu 
    (4) alu pratyayavannu A vAkyada kriyApadakke sErisuvudu. 
ondu  ghaTane  naDedide  illavE  naDeyalide  emba  sangatiya  kuritAgi 
modalaneya  vidhAnavannU,  ghaTanege 
EnAdarU  hELabEkiddalli 
sambandhisida  vastu,  viSaya  modalAdavugaLa  kuritAgi  EnAdarU 
hELabEkAgiddalli eraDaneya vidhAnavannU mattu nEravAgi A ghaTaneya 
kuritAgi  (endare  adaralli  bandiruva  kriyeya  kuritAgi)  EnAdarU 
hELabEkiddalli mUraneya vidhAnavannU baLasalu sAdhyavide.  
    idallade,  ondu  ghaTane  innondu  ghaTaneya  uddESa  embudannu 
tiLisabEkiddalli  illavE  ondu  guNadharma  innondu  ghaTaneyadu 
embudannu  sUcisabEkAdalli  nAlkaneya  vidhAnavannu  baLasabahudu. 
idallade  eraDaneya  mattu  nAlkaneya  vidhAnagaLannu  modalaneya 
sandabhradallU baLasalu sAdhyavide. I bEre bEre sAdhyategaLannu keLagina 
vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu. 
(20ka)  avaLu hADuttALembudannu nAnu kELiddEne. 
(20kha)  avaLu hADidudannu nAnu kELiddEne.

(20gha)  avaLu hADuvudu nanage iSTa. 
(20Ga)  avaLige hADalu bahaLa iSTa. 
(20ka)  vAkyada  prakAra,  adara  ADuganu  kELiruvudu  avaLu  hADu 
ttALe emba sangatiyannu mAtra (modalaneya uddESa); idE artha 
dalli (20kha) vAkyavU baLakeyAgiralu sAdhyavide. Adare adakke `avaLu 
hADiddALe  emba  sangatiyannu  nAnu  kELiddEne'  emba  artha  mAtra 
vallade,  `avaLu  hADuva  ghaTaneyalli  nAnu  kELuganAgidde'  emba 
arthavU (endare eraDaneya uddESavU) baraballudu. (20ka) vAkyakke 
I artha baralAradu. 
     (20ga)  vAkyakke  I  eraDu  arthagaLigintalU  bhinnavAgiruva  artha 
vide.  illi  iSTavAgiruvudu  hADuva  ghaTaneyallade  hADuttALe  emba 
sangatiyalla  (mUraneya  uddESa).  eraDaneya  vidhAnavannu  baLasiruva 
(20gha) vAkya I (20ga) vAkyakkinta arthadalli bhinnavAgide embudannU 
gamanisabahudu.  adakke  `avaLu  hADuttALe  emba  sangati  nanage  iSTa' 
emba  arthavAgali  (endare  (20ka-kha)  vAkyagaLa  arthakke  samanAda 
arthavAgali)  illavE  `avaLu  hADuva  hADu  nanage  iSTa'  emba 
bErondu arthavAgali baralu sAdhyavide. 
    alu  pratyayada  baLake  halavu  viSayagaLalli  mElina  mUru 
vidhAnagaLiginta  bhinnavAgide  embudannu  munde  (7.3.3ralli)  nODa 
liruvevu.  uLida  vidhAnagaLa  mUlaka  tayArAda  padakante  ondu 
nAmapadada  hAge  baLakeyAguvudAdare  idu  ondu  kriyAguNapadada 
hAge  baLakeyAguttade.  hAgAgi  I  pratyayada  baLakeyannu  bEreyE 
ondu vibhAgadalli vivarisalAguvudu. 
7.3.2 nAmapadada jAgadalli baLake 
mEle  vivarisida  vidhAnagaLalli  modalaneya  mUru  vidhAnagaLannu 
baLasuvudara  mUlaka  ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyada  nAmapada 
vondara  jAgadalli  irisi  hELalu  sAdhyavAguttade.  mattu  idakkAgi  I 
vAkyagaLa koneyalli baruva embudu, udu mattu ike embavugaLige 
bEre bEre vibhakti pratyayagaLannu sErisalu sAdhyavAguttade. 
(21ka)  nIvu kaSTapaTTu illivarege bandiddIrembudarinda nimage I 
kelasadalli bahaLa Sraddheyideyembudu spaSTavAguttade. 
(21kha) nIvu illige baruvudakke yAra oppigeyU bEkAgilla. 
(21ga)  Atana kuNiyuvikeyalli utsAhavide. 
    ondu  vAkyakke  embudu  padavannu  sErisi  adannu  oLavAkyavannAgi 
mADi  baLasuva  modalaneya  vidhAnadalli  A  vAkyada  ellA  amSagaLU 
badalAgade  hAgeyE  uLidukoLLuttave.  Adare  eraDu  mattu 
mUraneya  vidhAnagaLannu  baLasuvAga  vAkyadalli  bEre  bEre  rItiya 
badalAvaNegaLannu mADikoLLabEkAguttade. illi udu pratyayada baLake 
yalli  kANisuvudakkintalU  ike  pratyayada  baLakeyalli  heccina  badalA 
vaNegaLu kANisikoLLuttave.  
    udu  pratyayavannu  baLasuvAga  vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  kriyA 
padadalli  mAtra  badalAvaNegaLannu  mADidare  sAku.  vAkyada  uLida 
bhAgagaLannella  avugaLalli  yAva  badalAvaNeyannU  mADade  hAgeyE 
uLisikoLLalu sAdhyavide.  
    kriyApadada koneyalli baruva ghaTakavannu sUcisuva pratyayavannu 
biTTukoDabEku embudu intaha badalAvaNegaLalli mukhyavAdudu. I 
badalAvaNeyindAgi, I pratyayada baLakeyalli kriyeyannu naDesidavaru 
yAru  embudannu  kriyApadada  mUlaka  sUkSmavAgi  tiLisihELalu 
sAdhyavAgadu. 
(22ka)  mUru ganTe hADiddAnembudu nanage gottAgalilla. 
(22kha) mUru ganTe hADiddALembudu nanage gottAgalilla. 
(22ga)  mUru ganTe hADidudu nanage gottAgalilla. 
embudu padada baLakeyiruva (22ka) mattu (22kha) vAkyagaLa naDuve 
kANisalu  sAdhyavAgiruva  vyatyAsavannu  (hADidudu  ganDasO  athavA 
hengasO  embudannu)  udu  pratyayada  baLakeyiruva  (22ga)dalli 
kANisalu sAdhyavAguvudilla embudannu gamanisabahudu. 
    allagaLeyuva  vAkyavondara  mUlaka  mAtanADuva  samayakkinta 
munde  naDeyuva  ghaTaneyannu  allagaLeyalAgideyO  athavA  hinde 
naDeda ghaTaneyannu allagaLeyalAgideyO embudannu sUcisalu eraDu 
rItiya  kriyArUpagaLu  baLakeyAguttave  (23ka-kha  nODi).  intaha 
kriyArUpagaLiruva  vAkyagaLannu  udu  pratyayada  mUlaka  oLavAkya 
gaLannAgi  badalAyisabEkiddalli,  A  pratyayavannu  hindina  ghaTaneyannu 
allagaLeyuva kriyApadakke nEravAgi sErisabahudu (idakkAgi kannaDadalli 
ondu  viSiSTavAda  kriyArUpa  baLakeyallide  embudannu  (23ga)dalli 
kANabahudu). 
(23ka)  Ata nALe hOguvudilla. 
(23kha) Ata ninne hOgalilla. 
(23ga)  Ata ninne hOgadudu yArigU samAdhAnavilla. 
Adare munde naDeyaliruva ghaTaneyondannu allagaLeyuva kriyApadakke 
I  rIti  udu  pratyayavannu  nEravAgi  sErisi  hELalu  sAdhyavAgadu. 
adakke badalu allagaLeyuva kriyApadada munde iru kriyApadavannirisi 
adakke udu pratyayavannu sErisabEkAguttade. 
(23gha) Ata nALe hOgadiruvudu yArigU samAdhAnavilla. 
idu embudu mattu udu emberaDu padagaLa baLakeyalli kANisuva 
innondu vyatyAsa. 
    ike  pratyayavannu  baLasi  oLavAkyavannu  tayArisuvudiddalli  antaha 
vAkyada  kriyApadadondige  baruva  ghaTakavannu  sUcisuva  pratyayavannu 
mAtravallade samayavannu sUcisuva pratyayavannU biTTu koDabEkAgu 
(24ka)  avanu holiyuvudu cannAgiruttade. 
(24kha) avanu holidudu cannAgittu. 
(24ga)  avana holiyuvike cannAgiruttade/cannAgittu. 
udu pratyayavannu baLasi racisida oLavAkyagaLalli mAtanADuva samaya 
kkinta  hinde  naDeda  mattu  munde  naDeyuva  ghaTanegaLa  naDuviruva 
vyatyAsavannu  uv  mattu  d  emba  samaya  pratyayagaLa  mUlaka 
sUcisalu  sAdhyavide  embudannu  (24ka-kha)  vAkyagaLalli  kANabahudu.

vAguvudilla embudannu (24ga)dalli kANabahudu. 
    eraDaneyadAgi,  ike  pratyayavannu  ondu  vAkyada  kriyApadakke

7.3.3 kriyAguNapadagaLa jAgadalli baLake 
mEle  sUcisiruva  hAge,  vAkyavondannu  alu  pratyayavannu  baLasi 
oLavAkyavannAgi  mADidalli  adannu  innondu  vAkyada  kriyAguNapadada 
jAgadalli baLasalu sAdhyavAguttade. sAmAnyavAgi intaha oLavAkyavannu 
horavAkyavu  sUcisuva  ghaTaneya  uddESavondannu  sUcisalu  baLasa 
lAguttade. 
(29ka)  bAgilannu tereyalu kAvalugAranannu kaLisiddAre. 
(29kha) bengaLUrige hOgalu avanu ivattu bEga eddiddAne. 
    alu pratyayakke ondu ghaTaneyannu nEravAgi sUcisuva arthavU 
baraballudu  illavE  A  ghaTane  naDedide  athavA  naDeyalide  emba 
sangatiyannu  sUcisuva  arthavU  baraballudu.  I  viSayadalli  adu 
udu pratyayada hAgeyE baLakeyAguttade.  
(30ka)  Akege manege hOgalu maretide. 
(30kha)  Akege kAru biDalu maretide. 
(30ka) vAkyada prakAra Akege maretiruvudu `manege hOgabEku' emba 
sangati;  Adare  (30kha)  vAkyada  prakAra  Akege  maretiruvudu  `kArannu 
hEge  biDuvudu'  embudAgi  adannu  biDuva  vidhAna.  Adare  (30kha) 
vAkyakke  modalaneya  vAkyada  arthakke  samanAgiruva  arthavU  baralu 
sAdhyavide. 
    alu  pratyayavannu  baLasi  racisida  oLavAkya  bErondu  vAkyada 
(adara horavAkyada) kriyAguNapadada jAgadalli ( endare, kriyApadada 
`viSESaNa'vAgi)  baruvudallade  nAmapadakanteyAgi  baruvudilla.  I 
kAraNakkAgi,  antaha  vAkyakke  udu  pratyayavannu  baLasi  racisida 
oLavAkyada hAge vibhakti pratyayagaLannu sErisalu sAdhyavAguvudilla. 
    idallade,  oLavAkya  mattu  horavAkyagaLeraDU  mADuganemba 
ghaTakavannoLagonDiveyAdalli  antaha  ghaTaka  eraDarallU  obbanE 
vyaktiyannu  sUcisuttirabEkemba  innondu  niyamavU  alu  pratyayada 
kANisikoLLuttade.  udu  illavE  ike  pratyayagaLa 
baLakeyalli 
baLakeyalli I niyamavilla. I kAraNakkAgi rAmu akki taralu sIte 
aDuge  mADidaLu  embantaha  vAkyagaLu  kannaDadalli  aSTondu 
oppigeyAguvu dilla. 
    alu  pratyayavannu  baLasi  tayArisida  oLavAkyagaLu  innondu 
viSayadallU  itara  oLavAkyagaLinda  bhinnavAgive.  avu  sAmAnyavAgi 
horavAkyavu  tiLisuva  ghaTaneya  anantara  naDeyuva  (illavE  naDeya 
bEkAgiruva)  ghaTaneyondannu  sUcisuttave.  I  kAraNakkAgi  avu 
toDagu,  surumADu  embantaha  kriyApadagaLiruva  horavAkyagaLalli 
baraballuvu,  Adare  munduvarisu,  nillisu,  mugisu  embantaha 
kriyApadagaLiruva horavAkyagaLalli baralAravu. 
    ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyadondige  jODisabEkAgiruva 
sandabhradallU  alu  pratyayavannu  baLasalu  sAdhya  embudannu  nAvu 
mundina  (enTanE)  adhyAyadalli  nODaliruvevu.  ondu  ghaTane 
innondu ghaTaneya anantara naDeyuvantahadu embudannu sUcisuvu 
dakkAgi  I  pratyayada  baLakeyAguttade.  I  baLakegU  mattu  mEle 
vivarisiruva oLavAkyada baLakegU naDuve hattirada sambandhaviddu halavu 
sandabhragaLalli iveraDu baLakegaLalli yAvudu kANisikoLLuttide embu 
dannu nirdharisuvudu kaSTavAgi tOralu sAdhyavide. 
7.3.4 horavAkyada kriyApadagaLu 
vAkyavondannu  innondu  vAkyada  angavannAgi  mADalu  (endare  pada 
kanteyannAgi  baLasalu  illavE  kriyAguNapadada  jAgadalli  baLasalu) 
kannadadalli  nAlku  vidhAnagaLive  embudannu  nAvu  mEle  nODiruvevu. 
idallade, I nAlku vidhAnagaLa baLake bEre bEre sandabhragaLalli bEre 
bEre  rItiya  arthagaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  naDeyuvudembudannU 
nODiruvevu.  intaha  vAkyarUpada  vAkyAngagaLu  yAva  rItiya 
horavAkyagaLallella baraballuvu embudarallU kelavu nibrandhagaLive. 
    mEle mUru mattu nAlkanE adhyAyagaLalli pariSIlisiruva kriyA 
vAkya  mattu  viSayavAkyagaLigU  mattu  I  rIti  oLavAkyavondannu 
ghaTakavannAgi  paDediruva  (hora)vAkyagaLigU  naDuve  halakelavu  vyatyAsa 
gaLive.  udAharaNegAgi,  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  baruva  kriyApadagaLalli 
kelavE  kelavu  mAtra  intaha  horavAkyagaLalli  kriyApadagaLAgi  bara 
balluvu.  idakke  kAraNavEnendare,  ondu  vAkyavu  tiLisuva  sangati 
illavE  ghaTaneyannu  ghaTakavannAgi  paDeyaballa  kriyegaLu  kelavE  kelavu 
mAtra. 
(31ka)  pETeyinda baruva jAnakiyannu rAju nODiddAne. 
(31kha) jAnaki pETeyinda baruvudannu rAju nODiddAne. 
(31ka)  vAkyada  prakAra  rAju  nODiruvudu  jAnakiyannu,  endare 
obba  vyaktiyannu;  Adare  (31kha)  vAkyada  prakAra  Ata  nODiruvudu 
jAnaki  baruvudannu,  endare  ondu  ghaTaneyannu.  (31ka)  vAkyadalli 
nODu  kriyApada  pETe  emba  ondu  jAgavannU  mattu  jAnaki 
mattu  rAju  emba  eraDu  vyaktigaLannU  ghaTakagaLAgi  paDedide.  Adare 
(31kha)  vAkya  dalli  adE  kriyApada  jAnaki  pETeyinda  baruvudu 
emba oLavAkya sUcisuva ghaTaneyannU mattu rAju emba vyaktiyannU 
ghaTakavAgi paDedide.   
    kannaDadalli kELu, nODu, biDu, mare, hogaLu, kANu, nillu, 
nambu, hedaru, nene, tegaLu modalAda kelavE kelavu kriyApadagaLu 
mAtra  I  rIti  vyakti,  vastu,  jAga  modalAdavugaLannu  mAtravallade 
ghaTane illavE sangatigaLannU ghaTakagaLannAgi paDeyaballuvu. 
(32ka)  Ata sItAbAyiyannu hogaLuttiddAne. 
(32kha) Ata sItAbAyi hADuvudannu hogaLuttiddAne. 
(33ka)  Ake ramESanannu maretiddALe.

ddALe. 
(34ka)  rAju huDuganannu varAnDadalli nillisiddAne. 
(34kha) rAju kate bareyuvudannu nillisiddAne. 
(32ka)  vAkyadalli  hogaLu  kriyApada  ibbaru  vyaktigaLannu  ghaTakavAgi 
paDedideyAdare,  (32kha)  vAkyadalli  adE  kriyApada  ondu  ghaTane 
yannu (sItAbAyi hADuvudu embudannu) mattu obba vyaktiyannu 
ghaTakavAgi  paDedide.  (33ka)  vAkyadalli  mare  kriyApada  ibbaru  vyakti 
gaLannu ghaTakavAgi paDedideyAdare, (33kha) vAkyadalli adE kriyApada 
ondu  sangatiyannu  (tanage  ramESa  sahAya  mADiddanemba  sangati 
yannu) mattu obba vyaktiyannu ghaTakavAgi paDedide. 
    udu pratyayavannu baLasi tayArisida oLavAkya mAtra I viSaya 
dalli  itara  oLavAkyagaLinda  bhinnavAgide.  adu  ondu  ghaTane  illavE 
sangatiyannu  sUcisuva  badalu  ondu  vastuvannU  sUcisalu  sAdhya 
viddu, I arthadalli adu ellA rItiya kriyApadagaLondigU ghaTaka 
vAgi baraballudu.

7.3.5 horavAkyavAgi viSayavAkyagaLa baLake 
kriyAvAkyagaLa  hAgeyE  viSayavAkyagaLU  oLavAkyavondannu  ghaTaka 
vannAgi  paDediralu  sAdhya.  intaha  horavAkyagaLu  jAga,  guNadharma 
illavE  sambandhavannu  sUcisuttiralu  sAdhyavideyembudannu  anukrama 
vAgi (39ka-ga) vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu.

(39kha) rAju ivattu baruvudu samSaya. 
(39ga)  illi kuLitare yArigU kANalikkillavendu avanige bhrame. 
    guNadharmavannu  sUcisuva  horavAkyagaLu  ghaTaneyannu  illavE

7.4 padakanteya angavAgi baLake 
vAkyavondannu  innondu  vAkyadalli  baruva  ondu  padakanteya  anga 
vannAgi mADi baLasalu kannaDadalli nAlku vidhAnagaLive.   
    (1)  A vAkyada kriyApadakke O pratyayavannu sErisi baLasuvudu, 
    (2)  adakkEnE  O  pratyayada  badalu  a  pratyayavannu  sErisi 
baLasuvudu, mattu 
    (3)  A vAkyada ghaTakagaLige a pratyayavannu sErisi baLasuvudu. 
    (4)  vAkyada  koneyalli  emba  illavE  ennuva  padavannu  sErisi 
baLasuvudu. 
I nAlku vidhAnagaLa baLakeyannu keLagina vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu. 
(41ka)  jAnaki maysUrininda ondu sIre tandiddaLu.

ivugaLa  baLakeyannu  (42ka-ga)  vAkyagaLalli  kANabahudu.  (41ka)

(42kha)dalli  kANisuva  oLavAkyavannU,  mattu  A  vAkyada  eraDu 
ghaTakagaLige  nEravAgi  idE  a  pratyayavannu  sErisuvudara  mUlaka 
(42ga)dalli kANisuva oLavAkyavannU tayArisalAgide. 
    nAlkaneya  vidhAnada  baLakeyannu  (43ka-ga)  vAkyagaLalli  kANa 
bahudu. illi bandiruva (43ka) vAkyakke emba padavannu sErisuvudara

padakanteya oLavAkyavannAgi mADi (43ga) vAkyavannu tayArisalAgide.   
    I  oLavAkyagaLa  racaneyalli  bEreyU  kelavu  badalAvaNegaLannu 
mADikoLLabEkAguttade  embudannu  gamanisabahudu.  udAharaNegAgi,

baruva ondu ghaTakakke yAva emba padavannU sErisikoLLabEkAguttade 
((42ka) nODi).  
    idakke  badalu,  oLavAkyada  kriyApadakke  a  pratyayavannu  sErisuvu 
diddalli,  adara  ghaTakagaLallondannu  (ondu  sIre  embudannu)  biTTu 
koDabEkAguttade  embudannu  (42kha)dalli  kANabahudu.  a  pratyaya 
vannu  nEravAgi  oLavAkyada  ghaTakagaLige  sErisuvudiddallU  I  rIti 
ghaTaka  gaLallondannu  biTTukoDabEkAguttade.  Adare  idarondige  A 
embudannU) 
vAkyada 
biTTukoDabEkAguttade embudannu (42ga)dalli kANabahudu.  
    emba  illavE  ennuva  padavannu  baLasuvalli  mAtra  oLavAkyavAgi 
baruva vAkyadalli yAva badalAvaNeyannU mADabEkAguvudilla. Adare

7.4.1 O pratyayada baLake 
I  vidhAnavannu  baLasuvudiddalli  oLavAkyavAgi  baruva  vAkyada  ellA 
amSagaLU  badalAgade  heccukaDime  hAgeyE  uLidukoLLuttave.  A 
vAkyada  koneyalli  O  pratyayavannu  sErisuvudu  mattu  adara  ghaTaka 
vondakke  aniScita  savrapadavondannu  sErisuvudu  emba  eraDu 
badalAvaNegaLu mAtra I vAkyadalli naDeyuttave.  
(44ka)  huDuga ivattu SAlege hOgalilla. 
(44kha) A huDuganige cAkalETilla. 
(44ga)  yAva  huDuga  ivattu  SAlege  hOgalillavO  A 
huDuganige cAkalETilla. 
(44ka)  vAkyavannu  (44kha)dalli  bandiruva  A  huDuganige  emba  pada 
kanteya  oLavAkyavannAgi  mADi  (44ga)  vAkyavannu  tayArisalAgide. 
idakkAgi  (44ka)  vAkyada  koneyalli  O  pratyayavannu  sErisalAgide 
mattu  adaralli  bandiruva  huDuga  padadeduru  yAva  emba  aniScita 
savrapadavannu baLasalAgide.  
    vAkyavondara  mUlaka  gurutisabEkAguva  vyakti,  vastu,  viSaya 
modalAdavugaLalli  ondara  kuritAgi  heccina  mAhitiyannu  koDuvu 
dakkAgi  I  rIti  antaha  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu  gurutisuva 
padakanteyalli ondu  oLavAkyavannirisuttEve. mEle (44kha) vAkyadalli 
A  huDuga  emba  padakante  obba  vyaktiyannu  gurutisuttade.  Atana 
kuritAgi heccina mAhitiyannu koDuvudakkAgi (44ga) vAkyadalli (44ka) 
vAkyavannu A huDuga emba padakanteya oLavAkyavannAgi mADalAgide. 
    I  vidhAnada  baLakeyalli  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu  gurutisuva 
pada  illavE  padakante  eraDu  bAri  baruttade.  omme  oLavAkyadalli 
mattu innomme adannu oLavAkyavAgi paDediruva padakanteyalli. mEle 
(44ga) vAkyadalli A huDuga emba padakante eraDu bAri bandiruvu 
dannu  gamanisabahudu.  sAmAnyavAgi  I  rIti    ondE  pada  illavE 
padakanteyannu  eraDu  bAri  baLasuva  badalu  eraDaneya  salakke  savra 
padavondannu baLasuvudu rUDhi. 
(44gha) yAva  huDuga  ivattu  SAlege  hOgalillavO  Atanige 
cAkalETilla. 
    ondu  padakanteyalli  ondakkinta  jAsti  oLavAkyagaLannu  baLasalu 
sAdhyaviddu,  idakkAgi  A  vAkyagaLannu  mattu,  illavE,  athavA  moda 
lAda padagaLa mUlaka bEpraDisuva avaSyakateyide.
