7.4.2 kriyApadakke a pratyayavannu sErisuvudu 
vAkyavondannu innondu vAkyadalli bandiruva padakanteya angavannAgi 
mADalu  nAvu  baLasabahudAda  eraDaneya  vidhAnavEnendare,  adara 
kriyApadakke  a  pratyayavannu  sErisuvudu.  kannaDada  kriyApadagaLu  I 
pratyayadondige mUru rUpagaLalli baraballuvu, mattu I rUpagaLu 
hindina  samayada  ghaTane,  mundina  samayada  ghaTane  mattu  allagaLe 
yuva ghaTanegaLemba mUru rItiya ghaTanegaLannu sUcisaballuvu. 
(47ka)  ivattu SAlege hOda huDugarige cAkalET sikkide. 
(47kha) nALe SAlege hOguva huDugarige cAkalET siguttade. 
(47ga)  ivattu SAlege hOgada huDugarige cAkalET sigalilla. 
(47ka)da  oLavAkyadalli  hOda  kriyArUpa  bandiddu  adu  mAta 
nADuva  samayakkinta  hindina  samayadalli  naDeda  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisu 
ttade.  idakke  badalu,  (47kha)da  oLavAkyadalli  hOguva  emba  kriyA 
rUpa  bandiddu,  adu  mAtanADuva  samayada  anantara  naDeyaliruva 
mundina  samayada  ghaTaneyannu  sUcisuttade.  (47ga)da  oLavAkyadalli 
iveraDakkintalU bhinnavAda hOgada emba kriyArUpa bandiddu, idu 
naDeyada ghaTaneyondannu sUcisuttade.   
    allagaLeyuva  vAkyagaLannu  I  rIti  oLavAkyagaLannAgi  mADi 
baLasuvudiddalli,  avu  hindina  ghaTaneyondannu  allagaLeyuttiveyE 
athavA  mundina  ghaTaneyondannu  allagaLeyuttiveyE  emba  viSaya 
dalli samSayavunTAgalu sAdhyavide. I eraDu sandabhragaLallU intaha 
oLavAkyagaLalli  kriyApadakkiruva  rUpa  ondE  embudE  I  rIti 
samSayavunTAgalu  kAraNa.  udAharaNegAgi  mEle  (47ga)  vAkyadalli 
bandiruva  SAlege  hOgada  emba  oLavAkyavannu  I  huDugaru 
SAlege hOgalilla emba vAkyadinda tayArisirabEku.  
    Adare keLage koTTiruva (47gha) vAkyadalli bandiruva adE rUpada 
oLavAkyavannu  I  huDugaru  (nALe)  SAlege  hOguvudilla  emba 
bErondu vAkyadinda tayArisiralu sAdhyavide. 
(47gha) nALe SAlege hOgada huDugarige cAkalET sigalikkilla. 
    keLage  koTTiruva  (47Ga)  vAkyakke  I  eraDu  rItiya  arthagaLU 
baraballuvembudannu gamanisabahudu.  
(47Ga) SAlege hOgada huDuganige cAkalET koDabAradu. 
SAlege  hOgada  huDuganige  emba 
(47Ga)dalli  bandiruva 
padagucchakke  `yAva  huDuganu  SAlege  hOgalillavO  Atanige'  emba 
artha  baralu  sAdhyaviddu  adaralliruva  oLavAkya  `huDuga  SAlege

sAdhyavide,  illavE  `yAva  huDuganu  SAlege  hOguvudillavO 
Atanige' emba artha viralu sAdhyaviddu adE oLavAkya `huDuga SAlege 
ghaTaneyondannu 
hOguvudilla' 
allagaLeyuttiralU sAdhyavide.  
    Adare  sAmAnyavAgi  vAkyavannu  baLasuva  sandabhravE  ondu 
oLavAkyada  nijavAda  artha  yAvudu  embudannu  nirdharisuvalli 
sahAyakavAguttade. 
    I  vidhAnada  mUlaka  ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyadalliruva 
padakanteyondara  oLavAkyavannAgi  mADi  baLasuvAga,  A  padakantege 
mundina 
samanAgiruva  padakanteyannu  oLavAkyadinda  tegeduhAkabEkAguttade. 
udAharaNegAgi  mEle  (47ka)  vAkyadalli  bandiruva  ivattu  SAlege 
hOda  emba  oLavAkya  I  huDugaru  ivattu  SAlege  hOdaru 
emba vAkyada viSESaNa rUpavendu hELabahudu. adannu tayArisuvu 
dakkAgi  I  vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  kriyApadakke  a  pratyayavannu 
sErisi  adannu  hOda  embudAgi  badalAyisalAgide  mattu  adaralli 
bandiruva  I  huDugaru  emba  padakanteyannu  tegeduhAkalAgide 
embudannu gamanisabahudu. 
    I rIti mElina vidhAnavannu baLasidAga oLavAkyagaLalliruva ghaTaka 
gaLalli ondu bidduhOguvudAdarU A ghaTaka horavAkyadallU (oLa 
vAkyada  viSESyavAgi)  baruvudAda  kAraNa  biddu  hOgiruva  ghaTaka 
yAvudembudannu tiLidukoLLalu kaSTavAguvudilla. Adare, oLavAkyadalli 
adu  entaha  ghaTakavAgittu  embudannu  tiLiyuvudu  kelavu  sandabhra 
gaLalli svalpa kaSTavAguttade. udAharaNegAgi keLagina vAkyagaLannu gamanisa 
bahudu. 
(48ka)  ninne mAtanADisida muduka ivattu sattu hOgiddAne.

mundiruva  annu  vibhakti  pratyayavannU  biTTukoDabEkAguvudarinda

nAnu  mattu  nannannu  emba  padagaLannU  oLavAkyadalli  baLasidevAdare

7.4.3 vAkyada ghaTakagaLige a pratyayavannu sErisuvudu 
vAkyavondaralli  baruva  ghaTakagaLalli  pratiyondakkU  a  pratyayavannu 
sErisuvudara mUlaka adannu padakanteyondara oLavAkyavannAgi mADi 
baLasuvudu  mUraneya  vidhAna.  I  vidhAnadalli  oLavAkyada  kriyApada 
bidduhOguttade,  mattu  adara  padakantegaLondige  baruva  vibhakti 
pratyayagaLU bidduhOguttave. 
(54ka)  kaLeda vAra avaru maysUrinalli bhASaNa mADiddaru. 
(54kha) (A) bhASaNa cannAgiralilla. 
(54ga)  kaLeda vArada avara maysUrina (A) bhASaNa cannAgiralilla.
(54ka) vAkyavannu (54kha)dalli bandiruva A bhASaNa emba padakantege 
oLavAkyavannAgi  mADi  (54ga)  vAkyavannu  tayArisalAgide.  mattu 
idakkAgi (54ka) vAkyada bhASaNa emba ghaTakavannU mattu mADiddaru 
emba  kriyArUpavannU  biTTukoDalAgide,  idallade  (54ka)  vAkyada 
uLida mUru ghaTakagaLige (kaLeda vAra, avaru mattu maysUrinalli 
embavugaLige) a pratyayavannu sErisalAgide.  
    I  rIti  ghaTakagaLige  a  pratyayavannu  sErisuvAga  avugaLa  munde 
vibhakti  pratyayagaLiddalli  avu  bidduhOguttave.  mElina  udAharaNe 
yalli  maysUru  padada  mundidda  alli  emba  vibhakti  pratyaya  biddu 
hOgiruvudannu  kANabahudu.  keLagina  udAharaNeyalli  ige  mattu 
alli emba eraDu pratyayagaLU bidduhOgive. 
(55ka)  rAmuvige nATakadalli ondu bahumAna sikkide. 
(55kha) rAmuvina nATakada bahumAna kaLeduhOgide. 
7.4.4 emba illavE ennuva padagaLa baLake 
vAkyavondannu  padakanteya  angavannAgi  mADuvudakkAgi  baLasida 
mElina  mUru  vidhAnagaLallU  A  vAkyadalli  bEre  bEre  rItiya 
badalAvaNegaLannu mADabEkAgittade. idallade I ellA vidhAnagaLallU 
oLavAkya  mattu  horavAkyagaLa  naDuve  ondu  padada  maTTigAdarU 
samAnateyiddE irabEkemba niyamavide. 
    emba  illavE  ennuva  padavannu  baLasi  naDesuva  I  nAlkaneya 
vidhAnadalli  oLavAkyavAgi  baruva  vAkyadalli  yAva  badalAvaNeyannU 
mADabEkAguvudilla.  Adare  I  vidhAnavannu  kelavE  kelavu  sandabhra 
gaLalli  mAtra  baLasalu  sAdhyavide.  illi  viSESyavAgi  viSaya,  suddi, 
sangati, vicAra, modalAda kelavE kelavu padagaLu mAtra baraballuvu. 
(56ka)  avaLu  bAvige  hAriyALemba  sangatiyannu  yArU 
Uhi siralilla. 
(56kha) nALe mantrigaLu baruttAremba suddi elleDegU haraDide. 
    viSESyavAgi ondu nAmapadavannu baLasuva badalu emba padavannE 
adakke  udu  pratyayavannu  sErisuvudara  mUlaka  nAmapadavAgi 
badalAyisikoLLalu  sAdhyavide.  I  sAdhyateyannu  mEle  (7.3.2)ralli 
nODiruvevu. idannE keLagina vAkyagaLallU kANabahudu. 
bAvige

Uhisiralilla.

(57ga)  nIvillige bandiruvirembudu bahaLa guTTina viSaya.

7.5 sArAmSa 
ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyada  oLavAkyavannAgi  mADi  baLasalu 
bEre  bEre  vidhAnagaLu  baLakeyalliddu  ivugaLalli  yAvudannu  elli 
baLasabEku  embudu  ivannu  yAva  uddESakkAgi  baLasabEkAgide 
embudara mEle avalambiside. 
    innobbana mAtu illavE abhiprAyavannu etti hELuvudu intaha 
uddESagaLalli  ondu.  I  uddESavannu  sAdhisuvudakkAgi,  endu 
padavannu (illavE O pratyayavannu) A mAtige illavE A abhiprAya 
vannu  sUcisuva  vAkyakke  sErisi  adannu  bErondu  vAkyada  oLavAkya 
vannAgi  mADabahudu.  idakke  badalu,  A  vAkyakke  ante  pratyayavannu 
sErisuvudara mUlaka adannu hAgeyE baLasalU sAdhyavide. 
    oLavAkyavannu  tayArisuva  itara  vidhAnagaLannella  vyakti,  vastu, 
viSaya,  ghaTane  modalAdavugaLannu  varNisuvudakkAgi  baLasalAguttade. 
illi  mukhyavAgi  eraDu  rItiya  vidhAnagaLu  baLakeyAguttave.  ondu 
vAkyavannu innondu vAkyada angavannAgi mADi baLasuvudu ivugaLalli 
ondu  rItiya  vidhAna,  mattu  ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyadalli 
baruva  ghaTakada  angavannAgi  mADi  baLasuvudu  innondu  rItiya 
vidhAna. 
    ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyada  angavannAgi  mADalu  vAkyakke 
embudu  padavannu  sErisuvudu,  mattu  vAkyada  koneya  kriyApadakke 
udu,  ike  mattu  alu  emba  pratyayagaLallondannu  sErisuvudu 
embudAgi nAlku vidhAnagaLu baLakeyallive.  
    ondu  vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyadalli  bandiruva  padakanteya 
angavannAgi  mADalu  A  vAkyakke  emba  padavannu  sErisuvudu,  A 
vAkyada  kriyApadakke  O  mattu  a  pratyayagaLallondannu  sErisuvudu 
mattu  A  vAkyada  ghaTakagaLalli  pratiyondakkU  a  pratyayavannu  sErisu 
vudu  embudAgi  nAlku  vidhAnagaLu  baLakeyallive.  I  vidhAnagaLannu 
baLasidAga vAkyadalli bEreyU halavu badalAvaNegaLu naDeyuttave. I 
vidhAnagaLigella bEre bEre uddESagaLive.

adhyAya enTu 
vAkyagaLa jODaNe 
8.1 pIThike 
ondakkondu  sambandhisiruva  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  oTTige  jODisi 
hELalu kannaDadalli mUru vidhAnagaLu baLakeyallive.  
(1)  mattu,  illavE,  Adare  modalAda  padagaLallondannu 
baLasi jODisuvudu, 
(2) U illavE O pratyayavannu baLasi jODisuvudu, mattu 
(3)  vAkyagaLa  koneyalli  bandiruva  kriyApadadalli  kelavu 
badalAvaNegaLannu mADi jODisuvudu. 
I  mUru  vidhAnagaLa  baLakeyannu  keLagina  mUru  vAkyagaLalli  kANa 
bahudu. 
(1ka)  doDDa kOti mancada mEle kuLitide mattu cikka kOti 
bAgilina baLi kuLitide. 
(1kha)  doDDa  kOti  mancada  mElU  mattu  cikka  kOti 
bAgilina baLiyU kuLitive. 
(1ga)  doDDa  kOti  mancada  mEle  kuLitu  cikka  kOtiyannu 
aNakisuttide. 
(1ka)  vAkyadalli  mattu  padavannu  baLasuvudara  mUlaka  eraDu  vAkya 
gaLannu  jODisalAgide.  ivE  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  (1kha)dalli  U 
pratyayavannu baLasuvudara mUlaka jODisalAgide. (1ga)dalli ivakkinta 
svalpa  bhinnavAgiruva  vAkyagaLeraDannu  avugaLalli  modalaneya  vAkyada 
kriyApadavannu  adara  `jODisuva  rUpa'kke  badalAyisi  jODisa 
    mattu  padavannu  baLasade  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  ondara  anantara 
ondarante irisi hELidarU adE artha baralu sAdhyavide. 
(2ka)  doDDa  kOti  mancada  mEle  kuLitide,  cikkadu  bAgilina 
baLi nintide. 
(2kha)  avara  maga  mumbayige  hOda,  magaLu  cennayge 
hOdaLu. 
8.1.1 jODaNeyalli vAkyagaLu mattu vAkyAngagaLu 
I  mUru  vidhAnagaLa  mUlaka  vAkyagaLeraDannu  jODisuva  badalu 
ondu  vAkyadallEnE  eraDu  pada  illavE  padakantegaLannu  jODisalu 
sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi keLagina vAkyagaLannu gamanisabahudu. 
ramESa  mattu SrIpati geLeyaru. 
(3kha)  nAyiyU bekkU jagaLADikoLLuttive. 
rAjuvina  tammanU  avana  geLeyanU  ondE  divasa 
mumbayige hOdaru. 
(3gha)  tannallidda  haNavannella  Ata  rAjuvigU  mattu  harigU 
mElina  vAkyagaLalli  mattu  mattu  U  embavugaLa  baLakeyAgide 
yAdarU  avugaLalli  yAvudannU  eraDu  vAkyagaLa  jODaNeyinda 
tayArisalAgideyendu  hELalu  sAdhyavAgadu.  udAharaNegAgi,  (3ka) 
vAkyadalli mattu padavannu baLasalAgide. Adare, A vAkyavannu ramESa 
geLeya mattu SrIpati geLeya emba eraDu vAkyagaLa jODaNeyinda 
tayArisalAgideyendu  hELidalli,  adakkiruva  `ramESa  SrIpatiya 
geLeya'  emba  arthavAgalI  illavE  `SrIpati  ramESana  geLeya'  emba 
arthavAgalI baralAradu. itara vAkyagaLallU hIgeyE. 
    eraDu nAmapadagaLannu I rIti mattu pada illavE U pratyaya 
vannu  baLasadeyU  jODisalu  sAdhyavide.  Adare  intaha  jODaNege 
mElinadakkinta  svalpa  bhinnavAda  arthavide.  udAharaNegAgi,  tande 
tAyi,  aNNa  tamma,  atte  sose  modalAda  nanTastikeyannu 
sUcisuva  padagaLa  jODaNeyalli  mattu  illavE  U  embavugaLa 
baLakeyilla.  idE  rItiyalli  ele  aDike,  mEju  kucri,  hAlu 
mosaru,  modalAda  hattirada  sambandhagaLannu  sUcisuva  padagaLa 
jODaNeyallU avugaLa baLakeyilla.  
    kelavu sandabhragaLalli ondu vAkyavannu eraDu vAkyagaLa jODaNe 
yinda  tayArisalAgideyO  athavA  eraDu  pada  illavE  padakantegaLa 
jODaNeyinda  tayArisalAgideyO  emba  viSayadalli  samSaya 
vunTAgalu  sAdhyavide.  idallade,  ondE  vAkyakke  I  eraDu  rItiya 
jODaNegaLU  kAraNavAgiralu  sAdhyaviddu  adarindAgi  A  vAkyakke 
eraDu rItiya arthagaLu baralU sAdhyavide. 
(4ka)  barahagAraru 
mattu 
kANalu hOgiddAre. 
prakASakaru

kANalu hOgiddAre. 
(4ka) vAkyavannu (4kha) mattu (4ga) vAkyagaLa jODaNeyinda tayAri 
siralu  sAdhyavideyEnO  nija.  Adare,  adannE  (4gha)  vAkyada  artha

bEkiddalli,  adannu  ((4ka)  vAkyavannu)  eraDu  padagaLa  jODaNeyinda 
mAtravE tayArisiralu sAdhya. 
8.1.2 jODisida vAkya mattu oLavAkya 
ondu vAkyadalli eraDu vAkyagaLannu jODisalAgideyE athavA ondu 
vAkyavannu  innondu  vAkyada  oLavAkyavAgi  baLasalAgideyE  emba 
viSayadallU  samSayavunTAgalu  sAdhyavide.  udAharaNegAgi  keLagina 
eraDu vAkyagaLannu gamanisabahudu. 
(5ka)  avanu rAjuvannu UTakke kareyalu bandiddAne. 
(5kha)  avanige rAjuvannu UTakke kareyalu maretide. 
(5ka)dalli eraDu vAkyagaLannu jODisalAgiddu, avu sUcisuva ghaTane 
gaLalli  modalaneyadu  eraDaneyadara  anantara  jaraguvudembudAgi 
alu  pratyayada  mUlaka  sUcisalAgide  (8.3.2  nODi).  Adare 
(5kha)dalli  modalaneya  vAkya  eraDaneya  vAkya  sUcisuva  ghaTaneya 
ondu  ghaTakavAgi  bandiddu,  adu  A  vAkyada  oLavAkyavAgide  (7.3.3 
nODi). 
    I  rIti  alu  pratyayada  baLakeyalli  mAtravallade,  kriyApadagaLa 
itara  jODaNeya  rUpagaLa  baLakeyallU  intaha  samSayagaLu  baralu 
sAdhyavide.  oTTige  bandiruva  eraDu  vAkyagaLa  naDuve  entaha  sambandha 
vide  embudannu  pariSIlisuvudara  mUlaka  intaha  samSayagaLannu 
hOgalADisabahudu. 
8.2 jODaNeya niyamagaLu 
mEle vivarisiruva mUru vidhAnagaLalli yAvudannu elli baLasabahudu 
emba  viSayadalli,  mattu  A  vidhAnagaLannu  baLasidAga  vAkyagaLalli 
entaha badalAvaNegaLannella naDesabEkAguttade emba viSayadalli kelavu 
niyamagaLannu  anusarisabEkAguttade.  intaha  niyamagaLu  yAvuvu 
mattu  mElina  mUru  vidhAnagaLa  baLakeyalli  avu  hEge  kANisi 
koLLuttave embudannu keLagina vibhAgagaLalli vivarisalAgide. 
8.2.1 ondE kriyApadada baLake 
pratyayagaLa  mUlaka  kriyAvAkyagaLannu  jODisabEkiddalli,  avugaLalli 
baruva kriyApada ondE AgirabEkemba niyamavide. Adare pada illavE 
kriyArUpagaLa  mUlaka  jODisabEkiddalli,  I  kriyApadagaLu  bEre 
bErAgiddarU tondareyilla.  
    pratyayagaLa  baLakeyalli  I  niyama  kANisikoLLalu  mukhya  kAraNa 
vEnendare,  avugaLa  mUlaka  vAkyagaLeraDannu  jODisuvAga  avugaLa 
kriyApadagaLannu  oTTu  sErisi  jODaNeya  horage  irisabEkAguttade, 
mattu idakkAgi A eraDu vAkyagaLallU ondE kriyApada bandiruvudu 
avaSya. eraDaneya vidhAnakkU mattu uLida eraDu vidhAnagaLigU naDu 
viruva I vyatyAsavannu keLagina udAharaNegaLalli kANabahudu. 
rAju nALe Dellige hOguttAne.

spaSTapaDisuttave.

8.2.2 jODisuva pada illavE pratyayagaLa jAga 
eraDaneya  vidhAnakkU  mattu  uLida  vidhAnagaLigU  naDuviruva 
innondu  vyatyAsavannU  nAvu  mEleyE  nODiruvevu.  eraDaneya 
vidhAnadalli  baLakeyAguva  U,  O  modalAda  pratyayagaLannu  eraDu 
vAkyagaLigU  sErisabEkAguttade,  Adare  modalaneya  vidhAnadalli 
baLakeyAguva  mattu,  illavE  modalAda  padagaLannu  ondu  bAri 
mAtra, eraDu vAkyagaLa naDuvinalli irisidare sAku.  
    mUraneya  vidhAnadalli  baLakeyAguva  `jODisuva'  kriyArUpa 
vannU  idE  rItiyalli  ondu  bAri  mAtra  (modalaneya  vAkyada 
koneyalli mAtra) baLasidare sAku. 
(11ka)  avaLu  SAlege  hOgiddaLu  mattu  nAnu  pETege 
hOgidde. 
(11kha) avaLu SAlegU nAnu pETegU hOgiddevu. 
(11ga)  avaLu SAlege hOgi (allinda) pETege hOgiddaLu. 
(11ka)dalli  mattu  padannu  ondu  bAri  mAtra  baLasalAgide,  mattu 
idE  rItiyalli  (11ga)dalli  hOgi  emba  jODisuva  kriyArUpa 
vannu  modalaneya  vAkyadalli  mAtra  baLasalAgide.  Adare,  (11kha)dalli 
U  pratyayavannu  eraDu  bAri,  jODisalAgiruva  eraDu  vAkyaga 
LondigU sErisi baLasalAgide. 
    eraDakkinta jAsti vAkyagaLannu jODisuvudiddalli, mattu padavannu 
koneya  vAkyada  modaligomme  baLasidare  sAku,  Adare  jODisuva 
kriyArUpavannu  koneya  vAkyavondannu  biTTu  uLida  ellA  vAkyaga 
LondigU baLasabEkAguttade. U pratyayavannu koneya vAkyavU sEri 
dante pratiyondu vAkyadondigU baLasabEkAguttade.

haccalu surumADida.

8.2.3 jODisuva kriyArUpada baLake 
jODisuva kriyArUpavannu baLasuva mUraneya vidhAna itara eraDu 
vidhAnagaLiginta  halavu  viSayagaLalli  bhinnavAgide.  pratiyondu  kriyA 
padakkU  nAlku  jODisuva  kriyArUpagaLiddu  ivannu  bEre  bEre 
sandabhragaLalli  baLasabEkAguttade.  udAharaNegAgi  keLagina  vAkyagaLannu 
pariSIlisabahudu. 
(14ka)  avanu UTa mADuttA nammondige mAtanADida. 
(14kha) avanu UTa mADi nammondige mAtanADida. 
(14ga)  avanu UTa mADalu nammallige banda. 
(14gha) avanu UTa mADade nammallige banda. 
mADu  kriyApadakke  mADuttA,  mADi,  mADalu  mattu  mADade 
embudAgi  nAlku  kriyArUpagaLiddu,  avugaLa  baLake  hEge  embudannu 
(14ka-gha) vAkyagaLalli tOrisalAgide.  
    eraDu  ghaTanegaLu  ondE  samayadalli  jaraguttive  embudannu 
sUcisuvudakkAgi (14ka)dalli mADuttA emba jODisuva rUpavannu 
baLasalAgide.  idakke  badalu,  (14kha)dalli  modalanE  ghaTane  eraDanE 
ghaTaneginta  modalE  naDeyuvudembudannu  sUcisalu  mADi  emba 
rUpavannu baLasalAgide.  
    modalanE  ghaTane  eraDanE  ghaTaneya  anantara  naDeyuvudembu 
dannu sUcisalu (14ga)dalli mADalu embudannu baLasalAgide mattu 
eraDanE  ghaTane  naDeyuva  samayadalli  modalanE  ghaTane  naDedira 
lillavembudannu  sUcisalu  (14gha)dalli  mADade  embudannu  baLasa 
    I  rIti,  jODisuva  kriyArUpagaLalli  baruva  pratyayagaLu 
samayada  maTTige  A  kriyApadagaLu  tiLisuva  ghaTanegaLa  naDuviruva 
sambandhavEnu embudannu sUcisuttave (5.4.2 nODi). idu mattu 
padada  baLakeginta  bhinnavAgide  embudannu  keLagina  udAharaNegaLu  spaSTa 
paDisuttave. 
(15ka)  rAju manege banda mattu snAna mADida. 
(15kha) rAju manege bandu snAna mADida. 
(16ka)  rAju manege baruttAne mattu snAna mADuttAne. 
(16kha) rAju manege bandu snAna mADuttAne. 
(15ka) vAkyadalli banda mattu mADida emba eraDu kriyApadagaLU 
A  vAkyavannADiruva  samayakke  sambandhisidante  ghaTaneya  samayavannu 
sUcisuttave.  Adare,  (15kha)  vAkyadalli  mADida  emba  eraDaneya 
kriyArUpa  mAtra  A  vAkyavannADiruva  samayakke  sambandhisidante 
ghaTaneya  samayavannu  sUcisuttade;  bandu  emba  innondu  kriyA 
rUpa  eraDanE  ghaTaneya  samayakke  sambandhisidante  modalanE 
ghaTaneya samayavannu sUcisuttade. 
    I vyatyAsa (16ka-kha) vAkyagaLalli innaSTu spaSTavAgi kANisuttade. 
illi ghaTanegaLeraDU A vAkyavannADiruva samayakkinta anantara naDeyu 
vantahavugaLu. idannu sUcisuvudakkAgi (16ka)dalli baruttAne mattu 
mADuttAne  embudAgi  eraDu  kriyArUpagaLU  mundina  samaya 
vannu  sUcisuttive.  sAmAnyavAgi  I  rIti  mattu  padada  mUlaka 
illavE  U  pratyayada  mUlaka  jODisiruva  vAkyagaLallella  modalu 
tiLisiruva  ghaTane  modalu  naDeyuvantahadu  emba  artha  dhvanitavAgu 
    I rIti (16ka)dalli dhvanitavAguva arthavannu (16kha)dalli bandu 
emba  jODisuva  kriyArUpada  mUlaka  spaSTavAgi  sUcisalAgide. 
(16ka)  vAkyada  hAge  (16kha)  vAkyadallU  mAtina  samayada  anantara 
naDeyuva  eraDu  ghaTanegaLannu  tiLisalAgide.  Adare  I  viSayavannu 
vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  mADuttAne  kriyArUpa  mAtra  sUcisa 
balludu.  bandu  kriyArUpakke  ghaTaneya  samayakkU  mattu  mAtina 
samayakkU naDuviruva sambandhavannu sUcisuva arthavilla.  
    ghaTanegaLannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  kriyA 
padagaLigella  samayavannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  eraDu  rUpagaLu  mAtra 
ive  embudannu  nAvu  hinde  aydanE  adhyAyadalli  (5.2ralli) 
nODiruvevu.  ivu  vAkyavannADiruva  samayakkinta  modalu  mattu 
anantara naDeyuva ghaTanegaLannu sUcisuttave.  
    udAharaNegAgi  hOgu  kriyApadakke  hOguttAne  mattu 
hOda  embudAgi  eraDu  samayagaLannu  sUcisuva  kriyArUpagaLu 
mAtra ive (keLage koTTiruva (17ka-kha) vAkyagaLannu nODi). 
    ondu  ghaTane  adannu  tiLisuva  vAkyavannADiruva  samayadallEnE 
naDedideyembudAgi ghaTaneya `Igina samaya'vannu sUcisuva avaSyakate 
kelavu sandabhragaLalli baruvudAdarU, adakkAgi kannaDadalli pratyEkavAda 
kriyArUpavilla.  intaha  ghaTanegaLu  heccu  hottu  (endare  antaha 
varNaneyannu  tayArisikoLLalu  bEkAguvaSTu  hottAdarU)  naDedira 
bEkAguttade.  hAgAgi,  avannu 
varNisuvudakkAgi  kriyApadagaLa 
jODisuva  rUpadondige  iru  kriyApadada  Igina  samayada 
rUpavannu baLasabEkAguttade ((17ga) nODi). 
(17ka)  rAju manege hOguttAne. 
(17kha) rAju manege hOda. 
(17ga)  rAju manege hOguttA iddAne. 
    Adare,  I  kriyApadagaLa  jODisuva  rUpagaLu  eraDara  badalu 
mUru  samayagaLannu  sUcisuva  avaSyakateyide.  yAkendare,  avu 
eraDu  ghaTanegaLa  naDuve  kANisabahudAda  mUru  rItiya  sambandha 
gaLannu  (ondu  ghaTane  innondu  ghaTaneya  modalu  naDedirabahudu, 
anantara  naDedirabahudu  illavE  averaDU  ondE  samayadalli 
naDedirabahudu embudAgi) sUcisuva avaSyakateyide.  
    I  mUru  rItiya  sambandhagaLu  ellA  rItiya  ghaTanegaLa 
naDuveyU  kANisikoLLalu    sAdhyavideyAda  kAraNa,  ellA  kriyApada 
gaLigU  modalina  samaya,  anantarada  samaya  mattu  ondE  samaya 
embudAgi  mUru  vidhavAda  samayagaLannu  sUcisaballa  jODisuva 
rUpagaLive.  
    idallade,  ellA  kriyApadagaLigU  nAlkaneya  allagaLeyuva  rUpa 
vondiddu,  adu  samayada  maTTige  ghaTanegaLa  naDuve  sambandha 
illadiruvudannu sUcisuttade. 
8.2.4 ghaTaneya hatOTi 
eraDu  ghaTanegaLu  avannu  naDesuva  vyaktigaLa  hatOTiyalliruvavu 
gaLAdare,  avannu  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLannu  mattu  padada  mUlaka  illavE 
U  pratyayada  mUlaka  jODisalu  sAdhyavide.  Adare,  jODisuva 
kriyArUpada  mUlaka  intaha  vAkyagaLannu  jODisabEkiddalli,  A 
ghaTanegaLeraDannU obbanE vyakti naDesuttiruvudu avaSya.  
bEyisida 
bEyisidaLu. 
(18kha) rAju tarakAriyannU jAnaki annavannU bEyisidaru. 
(18ga)  rAju tarakAriyannu bEyisi sAmbAr mADida. 
mattu 
jAnaki  anna 
(18ka-kha)gaLalli  naDesuvavara  hatOTiyalliruva  eraDu  ghaTanegaLannu, 
avannu bEre bEre vyaktigaLu naDesuttiruvarAdarU, mattu pada mattu 
U  pratyayagaLa  mUlaka  jODisalu  sAdhyavAgide;  Adare,  (19ga)dalli 
antaha  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  jODisuva  kriyArUpada  mUlaka 
jODisabEkAda kAraNa, adakkAgi A eraDu ghaTanegaLannU obbanE vyakti 
(rAju) mADiddAnendu hELabEkAgide. 
    eraDu  vAkyagaLu  tiLisuva  ghaTanegaLalli  ondu  (illavE  eraDU) 
naDesuvavana  hatOTiyalli  illavAdalli  avannu  naDesuva  vyaktigaLu 
bEre  bErAgiddarU  jODisuva  kriyArUpagaLa  mUlaka  avannu 
jODisalu sAdhyavide.

(19kha) jOrAgi 
banduvu. 
(19ga)  maDake oDedu rAmuvina mukhakke mosaru cimmitu. 
gALi  bIsi 
taragelegaLella  maneyoLage 
(19ka)dalli  modalaneya  ghaTane  naDesuvavara  hatOTiyallide,  Adare 
eraDaneyadu  hatOTiyallilla;  (19kha-ga)gaLalli  eraDu  ghaTanegaLU 
hatOTiyallilladavu; I kAraNakkAgi ivannu jODisuva kriyArUpada 
mUlaka jODisi hELalu sAdhyavAgide. 
    idallade, jODisuva kriyArUpagaLu eraDu ghaTanegaLa naDuviruva 
sambandhavannu allagaLeyuttiveyAdare, antaha kriyArUpagaLa mUlaka 
eraDu  vAkyagaLannu,  avu  naDesuvavana  hatOTiyalliruvantaha  ghaTane 
yannu sUcisuvudiddarU, jODisi hELalu sAdhyavide. ghaTane hatOTi 
yalliruvantahadAdarU  adannobba  vyakti  naDesuttilla  embudE  idakke 
kAraNavirabahudu. 
(20ka)  avaru UTamADade nAnu UTamADuvudilla. 
(20kha)  avaru  A  bAgilannu  tereyade  nAnu  nimage  pustaka 
koDuvudu hEge? 
Adare illU eraDaneya vAkya adannu naDesuvavana hatOTiyalliruva 
ghaTaneyannu sUcisuttideyAdare, adondu allagaLeyuva vAkyavAgira 
bEku (20ka) illavE kELviyAgirabEku (20kha) emba nibrandhaviruva 
hAge kANisuttade. 
8.3 jODaNeyalli mUru bage 
eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  mEle  vivarisida  hAge  jODisi  hELalu  mUru 
rItiya  uddESagaLiruttave.  ivu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatigaLa  naDuve 
kANisikoLLuva mUru rItiya sambandhagaLannu sUcisuttave.  
    modalaneyadAgi,  eraDu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatigaLa  naDuve 
ondaroDanondu  kUDikoLLuva  sambandhavide  embudannu  sUcisuvu 
dakkAgi  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  jODisi  hELabahudu.  udAharaNegAgi, 
mattu  padada  mUlaka,  U  pratyayada  mUlaka  illavE  jODisuva 
kriyArUpada  mUlaka  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  oTTu  sErisidalli,  avu 
tiLisuva  ghaTane  illavE  sangatigaLa  naDuve  I  rIti  ondaroDanondu 
kUDikoLLuva sambandhavideyendu sUcitavAguttade. 
(21ka)  rAmu puNege mattu hari Dellige hOguttAre. 
(21kha) rAmu puNegU hari DelligU hOguttAre. 
(21ga)  rAmu puNege hOgi (allinda) Dellige hOguttAne. 
mElina  mUru  vAkyagaLallU  eraDu  vAkyagaLu  tiLisuva  ghaTanegaLa 
naDuve `kUDikeya' sambandhavideyembudannu gamanisabahudu. 
    eraDaneyadAgi,  illavE  padada  mUlaka  athavA  O  pratyayada 
mUlaka  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  jODisi,  avu  tiLisuva  ghaTane  illavE 
sangatigaLa  naDuve  eraDarallondu  embudAgi  `badali'  sambandhavide 
endu sUcisabahudu. 
(22ka)  rAju puNege illavE hari Dellige hOguttAre. 
(22kha) rAju puNegO hari DelligO hOguttAre. 
(22ka)dalli eraDu vAkyagaLu tiLisuva ghaTanegaLa naDuve badali sambandha 
videyembudannu, endare avugaLalli ondu naDeyuvudAdare innondu 
naDeyuvudilla  embudannu,  averaDannu  illavE  padada  mUlaka 
jODisi  sUcisalAgide.  idE  rItiyalli  (22kha)dalli  eraDu  vAkya 
gaLannu  jODisuvudakkAgi  O  pratyayavannu  baLasuvudara  mUlaka  idE 
arthavannu sUcisalu sAdhyavAgide. 
    mUraneyadAgi,  Adare  padada  mUlaka  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu 
jODisidalli, avu tiLisuva  ghaTane illavE sangatigaLalli  eraDaneyadu 
modalaneyadakke pratikUlavAgideyemba artha sUcitavAguttade. 
(23ka)  rAju puNege hOgidda, Adare hari Dellige hOgidda. 
(23kha) Ata hariyannu kanDidda, Adare satISanannu kanDiralilla. 
(23ga)  maLe bandide, Adare TAnki tumbalilla. 
    jODisiruva  eraDu  vAkyagaLalli  eraDaneyadara  munde  Adare 
padavannu  baLasuva  badalu  modalaneya  vAkyada  kriyApadakke  re 
pratyayavannu  sErisidalli  modalaneya  vAkya  sUcisuva  ghaTane  illavE 
sangati  eraDaneya  vAkya  sUcisuva  ghaTane  illavE  sangatige  Sarattu 
emba artha baruttade. 
(24ka)  avanu bandare nAnu hOguttEne. 
(24kha) maLe bandare TAnkiyalli nIru tumbuttade. 
(24ga)  bEgane hOgiddare avarige tondareyAguttittu. 
8.4 jODisida vAkyagaLu mattu kUDupadagaLu 
kannaDadalli  `kUDupada'vemba  ondu  viSiSTavAda  racane  baLakeyalliddu, 
cAritrikavAgi  idu  eraDu  vAkyagaLa  jODaNeyinda  beLedu  bandide. 
udAharaNegAgi keLagina vAkyagaLannu pariSIlisabahudu. 
(25ka)  kappu nAyi A huDuganannu kaccibiTTitu. 
(25kha) Ake tanna kayberaLannu kattarisikonDaLu. 
(25ga)  sItApati cennayge hOgiddAne. 
(25gha) yArO IsicErina baTTeyannu hariduhAkiddAre. 
(25Ga) Ata hoTTenOvininda nelada mEle horaLADida. 
(25ka)  vAkyadalli  kaccu  mattu  biDu  emba  eraDu  kriyApadagaLu 
bandiddu,  avugaLalli  modalaneyadu  adara  jODisuva  rUpadallU 
mattu  eraDaneyadu  adara  tiLisuva  rUpadallU  bandive.  Adare  I 
vAkyadalli  eraDu  vAkyagaLa  jODaNeyAgideyendu  hELuvudu  svalpa 
kaSTa.  yAkendare,  keLage  koTTiruva  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  jODisidalli 
(25ka) vAkyada artha baruvudilla. 
(26ka)  kappu nAyi A huDuganannu kaccitu. 
(26kha) kappu nAyi A huDuganannu biTTitu. 
idE  rItiyalli  mEle  koTTiruva  itara  (25kha-Ga)  vAkyagaLallU 
eraDu  vAkyagaLa  jODaNeyAgideyendu  hELuvudu  kaSTa.  yAkendare, 
intaha  vAkyagaLalli  baruva  eraDaneya kriyApadakke tannadE Ada ondu 
ghaTaneyannu sUcisuva arthavilla.  
    idakke  badalu,  I  kriyApadagaLu  vAkyadalli  avakkinta  modalu 
bandiruva  kriyApada  sUcisuva  ghaTaneya  kuritAgi  EnAdarU  tiLisuva 
kelasavannu  naDesuttave.  intaha  racanegaLa  kuritu  heccina  vivaragaLannu 
(5.6)ralli nODabahudu. 
8.4 sArAmSa 
eraDu  (athavA  jAsti)  vAkyagaLannu  oTTu  sErisuvudakkAgi  mattu, 
illavE,  Adare  modalAda  padagaLannAgali,  illavE  U,  O,  re 
modalAda  pratyayagaLannAgali  baLasalu  sAdhyavide.  idallade,  vAkya 
vondara  koneyalli  baruva  kriyApadada  jODaNeya  rUpavannu 
baLasiyU adannu innondu vAkyadondige jODisalu sAdhyavide. 
    I  rIti  vAkyagaLannu  jODisi  hELalu  mUru  mukhyavAda 
uddESa gaLiruttave. vAkyagaLu tiLisuva ghaTane illavE sangatigaLa naDuve 
kUDikeya  sambandhavideyendAgalI,  badali  sambandhavideyendAgalI 
illavE  pratikUla  (athavA  Sarattina)  sambandhavideyendAgalI  sUcisu 
vudE I mUru uddESagaLu.

allagaLeyuvudu 
9.1 pIThike 
tiLisuva vAkyagaLalli kriyAvAkyagaLu mattu viSayavAkyagaLu embudAgi 
eraDu rItiya vAkyagaLiveyembudannu mEle nODiruvevu. ivugaLalli 
kriyAvAkyagaLu  ondu  ghaTaneyannU  mattu  viSayavAkyagaLu  ondu 
sangatiyannU  tiLisuvudakkAgi  baLakeyAguttave.  I  eraDu  rItiya 
vAkyagaLU I rIti ghaTane illavE sangatiyannu nEravAgi tiLisuvantaha 
rUpadalli mAtravallade bEre eraDu rUpagaLallU baraballuvu. ivannu 
sambandhisuva  vAkyagaLu  mattu  allagaLeyuva  vAkyagaLu  embudAgi 
kareyabahudu. 
    ondu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyannu  nEravAgi  tiLisuva  badalu, 
adaralli  toDagiruva  ghaTakagaLalli  ondu  A  ghaTane  illavE  sangatige 
sambandhiside embudAgi tiLisalu sAdhyavide. idakkAgi tiLisuva vAkyavannu 
adara sambandhisuva rUpakke badalAyisikoLLabEku. I vidhAnada baLake 
yannu keLagina vAkyagaLalli kANabahudu. 
(1ka)  mosarina gaDige oDedide. 
(1kha)  oDedaddu mosarina gaDige. 
(2ka)  A DabbadoLage ondu iliyide. 
(2kha)  A DabbadoLagiruvudu ondu ili. 
(1ka)dalli  mosarina  gaDige  oDedide  emba  ghaTaneyannu  nEravAgi 
tiLisalAgide.  Adare  (1kha)dalli  I  rIti  ondu  ghaTane  naDedide 
embudannu nEravAgi tiLisuva badalu, mosarina gaDige emba ghaTakakkU 
mattu A ghaTanegU naDuve sambandhavide embudannu tiLisalAgide. idE 
rItiyalli (2ka)dalli ondu viSayavannu nEravAgi tiLisalAgideyAdare, 
(2kha)dalli  A  viSayakkU  mattu  ondu  ghaTakakkU  (ondu  ili 
embudakkU) naDuve sambandhavide embudannu tiLisalAgide. 
    ondu  ghaTane  naDediruvudannu  (athavA  naDeyaliruvudannu)  mattu 
ondu  sangati  iruvudannu  nEravAgi  tiLisuva  badalu,  ondu  ghaTane 
naDedilla  embudannu  illavE  ondu  sangati  nijavalla  embudannu 
tiLisuvudakkAgi  `allagaLeyuva'  vAkyavannu  baLasalAguttade.  idakkAgi 
tiLisuva vAkyakke  illa padavannu sErisi hELabEkAguttade. 
(3ka)  mosarina maDike oDeyitu. 
(3kha)  mosarina maDike oDeyalilla. 
(4ka)  A DabbadoLage iliyide. 
(4kha)  A DabbadoLage iliyilla. 
I  rIti  ondu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyannu  nEravAgi  allagaLeyuva 
badalu  adakkU  mattu  ondu  ghaTakakkU  naDuviruva  sambandhavannU 
allagaLeyalu 
sambandhisuva  vAkyagaLU 
allagaLeyuva  rUpadalli  baraballuvu.  Adare  idakkAgi  kannaDadalli  alla 
emba bEreyE ondu allagaLeyuva padavannu baLasalAguttade. 
sAdhyavideyAda 
(5ka)  oDedaddu mosarina gaDige. 
(5kha)  oDedaddu mosarina gaDigeyalla. 
(5ga)  marada mEliruvudu ondu kOti. 
(5gha)  marada mEliruvudu (ondu) kOtiyalla.  
sambandhisuvudu mattu allagaLeyuvudu 
    tiLisiruva  ghaTanegU  mattu  adara  ghaTakakkU  naDuviruva  sambandha 
vannu  mAtravallade,  allagaLediruva  ghaTane(illavE  sangati)gU  mattu 
ghaTakakkU  naDuviruva  sambandhavannU  intaha  vAkyada  mUlaka  alla 
gaLeyalu sAdhyavide. 
(6ka)  mosarina gaDige oDeyalilla. 
(6kha)  oDeyadudu mosarina gaDige. 
(6ga)  maDakeyalli bisinIrilla. 
(6gha)  maDakeyallilladiruvudu bisinIralla. 
    sambandhisuvudakkAgi  mattu  allagaLeyuvudakkAgi  baLakeyAguva  I 
eraDu rItiya vAkyagaLa oLaracane hEgide embudannu keLage svalpa vivara 
vAgi pariSIlisalAgide. 
    vAkyagaLa koneyalli ante padavannu sErisuva mUlaka bErobbana 
mAtannu  illavE  abhiprAyavannu  ettihELalu  sAdhya  embudannu 
ELaneya  adhyAyadalli  (7.2.1ralli)  nODiruvevu.  ivannu  mUranE 
rItiya tiLisuva vAkyagaLendu parigaNisalu sAdhyavide.  
9.2 sambandhisuva vAkyagaLu 
vAkyada  ondu  ghaTakavannu  adara  itara  bhAgakke  sambandhisiruvante 
hELalu  A  ghaTakavannu  vAkyada  koneyalli  irisabEku  mattu  vAkyada 
kriyApadavannu  adara  nAmapadarUpakke  badalAyisikoLLabEku.  udA 
haraNegAgi keLagina eraDu vAkyagaLannu pariSIlisabahudu.  
(7ka)  jAnakiya citra pEparinalli bantu. 
(7kha)  pEparinalli bandudu jAnakiya citra. 
(7ka)dalli  bandiruva  tiLisuva  vAkyavannu  (7kha)dalli  sambandhisuva 
vAkyavannAgi  badalAyisalAgide,  mattu  idakkAgi,  adara  eraDu  ghaTaka 
gaLalli  ondannu  (jAnakiya  citra  embudannu)  vAkyada  koneyalli 
irisalAgide mattu bantu emba adara kriyApadavannu bandudu emba 
nAmapadarUpakke badalAyisalAgide. 
9.2.1 ghaTakagaLannu pratyEkisuvudu 
ondu  vAkyadalli  bandiruva  bEre  bEre  ghaTakagaLannu  I  rIti  adara 
uLida bhAgakke sambandhisiruvante pratyEkisi hELalu sAdhyavide.  
rAju A vyApArige tanna maneyannu mAriddAne. 
(8kha)  rAju A vyApArige mAriruvudu tanna maneyannu. 
rAju tanna maneyannu mAriruvudu A vyApArige. 
(8gha)  A vyApArige tanna maneyannu mAriruvudu rAju. 
mEle  (8ka)dalli  bandiruva  vAkyadalli  mUru  ghaTakagaLiddu  anantarada 
mUru  vAkyagaLalli,  endare  (8kha-gha)gaLalli  A  mUru  ghaTakagaLalli 
ondondannU  pratyEkisi,  adu  A  vAkyada  itara  bhAgakke  sambandhiside 
endu sUcisalAgide. 
    sAmAnyavAgi vAkyadalli baruva ghaTakagaLalli ondannu mAtravE I 
rIti  pratyEkisi  hELuvudu  rUDhi.  Adare  kelavu  viSiSTavAda  sandabhra 
gaLalli  ondakkinta  jAsti  ghaTakagaLannU  I  rIti  pratyEkisalu  sAdhyavide 
embudannu keLagina vAkyagaLalli nODabahudu. 
rAju koTTudu harigondu pustaka. 
(9kha)  SAmarAyaru  varNisida  apaghAta  naDedudu  ninne  rAtri 
yaravADada sakralinalli. 
(9ga)  jAsti maLe bandiruvudu ninne bombAyiyalli. 
   idallade, vAkyavu sUcisuva ghaTaneyannE adara ghaTakagaLige sambandhi 
siruva hAgeyU intaha sambandhisuva vAkyada mUlaka tiLisalu sAdhya 
vide.  idakkAgi  intaha  vAkyagaLalli  nAmapadarUpadalliruva  kriyApada 
vannu vAkyada koneyallirisabEku. 
(10ka)  Ake rAjuvannu hogaLidudu (tegaLidudalla). 
(10kha) rAju I danavannu mAruvudu (dAna koDuvudalla). 
9.2.2 kriyApadavannu badalAyisuvudu 
tiLisuva  vAkyavondarinda  sambandhisuva  vAkyavannu  tayArisabEkiddalli, 
adara kriyApadavannu nAmapadarUpakke badalAyisabEkembudannu nAvu 
sambandhisuvudu mattu allagaLeyuvudu 
mEle  nODiruvevu.  I  badalAvaNege  sambandhisidante  kelavu  samasye 
gaLiveyembudannu I vibhAgadalli nODaliruvevu. 
    viSayavAkyagaLannu avugaLa koneyalli baruva iru kriyApadavannu 
tegedu  hAkiyU  baLasalu  sAdhya  embudannu  nAvu  3.1ralli  nODiru 
vevu. Adare intaha vAkyagaLannu avugaLa sambandhisuva rUpakke badalA 
yisabEkiddalli  I  rIti  tegedu  hAkida  kriyApadavannu  tirugi  paDedu 
adannu nAmapadarUpadalli baLasikoLLabEkAguttade. 
(11ka)  jAnakige SrIhariya mEle kOpavide. 
(11kha) jAnakige SrIhariya mEle kOpa. 
(11ga)  jAnakige kOpaviruvudu SrIhariya mEle. 
(11ka)dalli  bandiruva  viSayavAkyada  ide  kriyArUpavannu  (11kha) 
dalli  tegedu  hAkalu  sAdhyavAgide.  Adare  (11ga)dalli  bandiruva  I 
vAkyada  sambandhisuva  rUpadinda  I  rIti  A  kriyApadada    iruvudu 
emba nAmapadarUpavannu tegedu hAkalu sAdhyavAguvudilla. 
    viSayavAkyagaLalli  baruva  iru  kriyApadakke  mUru  kriyArUpaga 
Liddu  (udA:  iddAne,  iruttAne,  idda),  avu  hindina,  mundina 
mattu  Igina  ghaTanegaLannu  tiLisaballuvu  embudannu  nAvu  mEle 
3.1.1ralli  nODiruvevu.  Adare,  I  kriyApadakke  iruvudu  mattu 
iddudu  embudAgi  eraDu  nAmapadarUpagaLu  mAtra  ive.  hAgAgi, 
sambandhisuva  vAkyagaLalli  mundina  mattu  Igina  ghaTanegaLa  naDuvina 
vyatyAsavannu sUcisalu sAdhyavAgadu. 
(12ka)  rAmamUtri I maneyalliruttAne. 
(12kha) rAmamUtri I maneyalliddAne. 
(12ga)  rAmamUtri I maneyallidda. 
(13ka)  rAmamUtri iruvudu I maneyalli. 
(13kha) rAmamUtri iddudu I maneyalli. 
(13ka-ga)gaLalliruva  mUru  kriyAvAkyagaLige  badalAgi  (13ka-kha) 
gaLalli  kANisiruva  hAge  eraDu  sambandhisuva  vAkyagaLannu  mAtra 
tayArisalu  sAdhyavAgide  embudannu  gamanisabahudu.  ivugaLalli 
modalaneyadu  (12ka)  vAkyadindalU  tayArAgirabahudu  illavE 
(12kha)dindalU tayArAgirabahudu. 
    allagaLeyuva  kriyAvAkyagaLalli  hindina  ghaTaneyannu  allagaLeyu 
vavu  mattu  mundina  ghaTaneyannu  allagaLeyuvavu  embudAgi  eraDu 
rItiya  vAkyagaLiveyembudannu  munde  (9.3ralli)  nODaliruvevu. 
ivugaLalli modalaneyadara sambandhisuva rUpavannu nEravAgi adaralli 
bandiruva kriyApadavannu nAmapadarUpakke badalAyisuvudara mUlaka 
tayArisalu sAdhyavide. 
(14ka)  jAnaki SAlege hOgalilla. 
(14kha) SAlege hOgadudu jAnaki. 
mundina 
ghaTaneyannu  allagaLeyuva  eraDaneya 
kriyAvAkyada  sambandhisuva  rUpavannu  I  rIti  nEravAgi  tayArisalu 
sAdhyavAgadu. 
ghaTaneyannu 
allagaLeyuva  kriyApadakke  nAmapadarUpavilla.  hAgAgi  intaha 
sandabhragaLalli  kriyApadadondige  iru  embudara  nAmapadarUpavannu 
baLasabEkAguttade. 
yAkendare, 
kannaDadalli 
mundina 
(15ka)  jAnaki SAlege hOguvudilla. 
(15kha) SAlege hOgadiruvudu jAnaki.   
9.3 allagaLeyuva vAkyagaLu 
mEle 9.1ralli sUcisiruva  hAge, ondu ghaTane illavE sangatiyannu 
allagaLeyuvudakkAgi  kannaDadalli  illa  padada  baLakeyAguttade.  I  pada 
vannu  baLasidAga,  tiLisuva  vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  kriyApadadallU 
kelavu badalAvaNegaLannu mADikoLLabEkAguttade. udAharaNegAgi keLage 
koTTiruva eraDu vAkyagaLannu gamanisabahudu. 
(16ka)  jAnaki aDige mADidaLu. 
(16kha) jAnaki aDige mADalilla. 
(17ka)  rAju upparigeyalli malaguttAne. 
(17kha) rAju upparigeyalli malaguvudilla. 
sambandhisuvudu mattu allagaLeyuvudu 
    hindina  ghaTaneyondannu  tiLisuva  (16ka)  vAkyakke  illa  padavannu 
sErisuvudara  mUlaka  (16kha)  vAkyadalli  A  ghaTaneyannu  allagaLeya 
lAgide,  mattu  idakkAgi  (16ka)  vAkyada  koneyalli  bandiruva 
mADidaLu  kriyArUpavannu  mADalu  embudAgi  modalina  ghaTane 
yannu sUcisuva rUpakke badalisikoLLalAgide.  
    idE rItiyalli mundina ghaTaneyondannu tiLisuva (17ka) vAkyakke 
illa  padavannu  sErisi  (17kha)  vAkyadalli  A  ghaTaneyannu  allagaLeya 
lAgide,  mattu  idakkAgi  (17ka)  koneyalli  bandiruva  malaguttAne 
kriyArUpavannu  malaguvudu  embudAgi  adara  nAmapadarUpakke 
badalisikoLLalAgide. 
    sangatigaLannu  tiLisuva  viSayavAkyagaLannu  allagaLeyabEkiddalli, 
avugaLa koneyalli baruva iru kriyApadada rUpagaLallU badalAvaNe 
gaLannu  mADikoLLabEkAguttade.  ivugaLalli  hindina  mattu  mundina 
samayada  rUpagaLannu  itara  kriyApadagaLa  rUpagaLa  hAgeyE  mEle 
sUcisidante badalAyisikoLLabEkAguttade. 
(18ka)  SAmarAyaru AphIsinalli iddaru. 
(18kha) SAmarAyaru AphIsinalli iralilla. 
(19ka)  SAmarAyaru AphIsinalli iruttAre. 
(19kha) SAmarAyaru AphIsinalli iruvudilla. 
hindina  sangatiyannu  sUcisuva  iddaru  kriyApadakke  badalAgi  (18kha) 
dalli  iralu  emba  mundina  samayavannu  sUcisuva  kriyArUpavannU 
mattu mundina (illavE rUDhiya) sangatiyannu sUcisuva iruttAre 
kriyApadakke  badalAgi  (19kha)dalli  adara  iruvudu  emba  nAmapada 
rUpavannU illa emba padadondige baLasalAgide. 
    Adare,  Igina  samayavannu  sUcisuva  iddAne,  iddALe,  ide 
modalAda  rUpagaLu  avugaLa  munde  illa  padavannu  baLasidAga  I 
rIti badalAguva badalu summage biddu hOguttave. 
(20ka)  SAmarAyaru AphIsinalli iddAre. 
(20kha)  SAmarAyaru AphIsinalli illa. 
(21ka)  avaLige nimma mEle kOpa ide. 
(21kha) avaLige nimma mEle kOpa illa. 
    tiLisuva  vAkyagaLu  ondu  ghaTaneyalli  toDagikonDiruva  vyakti, 
vastu modalAdavugaLalli ondannu cuTukAgi sUcisaballuvu. I kelasa 
vannu  avugaLa  kriyApadagaLa  koneyalli  baruva  ondu  pratyaya  naDesu 
ttade. Adare, I vAkyagaLa allagaLeyuva rUpagaLu I rIti ghaTaneyalli 
toDagikonDiruva  (illavE  toDagikonDillavembudAgi  allagaLeyuva) 
vyakti  illavE  vastuvondannu  cuTukAgi  sUcisalAravu.  allagaLeyuva 
vAkyagaLalli  kriyApadada  nAmapada  rUpavAgalI  illavE  mundina 
samayavannu sUcisuva rUpavAgalI baruvudE idakke kAraNa. 
(22ka)  rAju makkaLige kAphi koDuttAne. 
(22kha) rAju makkaLige kAphi koDuvudilla. 
(23ka)  jAnaki makkaLige hAlu koDuttALe. 
(23kha) jAnaki makkaLige hAlu koDuvudilla. 
(22ka)dalli ghaTaneyannu naDesuva vyakti obba ganDasu embudannu adara 
koneyalli  bandiruva  koDuttAne  kriyArUpa  (Ane  pratyayada 
mUlaka)  cuTukAgi  sUcisuttade.  idE  rItiyalli  (23ka)dalli 
bandiruva  koDuttALe  kriyArUpa  A  vAkya  tiLisuva  ghaTaneyannu 
naDesuva  vyakti  obba  hengasu  embudannu  (ALe  pratyayada  mUlaka) 
cuTukAgi sUcisuttade.  
    Adare  I  eraDu  vAkyagaLa  allagaLeyuva  rUpagaLalli  ((22kha) 
mattu  (23kha)gaLalli)  I  eraDu  kriyArUpagaLa  nAmapadarUpa 
(koDuvudu)  bandideyAda  kAraNa,  mattu  I  rUpadalli  vyakti 
illavE vastuvannu sUcisuva pratyaya baruvudillavAda kAraNa, avu I 
rIti (ghaTaneyannu naDesadiruva) vyaktiyannu cuTukAgi sUcisalAravu. 
    hindina  vibhAgadalli  vivarisiruva  `sambandhisuva'  vAkyagaLallU  I 
rIti  ghaTaneyannu  naDesuva  vyaktiyannu  cuTukAgi  sUcisalu  sAdhya 
vAguvudilla embudannu illi gamanisabahudu. 
sambandhisuvudu mattu allagaLeyuvudu

(23ga)  makkaLige hAlu koDuvudu jAnaki. 
9.3.1 sambandhavannu allagaLeyuvudu 
ondu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyannu  I  rIti  nEravAgi  allagaLeyuva 
badalu,  adakkU  mattu  ondu  ghaTakakkU  naDuviruva  sambandhavannu 
allagaLeyabEkiddalli  illa  embudara  badalu  alla  emba  bErondu 
padavannu  baLasabEkAguttade.  intaha  vAkyagaLalli  kriyApada  adara 
nAmapadarUpadallideyAda  kAraNa,  adaralli  yAva  badalAvaNeyannU 
mADabEkAguvudilla. 
(24ka)  avaru hOdudu mangaLUrige. 
(24kha) avaru hOdudu mangaLUrigalla. 
(25ka)  avaru hOguvudu mangaLUrige. 
(25kha) avaru hOguvudu mangaLUrigalla. 
(26ka)  avaru iruvudu mangaLUralli. 
(26kha) avaru iruvudu mangaLUralli alla. 
    sangatiyondannu  sUcisuva  viSayavAkyagaLannu  antaha  sangatigU 
mattu  vAkyada  ondu  ghaTakakkU  naDuviruva  sambandhavannu  sUcisuvu 
dakkAgi  `sambandhisuva'  vAkyagaLannAgi  badalAyisabEkiddalli  avugaLalli 
baruva  iru  kriyApadavannu  nAmapadarUpakke  badalAyisabEkAguvu 
dembudannu  nAvu  mEle  9.2ralli  nODiruvevu.  I  iru  kriyApada 
vannu  nEravAgi  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLalli  baLasadiralU  sAdhyavide,  Adare 
sambandhisuva  vAkyagaLalli  adara  nAmapadarUpavannu  A  rIti  baLasa 
diralu sAdhyavAgadu embudannU hinde (9.2.2ralli) sUcisalAgittu. 
    Adare,  intaha  vAkyagaLannu  allagaLeyuvudakkAgi  avugaLondige 
alla  padavannu  baLasidAga,  iru  kriyApadada  nAmapadarUpa  biddu 
hOgalu sAdhyavide. 
(27ka)  A huDugi kappu (iddALe). 
(27kha) A huDugiyiruvudu kappu. 
(27ga)  A huDugiyiruvudu kappalla. 
(27gha) A huDugi kappalla. 
(27Ga) A huDugi kappilla. 
(27ka)dalli  bandiruva  tiLisuva  vAkyavannu  (27kha)dalli  sambandhisuva 
vAkyavannAgi  badalAyisalAgide,  mattu  (27ga)dalli  I  sambandhisuva 
vAkyavannu  allagaLeyalAgide.  (27gha)  vAkyavU  idE  (27kha)  vAkyada 
allagaLeyuva  rUpavendu  hELalu  sAdhyavide.  yAkendare  adakke 
(27ga)da arthavE ide.  
    Adare (27Ga)dalli illa padada baLakeyAgideyAda kAraNa, adannu 
sangatiyondannu  tiLisuva  (27ka)  vAkyada  allagaLeyuva  rUpavendu 
hELabEkAguttade.  yAkendare,  adu  nEravAgi  ondu  sangatiyannE 
allagaLeyuttideyallade  adakkU  mattu  ondu  ghaTakakkU  naDuviruva 
sambandhavannu allagaLeyuvudilla.  
9.3.2 padagaLannu allagaLeyuvudu 
samskxtadalli vAkyagaLu sUcisuva arthada hAgeyE padagaLu sUcisuva

bEkAguttade. kannaDadallU intaha pratyayagaLa baLakeyannu samskxtadinda 
eravalAgi bandiruva kelavu padagaLalli kANabahudu.

9.3.3 allagaLeyuva kriyArUpagaLu 
tiLisuva  vAkyagaLannu  bErondu  vAkyada  illavE  padakanteya

kanteya angagaLannu allagaLeyuvudakkAgi kelavu viSiSTavAda kriyArUpa 
gaLannu baLasalAguttade. 
(29ka)  jAnaki aDige mADalilla. 
(29kha) jAnaki aDige mADadudannu yArU gamanisalilla. 
(29ga)  aDige mADada jAnaki UTavannU mADalilla. 
(29ka)dalli  bandiruva  vAkyavannu  (29kha)dalli  bErondu  vAkyada 
angavannAgi  (oLavAkyavannAgi)  mADi  baLasalAgide,  mattu  hIge 
mADuvAga,  adara  koneyalli  bandiruva  mADalilla  emba  kriyA 
rUpada  badalu  mADadudu  emba  adE  kriyApadada  nAmapada 
rUpavannu  baLasalAgide.  I  mADadudu  emba  kriyArUpakkEnE 
allagaLeyuva  arthavideyAda  kAraNa  adarondige  illa  padavannu 
baLasabEkAgilla embudannu gamanisabahudu. 
    idE  rItiyalli,  (29ga)  vAkyadalli  (29ka)  vAkyavannu  ondu 
padakanteya  angavannAgi  mADi  baLasalAgide  mattu  adakkAgi  adara 
koneyalli  baruva  mADalilla  kriyApadavannu  mADada  embudAgi 
badalAyisalAgide. I kriyArUpakkU allagaLeyuva arthavide.  
    eraDu athavA jAsti vAkyagaLannu kelavu viSiSTavAda kriyArUpagaLa 
mUlaka  jODisuvantaha  sandabhragaLallU  illa  illavE  alla  emba 
padagaLa  badalu  viSiSTavAda  kriyArUpagaLannu  baLasuvudara  mUlaka 
allagaLeyuva arthavannu sUcisalu sAdhyavide. udAharaNegAgi keLagina 
vAkyagaLannu gamanisabahudu. 
(30ka)  jAnaki UTa mADalilla; hAgeyE malagiddALe. 
(30kha)  jAnaki UTa mADade malagiddALe. 
(30ka)dalli  bandiruva  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu  modalaneya  vAkyadalli 
bandiruva mADalilla kriyArUpada badalu mADade kriyArUpavannu 
baLasi  jODisalAgide  (8.2.3  nODi).  I  mADade  kriyArUpakke 
allagaLeyuva arthavideyAda kAraNa (30kha)dalli illa padavannu baLasa 
diddarU allagaLeyuva artha uLidukonDide. 
    allagaLeyuva  vAkyavannu  sambandhisuva  vAkyavannAgi  badalAyisi 
dAgalU  allagaLeyuva  arthavannu  sUcisalu  intaha  viSiSTavAda 
kriyArUpada baLakeyAguttade. 
(31ka)  Ake maduvege sItAbAyiyannu kareyalilla. 
(31kha) Ake maduvege kareyadudu sItAbAyiyannu. 
sambandhisuvudu mattu allagaLeyuvudu 
    idallade, innobba vyaktiya mUlaka kelasa mADisikoLLuva vAkyagaLa 
baLakeyallU  (10.5  nODi)  intaha  allagaLeyuva  kriyArUpada 
baLakeyannu  kANabahudu.  udAharaNegAgi,  innobba  vyaktiya  mUlaka 
kelasavondannu  mADisikoLLuva  badalu  Ata  A  kelasavannu  mADadante 
taDegaTTabEkiddalli  bEDa  illavE  bEDi  emba  kriyArUpada  baLake 
yAguttade. 
(32ka)  nIvu mEle hOgi. 
(32kha) nIvu mEle hOgabEDi. 
(33ka)  rAju manege hOgali. 
(33kha) rAju manege hOguvudu bEDa.

9.3.4 eraDu bAri allagaLeyuvudu 
vAkyavondannu eraDaneya bAri allagaLeyabEkiddalli adara koneyalli 
endu padavannu baLasabEkAguttade. endare, illi ondu allagaLeyuva 
vAkyavannu `ettihELi', adannE innomme allagaLeyalAguttade.  
(34ka)  avanu pattEdAri kate OduttAne. 
(34kha) avanu pattEdAri kate Oduvudilla. 
(34ga)  avanu pattEdAri kate Oduvudillavendilla.  
(34ka)dalli  bandiruva  tiLisuva  vAkyavannu  (34kha)dalli  allagaLeya 
lAgide.  idannE  (34ga)dalli  mattomme  allagaLeyalAgide.  I  rIti 
eraDaneya  bAri  allagaLediruva  vAkya  `ghaTaneyondu  naDeyuttade' 
embudAgi  `allagaLeyada'  arthavannu  koDuvudAdarU,  adakkU  nEra 
vAgi  ondu  ghaTane  naDedide  embudannu  tiLisuva  vAkyakkU  naDuve 
arthadalli vyatyAsavide embudannu gamanisabahudu.  
    mEle  (34ga)  vAkyadalli  eraDaneya  bArige  bandiruva  illa  pada 
modalaneya  bArige  bandiruva  adE  padavannu  hoDedu  hAkiruvu 
dEnO  nija.  AdarU  A  vAkyakke  (34ka)  vAkyada  arthakkinta  svalpa 
maTTige  bhinnavAda  arthavide.  adu  sUcisuva  ghaTane  aparUpavAgi 
mAtra  naDeyuttade  embudAgi  ondu  viSiSTavAda  artha  A  vAkyakke 
sErikoLLuttade. 
9.3.5 aLateyannu allagaLeyuvudu 
ondu  vastuvina  aLate  illavE  parimANavannu  tiLisuva  vAkyavannu 
allagaLedAga,  sAmAnyavAgi  A  vastuvu  A  vAkyadalli  sUcisida 
parimANakkinta  kaDime  parimANadallideyemba  artha  baruttade.  Adare 
intaha  vAkyagaLannu  `sambandhisuva'  rUpadalli  baLasidevAdare  I  rIti 
`kaDime' emba artha baruvudilla. 
(35ka)  I Dabbadalli nAlku sEru akki ide. 
(35kha) I Dabbadalli nAlku sEru akki illa. 
(36ka)  I Dabbadalli akkiyiruvudu nAlku sEru. 
(36kha) I Dabbadalli akkiyiruvudu nAlku sEralla. 
(35kha)  vAkyakke  sAmAnyavAgi  I  Dabbiyalli  nAlku  sEriginta 
kaDime  akki  ide  emba  artha  baruttade.  Adare  (36kha)  vAkyakke  I 
rIti  kaDime  emba  artha  baruvudilla  embudannu  gamanisabahudu. 
Dabbiyalli  nAlku  sEriginta  jAsti  akkiyideyAdalli  (36kha)vannu 
baLasalu sAdhyavide, Adare (35kha)vannu baLasalu sAdhyavAgadu. intaha 
allagaLeyuva  vAkyagaLa  baLakege  bEre  kelavu  udAharaNegaLannu  keLage 
koDalAgide. 
(37ka)  I gODe aydaDi ettara illa. 
(37kha) I gODeya ettara aydaDi alla. 
(38ka)  Ake mUru maylu naDeyalilla. 
(38kha) Ake naDedudu mUru maylalla. 
9.3.6 kelavu viSiSTa padagaLa baLake 
allagaLeyuva  vAkyagaLalli  mAtravE  baLakeyAgaballa  kelavu  viSiSTavAda 
pada mattu padakantegaLu kannaDadallive. ivugaLalli kelavannu kELvigaLallU 
sambandhisuvudu mattu allagaLeyuvudu 
baLasabahudu  10.4.7  nODi).  udAharaNegAgi,  goDave  padavannu 
allagaLeyuva  vAkyagaLalli  illavE  kELvigaLalli  baLasuttEvallade,  itara 
vAkyagaLalli baLasuvudilla. 
(39ka)  Ake yAra goDavegU hOguvudilla. 
(39kha) Ake rAjuvina goDavege hOdudu yAke? 
    yAru,  Enu,  elli  modalAda  savrapadagaLige  U  pratyayavannu 
sErisi tayArisida yArU, EnU, ellU modalAda aniScayArthada 
padagaLU allagaLeyuva vAkyagaLalli illavE kELvigaLalli baraballuvallade 
nEravAgi  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLalli  illavE  sambandhisuva  vAkyagaLalli  bara 
lAravu. 
(40ka)  rAjuvina pATrige yArU baralilla. 
(40kha)  rAjuvina pATrige yArU baralillavE? 
    tiLisuva  vAkyagaLalli  aniScayateyideyAdare  mAtra  antaha 
vAkyagaLalli I padagaLannu baLasalu sAdhya. 
(40ga)  rAjuvina pATrige yArU hOgabahudu. 
intaha aniScayArthaka padagaLa baLakeyalli kANisikoLLuva nibrandhagaLa 
kuritAgi jAsti vivaragaLige bhaT 2003: 167) nODi. 
    idE  rItiyalli  allagaLeyuva  vAkyagaLalli  baLakeyAgadantaha 
(mattu  nEravAgi  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLalli  baLakeyAguva)  bEre  kelavu 
viSiSTavAda  pada  mattu  padakantegaLU  kannaDadallive.  udAharaNegAgi, 
AgalE  padavannu  baLasiruva  keLagina  vAkyavannu  allagaLeyalu  sAdhya 
vAgadu. 
(41)  avaLu AgalE bandiddALe. 
    idallade, allagaLeyuva vAkyagaLalli bahaLa padada badalu sAmAnya 
vAgi jAsti illavE aSTondu embudannu baLasuvudu rUDhi. 
(42ka)  avaLa maduvege bahaLa jana bandiddaru.

(43ka)  cunAvaNeya sabheyalli bahaLa jana sEriddaru. 
(43kha) cunAvaNeya sabheyalli aSTondu jana sEriralilla. 
9.4 sArAmSa 
ondu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyannu  nEravAgi  tiLisuva  badalu  adakkU 
adara  ondu  ghaTakakkU  naDuve  sambandhavide  embudAgi  sUcisalu 
sAdhyavide. idakkAgi sambandhisuva vAkyagaLa baLakeyAguttade. 
    idE  rItiyalli  ondu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyannu  nEravAgi 
tiLisuva badalu adara naDeyuvike illavE iruvikeyannu allagaLeyalu 
sAdhyavide. idakkAgi allagaLeyuva vAkyagaLa baLakeyAguttade. 
    I  eraDu  rItiya  vAkyagaLannU  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLallEnE  kelavu 
badalAvaNegaLannu mADuvudara mUlaka tayArisikoLLalu sAdhyavide.

adhyAya hattu 
mAtina kelasagaLu 
10.1 pIThike 
mAtina mUlaka nAvu halavAru kelasagaLannu naDesaballevu. yAvudAda 
rondu  sangatiyannu  innobbarige  tiLisuvudu  ivugaLalli  atyanta 
prAmukhyavAda  kelasa.  idallade,  tiLiyadiruva  sangatiyannu  bEreyava 
rinda  tiLidukoLLuvudakkAgi  kELviyondannu  baLasuvudu,  mADalu 
sAdhyavillada  kelasavannu  innobbarinda  mADisikoLLuvudakkAgi  avarannu 
bEDikoLLuvudu  illavE  avarige  appaNemADuvudu,  mADabArada 
kelasavannu  mADadante  taDeyuvudu,  modalAda  bEreyU  halavAru 
rItiya kelasagaLannu nAvu mAtina mUlaka naDesaballevu.  
I bEre bEre rItiya  mAtina kelasagaLannu naDesuvudakkAgi kannaDa 
dalli  bEre  bEre  rItiya  vAkyaracaneya  vidhAnagaLu  baLakeyallive. 
intaha kelasagaLannu naDesuvudakkAgiyE baLasabahudAdantaha kelavu pada 
gaLu  kannaDadalliddu,  avannu  baLasi  racisida  horavAkyagaLoLage  vAkya 
vondannirisi hELuvudu intaha vidhAnagaLallondu.  
(1ka)  dEvaru nimage oLLeyadu mADalendu harasuttEne. 
(1kha)  sAlavannu 
tIrisuttEnendu 
nALeyE 
mADuttEne. 
kaDimege nUrAdarU koDabEkendu nanna prArthane.  
(1gha)  I  kAryakramadalli  sahakarisidavarellarigU  nanna  kxtajYate 
gaLu. 
(1Ga)  adhyakSaru bandiddArEnri? 
(1ka) vAkyadalli `harasuva' kelasavannu naDesuvudakkAgi harasu kriyApada 
horavAkyadalli  bandiddu,  `Enendu  harasiddu'  embudannu  adara  oLa 
vAkyavAgi  bandiruva  dEvaru  nimage  oLLeyadu  mADali  embudu 
tiLisuttade.  idE  rItiyalli  (1kha)dalli  ANe  mADi  hELuttEne 
emba  horavAkyavU,  (1ga)dalli  nannaprArthane  emba  horavAkyavU, 
(1gha) dalli nanna kxtajYategaLu emba horavAkyavU mattu (1Ga)dalli 
Enri? emba horavAkyavU avu naDesaballa kelasagaLannu sUcisuttave. 
vAkyagaLallEnE  kelavu  badalAvaNegaLannu  mADi  antaha  badalA 
giruva  vAkyagaLa  mUlaka  mAtina  kelasagaLannu  naDesuvudu  innondu 
vidhAna. 
(2ka)  magu kucriyalli kuLitide. 
(2kha)  magu kucriyalli kuLitideyE? 
(2ga)  magu elli kuLitide? 
(2gha)  magu kucriyalli kuLitirali. 
(2Ga)  magU, kucriyalli kuLituko. 
(2ka)dalli  tiLisuva  kelasavannu  naDesuva  vAkyavondu  bandiddu,  (2kha-
Ga)gaLalli  A  vAkyadallEnE  badalAvaNegaLannu  mADuvudara  mUlaka 
adu nijavE endu kELuvudu, adakke oppige koDuvudu, modalAda 
bEre kelavu kelasagaLalli toDagisalu sAdhyavAguvante mADalAgide. 
idallade,  vAkyavondannu  yAva  rItiyalli  nuDiyalAgide  embu 
dara  mElU  adu  entaha  kAryavannu  naDesaballudu  emba  viSaya 
avalambisiruttade.  udAharaNegAgi,  ondu  vAkyavannu  ettarada  dhvani 
yalli  hELuvudakkU  mattu  taggina  dhvaniyalli  hELuvudakkU  naDuve 
avugaLa mUlaka naDesikoLLabahudAda kelasagaLalli vyatyAsavide. ettarada 
dhvaniyalli  hELi  kELuganannu  hedarisabahudu  mattu  taggina  dhvaniyalli 
hELi Atanannu santaysabahudu.  
ondu  vAkyavannu  yAru  baLasiddAre,  mattu  yArannu  uddESisi 
adannu baLasalAgide embudara mElU vAkyavondu entaha kelasavannu 
naDesaballudu  embudu  avalambisiruttade.  udAharaNegAgi,  mAvina 
marada  hattira  hOgabEDa  emba  vAkyavannu  obba  huDuga  innobba 
huDugana hattira hELiruvanAdare, adu kAvalugAra nODuttiddAne, 
hoDeyabahudu embudAgi `eccarisuva' kelasa mADabahudu. Adare 
adE  vAkyavannu  obba  huDugana  hattira  obba  kAvalugAra  hELiruva 
nAdare,  adu  marada  hattira  A  huDuga  hOgadante  `taDehiDiyuva' 
kelasavannu mADabahudu. 
vAkyavondannu  baLasiruva  sandabhrakkanusAravAgiyU  adu  naDesa 
balla  kelasagaLu  bEre  bErAgiralu  sAdhyavide.  udAharaNegAgi,  kiTike 
teredideyO  emba  vAkyavannu  caLigALi  bIsuttiruva  sandabhradalli 
obba vyakti hELiruvanAdare, `terediddare adannu muccabEku' emba artha 
baruttade,  Adare  adE  vAkyavannu  jAsti  sekheyiruva  sandabhradalli 
hELiruvanAdare, `teredillavAdalli tereyabEku' emba artha baruttade. 
I rIti vAkyavondara mUlaka entaha kelasagaLannu naDesalu sAdhya 
embudu  bEre  bEre  viSayagaLannu  avalambisiddu,  avugaLalli  kelasa 
gaLannu naDesikoDuva horavAkyagaLa baLake mattu vAkyadallEnE naDesuva 
badalAvaNegaLa  baLake  emba  modalaneya  eraDu  viSayagaLannu  mAtra 
I  adhyAyadalli  vivarisalAgide.  yAkendare,  I  eraDu  viSayagaLalli 
mAtra vAkyada oLaracaneyalli vyatyAsagaLu tOribaruttave.  
    mAtina  kelasagaLalli  heccinavU  prAmukhyavAgi  mAtinalli  baLake 
yAguva  vAkyagaLalli  kANisikoLLuttave.  barahadalli  baruva  vAkyagaLalli 
intaha  kelasagaLalli  kelavu  mAtra  kANisikoLLuttave.  I  pustakadalli 
prAmukhyavAgi  barahada  kannaDadalli  baruva  vAkyagaLa  oLaracaneyannu 
vivarisalAgideyAda  kAraNa,  mAtina  kelasagaLalli  kelavannu  mAtravE 
illi vivarisuva avaSyakate kanDubandide. 
10.2 naDesikoDuva padagaLu 
kannaDadalli  sUcisu,  kSamisu,  ASIvradisu,  hAraysu,  svAgatisu, 
mAtukoDu  modalAda  kelavu  kriyApadagaLannAgali  illavE  suLLu, 
appaNe,  kxtajYate,  svAgata,  modalAda  kelavu  nAmapadagaLannAgali 
baLasi, avugaLa mUlaka kelavu mAtina kelasagaLannu naDesalu sAdhyavide.

kriyApadavannu  baLasuvudara  mUlakavU  naDesalu  sAdhyavAgide.  idakke

sAmAnyavAgi  kriyApadagaLa  mUlaka  mAtina  kelasagaLannu  naDesa 
bEkiddalli  avannu  ADuganE  naDesuva  hAge  mattu  avu  mundina 
samayadalli naDeyuva hAge hELuvudu avaSya. itararu naDesuva hAge

10.2.1 kelavu apavAdagaLu 
mElina  niyamakke  kelavu  apavAdagaLive.  udAharaNegAgi,  mAtina

yannu sUcisidAgalU adu naDedu hOguva sAdhyateyide. 
(6ka)  nimmellarigU nAnu kxtajYategaLannu aprisabayasuttEne.

vAguttade. 
mAtina  kelasavondannu  naDesuva  `bayake'yannu  mAtravE  sUcisuva 
(6ka) vAkya mattu antaha kelasavannu naDesuvalli dorakuva `santOSa' 
vannu  mAtravE  sUcisuva  (6kha)  vAkya  iveraDU  avu  naDesabEkA

idE  rItiyalli

Adare,  udghATisu,  ANeyiDu,  kSamisu,  svAgatisu  modalAda 
bEre  kelavu  kriyApadagaLannu  (illavE  avakke  samAnavAda  nAmapada 
gaLannu)  vAkyadalli  baLasidarEnE  avu  naDesaballa  mAtina  kelasagaLu 
naDeyaballuvu emba niyamaviruvante tOruttade.  
idallade, kelavu sandabhragaLalli mAtina kelasagaLannu naDesaballa I 
kriyApadagaLu  sariyAda  kriyArUpadallE  bandiveyAdarU,  avu 
sUcisuva  mAtina  kelasagaLannu  naDesuvudakkAgi  baLakeyAgiruva  badalu 
itara kriyApadagaLa hAge antaha ghaTaneyondu naDeyalideyembudannu 
tiLisuvudakkAgi mAtravE baLakeyAgiralu sAdhyavide. 
nAlku ganTege baruttEnendu mAtu koDuttEne. 
I  vAkyavannu  obba  vyakti  mAtu  koDuva  kelasavannu  naDesuvudakkAgi 
baLasirabahudu, illavE antaha kelasavannu mADaliruvenendu tiLisuvu 
dakkAgi  mAtravE  baLasiralU  bahudu.  eraDaneya  baLakeyalli  adu 
`tiLisuva'  kelasavannu  naDesuttideyallade  `mAtukoDuva'  kelasavannu 
naDesuvudilla. 
10.3 kELuva vAkyagaLu 
tiLiyadiruva sangatiyondannu innobbarinda kELi tiLidukoLLuvudakkAgi 
baLasuva vAkyagaLE `kELuva' vAkyagaLu. kannaDadalli I mAtina kelasakkAgi 
eraDu  rItiya  vAkyagaLu  baLakeyAguttave.  ivannu  `vAkyakELvigaLu' 
mattu `vAkyAnga kELvigaLu' embudAgi hesarisabahudu.  
    vAkyakELvigaLu ondu iDI vAkyavu tiLisuva sangati nijavE endu 
kELuttave. Adare vAkyAnga kELvigaLu vAkyavu tiLisuva sangatiya ondu 
amSa  entahadu  endaSTE  kELuttave.  A  sangatiya  uLida  amSagaLella 
tanage gottiveyendE intaha vAkyAnga kELvigaLannu baLasiruva vyaktiya 
tIrmAnavAgiruttade. 
(10ka)  rAju mangaLUrige hOgiddAnO? 
(10kha) rAju ellige hOgiddAne? 
(10ka) ondu vAkyakELvi, mattu (10kha) ondu vAkyAnga kELvi. (10ka) 
dalli  ondu  iDI  vAkyavu  tiLisuva  sangati  (endare  rAju 
mangaLUrige hOgiddAne embudu) nijavE endu kELalAgide.

tiLisuva sangatiya uLida amSa tanage tiLidide mattu nija embudu I 
kELviyannu baLasuva vyaktiya nambikeyAgide.  
vAkyakELviyalli kELviya vyApti iDI vAkyada mEle bILuvudAda 
kAraNa, adondu kELvi embudanniSTE tiLisidare sAku. idakkAgi vAkyada 
koneyalli  O,  A  illavE  E  pratyayavannu  baLasalAguttade.  idallade 
vAkyada  Sruti  koneyalli  keLage  iLiyade  hAgeyE  uLiyuvanteyU

kELvigaLinda  bhinnavAgiveyembudannu  keLagina  udAharaNegaLalli  kANa

10.3.1  vAkyakELvigaLa svarUpa 
vAkyakELvigaLa  koneyalli  O,  A  illavE  E  pratyayagaLalli  yAvu 
dAdarU ondu baLakeyAguttade. I mUru pratyayagaLu kannaDada bEre 
bEre  UrugaLalli  kANisikoLLuva  mAtina  bhEdagaLAgiddu  barahadallU 
I mUru pratyayagaLannu kANabahudu.  
    udAharaNegAgi mangaLUru kannaDada vAkya kELvigaLa koneyalli O 
pratyaya  kANisikoLLuvudE  jAsti.  idakke  badalu,  maysUru  kannaDada 
vAkyakELvigaLalli A pratyayavE heccAgi kANisikoLLuttade.  
vAkyakELvigaLa  koneyalli  I  rIti  O,  A  illavE  E  pratyayagaLa 
llondu  (athavA  Enu  embudu)  baruvudu  mAtravallade,  vAkya 
mugidAga avugaLa koneyalliruva Sruti keLagiLiyade hAgeyE uLiyu 
ttade,  illavE  svalpa  mElakke  Eruttade.  nijakkU  kannaDada  vAkya 
kELvigaLalli  `avu  kELvigaLu'  embudannu  sUcisuvudu  avugaLa 
koneyalli baruva I Srutiya svarUpa mAtra. adarondige baruva E, 
O mattu AgaLige nEravAgi kELuvikeya arthavilla.  
yAkendare,  tiLisuva  vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  Srutiyannu 
mAtravE badalAyisidAgalU adu kELviyAgaballudu.

10.3.2 vAkyakELvigaLige uttara 
sAmAnyavAgi 
vAkyakELviyondannu  baLasiruva  ADuganige  adu 
sUcisuva  ghaTane  illavE  sangati  nijavO  athavA  suLLO  embudannu 
tiLidukoLLa  bEkendiruttade.  hAgAgi  antaha  kELvigaLige  havdu  athavA 
illa emba uttara koTTare sAkAguttade.  
    kelavu sandabhragaLalli gottilla emba uttaravannU koDalu sAdhya 
videyAdarU  sAmAnyavAgi  ondu  kELviyannu  baLasuvavanu  antaha 
uttaravannu nirIkSisuvudilla. yAkendare, tAnu baLasuva kELvige kELuga 
ninda  uttara  sigabahudemba  abhiprAyaviruvAga  mAtra  tAnE  Ata 
ondu kELviyannu baLasuttAne? 
intaha  kELvigaLu  sUcisuva  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiyannu  allagaLe 
yuvudakkAgi kannaDadalli alla mattu illa emba eraDu padagaLa baLake 
yAguttade.  ivugaLalli  alla  embudu  eraDu  ghaTakagaLa  naDuviruva 
sambandhavannu  allagaLeyuvudakkAgi  baLakeyAguttade  mattu  illa 
embudu ghaTane, sangati modalAdavugaLa iruvikeyannu allagaLeyuvu 
dakkAgi baLakeyAguttade (9.1 mattu 9.3.1 nODi).

rIti  sambandhaviruvudu  nijavalla  embudAgi  A  sambandhavannu  allagaLe 
yalu  alla  padada  baLakeyAgide.  Adare  (23kha)dalli  jAnaki

10.3.3 vAkyakELvigaLalli vayvidhya 
ellA  rItiya  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLannU  vAkyakELvigaLAgi  badalAyisalu 
sAdhyavide.  hAgAgi  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLalli  kANisuva  vayvidhya  vAkyakELvi 
gaLallU kANisikoLLuttade. udAharaNegAgi, tiLisuva vAkyagaLalli ondu 
ghaTane naDedudannu illavE naDeyaliruvudannu tiLisuva vAkyagaLu mattu 
ondu  sangatiya  iruvikeyannu  tiLisuva  vAkyagaLu  embudAgi  eraDu 
rItiyavugaLiveyembudannu nAvu 1.2ralli nODiruvevu.  
    idakke  anuguNavAgi  vAkyakELvigaLallU  ondu  ghaTane  naDedideyE

Adare, I rIti ondu ghaTane naDediruvudu illavE ondu sangati 
iruvudu  nijavE  embudAgi  kELuva  vAkyagaLigU  mattu  antaha 
ghaTaneyannu illavE sangatiyannu allagaLediruvudu nijavE embudAgi 
kELuva vAkyagaLigU naDuve ondu mukhya vyatyAsavide.  
allagaLediruvudu nijavE embudAgi kELuva vyaktige sAmAnyavAgi 
adu  nijaviralAradu  emba  abhiprAyaviruvante  tOruttade.  ghaTane 
naDediruvudu  illavE  sangati  iruvudu  nijavE  embudAgi  kELuvava 
nalli intaha yAva abhiprAyavU iruva hAge kANisuvudilla.  
(31ka)  SrIpati maysUrige hOguttAnO? 
(31kha) SrIpati maysUrige hOguvudillavO?

viSayadalli  yAva  abhiprAyavU  iruva  hAge  kANisuvudilla.  Adare 
(31kha)  vAkyavannu  baLasiruva  vyaktiyalli  Ata  maysUrige  hOga 
liddAne  emba  abhiprAyaviruva  hAge  kANisuttade.  SrIpati  maysUrige 
hOgabEkemba  viSaya  niScitavAgittAdarU  Ata  horaDuva  tayAri 
mADuva  hAge kANisuvudillavAda kAraNa kELuganalli samSaya huTTira 
bEku. adakkE Ata (31kha) vAkyavannu baLasiddAne. 
tiLisuva  vAkyagaLu  ondu  ghaTane  naDediruvudannu  illavE  naDeya 
liruvudannu  hAgeyE  tiLisuva  badalu  adara  bEre  bEre  amSagaLalli 
ondannu mAtra otti hELuttiralu sAdhyavide. idakkAgi A amSada mEle 
ottu koTTu hELabahudu illavE adarondige E pratyayavannu baLasi 
hELabahudu. 
(32ka)  rAju mangaLUrininda ninne bandidda.

adarondige E pratyayavannu baLasi, A ondu amSada kuritAgi mAtra

(33ka)  rAju mangaLUrininda ninne bandiddanO? 
(33kha) rAju mangaLUrininda ninneyE bandiddanO?

pratyEkisi  adu  vAkyada  uLida  amSadondige  sambandhiside  embudannu 
tiLisuvudakkAgi  kannaDadalli  bEreyE  ondu  rItiya  vAkyada  baLake 
yAguttade.  idakkAgi  vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  kriyApadavannu  adara

(9.2 nODi). 
rAju illinda hattu ganTege horaTa.

10.3.4 dxDhIkarisuva kELvigaLu 
tiLisuva  vAkyavondannu  ondu  vAkyakELviyAgi  badalAyisuva  badalu 
A  vAkyavannu  hAgeyE  uLisi,  adu  tiLisuva  sangati  nija  embudannu 
kELugana  mUlaka  dxDhIkarisuvudakkAgi  illavE  athavA  tAnE  emba 
padavannu  adakke  sErisiyU  vAkyakELvigaLannu  tayArisalu  sAdhyavide. 
ondu  vAkya  tiLisuva  sangati  nijavirabahudu  embudAgi  ADugana 
abhiprAyaviruva sandabhragaLalli intaha vAkyakELvigaLa baLakeyAguttade. 
(36ka)  sItege daNivAgideyO? 
(36kha) sItege daNivAgide, allavE? 
(37ka)  lekka baredAgideyO? 
(37kha) lekka baredAgide, tAne? 
(36ka)dalli  ondu  saraLavAda  vAkyakELvi  bandide.  idakke  badalu 
(36kha)  dalli  ondu  dxDhIkarisuva  kELvi  bandide.  (36ka)dalli  sItege 
daNivA  gideyO  athavA  illavO  emba  viSayadalli  A  kELviyannu 
baLasi  davanige  yAva  abhiprAyavU  illa.  Adare  (36kha)vannu 
baLasidavanige  `sItege  daNivAgide'  emba  abhiprAyaviddu,  adannu 
dxDhIkarisuvudakkAgi  Ata  A  vAkyavannu  baLasiddAne.  (37ka-kha)dallU 
hIgeyE. 
allavE  mattu  tAnE  embavugaLa  baLakeya  naDuveyU 
arthadalli vyatyAsavide embudannu gamanisabahudu. tAnE embudannu 
baLasu  vavarige  allavE  embudannu  baLasuvavariginta 
kELuva 
viSayadalli heccu dxDhavAda abhiprAyaviruva hAge kANisuttade. 
vAkyakELvigaLa  koneyalli  baruva  O,  E  modalAdavugaLa  hAge 
dxDhIkarisuva  allavE  (38ka-gha  nODi)  mattu  tAnE  (39ka-gha 
nODi)  embavugaLannU  vAkyada  bEre  bEre  amSagaLige  sErisi  hELalu 
sAdhyavide.  vAkyada ondu amSakkU mattu uLida amSakkU naDuviruva 
sambandhavannu  dxDhIkarisuvudE  intaha  kELvigaLa  uddESavendu  hELa 
bahudu.

10.3.5 badali kELvigaLu 
eraDu  athavA  jAsti  vAkyagaLalli  yAvudu  sari  embudAgi  kELuva 
vAkyagaLu `badali kELvi'gaLu. intaha kELvigaLa mUlakavU ondu iDI 
vAkyavu  tiLisuva  sangati  nijavE  athavA  allavE  endu  tiLiya 
bEkAgideyAda kAraNa ivannU vAkyakELvigaLendE parigaNisabahudu. 
(40ka)  raghu hOdaddu puNegO, bombAyigO? 
(40kha)  avanu pATha OduvudO, katepustaka OduvudO? 
(40ga)  Iga  nIvu  snAna  mADuttIrO  athavA  nAnu  mADa 
bEkO? 
(40gha)  Ake  inTarvyUge  hOdaddu  bengaLUrigO,  cennaygO 
athavA DilligO? 
intaha  badali  kELvigaLigU  mattu  saraLavAda  vAkyakELvigaLigU  naDuve 
ondu  mukhyavAda  vyatyAsavide.  saraLavAda  vAkyakELvigaLige  havdu 
endAgali,  illavE  illa  athavA  alla  endAgali  uttara  koTTare 
sAku,  Adare  intaha  badali  kELvigaLige  uttaravAgi  avu  sUcisuva 
eraDu athavA jAsti sangatigaLalli yAvudAdarU ondannu Arisi hELa 
bEkAguttade.  
    yAkendare,  tAnu  sUcisuva  `badali'  sangatigaLalli  yAvudAdarU 
ondu  sariyirabahudu  embudAgi  intaha  badali  kELviyannu  baLasuva 
vyaktiya abhiprAyaviruttade. hAgAgi intaha kELvigaLige havdu athavA 
illa/alla  endiSTE  uttara  koTTare  kELviyannu  baLasidavanige  samA 
dhAnavAgalAradu. 
10.4. vAkyAnga kELvigaLu 
vAkyAnga  kELviyondannu  baLasuva  vyaktige  avanu  sUcisuva  ghaTaneya 
ondu  amSada  kuritAgi  mAtra  mAhiti  bEkAgiruttade.  uLida  amSa 
gaLella Atanige tiLidiruttade. hAgAgi intaha kELvigaLannu baLasuva vyaktige 
yAva  amSavannu  tiLiyabEkAgideyO  adannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  I 
kELvigaLalli ondu `aniScita' padavannu baLasuva avaSyakateyide. 
(41ka)  rAju ivattu ellige hOgiddAne? 
(41kha) nimma manege ivattu yAru bandiddAre? 
(41ga)  nAvilli eSTu ganTeya varege kAyuttirabEku? 
(41gha) nIvu ninne maduvege yAke baralilla? 
(41Ga) nIvu I manege yAvAga bandiri? 
(41ca) avarige yAva pustaka bEkAgide? 
(41ka)vannu  baLasida  vyaktige  rAju  ivattu  elligO  hOgiddAne 
endu  gottide,  Adare  ellige  endu  tiLidilla;  idE  rItiyalli 
(41kha)  vannu  baLasida  vyaktige  nimma  manege  ivattu  yArO 
bandiddAre  endu  tiLidide,  Adare  bandavaru  yAru  endu  tiLidilla. 
I  rIti  tiLiyadiruva  ondu  amSavannu  mAtra  tiLidukoLLuvudakkAgi 
intaha  vAkyAnga  kELvigaLalli  ellige,  yAru,  eSTu,  yAke, 
yAvAga modalAda aniScita padagaLa baLakeyAguttade. 
vAkyAnga  kELvigaLige  uttara  koDuvavaru  avugaLalli  bandiruva 
aniScita padagaLige samanAgiruva niScita padagaLannu (endare, jAga, vyakti,  
motta,  kAraNa,  samaya  modalAduvannu  tiLisuva  padagaLannu)  baLasa 
bEkAguttade.  udAharaNegAgi  ondu  vAkyAnga  kELviyalli  yAru 
emba  pada  bandideyAdare  adakke  koDuva  uttaradalli  intahavaru 
embudannU,  eSTu  emba  pada  bandideyAdare  intiSTu  embudannU 
tiLisabEkAguttade. 
(42ka)  maduvege yAru hOguttAre? 
(42kha) rAju hOguttAne. 
(43ka)  I manege eSTu khacrAyitu? 
(43kha) enTu lakSa khacrAyitu. 
10.4.1 aniScita padagaLu 
vAkyAnga  kELvigaLa  mUlaka  ondu  sangatiya  bEre  bEre  amSagaLa 
kuritu  mAhiti  sangrahisuvudakkAgi  antaha  vAkyagaLalli  yAru,  Enu, 
yAke,  elli,  yAvAga,  hEge,  eSTu,  entaha  modalAda  aniScita 
padagaLa  baLakeyAguttade  embudannu  mEle  nODiruvevu.  kannaDa 
vyAkaraNagaLalli  I  padagaLannu  sAmAnyavAgi  `praSnArthaka'  padagaLendu 
kareyuvudu rUDhi.  
    Adare  mEle  (10.3.1ralli)  sUcisida  hAge  nijakkU  praSneya 
illavE  kELviya  arthaviruvudu  vAkyada  koneyalli  baruva  Srutiya 
svarUpakkallade  I  aniScita  padagaLigalla.  vAkyada  Sruti  koneyalli  keLage 
iLiyuvudAdare adondu tiLisuva vAkya, mattu hAge keLage iLiyade 
uLiyuvudAdare adondu kELvi. 
bEre  halavu  baLakegaLalli  ivE  padagaLige  aniScitArtha  mAtra  ide 
yallade  kELviya  arthavilla.  udAharaNegAgi,  `athavA'  emba  artha 
viruva  O  pratyayadondige,  illavE  `mattu'  emba  arthaviruva  U 
pratyayadondige  I  padagaLannu  baLasidAga  avakke  aniScitArtha  mAtra 
ideyallade kELviya arthavilla.  
(44ka)  Atana manege yArO bandiddAre. 
(44kha) Ake ivattu beLiggEnE elligO hOgiddALe. 
(44ga)  sOmaSEkharana mane illE ellO ide. 
(44gha) kOpa bandare Ata EnU mADabahudu. 
(44ka-gha)  vAkyagaLalli  yAru,  ellige,  elli  mattu  Enu  emba 
padagaLige  kELviya  arthavilla  embudannu  gamanisabahudu.  aniScita 
vAgiruva  obba  vyakti,  ondu  jAga,  illavE  ondu  kelasavannu  mAtra 
avu sUcisuttave. 
bEreyU  halavu  rItiya  vAkyagaLalli  I  padagaLannu  baLasalu 
sAdhyaviddu antaha baLakegaLallU avakke kELviya arthavilla.  
(45ka)  santeyalli ivattu eSTu jana sEriddAre! 
(45kha) haNavannu elli aDagisiTTiddArendu avanu tanna Dayriyalli 
barediddAne. 
(45ga) I kateyannu yAru barediddArO avarige tale sariyilla. 
oTTu  sEriruva  janara  mottada  kuritAgi  tanna  AScaryavannu  sUcisalu 
(45ka)vannu  baLalAgide.  idaralli  bandiruva  eSTu  emba  padakke  A 
mottada  kuritu  aniScitateyannu  sUcisuva  arthavideyallade  kELviya 
arthavilla.  (45kha)dalli  bandiruva  elli  emba  pada  sUcisuva  jAga 
ADuganige  tiLidilladirabahudu,  Adare  adannu  tiLiyuva  icche  Atanige 
iruva hAge kANisuvudilla.  
    (45ga)dalli  yAru  emba  aniScita  padavannu  eraDu  vAkyagaLannu 
oTTige  sErisi  hELuva  ondu  sAdhanavAgi  baLasalAgide.  illU  I 
padakke kELviya arthavilla. 
yAru,  Enu,  yAke  modalAda  padagaLige  kannaDadalli  I  rIti 
halavu  baLakegaLiddu,  avugaLa  naDuve  heccinavugaLallU  kANisikoLLuva 
arthavendare  aniScitArtha  mAtra.  hAgAgi  avannu  aniScitArthada 
padagaLendu  karedu,  avu  baruva  kelavu  vAkyagaLalli  mAtra  kANisuva 
kELviya  arthakke  antaha  vAkyagaLa  koneyalli  baruva  Srutiya 
svarUpavE  kAraNa  endu  hELuvudE  sariyendu  tOruttade  (I 
viSayada kuritu heccina vivaragaLannu (bhaT 2003 mattu bhaT 2004) 
ralli nODabahudu). 
10.4.2 kELuva angagaLu 
vAkyAnga  kELvigaLa  mUlaka  ondu  vAkyavu  tiLisuva  ghaTane  illavE 
sangatiya  bEre  bEre  amSagaLa  kuritAgi  heccina  mAhitiyannu  kELi 
tiLiyalu  sAdhyavide.  udAharaNegAgi  keLage  (46)nE  vAkyavu  tiLisuva 
ghaTaneyalli  Aru  mukhya  amSagaLiddu,  I  amSagaLa  kuritAgi  heccina 
mAhitiyannu  paDeyalu  Aru  rItiya  vAkyAnga  kELvigaLannu  baLasalu 
sAdhyavide. 
raghu  ninne  nimmannu  nODuvudakkAgi  bengaLUrininda 
TyAksiyalli bandidda. 
(46ka)  yAru bandiddaru? 
(46kha) raghu Enu mADidda? 
(46ga)  yAvAga bandidda? 
(46gha) ellinda bandidda? 
(46Ga)  hEge bandidda?  
(46ca)  yAke bandidda?  
-bandidda. 
-ninne. 
-bengaLUrininda. 
-TyAksiyalli. 
-nimmannu nODuvudakkAgi. 
I  rIti  kriyeya  mukhya  amSagaLannu  mAtravallade  itara  mukhya 
vallada  amSagaLannU  intaha  vAkyAnga  kELvigaLa  mUlaka  kELi  tiLidu 
koLLalu sAdhyavide. 
(46cha)  raghu yArannu nODuvudakkAgi bandidda?  -nimmannu. 
(46ja)  raghu yAva rAtri bandidda? 
-ninne rAtri. 
ondE kELviyalli ondakkinta jAsti aniScita padagaLannu baLasuvudara 
mUlaka  ommegEnE  ondakkinta  jAsti  amSagaLa  kuritAgi  tiLiya 
bEkAgide embudannu sUcisalu sAdhyavide. 
(47ka)  nIvu yAra manege yAvAga hOdiri? 
(47kha) I pustakavannu yAru yAvAga ellinda tandaru? 
(47ga)  yAru yArannu yAvAga elli hatye mADidaru? 
(47gha) I  mElina  mAtannu  yAru  yAvAga  elli  mattu 
yAkAgi hELidaru? 
Adare  mAtinalli  intaha  ondakkinta  jAsti  aniScita  padagaLiruva 
vAkyAnga kELvigaLa baLake bahaLa aparUpavendE hELabahudu. sAmAnya 
vAgi  parIkSegaLalli  koDuva  praSnapatrikegaLalli  mAtravE  intaha  baLake 
kanDubaruttade. mAtinalli illavE barahadalli intaha kELvigaLannu bEre 
bErAgi  oDedu,  ondu  kELviyalli  ondu  aniScita  pada  mAtra  uLi 
diruva hAge baLasuvudE jAsti.

yAru nimmannu barahELidaru?

ellinda nODiddu? hEge nODiddu? 
aniScita  padagaLu  ondannondu  avalambisikonDiruvantaha  kELvi 
gaLalli mAtra avannu I rIti oDedu hELalu sAdyavAgadu.  
(49ka)  yAva kapATinalli yAva vastugaLannirisabEku? 
(49kha) yAva bekkige yAva pAtreyalli hAlu koDabEku? 
intaha  kELvigaLalli  pratiyondu  aniScita  padavU  ondakkinta  jAsti 
vyakti  illavE  vastugaLannu  sUcisuttiddu,  avugaLoLage  anukramavide 
yAdalli  I  aniScita  padagaLannu  eraDeraDu  bAri  baLasuva  krama  kannaDa

(50ka)  yAru yArige yAva yAva pustaka bEku?

idallade, intaha kELvigaLige uttara koDuvAgalU avannu jODi

yannu baLasidavanadAgiruttade.

10.4.3 padavagradalli vyatyAsa 
vAkyAnga  kELvigaLa  mUlaka  tiLidukoLLabEkAgiruva  vAkyAmSa  ondu 
nAmapadada  mUlaka  sUcisuvantahadirabahudu  illavE  ondu  guNa 
padada  mUlaka  sUcisuvantahadirabahudu.  udAharaNegAgi,  yAru 
illavE yAvudu embudannu ondu vAkyAnga kELviyalli baLasidAga 
adakke uttaravAgi ondu nAmapadavannu koDabEkAguttade. 
    idakke  badalu,  yAva  illavE  entaha  embudannu  baLasidalli 
adakke  uttaravAgi  ondu  guNapadavannu  koDabEkAguttade,  illavE 
ondu  guNapadada  sthAnadalli  baraballa  nAmapada  illavE  kriyApadada 
sambandhisuva  rUpavannu  koDabEkAguttade.  eSTu  embudannu  baLasi 
dalli  adakke  uttaravAgi  ondu  eNikeya  illavE  aLateya  padavannu 
koDabEkAguttade. 
(52ka)  yAva cenDu sikkitu? 
(52kha) kempu cenDu sikkitu. 
(53ka)  avaLu entaha sIreyannu uTTukonDiddALe? 
(53kha) avaLu nIlibaNNada sIreyannu uTTukonDiddALe. 
(54ka)  eSTu rUpAyi koTTaru? 
(54kha) nUra ayvattu rUpAyi koTTaru. 
(52ka)  kELviyalli  bandiruva  yAva  emba  padakke  uttaravAgi 
(52kha)dalli kempu emba guNapada bandide, (53ka)dalli banda entaha 
embudakke  badalAgi  (53kha)dalli  nIlibaNNada  emba  guNapadada  sthAna 
dalli baraballa nAmapadada sambandhisuva rUpa bandide, mattu (54ka) 
dalli  banda  eSTu  embudakke  badalAgi  (54kha)dalli  ayvattu  emba 
eNikeya pada bandide. 
vAkyAnga  kELvigaLalli  baruva  aniScita  padagaLu  ghaTaneyondaralli 
bEre  bEre  kelasagaLalli  toDagiruva  vyakti,  vastu  modalAduvannu 
sUcisalu  sAdhyaviddu,  I  kelasagaLannavalambisi  avu  bEre  bEre  vibhakti 
rUpagaLalli baraballuvu. udAharaNegAgi, aniScitavAgiruva vyaktiyobba 
nannu  sUcisuva  yAru  emba  pada  ellA  vibhakti  rUpagaLallU  bara 
balludu.  
(55ka)  ivattu nIvu pUjege yArannu karediddIri? 
(55kha) rAju lekkada pustakavannu yArige koTTa? 
(55ga)  I pustakavannu yArinda tandiri? 
(55gha) I pustaka yArallide? 
idE  rItiyalli  eSTu  emba  pada  vyakti,  vastu  modalAdavugaLa 
eNike  illavE  pramANada  aniScitateyannu  sUcisuttideyAda  kAraNa, 
adarondige  ellA  vibhaktipratyayagaLU  baraballuvu.  adakke  badalAgi 
uttaradalli baraballa eNike illavE pramANavannu sUcisuva padagaLU 
I rIti ellA vibhaktipratyayagaLondigU baraballuvu. 
(56ka)  eSTannu IgalE koDabEkAguttade? 
(56kha) I sankhyeyannu eSTarinda kaLeyabEkAguttade? 
(56ga)  idannu eSTakke konDukonDiri? 
(56gha) nimma SEru eSTaralli nintide? 
eSTu  emba  padakke  (nE  athavA  neya)  pratyayavannu  sErisi, 
eNikeyalli yAvudAdarondu vyakti illavE vastuvina jAga yAvudu 
embudannu kELalu sAdhyavide. Adare I pada nEravAgi vibhakti pratyaya 
gaLondige baralAradu. 
(56Ga) rAju eSTanE klAsinalli kaliyuttiddAne? 
idE  rItiyalli  guNapadagaLa  jAgadalli  baruva  yAva  mattu 
entaha  emba  padagaLu  yAva  vibhaktipratyayadondigU  baralAravu. 
entaha  embudakke  du  pratyayavannu  sErisidAga  mAtra  adu  nAma 
padagaLa  sthAnadalli  baraballudAgiddu,  adakke  bEre  bEre  vibhaktipratyaya 
gaLannu sErisalu sAdhyavAguttade.  
ondu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiya  jAgavannu  tiLiyuvudakkAgi  baLasa 
bEkAgiruva  elli  emba  pada  inda  mattu  ge  emba  eraDu  vibhakti 
pratyayagaLondige mAtra baraballudu. alli pratyayada artha adakkEnE 
ide mattu annu pratyayada avaSyakate adakkilla. 
(57ka)  iSTellA iruvegaLu ellinda banduvu? 
(57kha) meravaNige ellige hOguttide? 
(57ga)  I mUru kAlina ettu nimage elli sikkitu? 
ondu  ghaTane  illavE  sangatiya  samayavannu  tiLiyuvudakkAgi 
baLasabEkAgiruva  yAvAga  emba  pada  inda  pratyayadondige  mAtra 
baraballudu.  ge  pratyayada  arthavannu  I  padada  mUlaka  nEravAgi 
sUcisalu sAdhyavAgadu. 
(58ka)  avaru yAvAgininda I Uralli kelasa mADuttiddAre? 
(58kha) nIvu I manege yAvAga bandiri? 
(58ga)  eSTu divasagaLa varege nIvilli iruttIri? 
Enu  emba  pada  ondu  nAmapadakke  badalAgi  baraballudAdarU 
adannu  annu  pratyayadondige  mAtra  baLasalu  sAdhyavideyallade, 
inda,  ge  illavE  alli  pratyayagaLondige  baLasalu  sAdhyavAgadu.  I 
pada  sUcisuva  aniScitate  bahaLa  sthUlavAgiruvudE  idakke  kAraNavira 
bEku.  
udAharaNegAgi I padavannu ondu kelasavannu naDesiruva illavE 
naDesaliruva prANiya gurutu kELuvalli baLasalu sAdhyavAgadu. intaha 
sandabhragaLalli yAvudu emba padavannE baLasabEkAguttade. 
(59ka)  I cIlavannu kaccihAkiddu yAvudu? 
(59kha) bekkannu hedarisiddu yAvudu? 
idE  rItiyalli  ondu  kadaluvikeya  suru,  kone  illavE  jAga 
vannu  tiLiyabEkAgiruvAgalU  yAvudu  embudannu  baLasalu  sAdhya

padavannu baLasalu sAdhyavAgadu.

sAdhyavide.  kriyApada  vAkyada  kEndravAgiruva  kAraNa  adannu  aniScita 
goLisalu kannaDadalli sAdhanavilla.  
idakke  badalu  mADu  mattu  Agu  emba  kriyApadagaLondige

10.4.4 vacanada aniScitate 
yAru emba bahuvacana rUpa nijakkU sankhye mattu lingagaLa maTTige 
aniScitateyannu  sUcisuvudakkAgi  bandideyallade  `ondakkinta  jAsti' 
emba  arthadalli  bandilla.  udAharaNegAgi,  yArO  obba  emba 
padakanteya  baLakeyalli  yAru  embudu  obba  vyaktiyannu  mAtravE 
sUcisuttade.  illi  yAru  emba  bahuvacana  rUpa  gavravArthavannU 
koDuvudilla embudannu (63)ralli nODabahudu. 
(63)  yArO obba I maDakeyannu oDedu hAkiddAne. 
kannaDadalli  vyaktiyannu  sUcisuva  aniScita  padagaLu  Ekavacanadalli 
bandiveyAdare  avu  sankhye  mattu  linga  iveraDu  viSayagaLallU 
niScitavAgiruttaveyembudannu  yAvanu  mattu  yAvaLu  embavugaLa 
prayOgadalli  kANabahudu.  hAgAgi,  I  eraDu  viSayagaLallU 
aniScitateyannu sUcisabEkAdAga yAru emba bahuvacana rUpavannE 
baLasabEkAguttade.  
idallade  yAvanu  mattu  yAvaLu  emberaDu  padagaLige  svalpa 
maTTige  agavravavannu  sUcisuva  arthavU  ideyAda  kAraNa,  kannaDa 
barahadalli avugaLa baLake aparUpa.  
Enu  mattu  yAvudu  embavugaLa  naDuve  intaha  vyatyAsavilla. 
averaDU samAnavAgi baLakeyalliddu, avugaLalli eraDaneyadakke ondu 
gumpinalliruva  vastugaLalli  ondannu  Arisi  hELabEkemba  viSiSTavAda 
arthavide.  idE  rItiyalli  yAvuvu  embudakkU  ondu  gumpina 
lliruva vastugaLalli kelavannu Arisi hELabEkemba arthavide. 
(63ka)  nimage yAvudu bEku? 
(63kha) nimage Enu bEku? 
(63ga)  I pustakagaLalli nimmavu yAvuvu? 
Adare  ondu  gumpinalliruva  vyaktigaLalli  obbanannu  (athavA 
halavarannu)  Arisi  hELabEkendiruvallU  yAru  embudannE  baLasalu 
sAdhyavide.  yAvanu  mattu  yAvaLu  embuvakke  agavravArthaviruva 
kAraNa intaha sandabhragaLalli avannE baLasabEkemba niyamavilla. 
(64ka)  I huDugaralli lETAgi bandavaru yAru? 
(64kha) I nAlku janaralli kolegAranu yAru? 
(64ga)  A haLE cappaliyannu yAru kaddirabahudu? 
10.4.5 oLavAkyagaLAgi baLake

avalambiside.

(66ka)  eSTu haNa bEkAgabahudendu avaru barediddAre?

sUcisuva  sangati  tiLidide'  emba  arthavannu  avugaLa  horavAkya 
sUcisuttideyAdalli mAtra oLavAkya ondu aniScita vAkyavAgaballudu. 
hAgAgi itara sandabhragaLalli intaha vAkyagaLannu `tiLisuvavAkya'da Sruti 
vinyAsadondige baLasalu sAdhyavAgadu. 
(67ka)  avaru ellirabahudendu nimaganisuttade? 
(67kha) eSTu jana bandirabahudendu Akeya abhiprAya? 
(67ga)  idannu yAvAga koDuttEnendu nIvu hELiddu? 
(67ka-ga)gaLalli  bandiruva  oLavAkyagaLu  avugaLa  ADuganige  tiLidiru 
vantaha  sangatiyannu  sUcisuvudillavAda  kAraNa  avannu  kELvigaLannAgi

vAgadu. 
10.4.6 vAkyAnga kELvigaLalli vayvidhya 
tiLisuva  vAkyagaLalli  baruva  ghaTakavondara  kuritAgi  heccina  mAhiti 
yannu paDeyalu vAkyAnga kELvigaLannu baLasuvevAda kAraNa,  tiLisuva 
vAkyagaLalli kANisuva vayvidhya vAkyAnga kELvigaLallU kANisaballudu.  
    udAharaNegAgi, tiLisuva vAkyagaLa mUlaka  ondu ghaTane naDeya 
lilla illavE naDeyuvudilla embudannU tiLisaballevu.  idakkAgi nAvu 
`allagaLe'yuva  vAkyagaLannu  baLasabEkAguttade.  intaha  vAkyagaLa 
mUlaka  allagaLediruva  ghaTaneya  ondu  ghaTakada  kuritAgi  mAtra 
mAhitiyannu  paDeyabEkAgiddalli  avannu  vAkyAnga  kELvigaLannAgi 
badalAyisikoLLalu sAdhyavide. 
(68ka)  rAju maduvege yAke baralilla? 
(68kha) sIme eNNe nimage yAva angaDiyalli sigalilla? 
(68ga)  I kONeyalli yArige UTa Agilla? 
(68gha) nimmalli TikETannu yAru konDukonDilla? 
(68ka)  vAkyavannu  baLasida  vyaktige  `rAju  maduvege  baralilla'  emba 
viSaya  tiLidide,  Adare  idakke  kAraNavEnendu  mAtra  tiLidilla.  I 
ondu  viSayavannu  tiLiyuvudakkAgi  (68ka)vannu  baLasalAgide.  itara 
vAkyagaLallU hIgeyE. 
tiLisuva  vAkyagaLalli  kriyAvAkya  mattu  viSayavAkya  embudAgi 
eraDu  vidhadavugaLiveyembudannu  (1.2)ralli  nODiruvevu.  kriyA 
vAkyagaLu  ondu  ghaTane  naDediruvudannu  illavE  naDeyaliruvudannu 
tiLisuttave  mattu  viSayavAkyagaLu  ondu  sangatiya  iruvikeyannu 
tiLisuttave.  
mEle koTTiruva vAkyAnga kELvigaLalli heccinavU kriyAvAkyagaLannu 
vAkyAnga  kELvigaLannAgi  badalAyisidantahavugaLu.  intaha  vAkyagaLu 
ghaTanegaLa  ghaTakavondara  kuritAgi  heccina  mAhitiyannu  paDeyalu 
prayatnisuttave. idakke badalu sangatigaLa ghaTakavondara kuritAgi heccina 
mAhitiyannu  paDeyabEkAdAga  antaha  sangatigaLannu  tiLisuvantaha 
kELvigaLannAgi 
viSayavAkyagaLannu 
badalAyisikoLLabEkAguttade. 
vAkyAnga 
(69ka)  kangArOgaLu AsTrEliyAdalli iruttave? 
(69kha) kangArOgaLu elli iruttave? 
(70ka)  Akege eraDu mandi makkaLiddAre? 
(70kha) Akege eSTu mandi makkaLiddAre?

tiLisuva  vAkyagaLu  ondu  sangatiyannu  nEravAgi  tiLisuva  badalu 
adakkU adara ondu ghaTakakkU naDuviruva sambandhavannu tiLisuvantaha 
vAkyagaLAgiralu  sAdhyavide.  intaha  vAkyagaLannU  vAkyAnga  kELvigaLAgi 
badalAyisabahudu.  Adare  hIge  badalAyisuvAga  avugaLa  mUlaka

paDeyalu sAdhya.

yisuvudara  mUlaka  rAju  ghaTakada  kuritAgi  mAtra  heccina 
mAhitiyannu  paDeyalu  sAdhya.  hOguva  samaya  illavE  hOguva 
jAgada  kuritAgi  heccina  mAhitiyannu  paDeyabEkiddalli  antaha  ghaTaka 
gaLannu  vAkyada  uLida  amSadondige  sambandhisuva  vAkyagaLannE  kELvi 
gaLAgi badalAyisalu baLasabEkAguttade.
